ALTERATIONS: Superficial re-formatting of headers, sutta titles, and page numbers adding 'ids,' and tag changes to make the file conform to HTML 5 standards. The lower-case mg [ɱ] has been substituted throughout for the lowercase m-underdot [ɱ]; the lower-case ng [ŋ] has been substituted throughout for the lowercase n-overdot [º]. Content straddling page breaks has been moved to the preceding page. The notice of this change that appeared in the originals has been deleted. In order to fascilitate word search, all annotations have been remove, and the line breaks of the printed edition have been converted into floating text. Otherwise the internal text of the suttas remains untouched.

Saɱyutta-Nikāya
V. Mahā Vaggo

Book I

Magga Saɱyutta

Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammā sambuddhassa

Chapter I: Avijjā Vaggo

1. Avijjā

1. Evam me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapindikassa ārāme|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi Bhikkhavo ti|| ||

Bhadante ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

3. Avijjā bhikkhave pubbaŋgamā akusalānaɱ dhammānam samāpattiyā anudeva ahirikam anottappaɱ|| ||

Avijjāgatassa bhikkhave aviddasuno micchādiṭṭhi pahoti||
micchādiṭṭhissa micchāsaŋkappo pahoti||
micchāsaŋkappassa micchāvācā pahoti||
micchāvācassa micchākammanto pahoti||
micchākammantassa micchāājīvo pahoti||
micchāājīvassa micchāvāyāmo pahoti||
micchāvāyāmassa micchāsati pahoti||
micchāsatissa micchāsamādhi pahoti|| ||

4. Vijjā ca kho bhikkhave pubbaŋgamā kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ samāpattiyā anudeva hirottappaɱ|| ||

Vijjāgatassa bhikkhave viddasuno sammādiṭṭhi pahoti

[page 002]

sammādiṭṭhissa sammāsaŋkāppo pa°||
sammāsaŋkappassa sammāvācā pahoti||
sammāvācassa sammākammanto pahoti||
sammākammantassa sammāājīvo pahoti||
sammāājīvassa sammāvāyāmo pahoti||
sammāvāyāmassa sammāsati pahoti||
sammāsatissa sammāsamādhi pahotī ti|| ||

 

 

2. Upaḍḍham

1. Evam me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sakyesu viharati Sakkaraɱ nāma Sakyānaɱ nigamo|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavantam etad avoca||
Upaḍḍham idam bhante brahmacariyassa yad idaɱ kalyāṇamittatā kalyānasahāyatā kalyāṇasampavaŋkatā ti|| ||

3. Mā hevam Ānanda mā hevam Ānanda|| ||

Sakalam eva hidam Ānanda brahmacariyaɱ yad idaɱ kalyāṇamittatā kalyāṇasahāyatā kalyāṇasampavaŋkatā|| ||

Kalyāṇamittassetam Ānanda bhikkhuno pāṭikaŋkham kalyāṇasahāyassa kalyāṇasampavaŋkassa ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvessati ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bahulīkarissati|| ||

4. Kathañcānanda bhikkhu kalyāṇamitto kalyāṇasahāyo kalyāṇasampavaŋko ariyam atthaŋgikam maggam bahulīkaroti|| ||

Idhānanda bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ virāganissitaɱ nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ||
sammāsaŋkappam bhāveti vivekanissitam ... pe ... sammāvācam bhāveti||
sammākammantam bhāveti||
sammāājīvam bhāveti||
sammāvāyāmam bhāveti||
sammāsatim bhāveti||
sammāsamādhim bhāveti vivekanissitam virāganissitam nirodhanissitam vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho Ānanda bhikkhu kalyāṇamitto kalyaṇasahāyo kalyāṇasampavaŋko ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikaɱ maggam bhāveti ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bahulīkaroti|| ||

[page 003]

5. Tad aminā petam Ānanda pariyāyena veditabbaɱ||
yathā sakalam evidam brahmacariyaɱ yad idam kalyāṇamittatā kalyāṇasahāyatā kalyānasampavaŋkatā|| ||

Mamaɱ hi Ānanda kalyāṇamittam āgamma jātidhammā sattā jātiyā parimuccanti||
jarādhammā sattā jarāya parimuccanti||
maraṇadhammā sattā maraṇena parimuccanti||
sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsadhammā sattā sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsehi parimuccanti|| ||

Iminā kho etam Ānanda pariyāyena veditabbaɱ yathā sakalam evidam brahmacariyaɱ yad idaɱ kalyāṇamittatā kalyāṇasahāyatā kalyāṇasampavaŋkatā ti|| ||

 

 

3. Sāriputto

1. Sāvatthinidānaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Sāriputto yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā ekam antam nisīdi|| ||

Ekam antam nisinno kho āyasmā Sāriputto Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Sakalam evidam bhante brahmacariyaɱ yad idam kalyāṇamittatā kalyāṇasahāyatā kalyāṇasampavaŋkatā ti|| ||

3. Sādhu sādhu Sāriputta||
sakalam evidam Sāriputta brahmacariyaɱ yad idaɱ kalyāṇamittatā kalyāṇasahāyatā kalyāṇasampavaŋkatā ti|| ||

Kalyāṇamittassetaɱ Sāriputta bhikkhave pātikaŋkhaɱ kalyāṇasahāyassa kalyāṇasampavaŋkassa ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvessati ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bahulīkarissati|| ||

4. Kathañca Sāriputta bhikkhu kalyāṇamitto kalyāṇasahāyo kalyāṇasampavaŋko ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāveti ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bahulīkaroti|| ||

Idha Sāriputta bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ virāganissitam nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmim ... pe ...||
sammāsamādhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ virāganissitaɱ nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ

[page 004]

Evaɱ kho Sāriputta bhikkhu kalyāṇamitto kalyāṇasahāyo kalyāṇasampavaŋko ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāveti ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bahulīkaroti|| ||

5. Tad aminā petam Sāriputta pariyāyena veditabbaɱ||
yathā sakalam evidam brahmacariyaɱ yadidaɱ kalyāṇamittatā kalyāṇasahāyatā kalyāṇasampavaŋkatā|| ||

Mamaɱ hi Sāriputta kalyānamittam āgamma jātidhammā sattā jātiyā parimuccanti||
jarādhammā sattā jarāya parimuccanti||
maraṇadhammā sattā maraṇena parimuccanti||
sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsadhammā sattā sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsehi parimuccanti|| ||

Iminā kho etaɱ Sāriputta pariyāyena veditabbaɱ||
yathā sakalam evidam brahmacariyaɱ yad idaɱ kalyāṇamittatā kalyāṇasahāyatā kalyāṇasampavaŋkatā ti|| ||

 

 

4. Brāhmaṇo

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando pubbaṇhasmayam nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Sāvatthim piṇḍāya pāvisi|| ||

3. Addasā kho āyasmā Ānando Jānusoṇiɱ brāhmaṇaɱ sabbasetena vaḷavābhirathena Sāvatthiyā niyyāyantaɱ||
setā sudam assā yuttā honti setālaŋkārā seto ratho setaparivāro setā rasmiyo setā patodalaṭṭhi setaɱ chattaɱ setaɱ uṇhīsaɱ setāni vatthāni setā upāhanā||
setāya sudaɱ vālavījaniyā vījīyati|| ||

Tam enaɱ jano disvā evam āha||
Brahmaɱ vata bho yānam brahmayānarūpaɱ vata hoti|| ||

4. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando Sāvatthiyaɱ piṇḍāya caritvā pacchābhattam piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami

[page 005]

upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi||
Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Idhāham bhante pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Sāvatthim piṇḍāya pāvisiɱ||
addasaɱ khoham bhante Jānusoniɱ brāhmaṇaɱ sabbasetena vaḷavābhirathena Sāvatthiyā niyyāyantam||
setā sudam assā yuttā honti setālaŋkarā seto ratho setaparivāro setā rasmiyo setā patodalaṭṭhi setaɱ chattaɱ setam uṇhīsaɱ setāni vatthāni setā upāhanā setāya sudam vālavījaniyā vījiyyati||
tam enaɱ jano disvā evam āha||
Brahmaɱ vata bho yānaɱ brahmayānarūpaɱ vata hoti||
sakkā nu kho bhante imasmim dhammavinaye brahmayānam paññāpetun ti|| ||

Sakkā Ānandāti Bhagavā avoca|| ||

Imasseva kho etam Ānanda ariyassa aṭṭhaŋgikassa maggassa adhivacanam brahmayānaɱ iti pi dhammayānam iti pi anuttaro saŋgāmavijayo iti pi|| ||

5. Sammādiṭṭhi Ānanda bhāvitā bahulīkatā rāgavinayapariyosānā hoti||
dosavinayapariyosānā hoti||
mohavinayapariyosānā hoti|| ||

Sammāsaŋkappo Ānanda bhāvito bahulīkato rāgavinayapariyosāno hoti||
dosavinayapariyosāno hoti||
mohavinayapariyosāno hoti|| ||

Sammāvācā Ānanda bhāvitā bahulīkatā rāgavinayapāriyosānā hoti||
dosa ... pe ...||
mohavinayapariyosānā hoti|| ||

Sammākammanto Ānanda bhāvito bahulīkato rāgavinayapariyosāno hoti||
dosa ... pe ...||
mohavinayapariyosāno hoti|| ||

Sammāājīvo Ānanda bhāvito bahulīkato rāgavinayapariyosāno hoti||
dosa ... pe ...||
mohavinayapariyosāno hoti|| ||

Sammāvāyāmo Ānanda bhāvito bahulīkato rāgavinayapariyosāno hoti||
dosa ... pe ...||
mohavinayapariyosāno hoti|| ||

Sammāsati Ānanda bhavitā bahulīkatā rāgavinayapariyosānā hoti||
dosa ... pe ...||
mohavinayapariyosānā hoti||
Sammāsamādhi Ānando bhāvito bahulīkato rāgavinayapariyosāno hoti

[page 006]

dosa ... pe ...||
mohavinayapariyosāno hoti|| ||

Iminā kho etam Ānanda pariyāyena veditabbaɱ||
yathā imassevetam ariyassa aṭṭhaŋgikassa maggassa adhivacanam brahmayānam iti pi dhammayānam iti pi anuttaro saŋgāmavijayo iti pīti|| ||

Idam avoca Bhagavā||
idaɱ vatvā sugato athāparam etad avoca satthā|| ||

Yassa saddhā ca paññā ca||
dhammā yuttā sadā dhuraɱ||
hirī īsā mano yottaɱ||
sati ārakkasārathi|| ||

Ratho sīlaparikkhāro||
jhānakkho cakkaviriyo||
upekkhā dhurasamādhi||
anicchā parivāraṇaɱ|| ||

Abyāpādo avihiɱsā||
viveko yassa āvudhaɱ||
titikkhā dhammasannāho||
yogakkhemāya vattati|| ||

Etad attaniyam bhūtaɱ||
brahmayānaɱ anuttaraɱ||
niyyanti dhīrā lokamhā||
aññadatthu jayaɱ jayanti|| ||

 

 

5. Kimattha

1. Sāvatthinidānaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho sambahulā bhikkhū yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkamiɱsu ... pe ... eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu|| ||

3. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū Bhagavantam etad avocuɱ|| ||

Idha no bhante aññatitthiyā paribbājakā amhe evam pucchanti||
Kimatthi yam āvuso samaṇe Gotame brahmacariyam vussatī ti|| ||

Evam puṭṭhā mayam bhante tesam aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam evam vyākaroma|| ||

Dukkhassa kho āvuso pariññattam Bhagavati brahmacariyaɱ vussatī ti||
kacci mayam bhante evam puṭṭhā evam vyākaramānā vuttavādino ceva Bhagavato homa na ca Bhagavantam abhūtena abbhacikkhāma||
dhammassa cānudhammaɱ vyākaroma

[page 007]

na ca koci sahadhammiko vādānuvādo gārayhaɱ ṭhānaɱ āgacchatīti|| ||

4. Taggha tumhe bhikkhave evam puṭṭhā evam vyākaramāṇā vuttavādino ceva me hotha||
na ca mam abhūtena abbhācikkhatha||
dhammassa cānudhammaɱ vyākarotha||
na ca koci sahadhammiko vādānuvādo gārayhaɱ ṭhānam āgacchati|| ||

Dukkhassa hi bhikkhave pariññattam mayi brahmacariyaɱ vussati|| ||

Sace vo bhikkhave aññatitthiyā paribbājakā evam puccheyyuɱ|| ||

Atthi panāvuso maggo atthi paṭipadā etassa dukkhassa pariññāyāti||
evam puṭṭhā tumhe bhikkhave tesam aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam evaɱ vyakareyyātha||
Atthi kho āvuso maggo atthi paṭipadā etassa dukkhassa pariññāyāti|| ||

5. Katamo ca bhikkhave maggo katamā paṭipadā etassa dukkhassa pariññāya|| ||

Ayam eva ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo||
seyyathīdam||
sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ... sammāsamādhi||
ayam bhikkhave maggo ayam paṭipadā etassa dukkhassa pariññāyāti|| ||

6. Evam puṭṭhā tumhe bhikkhave tesam aññatitthivānam paribbājakānam evam vyākareyyāthāti|| ||

 

 

6. Aññataro bhikkhu 1

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami ... pe ...|| ||

3. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Brahmacariyam brahmacariyanti bhante vuccati||
katamaɱ nu kho bhante brahmacariyam katamam brahmacariyapariyosānan ti|| ||

Ayam eva kho bhikkhu ariyo {aṭṭhaŋgiko} maggo brahmacariyaɱ||
seyyathīdaɱ||
Sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ... sammāsamādhi

[page 008]

Yo kho bhikkhu rāgakkhayo dosakkhayo mohakkhayo||
idam brahmacariyapariyosānan ti|| ||

 

 

7. Aññataro bhikkhu 2

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yena Bhagavā ten’ upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā ... pe ...|| ||

3. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Rāgavinayo dosavinayo mohavinayo ti bhante vuccati||
kissa nu kho etam bhante adhivacanaɱ rāgavinayo dosavinayo mohavinayo ti|| ||

Nibbānadhātuyā kho etam bhikkhu adhivacanam rāgavinayo dosavinayo mohavinayoti||
āsavānaɱ khayo tena vuccatī ti|| ||

4. Evam vutte so bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Amatam amatan ti bhante vuccati|| ||

Katanaɱ nu kho bhante amataɱ||
katamo amatagāmimaggo ti|| ||

Yo kho bhikkhu rāgakkhayo dosakkhayo mohakkhayo||
idaɱ vuccati amataɱ|| ||

Ayam eva ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo amatagāmimaggo||
seyyathīdaɱ||
sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ... sammāsamādhī ti|| ||

 

 

8. Vibhaŋgo

1. Sāvatthi nidānam|| ||

2. Ariyaɱ vo bhikkhave aṭṭhaŋgikaɱ maggaɱ desissāmi vibhajissāmi||
taɱ sunātha sādhukam manasi karotha bhāsissāmī ti|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ||
Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

3. Katamo bhikkhave ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo||
seyyathīdaɱ||
sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ... sammāsamādhi|| ||

4. Katamā ca bhikkhave sammādiṭṭhi|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave dukkhe ñāṇaɱ dukkhasamudaye ñāṇam dukkhanirodhe ñāṇaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ñaṇaɱ

[page 009]

ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave sammādiṭṭhi|| ||

5. Katamo ca bhikkhave sammāsaŋkappo|| ||

Yo kho bhikkhave nekkhammasaŋkappo abyāpādasaŋkappo avihiɱsāsaŋkappo||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave sammāsaŋkappo|| ||

6. Katamā ca bhikkhave sammāvācā|| ||

Yā kho bhikkhave musāvādāveramaṇī pisuṇāya vācāya veramaṇī pharusāya vācāya veramaṇī samphappalāpā veramaṇī||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave sammāvācā|| ||

7. Katamo ca bhikkhave sammākammanto|| ||

Yā kho bhikkhave pāṇātipātā veramaṇī adinnādānā veramaṇī abrahmacariyā veramaṇī||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave sammākammanto|| ||

8. Katamo ca bhikkhave sammāājīvo|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako micchāājīvaɱ pahāya sammāājīvena jīvitaɱ kappeti||
ayaɱ vuccati sammāājīvo|| ||

9. Katamo ca bhikkhave sammāvāyamo|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu anuppannānaɱ pāpakānaɱ akusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ anuppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabbhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati||
Uppannānam pāpakānam akusalānaɱ dhammānam pahānāya chandaɱ janeti ... pe ... Anuppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānam uppādāya chandaɱ janeti ... pe ... Uppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabbhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave sammāvāyāmo|| ||

10. Katamā ca bhikkhave sammāsati|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyanupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyyaloke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
vedanāsu vedanānupassi viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyyaloke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
citte cittānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyyaloke abhijjhādomanassaɱ

[page 010]

dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave sammāsati|| ||

Katamo ca bhikkhave sammāsamādhi|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu vivicceva kāmehi vivicca akusalehi dhammehi savitakkam savicāraɱ vivekajaɱ pītisukham pathamaɱ jhānam upasampajja viharati|| ||

Vitakkavicārāṇaɱ vūpasamā ajjhattaɱ sampasādanaɱ cetaso ekodibhavam avitakkam avicāraɱ samādhijam pītisukhaɱ dutiyaɱ jhānam upasampajja viharati|| ||

Pītiyā ca virāgā ca upekhako ca viharati||
sato ca sampajāno sukhañ ca kāyena paṭisaɱvedeti||
yan tam ariyā ācikkhanti upekhako satimā sukhavihārīti tatiyaɱ jhānam upasampajja viharati|| ||

Sukhassa ca pahānā dukkhassa ca pahānā pubbeva somanassadomanassānam atthagamā adukkhamasukham upekhāsatipārisuddhiɱ catutthaɱ jhānam upasampajja viharati|| ||

Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave sammāsamādhī ti|| ||

 

 

9. Suka

1.2. Sāvatthi|| ||

Seyyathā pi bhikkhave sālisukaɱ vā yavasukam vā micchāpaṇihitam hatthena vā pādena vā akkantam hatthaɱ vā pādaɱ vā bhindissati lohitaɱ vā uppādessatīti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati||
taɱ kissa hetu||
micchā paṇihitattā bhikkhave sukassa|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave so vata bhikkhu micchāpaṇihitāya diṭṭhiyā micchāpaṇihitāya maggabhāvanaya avijjaɱ bhindissati vijjam uppādessati nibbānaɱ sacchikarissatīti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati||
taɱ kissa hetu||
micchāpaṇihitattā bhikkhave diṭṭhiyā|| ||

3. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave sālisukaɱ vā yavasukaɱ vā sammāpaṇihitaɱ hatthena vā pādena vā akkantam hatthaɱ vā pādaɱ vā bhindissati||
lohitaɱ vā uppādessatīti thānam etam vijjati||
tam kissa hetu||
sammāpaṇihitattā bhikkhave sukassa

[page 011]

Evam eva kho bhikkhave so vata bhikkhu sammāpaṇihitāya diṭṭhiyā sammāpaṇihitāya maggabhāvanāya avijjaɱ bhindissati vijjam uppādessati nibbānaɱ sacchikarissatī ti ṭhānam etaɱ vijjati||
taɱ kissa hetu||
sammāpaṇihitattā bhikkhave diṭṭhiyā|| ||

4. Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu sammāpaṇihitāya diṭṭhiyā sammāpaṇihitāya maggabhāvanāya avijjam bhindati vijjam uppādeti nibbānam sacchikarotī ti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ virāganissitaɱ nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ ... pe ... sammāsamādhim bhāveti vivekanissitam virāganissitaɱ nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ ceso bhikkhave bhikkhu sammāpaṇihitāya diṭṭhiyā sammāpaṇihitāya maggabhāvanāya avijjam bhindati vijjam uppādeti nibbānam sacchikarotī ti|| ||

 

 

10. Nandiya

1.2. Sāvatthi|| ||

Atha kho Nandiyo paribbājako yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodi||
sammodānīyaɱ kathaɱ sārānīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

3. Ekaɱ antaɱ nisinno kho Nandiyo paribbājako Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Kati nu kho bho Gotama dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā nibbānagamā honti nibbānaparāyanā nibbānapariyosānā ti|| ||

4. Aṭṭhime kho Nandiya dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā nibbānagamā honti nibbānaparāyanā nibbānapariyosānā||
katame aṭṭha||
seyyathīdaɱ sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ... sammāsamādhi|| ||

Ime kho Nandiya aṭṭha dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā nibbānagamā honti nibbānaparayanā nibbānapariyosānā ti|| ||

5. Evaɱ vutte Nandiyo paribbājako Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Abhikkantam bho Gotama abhikkantam bho Gotama

[page 012]

... pe ... upāsakam mam bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatanti|| ||

Avijjāvaggo paṭhamo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Avijjā ca Upaḍḍhañca||
Sāriputto ca Brāhmaṇo||
Kimatthiyo dve Bhikkhu||
Vibhaŋgo Sūka Nandiyoti|| ||

 

 

Chapter II. Vihāra Vaggo

11. Vihāra 1

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Icchāmaham bhikkhave aḍḍhamāsam paṭisalliyituɱ||
namhi kenaci upasaŋkamitabbo aññatra ekena piṇḍapātanīhārakenāti|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho te bhikkhū Bhagavato paṭissutvā nāssudha koci Bhagavantam upasaŋkamati aññatra ekena piṇḍapātanīhārakena|| ||

3. Atha kho Bhagavā tassa aḍḍhamāsassa accayena paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Yena svāham bhikkhave vihārena paṭhamābhisambuddho viharāmi||
tassa padesena vihāsiɱ|| ||

4. So evam pajānāmi micchādiṭṭhipaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
sammādiṭṭhipaccayā pi vedayitaɱ ... pe ... micchāsamādhipaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
sammāsamādhipaccayā pi vedayitaɱ|| ||

Chandapaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
vitakkapaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
saññāpaccayā pi vedayitaɱ|| ||

5. Chando ca avūpasanto hoti||
vitakko ca avūpasanto hoti||
saññā ca avūpasantā hoti||
tappaccayā vedayitaɱ|| ||

[Chando ca vūpasanto hoti||
vitakkā ca avūpasantā honti saññā ca avūpasantā honti

[page 013]

tappaccayā pi vedayitaɱ|| ||

Chando ca vūpasanto hoti||
vitakkā ca vūpasantā honti||
saññā ca avūpasantā honti||
||] Chando ca vūpasanto hoti||
vitakko ca vūpasanto hoti||
saññā ca vūpasantā hoti||
tappaccayā vedayitaɱ|| ||

6. Appattassa pattiyā atthi āyāmaɱ|| ||

tasmim pi ṭhāne anuppatte tappaccayā pi vedayitan ti|| ||

 

 

12. Vihāra 2

1.2. Sāvatthi|| ||

Icchāmāham bhikkhave temāsam patisalliyituɱ|| ||

3. Atha kho Bhagavā tassa temāsassa accayena paṭisallāṇā vuṭṭhito bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Yena svāham bhikkhave vihārena pathamābhisambuddho viharāmi tassa padesena vihāsiɱ|| ||

4. So evam pajānāmi micchādiṭṭhipaccayā vedayitaɱ||
micchādiṭṭhivūpasamapaccayā vedayitaɱ||
sammādiṭṭhipaccayā vedayitaɱ||
sammādiṭṭhivūpasamapaccayā vedayitaɱ||
... pe ...
micchāsamādhipaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
micchāsamādhivūpasamapaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
sammāsamādhipaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
sammāsamādhivūpasamapaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
chandapaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
Chandavūpasamapaccayā p vedayitaɱ||
vitakkapaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
vitakkavūpasamapaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
saññāpaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
saññāvūpasamapaccayā pi vedayitaɱ|| ||

5. Chando ca avūpasanto hoti vitakko ca avūpasanto hoti||
saññā ca avūpasantā hoti tappaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
[Chando ca vūpasanto hoti vitakkā ca avūpasantā honti saññā ca avūpasantā honti tappaccayā pi vedayitaɱ||
Chando ca vūpasanto hoti vitakkā ca vūpasantā honti saññā ca avūpasantā honti tappaccayā pi vedayitam]

[page 014]

chando ca vūpasanto hoti vitakko ca vūpasanto hoti saññā ca vūpasantā hoti tappaccayā vedayitaɱ|| ||

6. Appattassa pattiyā atthi āyāmam||
tasmiɱ ṭhāne anuppatte tappaccayā pi vedayitan ti|| ||

 

 

13. Sekho

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami ... pe ...|| ||

Sekho sekho ti bhante vuccati|| ||

Kittāvatā nu kho bhante sekho hotī ti|| ||

4. Idha [bhikkhave] bhikkhu sekhāya sammādiṭṭhiyā sammannāgato hoti ... pe ... sekhena sammāsamādhinā samannāgato hoti|| ||

Ettāvatā kho bhikkhu sekho hotī ti|| ||

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

18. Kukkuṭārāma 1

1. Evam me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam āyasmā ca Ānando āyasmā ca Bhaddo Pāṭaliputte viharanti Kukkuṭārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Bhaddo sāyaṇhasamayam paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito yenāyasmā Ānando tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmatā Ānandena saddhiɱ sammodi||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

3. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Bhaddo āyasmantam Ānandam etad avoca|| ||

Abrahmacariyaɱ abrahmacariyanti āvuso Ānanda vuccati||
katamaɱ nu kho āvuso abrahmacariyan ti|| ||

[page 016]

Sādhu sādhu āvuso Bhadda bhaddako te āvuso Bhadda ummaggo bhaddakam paṭibhānaɱ kalyāṇī paripucchā|| ||

4. Evaɱ hi tvam āvuso Bhadda pucchasi|| ||

Abrahmacariyam abrahmacariyanti āvuso Ānanda vuccati||
katamaɱ nu kho āvuso abrahmacariyan ti|| ||

Evam āvuso ti|| ||

5. Ayam eva kho āvuso aṭṭhaŋgiko micchāmaggo abrahmacariyaɱ||
seyyathīdam||
Micchādiṭṭhi ... pe ... micchāsamādhī ti|| ||

 

 

19. Kukkuṭārama 2

1.2. Pāṭaliputtanidānaɱ|| ||

3. Brahmacariyam brahmacariyan ti āvuso Ānanda vuccati||
katamaɱ nu kho āvuso brahmacariyam katamam brahmacariyapariyosānan ti|| ||

Sādhu sādhu kho āvuso Bhadda bhaddako kho ti āvuso Bhadda ummaggo bhaddakam paṭibhānam kalyāṇī paripucchā|| ||

4. Evaɱ hi tvam āvuso Bhadda pucchasi Brahmacariyam brahmacariyan ti āvuso Ānanda vuccati||
katamaɱ nu kho āvuso brahmacariyaɱ katamam brahmacariyapariyosānan ti|| ||

Evam āvuso ti|| ||

5. Ayam eva kho āvuso ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo brahmacariyaɱ|| ||

seyyathīdaɱ||
Sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ... sammāsamādhi|| ||

Yo kho āvuso rāgakkhayo dosakkhayo mohakkhayo||
imam brahmacariyapariyosānan ti|| ||

 

 

20. Kukkuṭārama 3

1.2. Pāṭaliputtanidānaɱ|| ||

3. Brahmacariyam brahmacariyan ti āvuso vuccati||
katamaɱ nu kho āvuso brahmacariyaɱ||
katamo brahmacārī||
katamam brahmacariyapariyosānan ti|| ||

[page 017]

Sādhu sādhu āvuso Bhadda||
bhaddako kho te āvuso Bhadda ummaggo bhaddakam paṭibhānaɱ kalyāṇī paripucchā|| ||

4. Evaɱ hi tvam āvuso Bhadda pucchasi|| ||

Brahmacariyam brahmacariyanti āvuso Ānanda vuccati||
katamaɱ nu kho āvuso brahmacariyaɱ||
katamo brahmacārī||
katamam brahmacariyapariyosānan ti|| ||

Evaɱ āvuso ti|| ||

5. Ayam eva kho āvuso ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo brahmacariyaɱ||
seyyathīdaɱ||
Sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ... sammāsamādhi|| ||

Yo kho āvuso iminā ariyena aṭṭhaŋgikena maggena samannāgato ayaɱ vuccati brahmacārī|| ||

Yo kho āvuso rāgakkhayo dosakkhayo mohakkhayo||
idam brahmacariyapariyosānan ti|| ||

Imesam tiṇṇaɱ suttantantānam ekanidānaɱ|| ||

Vihāravaggo dutiyo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Dve Vihārā ca Sekho ca||
Uppādā apare duve||
Parisuddhena dve vuttā Kukkuṭārāmena tayo ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter III. Micchatta Vaggo

27. Kumbha

28. Samādhi

1.2. Sāvatthi|| ||

Tatravoca|| ||

taɱ suṇātha|| ||

seyyathīdaɱ||
Sammādiṭṭhi sammāsaŋkappo ° vācā °kammanto °ājīvo °āyāmo °sati|| ||

ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave ariyo sammāsamādhi saupaniso iti pi||
saparikkhāro iti pī ti|| ||

... pe ...||

30. Uttiya or Uttika

1.2. Sāvatthi|| ||

3. Atha kho āyasmā Uttiyo yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
... pe ...|| ||

4. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Uttiyo Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Idha mayham bhante rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaɱ cetaso parivitakko udapādi|| ||

Pañca kāmaguṇā vuttā Bhagavatā||
katame nu kho pañca kāmaguṇā Bhagavatā ti|| ||

5. Sādhu sādhu Uttiya||
pañcime kho Uttiya kāmaguṇā vuttā mayā|| ||

Katame pañca?|| ||

Cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmupasaɱhitā rajanīyā||
sotaviññeyyā saddā||
ghānaviññeyyā gandhā||
jivhaviññeyyā rasā||
kāyaviññeyyā phoṭṭhabbā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmupasaɱhitā rajanīyā|| ||

Ime kho Uttiya pañcakāmaguṇā vuttā mayā|| ||

6. Imesaɱ kho Uttiya pañcannaɱ kāmaguṇānam pahānāya ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo|| ||

Katamo ariyo aṭṭhāŋgiko maggo|| ||

Seyyathīdaɱ||
sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ... sammāsamādhi|| ||

Imesaɱ kho Uttiya pañcannaɱ kāmaguṇānam pahānāya ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

Micchattavaggo tatiyo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Micchattam Akusalaɱ||
duve Paṭipadā pi ca||
dve Sappurisena Kumbho||
Samādhi Vedan-Uttiyenāti|| ||

idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca satthā|| ||

dhamme dhammānuvattino||
te janā pāram essanti||
maccudheyyaɱ suduttaraɱ|| ||

Okā anokam āgamma||
viveke yattha dūramam|| ||

hitvā kāme akiñcano||
pariyodapeyya attānaɱ||

ādānapaṭinissagge||

Aññatitthiya Peyyālo

41. Virāga

1. Sāvatthinidānaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho sambahulā bhikkhū- °etad avocuɱ|| ||

Kim atthi yam āvuso samaṇe Gotame brahmacariyaɱ vussatī ti||
evam puṭṭhā tumhe bhikkhave tesam aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam evam vyākareyyātha|| ||

Rāgavirāgatthaɱ kho āvuso Bhagavati brahmacariyaɱ vussatī ti|| ||

4. Sace pana vo bhikkhave aññatitthiyā paribbājakā evam puccheyyuɱ|| ||

Atthi panāvuso atthi paṭipadā rāgavirāgāyā ti||
evam puṭṭhā tumhe bhikkhave tesam añña- parib- evam vyākareyyātha|| ||

Atthi kho avuso maggo atthi paṭipadā rāgavirāgāyāti|| ||

... pe ...||
sammāsamādhi|| ||

48. Anupādāya

2. Sa ce vo bhikkhave aññatitthiyā paribbājakā evam puccheyyuɱ|| ||

Aññatitthiya-peyyālo|| ||

Chapter V. Appamāda Vaggo

139. Tathāgata

I. Viveka°

1. Sāvatthinidānaɱ|| ||

2. Yāvatā bhikkhave sattā apadā vā dvipadā vā catuppadā vā bahuppadā vā rūpino vā arūpino vā saññino vā asaññino vā nevasaññināsaññino vā

[page 042]

Tathāgato tesam aggam akkhāyati arahaɱ sammāsambuddho||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ye keci kusalā dhammā sabbe te appamādamūlakā appamādasamosaraṇā||
appamādo tesaɱ dhammānam aggam akkhāyati|| ||

3. Appamattassetam bhikkhave bhikkhuno paṭikaŋkhaɱ ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvessati a° a° maggam bahulīkarissati|| ||

Kathañ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu appamatto ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāveti a° a° maggam bahulīkaroti|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ virāganissitaɱ nirodhanissitam vossaggaparināmim ... pe ... sammāsamādhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ virāganissitaɱ nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

5. Evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu appamatto ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāveti a° a° maggam bahulīkarotīti|| ||

Uparitiṇṇaɱ suttānaɱ vitthāretabbanti|| ||

II. Rāgavinaya

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti rāgavinayapariyosānaɱ dosavinayapariyosānaɱ mohavinayapariyosānaɱ ... pe ... sammāsamādhim bhāveti rāgavinaya- dosavinaya- mohavinayapariyosānaɱ|| ||

[page 043]

III. Amata°

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti amatogadham amataparāyanam amatapariyosānaɱ ... pe ... sammāsamādhim bhāveti amatogadham amataparāyanam amatapariyosānaɱ|| ||

IV. (Nibbāna°)

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti nibbānaninnaɱ nibbānapoṇam nibbānapabbhāraɱ ... pe ... sammāsamādhim bhāveti nibbānaninnaɱ nibbānapoṇam nibbānapabbhāraɱ|| ||

 

 

140. Padam (I-IV)

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave yāni kānici jaŋgamānaɱ pāṇānam padajātāni sabbāni tāni hatthipade samodhānaɱ gacchanti||
hatthipadaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam mahantattena||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ye keci kusalā dhammā sabbe te appamādamūlakā appamādasamosaraṇā||
appamādo tesaɱ dhammānam aggam akkhāyati|| ||

3. Appamattassetam bhikkhave bhikkhuno pāṭikaŋkhaɱ ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvessati a° a° maggam bahulīkarissati ... pe ...|| ||

kūṭaɱ tāsam aggam akkhāyati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave|| ||

Yathā heṭṭhimasuttantam evaɱ vitthāretabbaɱ|| ||

evam eva kho bhikkhave||
... pe ...|| ||

[page 045]

 

 

148. Vattham (I-IV)

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave yāni kānici tantāvutānaɱ vatthānaɱ||
kāsikaɱ vatthaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ye keci kusalā dhammā sabbe te appamādamūlakā appamādasamosaraṇā||
appamādo tesam dhammānam aggam akkhāyati||
3. Appamattassetam bhikkhave bhikkhuno pāṭikaŋkham ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvessati a° a° maggam bahulīkarissatī ti|| ||

Kathañ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu appamatto ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāveti a° a° maggam bahulīkaroti|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ virāga- nirodha- nissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ||
... pe ...
sammāsamādhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ virāganissitam nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

5. Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu appamatto ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāveti ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bahulīkarotī ti|| ||

Appamādavaggo pañcamo|| ||

Sabbam eva sāvatthinidānaɱ|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Tathāgatam Padaɱ Kūṭam||
Mūlaɱ Sāro ca Vassikaɱ||
Rājā Candima-Suriyā ca||
Vatthena dasamam padaɱ||
Yad api Tathāgataɱ tad api vitthāretabbaɱ|| ||

 

 

Chapter VI. Balakaranīya Vaggo

1. Sāvatthinidānaɱ|| ||

149. Balam

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci balakaraṇīyā kammantā karīyanti||
sabbe te pathaviɱ nissāya pathaviyam patiṭṭhāya evam eva te balakaraṇīya kammantā karīyanti

[page 046]

Evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāveti a° a° maggam bahulīkaroti|| ||

Kathañ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya a° a° maggam bhāveti a° a° maggam bahulīkaroti|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti vivekanissitam virāganissitam nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ||
... pe ...||
sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka- virāganirodhanissitaɱ vossaggaparināmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho abhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya a° a° maggam bhāveti||
a° a° maggam bahulīkarotī ti|| ||

Paragaŋgāpeyyālīvaṇṇiyato paripuṇṇasuttan ti vitthāramaggī|| ||

 

 

150. Bījā

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci bījagāmā bhūtagāmā vuddhim viruḷhim vepullaɱ āppajjanti||
sabbe te pathaviɱ nissāya pathaviyam patiṭṭhāya evam ete bījagāmā bhūtagāmā vuddhim virūḷhim vepullam āpajjanti||
evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlam nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto vuddhiɱ virūḷhiɱ vepullam pāpuṇāti dhammesu|| ||

Kathañ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya a° a° maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto vuddhiɱ {virūḷhiɱ} vepullam pāpuṇāti dhammesu|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ ... pe ... sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka- virāganirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ

[page 047]

evam kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya a° a° bhāvento a° abahulīkaronto vuddhiɱ {virūḷhiɱ vepullam} papuṇāti dhammesū ti|| ||

 

 

151. Nāgo

2. Himavantam bhikkhave pabbatarājaɱ nissāya nāgā kāyaɱ vaḍḍhenti balam gāhenti|| ||

Te tattha kāyaɱ vaḍḍhetvā balam gāhetvā kusubbhe otaranti||
kusubbhe otaritvā mahāsobbhe otaranti||
mahāsobbhe otaritvā kunnadiyo otaranti||
kunnadiyo otaritvā mahānadiyo otaranti||
mahānadiyo otaritvā mahāsamuddaɱ sāgaram otaranti||
te tattha mahantataɱ vepallatam āpajjanti kāyena|| ||

3. Evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlam nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvento a° amaggam bahulīkaronto mahantatam vepullatam pāpuṇāti dhammesu|| ||

Kathañ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvento ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bahulīkaronto mahantataɱ vepullatam pāpuṇāti dhammesu|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti||
sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka° viraga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggaparināmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvento aa- maggaɱ bahulīkaronto mahantatam vepullatam pāpuṇāti dhammesū ti|| ||

 

 

152. Rukkho

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave rukkho pācīnaninno pācī napoṇo pācīnapabbhāro||
so mūlechinno katamena papātena papateyyāti|| ||

[page 048]

Yena bhante ninno yena poṇo yena pabbhāro ti|| ||

3. Evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto nibbānaninno hoti nibbānapoṇo nibbānapabbhāro|| ||

Kathañ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu a° a° maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto nibbānaninno hoti nibbānapoṇo nibbānapabbhāro|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti viveka° ... pe ...
sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu a° a° maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto nibbānaninno hoti nibbānapoṇo nibbānapabbhāro ti|| ||

 

 

153. Kumbho

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave kumbho nikkujjo vamateva udakaɱ no paccāvamati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto vamateva pāpake akusale dhamme no paccāvamati|| ||

Kathañ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu a° a° maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto vamateva pāpake akusale dhamme no paccāvamati|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti viveka°||
... pe ...
sammāsamādhim bhaveti viveva- virāga- nirodhanisitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ||
evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu a° amaggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto vamateva pāpake akusale dhamme no paccāvamatī ti|| ||

 

 

154. Sukiya

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave sālisūkaɱ vā yavasūkaɱ vā sammāpaṇihitaɱ hatthena vā pādena vā akkantaɱ hatthaɱ vā pādaɱ vā chijjati lohitaɱ vā uppādessatī ti ṭhānam etam vijjati|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

sammāpaṇihitattā bhikkhave sūkassa|| ||

[page 049]

3. Evam eva kho so vata bhikkhu sammāpaṇihitāya maggabhāvanāya avijjam chijjati vijjam uppādessati nibbānaɱ sacchikarissatīti||
ṭhānam etaɱ vijjati||
taɱ kissa hetu||
sammāpaṇihitattā bhikkhave diṭṭhiyā|| ||

Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu sammāpaṇihitāya diṭṭhiyā sammāpaṇihitāya maggabhāvanāya avijjam bhindati vijjam uppādeti nibbānam sacchikaroti|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ ... pe ... sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka- virāganirodhanissitam vossaggaparināmiɱ||
evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sammāpaṇihitāya diṭṭhiyā sammāpaṇihitāya maggabhāvanāya avijjam bhindati vijjam uppādeti nibbānam sacchikarotī ti|| ||

 

 

155. Ākāsa

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ākāse vividhā vātā vāyanti||
puratthimā pi vātā vāyanti||
pacchimā pi vātā vāyanti||
uttarā pi vātā vāyanti||
dakkhiṇā pi vātā vāyanti||
sarajā pi vātā vāyanti||
arajā pi vātā vāyanti||
sītā pi vātā vāyanti||
uṇhāpi vātā vāyanti||
parittā pi vātā vāyanti||
adhimattā pi vātā vāyanti|| ||

3. Evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhuno ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvayato a° a° maggam bahulīkaroto cattāro pi satipaṭṭhānā bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchanti||
cattāro pi sammappadhānā°||
cattāro pi iddhipādā||
pañca pi indriyāni°||
pañca pi balāni°||
satta pi bojjhaŋgā bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchanti|| ||

Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhuno a° a° bhāvayato a° a° maggam bahulīkaroto cattāro pi satipaṭṭhānā||
cattāro pi sammappadhānā||
cattāro pi iddhipādā||
pañca pi indriyāni||
pañca pi balāni||
satta pi bojjhaŋgā bhāvanā pāripūrim gacchanti|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhu bhikkhave sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti ... pe ... sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhuno a° a maggam bhāvayato ā- a° maggam bahulīkaroto cattāro pi satipaṭṭhānā

[page 050]

cattaro pi sammappadhānā||
cattāro pi iddhipādā||
pañca pi indriyāni||
pañca pi balāni||
satta pi bojjhaŋgā bhāvanā paripūrim gacchantī ti|| ||

 

 

156. Megha 1

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave gimhānam pacchime māse uggataɱ rajojallaɱ tam enam mahā akālamegho ṭhānaso antaradhāpeti vūpasameti|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu a° a° maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto uppannuppānne pāpake akusale dhamme thānaso antaradhāpeti vūpasameti|| ||

Kathañca pana bhikkhave bhikkhu a° a° maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto uppannuppanne pāpake akusale dhamme thānaso antaradhāpeti vūpasameti|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti||
... pe ...||
sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ||
evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu a° amaggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto uppannuppanne pāpake akusale dhamme ṭhānaso antaradhāpeti vūpasametīti|| ||

 

 

157. Megha 2

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave uppannam mahāmegham tam evam mahāvāto antarāyeva antaradhāpeti vūpasameti||
evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu a° a° aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto uppannuppanne pāpake akusale dhamme antarāyeva antaradhāpeti vūpasameti|| ||

Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu a° a° maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto uppannuppanne pāpake akusale dhamme antarāyeva antaradhāpeti vūpasameti|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhiɱ bhāveti||
... pe ...||
sammāsamāddhiɱ bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ

[page 051]

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu a° a° maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto uppannuppanne pāpake akusale dhamme antarāyeva antaradhāpeti vūpasametī ti|| ||

 

 

158. Nāvā

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave sāmuddikāya nāvāya vettabandhanabandhāya chamasāni udake pariyenāya hemantikena thalam ukkhittāya vātātapaparetāni bandhanāni tāni pāvussakena meghena abhippavuṭṭhāni appakasireneva paṭipassambhanti pūtikāni bhavanti||
evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhuno a° a° maggam bhāvayato a° a° maggam bahulīkaroto appakasireneva saŋyojanāni paṭipassambhanti pūtikāni bhavanti|| ||

Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhuno a° a° maggam bhāvayato a° a° maggam bahulīkaroto appakasireneva saŋyojanāni paṭipassambhanti pūtikāni bhavanti|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti ... pe ... Sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhuno a° a° maggam bhāvayato a° a° maggam bahulīkaroto appakasireneva saŋyojanāni paṭipassambhanti pūtikāni bhavantī ti|| ||

 

 

159. Āgantukā

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave āgantukāgāraɱ tattha puratthimāya pi disāya āgantvā vāsaɱ kappenti||
pacchimāya pi disāya āgantvā vāsaɱ kappenti||
uttarāya pi disāya āgantvā vāsam kappenti||
dakkhiṇāya pi āgantvā disāya vāsaɱ kappenti||
khattiyā pi āgantvā vāsaɱ kappenti||
brāhmaṇā pi āgantvā vāsaɱ kappenti

[page 052]

vessā pi āgantvā vāsaɱ kappenti||
suddā pi āgantvā vāsaɱ kappenti|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto ye dhammā abhiññā pariññeyyā te dhamme abhiññā parijānāti ... pe ... ye dhammā abhiññā pahātabbā te dhamme abhiññā pajahati||
ye dhammā abhiññā sacchikātabbā te dhamme abhiññā sacchikaroti||
ye dhammā abhiññā bhāvetabbā te dhamme abhiññā bhāveti|| ||

3. Katame ca bhikkhave dhammā abhiññā pariññeyyā||
pañcupādānakkhandhā tissa vacaniyaɱ||
katāme pañca||
seyyathīdaɱ||
Rūpupādānakkhandho||
la [pe] viññāṇupādānakkhandho|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave dhammā abhiññā pariññeyyā|| ||

4. Katame ca bhikkhave dhammā abhiññā pahātabbā|| ||

Avijjā ca bhavataṇhā ca ime bhikkhave dhammā abhiññā pahātabbā|| ||

5. Katame ca bhikkhave dhammā abhiññā sacchikātabbā||
vijjā ca vimutti ca ime bhikkhave dhammā abhiññā sacchikātabbā|| ||

6. Katame ca bhikkhave dhammā abhiññā bhāvetabbā||
samatho ca vipassanā ca ime bhikkhave dhammā abhiññā bhāvetabbā|| ||

7. Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto ye dhammā abhiññā pariññeyyā te dhamme abhiññā parijānāti||
... pe ...||
ye dhammā abhiññā bhāvetabbā te dhamme abhiññā bhāveti|| ||

8. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti||
... pe ...||
sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu a° a° maggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto ye dhammā abhiññā pariññeyyā te dhamme abhiññā parijānāti ... pe ... ye dhammā abhiñña pahātabbā te dhamme abhiññā pajahati||
ye dhammā abhiññā sacchikātabbā te dhamme abhiññā sacchikaroti

[page 053]

ye dhammā abhiññā bhāvetabbā te dhamme abhiññā bhāvetī ti|| ||

 

 

160. Nadī

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave Gaŋgā nadī pācīnaninnā pācīnapoṇā pācīnapabbhārā||
atha mahā janakāyo āgaccheyya kuddālapiṭakam ādāya Mayam imaɱ Gaŋgaɱ nadim pacchāninnaɱ karissāma pacchāpoṇam pacchāpabbhāranti|| ||

Taɱ kim māññatha bhikkhave||
api nu so mahājanakāyo Gaŋgaɱ nadim pacchāninnaɱ kāreyya pacchāpoṇam pacchāpabbhāran ti|| ||

No hetam bhante|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

Gaŋgā bhante nadī pācīnaninnā pācīnapoṇā pācīnapabbharā||
sā na sukarā pacchāninnaɱ kātum pacchāpoṇam pacchāpabbhāraɱ||
yāvadeva pana so mahā janakāyo kilamathassa vighātassa bhāgī assā ti|| ||

3. Evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhum ariyam aṭṭhaŋgikam maggam bhāventam ariyam a° maggam bahulīkarontam rājāno vā rājamahāmattā vā mittā vā amaccā vā ñāti vā sālohitā vā bhogehi abhihaṭṭhum pavāreyyuɱ|| ||

Ehambho purisa kiɱ te ime kāsāvā anudahanti kim muṇḍo kapālam anusaɱcarasi||
ehi hīnāyāvattitvā bhoge ca bhuñjassa puññāni ca karohī ti|| ||

So vata bhikkhave bhikkhu a° amaggam bhāvento a° a° maggam bahulīkaronto sikkham paccakkhāya hīnāyāvattissati||
netam ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

Yañhitam bhikkhave cittaɱ dīgharattaɱ vivekaninnaɱ vivekapoṇam vivekapabbhāram taɱ vata hīnāyāvattissatī ti netam ṭhānam vijjati|| ||

Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu a° a° maggam bhāveti a° a° maggam bahulīkaroti|| ||

[page 054]

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ ... pe ... sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka- virāganirodhanissitaɱ vossaggaparināmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu a° a° maggam bhāveti a° a° maggam bahulīkarotī ti|| ||

Yad api balakaraṇīyaɱ tad api vitthāretabbaɱ|| ||

Balakaraṇīyavaggo chaṭṭho|| ||

Balaɱ Bījañca Nāgoca||
Rukkho Kumbhena Sūkiyā||
Ākāsena ca dve Meghā||
Nāvā Āgantukā Nadīti|| ||

 

 

Chapter VII. Esana Vaggo

1. Sāvatthinidānaɱ|| ||

161. Esanā

(I. Abhiññā)

2. Tisso imā bhikkhave esanā||
katamā tisso|| ||

Kāmesanā bhavesanā brahmacariyesanā|| ||

Imā kho bhikkhave tisso esanā|| ||

Imāsam kho bhikkhave tissannam esanānam abhiññāya ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo||
katamo ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ||
... pe ...||
sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka- virāganirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannam esanānam abhiññāya ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

4—5. °sammāsamādhim bhāveti rāga° dosa° mohapariyosānaɱ|| ||

6—7. °sammāsamāḍhim bhāveti amatogadham amataparāyanaɱ amatapariyosānam||

[page 055]

8—9. °sammāsamādhim bhāveti nibbānaninnam nibbānapoṇam nibbānapabbhāraɱ°|| ||

(II. Pariññā)

10—17. Tisso imā bhikkhave esanā||
katamā tisso|| ||

Kāmesanā bhavesanā brahmacariyesanā||
imā kho bhikkhave tisso esanā|| ||

Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannam esanānam pariññāya ... pe ... ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti||
... pe ...|| ||

Yad api abhiññā tad api pariññāya vitthāretabbaɱ|| ||

(III. Parikkhaya)

18—25. Tisso imā bhikkhave esanā||
katamā tisso|| ||

Kāmesanā bhavesanā brahmacariyesanā||
imā kho bhikkhave tisso esanā|| ||

Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannam esanānam parikkhayāya ... pe ... ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

Yad api abhiññā tad api parikkhayāya vitthāretabbaɱ|| ||

(IV. Pahāna)

26—33. tisso imā bhikkhave esanā|| ||

Katamā tisso?|| ||

Kāmesanā bhavesanā brahmacariyesanā||
imā kho bhikkhave tisso esanā|| ||

Imāsam kho bhikkhave tissannam esanānam pahānāya [pe] ||
ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

Yad api abhiññā tad api pahānāya vitthāretabbaɱ|| ||

[page 056]

 

 

162. Vidhā (I-IV)

[2—33] Tisso imā bhikkhave vidhā||
katamā tisso|| ||

Seyyo ham asmīti vidhā||
Sadiso ham asmīti vidhā||
Hīno ham asmīti vidhā|| ||

Imā kho bhikkhave tisso vidhā|| ||

Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannaɱ vidhānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo|| ||

katamo ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti ... pe ...||
sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitam vossaggapariṇāmim|| ||

Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannaɱ vidhānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

Yathā esanā evam vitthāretabbā|| ||

 

 

163. Āsavo (I-IV)

[2—33] Tayo me bhikkhave āsavā||
katame tayo|| ||

Kāmāsavo bhavāsavo avijjāsavo|| ||
ime kho bhikkhave tayo āsavā|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave tiṇṇannam āsavānam abhiññāya pariññāyaparikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ...ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

 

 

164. Bhavo (I-IV)

[2—33] Tayo me bhikkhave bhavā||
katame tayo|| ||

Kāmabhavo rūpabhavo arūpabhavo||
ime kho bhikkhave tayo bhavā|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave tiṇṇannam bhavānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ... ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

 

 

165. Dukkhatā (I-IV)

[2—33] Tisso imā bhikkhave dukkhatā||
katamā tisso|| ||

Dukkhadukkhatā saŋkhāradukkhatā vipariṇāmadukkhatā||
imā kho bhikkhave tisso dukkhatā|| ||

Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannam dukkhatānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ... ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

[page 057]

 

 

166. Khilā (I-IV)

[2—33] Tayo me bhikkhave khi... pe ...||

Rāgo khilo doso khilo moho khilo||
ime kho bhikkhave tayo khilā|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave tiṇṇannam khilānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ... ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

 

 

167. Malam (I-IV)

[2—33] Tīṇimāni bhikkhave malāni||
katamāni tīṇi|| ||

Rāgo malam doso malam moho malam||
imāni kho bhikkhave tīṇi malāni|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave tiṇṇannam malānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya||
... pe ...
ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

 

 

168. Nighā (I-IV)

169. Vedanā (I-IV)

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

[2—33] Tisso ima vedanā.|| ||

Katamā tisso?|| ||

Sukhā vedanā dukkhā vedanā adukkhamasukhā vedanā||
imā kho bhikkhave tisso vedanā|| ||

Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannaɱ vedanānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ... ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

 

 

170. Taṇhā (viveka°) (I-IV)

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

[page 058]

[2—3] Tisso imā bhikkhave taṇhā||
katamā tisso|| ||

Kāmataṇhā bhavataṇhā vibhavataṇhā||
imā kho bhikkhave tisso taṇhā|| ||

Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannam taṇhānaɱ abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo||
katamo ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti vivekaviraga° nirodhanissittaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ ... pe ... sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitam vossaggapariṇamiɱ|| ||

Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannam taṇhānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ... ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

 

 

170. Tasinā or Taṇhā 2—4 (Rāgavinaya°) (I-IV)

[4—33] Tisso imā bhikkhave tasinā ... pe ...Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannaɱ tasinānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ... rāgavinaya- dosavimaya- mohavinayapariyosānam ... pe ... amatogadham amataparāyanam amatapariyosānam ... pe ... nibbānaninnaɱ nibbānapoṇaɱ nibbānapabbhāraɱ|| ||

Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannam tasinānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ...ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

Esanavaggo sattamo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Esanā Vidhā Āsavo||
Bhavo Dukkhatā Khi... pe ...||
Malaɱ Nigho ca Vedanā||
Dve Taṇhā Tasināya cāti|| ||

[page 059]

 

 

Chapter VIII. Ogha Vaggo

1. Sāvatthinidānam|| ||

171. Ogho

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave oghā|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Kāmogho bhavogho diṭṭhogho avijjogho||
ime kho bhikkhave cattāro oghā|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam oghānam abhiññāya pariññaya parikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ... ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

3—33. Yathā esanā evaɱ vitthāretabbaɱ|| ||

 

 

172. Yogo

Kāmayogo bhavayogo diṭṭhiyogo avijjāyogo||
imekho bhikkhave cattāro yogā|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnaɱ yogānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya||
... pe ...||
ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

imāni kho bhikkhave cattāri upādānāni|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam upādānānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ... ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

sīlabbataparāmāso kāyagantho||
idaɱ saccābhiniveso kāyagantho|| ||

[page 060]

ime kho bhikkhave cattāro ganthā|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam ganthānam abhiññāya pariññaya parikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ... ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

 

 

175. Anusayā

Kāmarāgānusayo paṭighānusayo diṭṭhānusayo vicikicchānusayo mānānusayo bhavarāgānusayo avijjānusayo|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave satta anusayā|| ||

... pe ...
ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

 

 

176. Kāmaguṇa

2—33. Pañcime bhikkhave kāmaguṇā||
katame pañca|| ||

Cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaɱhitā rajanīyā||
sotaviññeyyā saddā ... pe ... ghānaviññeyyā gandhā ... pe ... jivhāviññeyyā rasā ... pe ... kāyaviññeyyā phoṭṭhabbā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaɱhitā rajanīyā|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave pañca kāmaguṇā|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannaɱ kāmaguṇānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ... ayam a° a° maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

 

 

177. Nivaraṇāni

2—3. Pañcimāni bhikkhave nivaraṇāni||
katamānipañca|| ||

Kāmacchandanīvaraṇaɱ vyāpādanīvaraṇaɱ thīnamiddhanīvaraṇam addhaccakukkuccanīvaraṇaɱ vicikicchānīvaraṇaɱ||
imāni kho bhikkhave pañca nīvaraṇāni|| ||

178. Khandā

2—33. Pañcime bhikkhave upādānakkhandhā||

seyyathīdaɱ|| ||

Rūpūpādanakkhando vedanūpādānakkhandho saññūpādānakkhando saŋkhārūpādānakkhandho {viññāṇūpādānakkhando}

[page 061]

ime kho bhikkhave pañcūpādānakkhandhā|| ||

179. Orambhāgiya

2—33. Pañcimāni bhikkhave orambhāgiyāni saŋyojanāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Sakkāyadiṭṭhi vicikicchā sīlabbataparāmāso kāmacchando byāpādo||
imāni kho bhikkhave pañcorambhāgiyāni saŋyojanāni|| ||

Imesam kho bhikkhave pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saɱyojānanam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ... pe ...ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

 

 

180. Uddhambhāgiya

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave uddhambhāgiyāni saŋyojanāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Rūparāgo arūparāgo māno uddhaccam avijjā||
imāni kho bhikkhave pañcuddhambhāgiyāni saŋyojanāni|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam uddhambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo||
katamo a° a° maggo|| ||

3—17. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ ... pe ... sammāsamādhim bhāveti viveka- virāganirodhanissitaɱ vossaggaparināmiɱ|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam uddhambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ayam a° amaggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

Seyyathā pi bhikkhave Gaŋgā nadī||
... pe ...|| ||

18. Pañcimāni bhikkhave uddhambhāgiyāni saŋyojanāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Rūparāgo arūparāgo māno uddhaccam avijjā||
imāni kho bhikkhave pañcuddhambhāgiyāni {saŋyojanāni}|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam uddhambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam abhiññaya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya a° a° maggo bhāvetabbo

[page 062]

katamo a° amaggo|| ||

19—33. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sammādiṭṭhim bhāveti||
... pe ...
sammāsamādhim bhāveti rāgavinaya- dosavinaya- mohavinayapariyosānam||
amatogadham amataparāyanaɱ amatapariyosānaɱ||
nibbānaninnaɱ nibbānapoṇam nibbānapabbhāraɱ|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam uddambhāgiyānam saŋyojanānam abhiññāya parikkhāya pahānāya ayam ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo bhāvetabbo ti|| ||

Oghavaggo aṭṭhamo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Ogho Yogo Upādānaɱ||
Ganthaɱ Anusayena ca||
Kāmaguṇā Nīvaraṇaɱ||
Khandhā Oruddhambhāgiyāti|| ||

Magga-Saɱyuttaɱ pathamaɱ|| ||
