Book II

Bojjhaŋga Saɱyutta

Chapter I. Pabbata Vaggo

1. Himavantaɱ

1.2. Sāvatthi|| ||

Tatravoca|| ||

3. Himavantam bhikkhave pabbatarājānaɱ nissāya nāgā kāyaɱ vaḍḍhenti balaɱ gāhenti||
te tattha kāyaɱ vaḍḍhetvā balaɱ gāhetvā kussubbhe otaranti||
kusubbhe otaritvā mahāsobbhe otaranti||
mahāsobbhe otaritvā kunnadiyo otaranti||
kunnadiyo otaritvā mahānadiyo otaranti||
mahānadiyo otaritvā mahāsamuddasāgaram otaranti|| ||

Te tattha mahantatam vepullatam āpajjanti kāyena|| ||

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya satta bojjhaŋge bhāvento satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkaronto mahantatam vepullatam pāpuṇāti dhammesu|| ||

Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya satta bojjhaŋge bhāvento satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkaronto mahantataɱ vepullataɱ pāpuṇāti dhammesu|| ||

5. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ virāga- nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ||

[page 064]

dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ... viriyasambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ... viriyasambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ...|| ||
pītisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ... passaddhisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ... samādhisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ... {upekhāsambojjhaŋgam} bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmim|| ||

6. Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya sattabojjhaŋge bhāvento satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkaronto mahantataɱ vepullatam pāpuṇāti dhammesū ti|| ||

 

 

2. Kāya

1.2. Sāvatthi|| ||

I.

3. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ayaɱ kāyo āhāraṭṭhitiko āhāram paticca tiṭṭhati anāhāro no tiṭṭhati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave pañcanīvaraṇā āhāraṭṭhitikā āhāram paṭicca tiṭṭhanti||
anāhārā no tiṭṭhanti|| ||

4. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā kāmacchandassa uppādāya uppannassa vā kāmacchandassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave subhanimittam||
tattha ayonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā kāmacchandassa uppādāya uppannassa vā kamacchandassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

5. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā byāpādassa uppādāya uppannassa vā byāpādassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave paṭighanimittam||
tattha ayoniso manasikārabahulīkāroayam āhāro anuppannassa vā byāpādassa uppādāya uppannassa vā byāpādassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

6. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā thīnamiddhassa uppādāya uppannassa vā thīnamiddhassa bhiyyobhāvaya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave arati tandi vijambhitā bhattasammado cetaso ca līnattaɱ||
tattha ayonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā thīnamiddhassa uppādāya uppannassa vā thīnamiddhassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

[page 065]

7. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā uddhaccakukkuccassa uppādāya uppannassa vā uddhaccakukkuccassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave cetaso avūpasamo||
tattha ayonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā uddhaccakukkuccassa uppādāya uppannassa vā uddhaccakukkuccassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

8. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppanāya vā vicikicchāya uppādāya uppannāya vā vicikicchāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave vicikicchaṭṭhāniyā dhammā tattha ayonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anupannāya vā vicikicchāya uppādāya uppannāya vā vicikicchāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

9. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ayaɱ kāyo āhāraṭṭhitiko āhāram paṭicca tiṭṭhati anāhāro no tiṭṭhati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ime pañca nīvaraṇā āhāraṭṭhitikā āhāram paṭicca tiṭṭhanti anāhārā no tiṭṭhanti|| ||

II.|| ||

10. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ayaɱ kāyo āhāraṭṭhitiko āhāram paṭicca tiṭṭhati anāhāro no tiṭṭhati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā āhāraṭṭhitikā āhāram paṭicca tiṭṭhanti anāhārā no tiṭṭhanti|| ||

11. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā satisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāyā uppannassa vā satisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave satisambojjaŋgaṭṭhaniyā dhammā||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā satisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā satisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

[page 066]

12. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anupannassa vā dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave kusalākusalā dhammā||
sāvajjā navajjā dhammā||
hīnapaṇītā dhammā||
kaṇhasukkasappatibhāgā dhammā||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā dhammavicayasambhojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

13. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā viriyasambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā viriyasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave ārambhadhātu nikkamadhātu parakkamadhātu||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā viriyasambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā viriyasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

14. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā pītisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā pītisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvānāya pāripuriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave pītisambhojjhaŋgaṭṭhāniyā dhammā||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā pīti° uppādāya uppannassa vā pīti- bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

15. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave kāyapassaddhi cittapasaddhi||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā passadhi° °ssa uppādaya uppannassa vā passadhi° °ssa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

16. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā samādhisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā samādhi- -ssa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave samathanimittam avyagganimittaɱ||
tatthayonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayaɱ āhāro anuppannassa vā samādhisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā samādhi- -ssa bhāvanāya pāripuriyā|| ||

[page 067]

17. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave upekhāsambojjhaŋgaṭṭhāniyā dhammā||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

18. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ayaɱ kāyo āhāraṭṭhitiko āhāram paṭicca tiṭṭhati anāhāro no tiṭṭhati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ime satta bojjhaŋgā āhāratiṭṭhikā āhāram paṭicca tiṭṭhanti anāhārā no tiṭṭhantī ti|| ||

 

 

3. Sīla

2. Ye te bhikkhave bhikkhū sīlasampannā samādhisampannā paññāsampannā vimuttisampannā vimuttiññāṇadassanasampannā||
dassanam pāham bhikkhave tesam bhikkhūnam bahukāram vadāmi|| ||

3. Savanam pāham bhikkhave tesam bhikkhūnam bahukāram vadāmi|| ||

Upasaŋkamanam pāham bhikkhave tesam bhi° bahukāraɱ vadāmi|| ||

Payirūpāsanam pāham bhikkhave tesaɱ bhi° bahukāraɱ vadāmi|| ||

Anussatim pāham bhikkhave tesam bhi° bahukāraɱ vadāmi|| ||

Anupabbajjam pāham bhikkhave tesam bhikkhūnam bahukāraɱ vadāmi|| ||

4. Taɱ kissa hetu|| ||

Tathārūpānam bhikkhave bhikkhūnam dhammaɱ sutvā dvayena vūpakāsena vūpakaṭṭho viharati kāyavūpakāsena ca cittavūpakāsena ca||
so tathā vūpakaṭṭho viharanto taɱ dhammam anussarati anuvitakketi|| ||

5. Yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhave bhikkhu tathā vūpakaṭṭho viharanto taɱ dhammam anussarati anuvitakketi||

[page 068]

satisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye tassa bhikkhuno āraddho hoti|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgaɱ yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
satisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati|| ||

So tathā sato viharanto taɱ dhammam paññāya pavicinati pavicarati parivīmaɱsam āpajjati|| ||

6. Yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhave bhikkhu tathā sato viharanto taɱ dhammam paññāya pavicinati pavicarati parivīmaɱsam āpajjati||
dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye tassa bhikkhuno āraddho hoti|| ||

Dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgaɱ yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhavanā pāripūriɱ gacchati||
tassa taɱ dhammam paññāya pavicinato pavicarato parivīmaɱsam āpajjato āraddhaɱ hoti viriyam asallīnam|| ||

7. Yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhave bhikkhuno taɱ dhammam paññāya pavicinato pavicarato parivīmaɱsam āpajjato āraddham hoti viriyam asallīnaɱ||
viriyasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti|| ||

Viriyasambojjhaŋgaɱ yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
viriyasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūrim gacchati||
āraddhaviriyassa uppajjati pīti nirāmisā|| ||

8. Yasmim samaye bhikkhave bhikkhuno āraddhaviriyassa uppajjati pīti nirāmisā||
pītisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti|| ||

Pītisambojjhaŋgaɱ yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
pītisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati|| ||

Pītimanassa kāyo pi passambhati cittam pi passambhati|| ||

9. Yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhave bhikkhuno pītimanassa kāyo pi passambhati cittam pi pāssambhati||
passaddhisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti|| ||

Passaddhisambojjhaŋgaɱ yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
passaddhisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanāpāripūrim gacchati

[page 069]

Passaddhakāyassa sukhaɱ hoti||
sukhino cittaɱ samādhiyati|| ||

10. Yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhave bhikkhuno passaddhakāyassa sukhino cittaɱ samādhiyati||
samādhisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhave bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
samādhisambojjhaŋgaɱ yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
samādhisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati|| ||

So tathā samāhitam cittaɱ sādhukam ajjhupekkhitā hoti|| ||

11. Yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhave bhikkhu tathāsamāhitaɱ cittaɱ sādhukam ajjhupekkhitā hoti||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgaɱ yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati|| ||

12. Evam bhāvitesu kho bhikkhave sattasu bojjhaŋgesu evam bahulikatesu satta phalā sattānisaɱsā pātikaŋkhā|| ||

Katame satta phalā sattānisaɱsā|| ||

13. Diṭṭheva dhamme paṭihacca aññam ārādheti||
no ce diṭṭheva dhamme paṭihacca aññam ārādheti||
atha maraṇakāle aññam ārādheti|| ||

14. No ce diṭṭheva dhamme paṭihacca aññam ārādheti no ce maraṇakāle aññam ārādheti||
atha pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ {saŋyojanānam} parikkayā antarāparinibbāyī hoti|| ||

15. No ce diṭṭheva dhamme patihacca aññam ārādheti||
no ce maraṇakāle aññam ārādheti||
no ce pañcannam orambhāgiyānam saŋyojanānam parikkhayā antarāparinibbāyī hoti||
atha pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā upahacca parinibbāyī hoti|| ||

16. No ce diṭṭheva dhamme paṭihacca aññam ārādheti||
no ce maraṇakāle aññam āradheti||
no ce pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saɱyojānam parikkhayā antarāparinibbāyī hoti

[page 070]

no ce pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā upahacca parinibbāyī hoti||
atha pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā asaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti|| ||

17. No ce diṭṭheva dhamme paṭihacca aññam ārādheti||
no ce maraṇakāle aññam ārādheti||
no ce pañcannam orambhāgiyānam saŋyojanānam parikkhayā antarāparinibbhāyī hoti||
no ce pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā upahacca parinibbāyī hoti||
no ce pañcannam orambhāgiyānam saŋyojanānam parikkhayā asaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti||
atha pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā sasaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti|| ||

18. No ce diṭṭheva dhamme paṭihacca aññam ārādheti||
no ce maraṇakāle aññam ārādheti||
no ce pañcannam orambhāgiyānam saŋyojanānam parikkhayā antarāparinibbāyī hoti||
no ce pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā upahacca parinibbāyī hoti||
no ce pañcanam saŋyojanānam parikkhayā asaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti||
no ce pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā sasaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti||
atha pañcannam orambhāgiyānam saŋyojanānam parikkhayā uddhaɱsoto hoti akaniṭṭhagāmī|| ||

19. Evam bhāvitesu kho bhikkhave sattasu bhojjhaŋgesu evam bahulīkatesu ime satta phalā sattānisaɱsā pāṭikaŋkhā ti|| ||

 

 

4. Vatta

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Sāriputto Sāvatthiyam viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme|| ||

2. Tatra kho āyasmā Sāriputto bhikkhū amantesi Āvuso bhikkhaveti|| ||

[page 071]

Āvuso ti te bhikkhū āyasmato Sāriputtassa paccassosuɱ|| ||

Āyasmā Sāriputto etad avoca|| ||

3. Sattime āvuso bojjhaŋgā||
katame satta||
satisambojjhaŋgo||
dhammavicaya°||
viriya°||
pīti°||
passaddhi°||
samādhi°||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgo||
ime kho āvuso satta bojjhaŋgā|| ||

4. Imesaɱ khvāham āvuso sattannam bojjhaŋgānaɱ yena yena bojjhaŋgena ākaŋkhāmi pubbaṇhasamayaɱ viharituɱ tena tena bojjhaŋgena pubbaṇhasamayaɱ viharāmi|| ||

Yena yena bojjhaŋgena ākaŋkhāmi majjhantikaɱ samayaɱ viharituɱ||
tena tena bojjhaŋgena majjhantikaɱ samayaɱ viharāmi|| ||

Yena yena bojjhaŋgena ākaŋkhāmi sāyanhasamayaɱ viharitum||
tena tena bojjhaŋgena sāyanhasamayaɱ viharāmi|| ||

5. Satisambojjhaŋgo iti ce me āvuso hoti||
Appamāṇo ti me hoti||
Susamāraddho ti me hoti||
tiṭṭhantaɱ ca naɱ Tiṭṭhatīti pajānāmi|| ||

Sa ce pi me cavati Idappaccayā me cavatīti pajānāmi|| ||

6—10. ti ... pe ...|| ||

11. Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo iti ce me āvuso hoti||
Appamāṇo ti me hoti||
Susamāraddho ti me hoti||
tiṭṭhantaɱ ca naɱ Tiṭṭhatīti pajānāmi|| ||

Sa ce pi me cavati Idappaccayā me cavatīti pajānāmi|| ||

12. Seyyathā pi āvuso rañño vā rājamahāmattassa vā nānārattānaɱ dussānam dussakaraṇḍako pūro assa||
so yaññadeva dussayugam ākaŋkheyya pubbaṇhasamayam pārupituɱ||
taɱ tad eva dussayugam pubbaṇhasamayam pārupeyya|| ||

Yaññad eva dussayuham ākaŋkheyya majjhantikaɱ samayam pārupituɱ||
tan tad eva dussayugam majjhantikaɱ samayam pārupeyya|| ||

Yaññadeva dussayugam ākaŋkheyya sāyaṇhasamayam pārupituɱ||
tan tad eva dussayugam sāyanhasamayam pārupeyya|| ||

[page 072]

13. Evam eva khvāham āvuso imesaɱ sattannam bojjhaŋgānaɱ yena yena bojjhaŋgena ākaŋkhāmi pubbaɱhasamayam viharituɱ||
tena tena bojjhaŋgena pubbaṇhasamayaɱ viharāmi|| ||

Yena yena- omajjhantikaɱ samayaɱ viharāmi||
Yena yena- osāyaṇhasamayaɱ viharāmi|| ||

14. Satisambojjhaŋgo iti ce me āvuso hoti Appamāno ti me hoti- ocavatīti pajānāmi|| ||

15—19. ti ... pe ...|| ||

20. Upekhāsambhojjhaŋgo- -Idappaccayā me cavatīti pajānāmīti|| ||

 

 

5. Bhikkhu

2. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkhami||
... pe ...||
Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Bojjhaŋgā bojjhaŋgā ti bhante vuccatīti||
Kittāvatā nu kho bhante bojjhaŋgāti vuccantīti|| ||

Bodhāya saɱvattantīti kho bhikkhu tasmā bojjhaŋgā ti vuccanti|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhu bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitam vossaggaparināmiɱ||
... pe ...||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossagapariṇamiɱ|| ||

4. Tassime satta bojjhaŋge bhāvayato kāmāsavā pi cittaɱ vimuccati||
bhavāsavā pi cittaɱ vimuccati||
avijjāsavā pi cittaɱ vimuccati||
Vimuttasmiɱ vimuttamhīti||
ñāṇaɱ hoti||
khīṇā jāti vusitam brahmacariyaɱ kataɱ karaṇīyaɱ nāparam itthattāyāti pajānāti|| ||

5. Bodhāya saɱvattantī ti kho bhikkhu tasmā bojjhaŋgā ti vuccantī ti|| ||

[page 073]

 

 

6. Kuṇḍali

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sākete viharati Añcanavane Migadāye|| ||

2. Atha kho Kuṇḍaliyo paribbājako yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodi||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyam vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Kuṇḍaliyo paribbājako Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3 Aham asmi bho Gotama ārāmanisādi parisāvacaro||
tassa mayham bho Gotama pacchābhattam bhuttapātarāsassa ayam ācāro hoti||
ārāmena ārāmam uyyānena uyyānam anucaŋkamāmi anuvicarāmi||
so tattha passāmi eke samaṇabrāhmaṇe itivādapamokkhānisaɱsaɱ ceva katham kathente upārambhānisaɱsañ ca||
bhavaɱ pana Gotamo kimānisaɱso viharatīti|| ||

Vijjāvimuttiphalānisaɱso kho Kuṇḍaliya tathāgato viharatīti|| ||

4. Katame pana bho Gotama dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā vijjāvimuttim paripūrentīti|| ||

Satta kho Kuṇḍaliya sambojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulikatā vijjāvimuttim paripūrentī ti|| ||

5. Katame pana bho Gotama dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā sattabojjhaŋge paripūrentī ti|| ||

Cattāro kho Kuṇḍaliya satipaṭṭhānā bhāvitā bahulīkatā sattabojjhaŋge paripūrentī ti|| ||

6. Katame pana bho Gotama dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā cattāro satipaṭṭhāne paripūrentī ti|| ||

Tīṇi kho Kuṇḍaliya sucaritāni bhāvitāni bahulīkatāni cattāro satipaṭṭhāne paripūrentīti|| ||

7. Katame pana bho Gotama dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā tiṇi sucaritāni paripūrentīti|| ||

[page 074]

Indriyasaɱvaro kho Kuṇḍaliya bhāvito bahulīkato tīni sucaritāni paripūrentīti|| ||

Katham bhāvito ca Kuṇḍaliya indriyasaɱvaro katham bahulīkato tīni sucaritāni paripūreti|| ||

8. Idha Kuṇḍaliya bhikkhu cakkhunā rūpaɱ disvā manāpaɱ nābhijjhati nābhihaɱsati na rāgaɱ janeti||
tassa ṭhito ca kāyo hoti ṭhitaɱ cittaɱ ajjhattaɱ susaṇṭhitaɱ suvimuttaɱ|| ||

Cakkhunā kho paneva rūpaɱ disvā amanāpaɱ na maŋku hoti||
apatiṭṭhitacitto ādīnamānaso avyāpannacetaso||
tassa ṭhito ca kāyo hoti ṭhitaɱ cittam ajjhattaɱ susaṇṭhitam suvimuttaɱ|| ||

9—12. Puna ca paraɱ Kuṇḍaliya bhikkhu sotena saddam sutvā||
... pe ...||
ghaneṇa gandhaɱ ghāyitvā||
... pe ...||
jivhāya rasaɱ sāyitvā||
... pe ...||
kāyena phoṭṭhabbaɱ phusitvā||
... pe ...|| ||

13. Manasā dhammaɱ viññāya manāpaɱ nābhijjhati nābhihaɱsati na rāgaɱ janeti||
tassa ṭhito va kāyo hoti ṭhitaɱ cittam ajjhattaɱ susaṇṭhitaɱ suvimuttaɱ|| ||

Manasā kho paneva dhammaɱ viññāya amanāpaɱ na maŋku hoti||
apatiṭṭhitacitto ādīnamanaso avyāpannacetaso||
tassa ṭhito va kāyo hoti ṭhitaɱ cittam ajjhattaɱ susaṇṭhitaɱ suvimuttaɱ|| ||

14. Yato kho Kuṇḍaliya bhikkhuno cakkhunā rūpam disvā manāpāmanāpesu rūpesu ṭhito ca kāyo hoti ṭhitaɱ cittam ajjhattaɱ susaṇṭhitam suvimuttam||
sotena saddaɱ sutvā||
... pe ...||
ghānena gandhaɱ ghāyitvā||
... pe ...jivhāya rasaɱ sāyitvā||
... pe ...||
kāyena poṭṭhabbam phusitvā||
... pe ...||
manasā dhammaɱ viññāya manāpāmanāpesu dhammesu ṭhito ca kāyo hoti ṭhitaɱ cittaɱ ajjhattaɱ susaṇṭhitam suvimuttaɱ

[page 075]

evam bhāvito kho Kuṇḍaliya indriyasaɱvaro evam bahulīkato tīni sucaritāni paripūreti|| ||

15. Katham bhāvitāni ca Kuṇḍaliya tīṇi sucaritāni katham bahulīkatāni cattāro satipaṭṭhāne paripūrenti|| ||

Idha Kuṇḍaliya khikkhu kāyaduccaritam pahāya kāyasucaritam bhāveti||
vacīduccaritam pahāya vacīsucaritam bhaveti||
manoduccaritam pahāya manosucaritam bhāveti|| ||

Evam bhāvitāni kho Kuṇḍaliya tīṇi sucaritāni evam bahulīkatāni cattāro satipaṭṭhāne paripūrenti|| ||

16. Katham bhāvitā ca Kuṇḍaliya cattāro satipaṭṭhānā katham bahulīkatā sattabojjhaŋge paripūrenti|| ||

Idha Kuṇḍaliya bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
vedanāsu||
... pe ...||
citte||
... pe ...||
dhamme dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Evam bhāvitā kho Kuṇḍaliya cattāro satipaṭṭhānā evam bahulīkatā satta bojjhaŋge paripūrenti|| ||

17. Katham bhāvitā ca Kuṇḍaliya satta bojjhaŋgā katham bahulīkatā vijjāvimuttim paripūrenti|| ||

Idha Kuṇḍaliya bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka- virāganirodanissitaɱ vossaggaparināmiɱ ... pe ... upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggaparināmiɱ|| ||

Evam bhāvitā kho Kuṇḍaliya satta bojjhaŋgā evam bahulīkatā vijjāvimuttiɱ paripūrentīti|| ||

18. Evaɱ vutte Kuṇḍaliyo paribbājako Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Abhikkantam bho Gotama ... pe ... pāṇupetam saraṇaɱ gatan ti|| ||

 

 

7. Kūṭa

3. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave kūṭāgārassa yā kāci gopānasiyo sabbā tā kūṭaninnā kūṭapoṇā kūṭapabbhārā||
evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu satta bojjhaŋge bhāvento satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkaronto nibbānaninno hoti nibbānapoṇo nibbānapabbhāro|| ||

[page 076]

4. Kathañ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu satta bojjhaŋge bhāvento satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkaronto nibbānaninno hoti nibbānapoṇo o pabbhāro|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgaɱ bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ||
... pe ...||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu satta bojjhaŋge bhāvento satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkaronto nibbānaninno hoti nibbānapoṇo nibbānapabbhāroti|| ||

 

 

8. Upavāna

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ āyasmā ca Upavāṇo āyasmā ca Sāriputto Kosambīyaɱ viharanti Ghositārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Sāriputto sāyānhasamayam paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito yenāyasmā Upavāṇo tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmatā Upavāṇena saddhiɱ sammodi||
sammodanīyaɱ sarāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Sāriputto āyasmantam Upavāṇam etad avoca|| ||

3. Jāneyya nu kho āvuso Upavāṇa bhikkhu Paccattaɱ yonisomanasikārā evaɱ susamāraddhā me sattabojjhaŋgā phāsuvihārāya {saɱvattantīti}|| ||

4. Jāneyya kho āvuso Sāriputta bhikkhu Paccattaɱ yonisomanasikārā evam sūsamāraddhā me satta bojjhaŋgā phāsuvihārāya {saɱvattantīti}|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgam āvuso bhikkhu ārambhamāno va janāti|| ||

Cittañ ca me suvimuttam thīnamiddhañca me susamūhataɱ uddhaccakukkuccañ ca me suppaṭivinītaɱ āraddhañca me viriyam aṭṭhikatvā manasikaromi no ca līnan ti ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgam āvuso bhikkhu ārambhamāno va jānāti Cittañ ca me suvimuttaɱ thīnamiddhañ ca me susamūhatam uddhaccakukuccañ ca me suppaṭivinītam āraddhañ ca me viriyam aṭṭhikatvā manasīkaromi no ca līnan ti

[page 077]

Evaɱ kho āvuso Sāriputta jāneyya Paccattam yonisomanasikārā evaɱ susamāraddhā me satta bojjhaŋgā phāsuvihārāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

 

 

9. Uppannā (or Uppāda) 1

2. Sattime bhikkhave bojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā anuppannā uppajjanti||
naññatra Tathāgatassa pātubhāvā arahato sammāsambuddhassa|| ||

Katame satta?|| ||

3. Satisambojjhaŋgo ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā anuppannā uppajjanti||
nāññatra Tathāgatassa pātubhāvā arahato sammāsambuddhassā ti|| ||

 

 

10. Uppannā (or Uppāda) 2

2. Sattime bhikkhave bojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā anuppannā uppajjanti||
nāññatra Sugatavinayā|| ||

Katame satta?|| ||

3. Satisambojjhaŋgo ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā anuppannā uppajjanti||
nāññatra Sugatavinayāti|| ||

Pabbatavaggo pathamo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Himavantaɱ Kāyaɱ Sīlaɱ||
Vattam Bhikkhu ca Kuṇḍali||
Kūṭañca Upavāṇañca||
Uppannā apare duveti|| ||

[page 078]

 

 

Chapter II. Gilāna Vaggo

11. Pāṇā

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci pāṇā cattāro iriyāpathe kappenti kālena gamanam kālena ṭhānaɱ kālena nisajjaɱ kālena seyyam||
sabbe te pathaviɱ nissāya pathaviyam patiṭṭhāya evam ete cattāro iriyāpathe kappenti||
evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkaroti|| ||

3. Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu silaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkaroti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ||
... pe ...||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlam nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkarotī ti|| ||

 

 

12. Suriyassa upamā 1

2. Suriyassa bhikkhave udayato etam pubbaŋgamam etam pubbanimittam yad idam aruṇuggam||
evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhuno sattannam bojjhaŋgānam uppādāya etam pubbaŋgamam etam pubbanimittaɱ yad idaɱ kalyāṇamittatā|| ||

Kalyaṇamittassetam bhikkhave bhikkhuno pātikaŋkham satta bojjhaŋge bhāvessati satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkarissati|| ||

3. Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu kalyāṇamitto satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti satta- bahulīkaroti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekanissitam ... pe ...||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitam vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu kalyāṇamitto satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti satta bhojjhaŋge bahulīkarotīti

[page 079]

 

 

13. Suriyassa upamā 2

2. Suriyassa bhikkhave udayato etam pubbaŋgamam etam pubbanimittaɱ yadidam aruṇuggam||
evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhuno sattannam bojjhaŋgānam uppādāya etam pubbaŋgamam etam pubbanimittaɱ yad idaɱ yonisomanasikāro|| ||

Yonisomanasikārasampannessetam bhikkhave bhikkhuno pāṭikaŋkhaɱ satta bojjhaŋge bhāvessati satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkarissati|| ||

3. Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu yoniso manasikārasampanno satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti sattabojjhaŋge bahulīkaroti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti||
... pe ...||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekavirāga- nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu yonisomanasikārasampanno satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti sattabojjhaŋge bahulīkarotī ti|| ||

 

 

14. Gilanā 1

1. Evaɱ me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Veḷuvane Kalandakanivāpe|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Mahā-Kassapo pipphalīguhāyam viharati ābādhiko dukkhito bāḷhagilāno|| ||

3. Atha kho Bhagavā sāyaṇhasamayam paṭisallāṇā vuṭṭhito yenāyasmā Mahā-Kassapo tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisidi|| ||

4. Nisajja kho Bhagavā āyasmantam Mahā-Kassapam etad avoca|| ||

Kacci te Kassapa khamanīyam kacci yāpanīyaɱ kacci dukkhā vedanā paṭikkamanti no abhikkamanti paṭikkamo sānaɱ paññāyati no abhikkamo ti|| ||

[page 080]

Na me bhante khamanīyaɱ na me yāpanīyaɱ bāḷhā me dukkhā vedanā abhikkamanti no paṭikammanti abhikkamo sānam paññāyati no patikkamo ti|| ||

4. Sattime Kassapa bojjhaŋgā mayā sammad akkhātā bhāvitā bahulīkatā abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya samvattanti||
katame satta|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo kho Kassapa mayā sammad akkhāto bhāvito bahulīkato abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattati ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo kho Kassapa mayā sammad akkhāto bhāvito bahulīkato abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattati|| ||

Ime kho Kassapa satta bojjhaŋgā mayā sammad akkhātā bhāvitā bahulīkatā abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

Taggha Bhagava bojjhaŋgā taggha Sugata bojjhaŋgā ti|| ||

5. Idam avoca Bhagavā||
attamano āyasmā Mahā-Kassapo Bhagavato bhāsitam abhinandi||
vuṭṭhāhi ca āyasmā Mahā-Kassapo tamhā ābādhā|| ||

Tathā pahīno cāyasmato Mahā-Kassapassa so ābhādho ahosī ti|| ||

 

 

15. Gilanā 2

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Veḷuvane Kalandakanivāpe|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Mahā-Moggalāno Gijjhakūṭe pabbate viharati ābhādhiko dukkhito bāḷhagilāno|| ||

3—5. Atha kho Bhagavā sāyanhasamayam paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito- -Tathā pahīno cāyasmato MahāMoggalānassa so ābādho ahosīti|| ||

[page 081]

 

 

16. Gilanā 3

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Veḷuvane Kalandakanivāpe|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Bhagavā ābādhiko hoti dukkhito bāḷhagilāno|| ||

3. Atha kho āyasmā Mahā-Cundo yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā ekam antam nisīdi|| ||

4. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnaɱ kho āyasmantam Mahā-Cundam Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

Paṭibhantu taɱ Cunda bojjhaŋgā ti|| ||

5. Sattime bhante bojjhaŋgā Bhagavatā sammad akkhātā bhāvitā bahulīkatā abhiññāya sambodāya nibbānāya {saɱvattanti}||
katame satta|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo kho bhante Bhagavatā sammadakkhāto bhāvito bahulīkato abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattati ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo kho bhante Bhagavatā sammadakkhāto bhāvito bahulīkato abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattati|| ||

Ime kho bhante satta bojjhaŋgā Bhagavatā sammadakkhātā bhāvitā bahulīkatā abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattantīti|| ||

Taggha Cunda bojjhaŋgā taggha Cunda bojjhaŋgā ti|| ||

6. Idam avocāyasmā Mahā-Cundo samanuñño satthā āhosi||
vuṭṭhāhi ca Bhagavā tamhā ābādhā|| ||

Tathā pahīno ca Bhagavato so ābādho ahosīti|| ||

 

 

17. Pāraŋgāmi or Aparam

2. Sattime bhikkhave bojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā apārāpāraŋgamanāya {saɱvattanti}||
katame satta|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo ... pe ...||
Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā apārāpāraŋgamanāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

3. Idam avoca||

[page 082]

Appakā te manussesu... pe ...||
Te loke parinibbutā ti|| ||

 

 

18. Viraddho or Āraddho

2. Yesaɱ kesañci bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā viraddhā||
viraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī|| ||

Yesaɱ kesañci bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā āraddhā||
āraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī|| ||

Katame satta?|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo|| ||

... pe ...||
Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo|| ||

3. Yesaɱ kesañci bhikkhave ime satta bojjhaŋgā viraddhā||
viraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammā dukkhakkhayagāmī|| ||

Yesaɱ kesañci bhikkhave ime satta bojjhaŋgā āraddhā||
āraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhagāmī ti|| ||

 

 

19. Ariyo

2. Sattime bhikkhave bojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā ariyā niyyānikā niyyanti takkarassa sammādukkhakkhayāya||
katame satta|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā ariyā niyyānikā niyyanti takkarassa sammādukkhakkhayāyāti|| ||

 

 

20. Nibbidā

2. Sattime bhikkhave bojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā ekantanibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattanti||
katame satta|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave satta bojjhāŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā ekantanibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

[page 083]

Gilānavaggo dutiyo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Pāṇā Suriyūpamā dve||
Gilānā apare tayo||
Pāraŋgāmī Viraddho ca||
Ariyo Nibiddāya cāti|| ||

 

 

Chapter III. Udāyi Vaggo

21. Bodhanā

2. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā ekām antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

3. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Bojjhaŋgā bojjhaŋgāti bhante vuccanti|| ||

Kittāvatā nu kho bhante Bhojjhaŋgā ti vuccantī ti|| ||

Bodhāya saɱvattantīti kho bhikkhu||
tasmā Bhojjhaŋgāti vuccanti|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti||
... pe ...||
{Upekhāsambojjhaŋgam} bhāveti vivekanissitam virāganissitaɱ nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇamiɱ|| ||

4. Bodhāya saɱvattantī ti kho bhikkhu tasmā Bojjhaŋgā ti vuccantī ti|| ||

 

 

22. Desanā

2. Satta vo bhikkhave bojjhaŋge desissāmi tam suṇātha|| ||

Katame ca bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo||
... pe ...||
Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā ti|| ||

[page 084]

 

 

23. Ṭhānā

2. Kāmarāgaṭṭhāniyānam bhikkhave dhammānam manasikārabahulīkārā anuppanno ceva kāmacchando uppajjati uppanno ca kāmacchando bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

3. Byāpādaṭṭhāniyānam bhikkhave dhammānam manasikārabahulīkārā anuppanno ceva byāpādo uppajjati||
uppanno ca byāpado bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

4. Thīnamiddhaṭṭhāniyānam bhikkhave dhammānam manasikārabahulīkārā anuppannañ ceva thīnamiddham uppajjati||
uppannañca thīnamiddham bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

5. Uddhaccakukkaccaṭṭhāniyānam bhikkhave dhammānam manasikārabahulīkārā anuppannañ ceva uddhaccakukkuccam uppajjati||
uppannañ ca uddhaccakukkuccam bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

6. Vicikicchāṭṭhāniyānam bhikkhave dhammānam manasikārabahulīkārā anuppannā ceva vicikicchā uppajjati||
uppannā ca vicikicchā bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

7. Satisambojjhaŋgaṭṭhāniyānam bhikkhave dhammānam manasikārabahulīkārā anuppanno ceva satisambojjhaŋgo uppajjati||
upanno ca satisambojjhaŋgo bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati ... pe ...|| ||

8. Upekhāsambojjhaŋgaṭṭhāniyānam bhikkhave dhammānam manasikārabahulīkārā anuppanno ceva upekhāsambojjhaŋgo uppajjati||
uppanno ca upekhāsambojjhaŋgo bhāvanā pāripūrim gacchatī ti|| ||

 

 

24. Ayoniso

2. Ayoniso bhikkhave manasikaroto anuppanno ceva kāmacchando uppajjati||
uppanno ca kāmacchando bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati||

[page 085]

3. Anuppanno ceva byāpādo uppajjati||
uppanno ca byāpādo bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

4. Anuppannaɱ ceva thīnamiddham uppajjati||
uppannañca thīnamiddham bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

5. Anuppannaɱ ceva uddhaccakukkaccam uppajjati||
uppannaɱ ca uddhaccakukkuccam bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

6. Anuppannā ceva vicikicchā uppajjati||
uppannā ca vivikicchā bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

7. Anuppanno ceva satisambojjhaŋgo nuppajjati uppano ca satisambojjhaŋgo nirujjhati ... pe ... Anuppanno ceva upekhāsambojjhaŋgo nuppajjati||
uppanno ca upekhāsambojjhaŋgo nirujjhati|| ||

8. Yoniso ca kho bhikkhave manasikaroto anuppanno ceva kāmacchando nuppajjati||
uppanno ca kāmacchando pahīyati|| ||

9. Anuppanno ceva byāpādo nuppajjati||
uppanno ca byāpādo pahīyati|| ||

10. Anuppannañ ceva thīnamiddhaɱ nuppajjati||
uppannaɱ ca ṭhīnamiddham pahīyati|| ||

11. Anuppannañ ceva uddhaccakukkuccaɱ nuppajjati||
uppannañca uddhaccakukkuccam pahīyati|| ||

12. Anuppannā ceva vicikicchā nuppajjati||
uppannā ca vicikicchā pahīyati|| ||

13. Anuppanno ceva satisambojjhaŋgo uppajjati||
uppanno ca satisambojjhaŋgo bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati||
... pe ...|| || anuppanno ceva upekhāsambojjhaŋgo uppajjati||
uppanno ca upekhāsambojjhaŋgo bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchatī ti|| ||

 

 

25. Aparihāni

2. Satta vo bhikkhave aparihāniye dhamme desissāmi||
taɱ suṇātha|| ||

[page 086]

3. Katame ca bhikkhave satta aparihāniyā dhammā||
yad idam satta bojjhaŋgā|| ||

Katame satta?|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo ... pe ... upekhāsambojjhaŋgo|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave satta aparihāniyā dhammā ti|| ||

 

 

26. Khayo

2. Yo bhikkhave maggo yā paṭipadā taṇhakkhayāya saɱvattati||
tam maggaɱ tam paṭipadam bhāvetha|| ||

3. Katamo ca bhikkhave maggo katamā ca paṭipadā taṇhakkhayāya {saɱvattati}||
yadidaɱ satta bojjhaŋgā||
katame satta|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo ... pe ... upekhāsambojjhaŋgo ti|| ||

4. Evaɱ vutte āyasmā Udāyi Bhagavantam etad avoca||
Katham bhāvitā nu kho bhante satta bojjhaŋgā katham bahulīkatā taṇhakkhayāya saɱvattantīti|| ||

5. Idha Udāyi bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossagaparināmiɱ vipulaɱ mahaggatam appamāṇam abyāpajjhaɱ||
tassa {satisambojjhaŋgam} bhāvayato viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇamiɱ vipulam mahaggatam appamāṇam abyāpajjhaɱ taṇhā pahīyati|| ||

tanhāya pahānā kammam pahīyati||
kammassa pahānā dukkham pahīyati|| ||

6—11. ti ... pe ...|| ||

12. Upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitam vossaggapariṇāmim vipulam mahaggatam appamāṇam abyāpajjhaɱ||
tassa upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāvayato viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ vipulam mahaggatam appamāṇam abyāpajjhaɱ taṇhā pahīyati

[page 087]

taṇhāya pahānā kammam pahīyati||
kammassa pahānā dukkham pahīyati|| ||

13. Iti kho Udāyi taṇhakkhayā kammakkhayo kammakkhayā dukkhakkhayo ti|| ||

 

 

27. Nirodho

2. Yo bhikkhave maggo yā paṭipadā taṇhānirodhāya saɱvattati||
tam {maggaɱ} tam paṭipadam bhāvetha|| ||

3. Katamo ca bhikkhave maggo katamā ca patipadā taṇhānirodhāya {saɱvattati}||
yad idaɱ satta bojjhaŋgā|| ||

Katame satta?|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo ... pe ... upekkāsambojjhaŋgo|| ||

4. Katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā katham bahulīkatā taṇhānirodhāya saɱvattanti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti||
viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇamiɱ ... pe ...||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

5. Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā evam bahulīkatā taṇhānirodhāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

 

 

28. Nibbedho

2. Nibbedhabhāgiyaɱ vo bhikkhave maggaɱ desissāmi||
taɱ suṇātha|| ||

3. Katamo ca bhikkhave nibbedhabhāgiyo maggo|| ||

Yad idam satta bojjhaŋgā||
katame sattā||
Satisambojjhaŋgo ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo ti|| ||

4. Evam vutte āyasmā Udāyi Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Katham bhāvitā nu kho bhante satta bojjhaŋgā katham bahulīkatā nibbedhāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

5. Idha Udāyi bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vipulam mahaggatam appamāṇam abyāpajjham

[page 088]

so satibojjhaŋgam bhāvitena cittena anibbiddhapubbam appadālitapubbam lobhakkhandham nibbijjhati padāleti||
anibbhiddhapubbam appadālitapubbam dosakkhandham nibbijjhati padāleti||
anibbiddhapubbam appadālitapubbam mohakkhandham nibbijjhati padāleti ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekavirāga- nirodhanissitām vipulam mahaggatam appamāṇam abyāpajjhaɱ||
So upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāvitena anibbiddhapubbam appadālitapubbaɱ lobhakkhandham nibbijjhati padāleti||
anibbiddhapubbam appadālitapubbaɱ dosakkhandham nibbijjhati padāleti||
anibbiddhapubbam appadālitapubbam mohakkhandhaɱ nibbijjhati padāleti|| ||

6. Evam bhāvitā kho Udāyi satta bojjhaŋgā evam bahulīkatā nibbedhāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

 

 

29. Ekadhamma

2. Nāham bhikkhave aññam ekadhammam pi samanupassāmi yo evam bhāvito bahulīkato saŋyojaniyānaɱ dhammānam pahānāya saɱvattati||
yathayidam bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā||
katame satta|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo||
... pe ...||
Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo|| ||

3. Katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā katham bahulīkatā saŋyojaniyānam dhammānam pahānāya saɱvattanti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ||
... pe ...||
Upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā evam bahulīkatā saŋyojaniyānaɱ dhammānam pahānāya saɱvattanti|| ||

[page 089]

4. Katame ca bhikkhave saŋyojaniyā dhammā|| ||

Cakkhum bhikkhave saŋyojaniyo dhammo|| ||

Etthete uppajjanti saŋyojanavinibandhā ajjhosānā||
Jivhāsaŋyojaniyo dhammo||
etthete uppajjanti saŋyojanavinibandhā ajjhosānā|| ||

Manosaŋyojaniyo dhammo||
etthete uppajjanti saŋyojanavinibandhā ajjhosānā|| ||

Ime vuccanti bhikkhave saŋyojaniyā dhammā ti|| ||

 

 

30. Udāyi

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sumbhesu viharati Setakam nāma Sumbhānam nigamo|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Udāyi yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
... pe ...|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Udāyi Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Acchariyam bhante abbhutam bhante yāva bahukatañca me bhante Bhagavati pemañca gāravo ca hiri ca ottappañca||
Ahaɱ hi bhante pubbe agārikabhūto samāno abahukato ahosiɱ dhammena||
abahukato saŋghena||
so khvāham bhante Bhagavati pemañca gāravañca hiriɱ ca ottapañca sampassamāno agārasmā anagāriyam pabbajito||
tassa me Bhagavā dhammaɱ desesi|| ||

Iti rūpam iti rūpassa samudayo iti rūpassa atthagamo|| ||

Iti vedanā||
... pe ...||
Iti saññā||
Iti saŋkhārā||
Iti viññāṇaɱ iti viññāṇassa samudayo iti viññāṇassa atthagamo ti|| ||

4. So khvāham bhante suññāgāragato imesam pañcupādānakkhandhānam ukkujjāvakujjam samparivattento Idaɱ dukkhanti yathā bhūtam abbhaññāsiɱ||
Ayaɱ dukkhasamudayo ti yathābhūtam abbhaññāsim

[page 090]

Ayaɱ dukkhanirodho ti yathābhūtam abbhaññāsiɱ||
Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam abbhaññāsiɱ|| ||

5. Dhammo ca me bhante abhisamito maggo ca paṭiladdho||
yo me bhāvito bahulīkato tathā tathā viharantam tathattāya upanessati||
yathāham Khīnā jāti vusitam brahmacariyaɱ nāparam itthattāyāti pajānissāmi||
Satisambojjhaŋgo me bhante paṭiladdho||
yo me bhāvito bahulīkato tathā tathā viharantam tathattāya upanessati yathāham Khīnājati- -itthattāyāti pajānissāmi ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo kho me bhante pariladdho||
yo me bhāvito bahulīkato tathā tathā viharantam tathattāya upanessati||
yathāham Khīnā jāti- -itthattāyati pajānissāmi|| ||

Ayaɱ kho me bhante maggo paṭiladdho||
yo me bhāvito bahulīkato tathā tathā viharantam tathattāya upanessati yathāhaɱ Khīnā jati- -nāparam itthattāyāti pajānissāmī ti|| ||

6. Sādhu sādhu Udāyi eso hi te Udāyi maggo paṭiladdho||
yo te bhāvito bahulīkato tathā tathā viharantam tathattāya upanessati||
yathā tvaɱ Khiṇā jāti vusitam brahmacariyaɱ kataɱ karaṇīyaɱ nāparam itthattāyā ti pajānissāmī ti|| ||

Udāyivaggo tatiyo|| ||

Tassa uddānaɱ:|| ||

Bodhanā Desānā Ṭhānā||
Ayoniso cāparihāni||
Khayo Nirodho Nibbedho||
Ekadhammo Udāyinā ti|| ||

[page 091]

 

 

Chapter IV. Nīvaraṇa Vaggo

31. Kusalā 1

2. Ye keci bhikkhave dhammā kusalākusalabhāgiyā kusalapakkhikā||
sabbe te appamādamūlakā appamādasamosaraṇā||
appamādo tesaɱ dhammānam aggam akkhāyati|| ||

3. Appamattassetam bhikkhave bhikkhuno pāṭikaŋkhaɱ satta bojjhaŋge bhāvessati||
satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkarissati|| ||

Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu appamatto satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti||
satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkaroti|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekavirāga- nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇamiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu appamatto satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti||
sattabojjhaŋge bahulīkarotī ti|| ||

 

 

32. Kusalā 2

2. Ye keci bhikkhave dhammā kusalākusalabhāgiyā kusalapakkhikā||
sabbe te yoniso manasikāramūlakā yonisomanasikārasamosaraṇā||
yonisomanasikāro tesaɱ dhammānam aggam akkhāyati|| ||

3. Yoniso manāsikārasampannassetam bhikkhave bhikkhuno pātikaŋkhaɱ sattabojjhaŋge bhāvessati sattabojjhaŋge bahulīkarissati|| ||

Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu yonisomanasikārasampanno sattabojjhaŋge bhāveti sattabojjhaŋge bahulīkaroti|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu yonisomanasikārasampanno satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti satta- bahulīkaroti|| ||

[page 092]

 

 

33. Kilesa 1

2. Pañcime bhikkhave jātarūpassa upakkilesā||
Yehi upakkilesehi upakkiliṭṭham jātarūpaɱ na ceva mudu hoti||
na ca kammaniyaɱ na ca pabhassaram pabhāŋgu ca na ca sammā upeti kammāya|| ||

Katame pañca?|| ||

3. Ayo bhikkhave jātarūpassa upakkileso||
yena upakkilesena upakkiliṭṭhaɱ jātarūpaɱ na ceva mudu hoti na ca kammaniyaɱ na ca pabhassaram pabhaŋgu ca na ca sammā upeti kammāya|| ||

4. Loham bhikkhave jātarūpassa upakkileso||
yena upakkilesena uppakkiliṭṭham jātarūpaɱ||
... pe ...|| ||

5. Tipu bhikkhave jātarūpassa upakkileso||
... pe ...|| ||

6. Sīsam bhikkhave jātarūpassa upakkileso||
... pe ...|| ||

7. Sajjhum bhikkhave jātarūpassa upakkileso yena upakkilesena uppakkiliṭṭham jātarūpam na ceva mudu hoti na ca kammaniyaɱ na ca pabhassaram pabhaŋgu ca na ca sammā upeti kammāya|| ||

8. Ime kho bhikkhave pañca jātarūpassa uppakkilesā yehi {upakkilesehi} uppakkiliṭṭhaɱ jātarūpaɱ na ceva mudu hoti||
na ca kammaniyaɱ na ca pabhassaram pabhaŋgu ca na ca sammā upeti kammāya|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave pañcime cittassa upakkilesā|| ||

yehi upakkilesehi upakkiliṭṭhaɱ cittaɱ na ceva mudu hoti||
na ca kammaniyaɱ na ca pabhassaram pabhaŋgu ca na ca sammā samādhiyati āsavānaɱ khayāya|| ||

Katame pañca?|| ||

9. Kāmacchando bhikkhave cittassa upakkileso||
yena upakkilesena upakkiliṭṭhaɱ cittaɱ na ceva mudu hoti na ca kammaniyam na ca pabhassaraɱ pabhaŋgu ca na ca sammā sammādhiyati āsavānaɱ khayāya|| ||

10—13. ... pe ...|| ||

[page 093]

14. Ime kho bhikkhave pañca cittassa upakkilesā||
yehi upakkilesehi upakkiliṭṭhaɱ cittam na ceva mudu hoti na ca kammaniyaɱ na ca pabhassaram pabhaŋgu ca na ca sammā samādhiyati āsavānaɱ khayāyā ti|| ||

 

 

34. Kilesa 2

2. Sattime bhikkhave bojjhaŋgā anāvaraṇā anīvaraṇā cetaso anupakkilesā bhāvitā bahulīkatā vijjāvimuttiphalasacchikiriyāya saɱvattanti||
katame satta|| ||

3. Satibojjhaŋgo bhikkhave anāvaraṇo anīvaraṇo cetaso anupakkileso bhāvito bahulīkato vijjāvimuttiphalasacchikiriyāya saɱvattati ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo bhikkhave anāvaraṇo anīvaraṇo cetaso anuppakileso bhāvito bahulīkato vijjāvimuttiphalasacchikiriyāya saɱvattati|| ||

4. Ime kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā anāvaraṇā anīvaraṇā cetaso anupakkilesā bhāvitā bahulīkatā vijjāvimuttiphalasacchiriyāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

 

 

35. Yoniso 1

2. Ayoniso bhikkhave manasikaroto anuppanno ceva kāmacchando uppajjati||
uppanno ca kāmacchando bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

3. Anuppanno ceva byāpādo uppajjati||
uppanno ca byāpādo bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

4. Anuppannaɱ ceva thīnamiddham uppajjati||
uppannaɱ ca thīnamiddham bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

5. Anuppannañceva uddhaccakukkuccam uppajjati||
uppannañca uddhaccakukkuccam bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya {saɱvattati}|| ||

[page 094]

6. Ayoniso ca bhikkhave manasikaroto anuppannā ceva vicikicchā uppajjati||
uppannā ca vicikicchā bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saɱvattati|| ||

 

 

36. Yoniso 2

2. Yoniso ca kho bhikkhave manasikaroto anuppanno ceva satisambojjhaŋgo uppajjati||
uppanno ca satisambojjhaŋgo bhāvanā pāripūrim gacchati||
... pe ...||
anuppanno ceva upekhāsambojjhāŋgo uppajjati||
uppanno ca {upekhāsambojjhaŋgo} bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchatīti|| ||

 

 

37. Vuddhi (or Aparihāni?)

2. Sattime bhikkhave bojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā vuddhiyā aparihānāya saɱvattanti|| ||

Katame satta?|| ||

3. Satisambojjhaŋgo ... pe ... upekhāsambojjhaŋgo|| ||

4. Ime kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā vuddhiyā aparihānāya saɱvattantīti|| ||

 

 

38. Āvaraṇa-Nīvaraṇa (or Nīvaraṇāvaraṇa)

2. Pañcime bhikkhave āvaraṇā nīvaraṇā cetaso uppakkilesā paññāya dubbalīkaraṇā|| ||

Katame pañca?|| ||

3. Kāmacchando bhikkhave āvaraṇo nīvaraṇo cetaso upakkileso paññāya dubbalīkaraṇo||
Byāpādo bhikkhave āvaraṇo nīvaraṇo cetaso uppakkileso paññāya dubbalīkaraṇo|| ||

Thīnamiddham bhikkhave āvaraṇaɱ nīvaraṇaɱ cetaso upakkilesam paññāya dubbalīkaraṇaɱ||
Uddhaccakukkuccam bhikkhave āvaraṇaɱ nīvaraṇaɱ cetaso upakkilesam paññāya dubbalīkaraṇaɱ

[page 095]

Vicikicchā bhikkhave āvaranā nīvaraṇā cetaso uppakkilesā paññāya dubbalīkaraṇā|| ||

4. Ime kho bhikkhave pañca āvaranā nīvaraṇā cetaso upakkilesā paññāya dubbulīkaraṇā|| ||

5. Sattime bhikkhave bojjhaŋgā anāvaraṇā anīvaraṇā cetaso anuppakkilesā bhavitā bahulīkatā vijjāvimuttiphalasacchikiriyāya saɱvattanti|| ||

Katame satta?|| ||

6. Satisambojjhaŋgo bhikkhave anāvaraṇo anīvaraṇo cetaso anupakkileso bhāvito bahulīkato vijjavimuttiphalasacchikiriyāya saɱvattati ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo bhikkhave anāvaraṇo anīvaraṇo cetaso anuppakkileso bhāvito bahulīkato vijjāvimuttiphalasacchikiriyāya saɱvattati|| ||

7. Ime kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā anāvaraṇā anīvaraṇa cetaso anupakkilesā bhāvitā bahulīkatā vijjāvimuttiphalasacchikiriyāya saɱvattanti|| ||

8. Yasmim bhikkhave samaye ariyasāvako aṭṭhiɱ katvā manasikatvā sabbacetaso sammannāharitvā ohitasoto dhammaɱ suṇāti||
imassa pañca nīvaraṇā tasmiɱ samaye na honti||
satta bojjhaŋgā tasmiɱ samaye bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchanti|| ||

9. Katame pañca nīvaraṇā tasmiɱ samaye na honti|| ||

Kāmacchandanīvaraṇaɱ tasmiɱ samaye na hoti|| ||

Byāpādanīvaraṇam ... pe ...Thīnamiddhanivaraṇaɱ tasmiɱ samaye na hoti|| ||

Uddhaccakukkuccanīvaraṇaɱ tasmiɱ samaye na hoti|| ||

Vicikicchānīvaraṇaɱ tasmiɱ samaye na hoti|| ||

Imassa pañca nīvaraṇā tasmiɱ samaye na honti.|| ||

10. Katame satta bojjhaŋgā tasmiɱ samaye bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchanti|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati||
... pe ...|| ||

Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhāvanā pāripūrim gacchati|| ||

[page 096]

11. Yasmiɱ bhikkhave samaye ariyasāvako aṭṭhiɱ katvā manasi katvā sabbacetaso samannāharitvā ohitasoto dhammaɱ suṇāṭi||
imassa pañca nīvaraṇā tasmiɱ samaye na honti||
ime satta bojjhaŋgā tasmiɱ samaye bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchantī ti|| ||

 

 

39. Rukkham

2. Santi bhikkhave mahārukkhā aṇubījā mahākāyā rukkhānaɱ ajjhārūhā||
ye hi rukkhā ajjhāruḷhā obhaggavibhaggā vipatitā senti|| ||

3. Katame ca bhikkhave mahārukkhā aṇubījā mahākāyā rukkhānam ajjhārūhā ye hi rukkhānam ajjhārūḷhā obhaggavibhaggā vipatitā senti|| ||

Seyyathīdam assattho nigrodho pilakkho udumbaro kacchako kapitthako|| ||

Ime kho te bhikkhave mahārukkhā aṇubījā mahākāyā rukkhānam ajjhārūhā ye hi rukkhā ajjhārūḷha obhaggavibhaggā vipatitā senti|| ||

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave idhekacco kulaputto yādisake kāme ohāya agārasmā anāgāriyam pabbajito hoti||
so tādisakehi vā kāmehi tato vā pāpiṭṭhatarehi obhaggavibhaggo vipatito seti|| ||

5. Pañcime bhikkhave āvaraṇā nīvaraṇā cetaso ajjhārūhā paññāya dubbalīkaraṇā|| ||

Katame pañca?|| ||

Kāmacchando bhikkhave āvaraṇo nīvaraṇo cetaso ajjhārūho paññāya dubbalīkaraṇo|| ||

Byāpādo bhikkhave āvaraṇo nīvaraṇo cetaso ajjhārūho paññāya dubbalīkaraṇo|| ||

Thīnamiddham bhikkhave āvaraṇaɱ nīvaraṇaɱ cetaso ajjhārūham paññāya dubbalīkaraṇaɱ|| ||

Uddhaccakukkuccam bhikkhave āvaraṇam nīvaraṇam cetaso ajjhārūhaɱ paññāya dubbalīkaraṇaɱ|| ||

Vicikicchā bhikkhave āvaraṇā nīvaraṇā ajjhārūhā paññaya dubbalīkaraṇā|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave pañca āvaranā nīvaraṇā cetaso ajjhārūhā paññāya dubbalīkaraṇā

[page 097]

6. Sattime bhikkhave bojjhaŋgā anāvaraṇā anīvaraṇā cetaso anajjhārūhā bhāvitā bahulīkatā vijjāvimuttiphalasacchikiriyāya saɱvattanti||
katame satta|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo bhikkhave anāvaraṇo anīvaraṇo cetaso anajjhārūho bhāvito bahulīkato vijjāvimuttiphalasacchikiriyāya saɱvattati||
... pe ...|| ||

Upekhāsambojjaŋgo bhikkhave anāvaraṇo anīvaraṇo cetaso anajjārūho bhāvito bahulīkato vijjāvimuttiphalasacchikiriyāya saɱvattati|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā anāvaraṇā anīvaraṇā cetaso anajjhārūhā bhāvitā bahulīkatā vijjavimuttiphalasacchikiriyāya saɱvatta tī ti|| ||

 

 

40. Nīvaraṇaɱ

2. Pañcime bhikkhave nīvaraṇā andhakaraṇā acakkhukaraṇā aññāṇakaraṇā paññānirodhikā vighātapakkhiyā anibbānasaɱvattanikā|| ||

Katame pañca?|| ||

Kāmacchandanīvaraṇam bhikkhave andhakaraṇam āññāṇakaraṇam acakkhukaraṇam paññānirodhikaɱ vighātapakkhiyam anibbāna{saɱvattanikaɱ}||
Byāpādanīvaraṇam bhikkhave ||... pe ...||
Thīnamiddhanīvaraṇam bhikkhave ||... pe ...||
Uddhaccakukkuccanīvaraṇam bhikkhave ||... pe ...|| ||

Vicikicchānīvaraṇam bhikkhave andhakaraṇam acakkhukaraṇam aññāṇakaraṇam aññānirodhikaɱ vighātapakkhiyam anibbānasaɱvattanikaɱ|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave pañcanīvaraṇā andhakaraṇā acakkhukaraṇā aññāṇakaraṇā paññānirodhikā vighātapakkhiyā anibbānasaɱvattanikā|| ||

3. Sattime bhikkhave bojjhaŋgā cakkhukaraṇā ñāṇakaraṇā paññāvuddhiyā avighātapakkhiyā nibbānasaɱvattanikā|| ||

Katame satta?|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo bhikkhave cakkhukaraṇo ñāṇakaraṇo paññāvuddhiyo avighātapakkhiyo nibbānasaɱvattaniko||
... pe ...|| ||

Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo bhikkhave cakkhukaraṇo ñāṇakaraṇo paññāvuddhiyo avighātapakkhiyo nibbānasaɱvattaniko|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave satta bojjhaŋgā cakkhukaraṇā ñaṇakaraṇā paññavuddhiyā avighātapakkhiyā nibbānasaɱvattanikāti

[page 098]

Nīvaraṇavaggo catuttho|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Dve Kusalā Kilesā ca||
Dve Yoniso ca Vuddhi ca||
Āvaraṇo Aparihāni||
Nīvaraṇavaraṇa Rukkhaɱ||
Nīvaraṇañca te dasāti|| ||

 

 

Chapter V. Cakkavatti Vaggo

41. Vidhā

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā tisso vidhā pajahiɱsu||
sabbe te satannam bojjhaŋgānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

Ye hi keci bhikkhave anāgatam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā tisso vidhā pajahissanti||
sabbe te sattannam bojjhaŋgānam bhavitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

Ye hi keci bhikkhave etarahi samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā tisso vidhā pajahanti||
sabbe te sattannam bojjhaŋgānam bhavitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

3. Katamesaɱ sattannaɱ bojjhaŋgānaɱ|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgassa ... pe ... upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa||
4. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā tisso vidhā pajahiɱsu||
... pe ...||
pajahissanti||
... pe ...||
pajahanti||
sabbe te imesaññeva sattannam bojjhaŋgānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā ti|| ||

[page 099]

 

 

42. Cakkavatti

2. Rañño bhikkhave cakkavattissa pātubhāvā sattannam ratanānam pātubhāvo hoti|| ||

Katamesaɱ sattannaɱ|| ||

3. Cakkaratanassa pātubhāvo hoti||
hatthiratanassaassaratanassa||
maṇiratanassa||
itthiratanassa||
gahapatiratanassa-||
parināyakaratanassa pātubhāvo hoti|| ||

Rañño bhikkhave cakkavattissa pātubhāvā imesaɱ sattannam ratanānam pātubhāvo hoti|| ||

4. Tathāgatassa bhikkhave pātubhāvā arahato sammāsambuddhassa sattannam bojjhaŋgaratanānam pātubhāvo hoti|| ||

Katamesaɱ sattannaɱ|| ||

5. Satisambojjhaŋgaratanassa pātubhāvo hoti||
... pe ...|| ||

Upekhāsambojjhaŋgaratanassa pātubhavo hoti|| ||

Tathāgatassa bhikkhave pātubhāvā arahato sammāsambuddhassa imesaɱ sattannam bojjhaŋgaratanānaɱ pātubhāvo hoti ti|| ||

 

 

43. Māro

2. Mārasenapamaddanaɱ vo bhikkhave maggaɱ desissāmi||
taɱ suṇātha|| ||

3. Katamo ca bhikkhave mārasenapamaddano maggo||
yadidam satta bojjhaŋgā|| ||

Katame satta?|| ||

Satisambojjhaŋgo||
pa-pe|| ||

Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo|| ||

Ayaɱ kho bhikkhave mārasenapamaddano maggo ti|| ||

 

 

44. Duppañño

2. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami|| ... pe ...|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Duppañño eḷamūgo duppañño eḷamūgo ti bhante vuccati||
kittāvatā nu kho bhante Duppañño eḷamūgo ti vuccatī ti|| ||

4. Sattannaɱ kho bhikkhu bojjhaŋgānam abhāvitattā abahulīkatattā duppañño eḷamūgo ti vuccati|| ||

[page 100]

Satisambojjhaŋgassa ... pe ... Upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa|| ||

45. Paññavā

Kittāvatā nu kho bhante paññavā anelamūgoti vuccatī ti|| ||

... pe ...|| ||

46. Daliddo

kittāvatā nu kho bhante Daliddo ti vuccatī ti|| ||

4. Sattannaɱ kho bhikkhu bojjhaŋgānam abhāvitattā abahulīkatattā Daliddo ti vuccati|| ||
