48. Ādicco

2. Adiccassa bhikkhave udayato etam pubbaŋgamaɱ etam pubbanimittam yadidam aruṇuggaɱ||
evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhuno sattannam bhojjhaŋgānam uppādāya etam pubbaŋgamam etam pubbanimittaɱ yad idaɱ kalyāṇamittatā|| ||

3. Kalyāṇamittassetam bhikkhave bhikkhuno pāṭikaŋkhaɱ satta bojjhaŋge bhāvessati||
satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkarissati|| ||

Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu kalyāṇamitto satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti- -bahulīkaroti|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ ... pe ... upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekavirāga- nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu kalyāṇamitto sattabojjhaŋge bhāveti sattabojjhaŋge bahulīkarotī ti|| ||

 

 

49. Aŋga

2. Ajjhattikam bhikkhave aŋgan ti karitvā nāññam ekaŋgam pi samanupassāmi sattannam bojjhaŋgānam uppādāya||
yathayidam bhikkhave yonisomanasikāro|| ||

3. Yonisomanasikarasampannassetam bhikkhave bhikkhuno pātikaŋkhaɱ satta bojjhaŋge bhāvessati- bahulīkarissati|| ||

Kathañ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu yoniso manasikārasampanno satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti satta bojjhaŋge bahulīkaroti|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ ... pe ... upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitam vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

5. Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu yoniso manasikārasampanno sattabojjhaŋge bhāveti||
satta bojjhaŋge bahulī karotī ti|| ||

[page 102]

 

 

50. Aŋga 2

2. Bāhiram bhikkhave aŋgan ti kāritvā nāññam ekaŋgam pi samanupassāmi||
sattannam bojjhaŋgānam uppādāya||
yathayidam bhikkhave kalyāṇamittatā|| ||

3. Kalyāṇamittassetam bhikkhave bhikkhuno pāṭikaŋkhaɱ satta bojjhaŋge bhāvessati- bahulīkarissati|| ||

Kathañ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu kalyāṇamitto satta bojjhaŋge bhāveti -bahulīkaroti|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ||
... pe ...||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggaparināmiɱ|| ||

5. Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu kalyāṇamitto sattabojjhaŋge bhāveti- bahulīkarotī ti|| ||

Cakkavattivaggo pañcamo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Vidhā Cakkavatti Māro||
Duppañño Paññavena ca||
Daliddo Adaliddo ca||
Ādicco Aŋgena te dasā ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter VI. Bojjaŋgasākaccaɱ

Sāvatthi nidānaɱ|| ||

51. Ahāra

2. Pañcannaɱ ca bhikkhave nīvaraṇānam sattannañca bojjhaŋgānam āhārañca anāhārañca desissāmi||
taɱ suṇātha|| ||

I. Āhāro Nīvaraṇāɱ

3. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā kāmacchandassa uppādāya uppannassa vā kāmacchandassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya

[page 103]

Atthi bhikkhave subhanimittaɱ||
tattha ayonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā kāmacchandassa uppādāya uppannassa vā kāmacchandassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

4. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā byāpādassa uppādāya uppannassa vā byāpādassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave paṭighanimittaɱ||
tattha ayonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā byāpādassa uppādāya uppannassa vā byāpādassa bhiyyo bhāvaya vepullāya|| ||

5. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā thīnamiddhassa upādāya uppannassa vā thīnamiddhassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhan arati tandivijambhitā bhattasammado cetaso ca līnattam||
tattha ayonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā thīnamiddhassa uppādāya uppannassa vā thīnamiddhassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

6. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā uddhaccakukkuccassa uppādāya uppannassa vā uddhaccakukkuccassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave cetaso avūpasamo||
tattha ayoniso manasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā uddhaccakukkuccassa uppādāya uppannassa vā uddhaccakukkuccassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

7. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannāya vā vicikicchāya uppādāya uppannāya vā vicikicchāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave vicikicchāṭṭhāniyā dhammā||
tattha ayoniso manasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannāya vā vicikicchāya uppādāya uppannāya vā vicikicchāya bhiyyobhāvanāya vepullāya|| ||

II. Āhāro Bojjhaŋgānaɱ

8. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā satisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā satisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave satisambojjhaŋgaṭṭhāniyā dhammā

[page 104]

tattha yoniso manasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā satisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā satisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

9. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya paripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave kusalākusalā dhammā sāvajjānavajjā dhammā hīnapaṇītā dhammā kaṇhasukkasappaṭibbāgā dhammā||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulikāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

10. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā viriyasambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā viriyasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave ārambhadhātu nikkamadhātu parakkamadhātu||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā viriyasambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā viriyasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

11. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā pītisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā pītisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave pītisambojjhaŋgaṭṭhāniyā dhammā||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā pītisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā pītisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

12. Ko ca bhi- āhāro anuppannassa vā passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya parīpūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhi- kāyapassaddhi cittapassaddhi||
tattha yoniso manasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

[page 105]

13. Ko ca bhi- āhāro anuppannassa vā samādhisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā samādhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripuriyā|| ||

Atthi bhi- samathanimittam avyagganimittam||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā samādhisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā samādhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

14. Ko ca bhikkhave āhāro anuppannassa vā upekhasambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya paripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave upekhāsambojjhaŋgaṭṭhaniyā dhammā||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam āhāro anuppannassa vā upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

III. Anāhāro Nīvaraṇānaɱ

15. Ko ca bhikkhave anāhāro anuppannassa vā kāmacchandassa uppādāya uppannassa vā kāmacchandassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave asubhanimittam||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam anāhāro anuppannassa vā kāmacchandassa uppādāya uppannassa vā kāmacchandassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

16. Ko ca bhikkhave anāhāro anuppannassa vā byāpādassa uppādāya uppannassa vā byāpādassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave mettācetovimutti||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam anāhāro anuppannassa vā byāpādassa uppādāya uppannassa vā byāpādassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

17. Ko ca bhikkhave anāhāro anuppannassa vā thīnamiddhassa uppādāya uppannassa vā thīnamiddhassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave ārambhadhātu nikkamadhātu parakkamadhātu||
tattha yoniso manasikāra bahulīkāro ayam anāhāro anuppannassa vā thīnamiddhassa uppādāya uppannassa vā thīnamiddhassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya

[page 106]

18. Ko ca bhikkhave anāhāro anuppannassa vā uddhaccakukkuccassa uppādāya uppannassa vā uddhaccakukkuccassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave cetaso vūpasamo||
tattha yoniso manasikārabahulīkāro ayam anāhāro anuppannassa vā uddhaccakukkuccassa uppādāya uppannassa vā uddhaccakukkuccassa bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

19. Ko ca bhikkhave anāhāro anuppannāya vā vicikicchāya uppādāya uppannāya vā vicikicchāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave kusalākusalā dhammā sāvajjānavajjā dhammā hīnapaṇītā dhammā kaṇhasukkasappaṭibhāgā dhammā||
tattha yonisomanasikārabahulīkāro ayam anāhāro anuppannāya vā vicikicchāya uppādāya uppannāya vā vicikicchāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya|| ||

IV. Anāhāro Bojjhaŋgānaɱ

20. Ko ca bhikkhave anāhāro anuppannassa vā satisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā satisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave satisambojjhaŋgaṭṭhāniyā dhammā||
tattha amanasikārabahulīkāro ayam anāhāro anuppannassa vā satisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā satisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

21. Ko ca bhikkhave anāhāro anuppannassa vā dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthibhikkhave kusalākusalā dhammā sāvajjānavajjā dhammā hīnapaṇītā dhammā kaṇhasukkasappaṭibhāgā dhammā||
tattha amanasikārabahulīkāro ayam anāhāro anuppannassa vā dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

22. Ko ca bhikkhave anāhāro anuppannassa vā viriyasambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā viriyasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā

[page 107]

Atthi bhikkhave ārambhadhātu nikkamadhātu parakkamadhātu||
tattha amanasikārabahulīkāro ayam anāharo anuppannassa vā viriyasambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā viriyasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

23. Ko ca bhikkhave anāhāro anuppannassa vā pītisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā pītisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave pītisambojjhaŋgaṭṭhāniyā dhammā||
tattha amanasikārabahulīkaro ayam anāhāro anuppannassa vā pītisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā pītisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

24. Ko ca bhikkhave anāhāro anuppannassa vā passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāyapāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave kāyapassaddhi cittapassaddhi||
tattha amanasikārabahulīkāro ayam anāhāro anuppannassa vā passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

25. Ko ca bhikkhave anāhāro anuppannassa vā samādhisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā samādhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave samathanimittam abyagganimittam||
tattha amanasikārabahulīkāro ayam anāhāro anuppannassa vā samādhisambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā samādhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

26. Ko ca bhikkhave anāhāro anuppannassa vā upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā|| ||

Atthi bhikkhave upekhāsambojjhaŋgaṭṭhāniyā dhammā||
tattha amanasikārabahulīkāro ayam anāhāro anuppannassa vā upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa uppādāya uppannassa vā uppekhāsambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya pāripūriyā ti|| ||

[page 108]

 

 

52. Pariyāya

2. Atha kho sambahulā bhikkhū pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Sāvatthim piṇḍaya pavisiɱsu|| ||

3. Atha kho tesam bhikkhūnam etad ahosi|| ||

Atippago kho tāva Sāvatthiyam piṇḍāya carituɱ||
yaɱ nuna mayaɱ yena aññatitthiyānam ārāmo tenupasaŋkamayyemā ti|| ||

4. Atha kho te bhikkhū yena aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam ārāmo tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā tehi aññatitthiyehi paribbājakehi saddhiɱ sammodiɱsu||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinne kho te bhikkhū aññatitthiyā paribbājakā etad avocuɱ|| ||

5. Samaṇo āvuso Gotamo sāvakānam evaɱ dhammaɱ deseti||
Etha tumhe bhikkhave pañca nīvaraṇe pahāya cetaso upakkilese paññāya dubbalīkaraṇe sattabojjhaŋge yathābhūtam bhāvethāti|| ||

Mayam pi kho āvuso sāvakānam evaɱ dhammaɱ desema||
Etha tumhe āvuso pañca nīvaraṇe pahāya cetaso upakkilese paññāya dubbalīkaraṇe satta bojjhaŋge yathābhūtam bhāvethāti|| ||

Idha no āvuso ko viseso ko adhippāyo||
kiɱ nānākaraṇaɱ samaṇassa vā Gotamassa amhākaɱ vā yadidam dhammadesanāya vā dhammadesanam anusāsaniyā vā anusāsanin ti|| ||

6. Atha kho te bhikkhū tesam aññatitthiyānam paribbajakānam bhāsitaɱ neva abhinandiɱsu nappaṭikkosiɱsu||
anabhinanditvā appaṭikkositvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkamiɱsu|| ||

Bhagavato santike etassa bhāsitassa atthaɱ ājānissāmāti|| ||

7. Atha kho te bhikkhū Sāvatthiyaɱ piṇḍaya caritvā pacchābhattaɱ piṇḍapātapatikkantā yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu|| ||

[page 109]

8. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū Bhagavantam etad avocuɱ|| ||

Idha mayam bhante pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Sāvatthim piṇḍaya pavisimha||
tesaɱ no bhante amhākam etad ahosi||
Atippago kho tāva Sāvatthiyam piṇḍāya carituɱ yaɱ nuna mayaɱ yena aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam ārāmo tenupasaŋkameyyāmā ti|| ||

Atha kho mayam bhante yena aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam ārāmo tenupasaŋkamimha||
upasaŋkamitvā tehi aññatitthiyehi paribbājakehi saddhiɱ sammodimha||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdimha||
Eka-m-antaɱ nisinne kho amhe bhante te aññatitthiyā paribbājakā etad avocuɱ|| ||

9. Samaṇo āvuso Gotamo sāvakānam evam dhammaɱ deseti -anusāsaniyā vā anusāsaninti|| ||

10. Atha kho mayam bhante tesam aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam bhāsitaɱ neva abhinandimha na paṭikkosimha||
anabhinanditvā appaṭikkositvā uṭṭhāyasanā pakkamimha Bhagavato santike etassa bhāsitassa attham ājānissāmāti|| ||

11. Evaɱ vādino bhikkhave aññatitthiyā paribbājakā evam assu vacaniyā|| ||

Atthi panāvuso pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma pañca nīvaraṇā dasa honti||
satta bojjhaŋgā catuddasā ti|| ||

Evam puṭṭhā bhikkhave aññatitthiyā paribbājakā na ceva sampāyissanti uttariñca vighātam āpajjissanti|| ||

12. Tam kissa hetu|| ||

Yathā tam bhikkhave avisayasmiɱ||
nāhaɱ tam bhikkhave passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sasamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya yo imesam pañhānaɱ veyyākaraṇena cittam ārādheyya aññatra tathāgatena vā Tathāgatasāvakena vā ito vā pana sutvā|| ||

[page 110]

I. Pañca Dasa Honti

13. Katamo ca bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma pañca nīvaraṇā dasa honti|| ||

14. Yad api bhikkhave ajjhattam kāmacchando tad api nīvaraṇaɱ||
yad api bahiddhā kāmacchando tad api nīvaraṇaɱ Kāmacchandanīvaraṇaɱ ti iti hidam uddesam āgacchati||
tad aminā petam pariyāyena dvayaɱ hoti|| ||

15. Yad api bhikkhave ajjhattam byāpādo tadapi nīvaraṇaɱ||
yad api bahiddhā byāpādo tad api nīvaraṇam Byāpādanīvaraṇan ti iti hidam uddesaɱ āgacchati||
tad aminā petam pariyāyena dvayaɱ hoti|| ||

16. Yad api bhikkhave thīnaɱ tad api nīvaraṇam||
yadapi middham tad api nīvaranaɱ Thīnamiddhanīvaraṇam ti iti hidam uddesam āgacchati||
tad aminā petam pariyāyena dvayaɱ hoti|| ||

17. Yad api bhikkhave uddhaccaɱ tad api nīvaraṇaɱ yad api kukkuccaɱ tad api nīvaraṇam Uddhacca kukkucca nīvaraṇan ti iti hidam uddesam āgacchati||
tad aminā petam pariyāyena dvayaɱ hoti|| ||

18. Yad api bhikkhave ajjhattam dhammesu vicikicchā tad api nīvaraṇaɱ||
yad api bāhiddhā dhammesu vicikicchā tad api nīvaraṇam Vicikicchānīvaraṇan ti Iti hidam uddesam āgacchati||
tad aminā petam pariyāyena dvayaɱ hoti|| ||

19. Ayam kho bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma pañca nīvaraṇā dasa honti|| ||

II. Satta Catuddasa Honti

20. Katamo ca bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma satta bojjhaŋgā catuddasa honti|| ||

21. Yad api bhikkhave ajjhattam dhammesu sati tad api satisambojjhaŋgo||
yad api bahiddhā dhammesu sati tad api satisambojjhaŋgo Satisambojjhaŋgo ti iti hidam uddesam āgacchati||
tad aminā petam pariyāyena dvayaɱ hoti|| ||

[page 111]

22. Yad api bhikkhave ajjhattaɱ dhammesu paññāya pavicinati pavicarati parivīmaɱsam āpajjati tad api dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgo|| ||

Yad api bahiddhā dhammesu paññāya pavicinati pavicarati parivīmaɱsam āpajjati||
tad api dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgo Dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgo ti iti hidam uddesaɱ āgacchati||
tad aminā petam pariyāyena dvayaɱ hoti|| ||

23. Yad api bhikkhave kāyikaɱ viriyaɱ tad api viriyasambojjhaŋgo||
yad api cetasikaɱ viriyaɱ tad api viriyasambojjhaŋgo Viriyasambojjhaŋgo ti iti hidam uddesam āgacchati||
tad aminā petam pariyāyena dvayaɱ hoti|| ||

24. Yad api bhikkhave savitakkasavicārā pīti tad api pītisambojjhaŋgo||
yad api avitakka avicārā pīti tad api pītisambojjhaŋgo Pītisambojjhaŋgo ti iti hidam uddesam āgacchati||
tad aminā petam parīyāyena dvayaɱ hoti|| ||

25. Yad api bhikkhave kāyapassaddhi tad api passaddhisambojjhaŋgo||
yad api cittapassaddhi tad api passaddhisambojjhaŋgo Passaddhisambojjhaŋgo ti iti hidam uddesam āgacchati||
tad aminā petam pariyāyena dvayam hoti|| ||

26. Yad api bhikkhave savitakko savicāro samādhi tad api samādhisambojjhaŋgo||
yad api avitakko avicāro samādhi tad api samādhisambojjhaŋgo Samādhisambojjhaŋgo ti iti hi uddesam āgacchati||
tad aminā petam pariyāyena dvayaɱ hoti|| ||

27. Yad api bhikkhave ajjhattam dhammesu upekhā tad api upekhāsambojjhaŋgo||
yad api bahiddhā dhammesu upekhā tad api upekhāsambojjhaŋgo Upekhāsambojjhaŋgo ti iti hidam uddesam āgacchati||
tad aminā petam pariyāyena dvayaɱ hoti|| ||

28. Ayaɱ kho bhikkhave pariyāyo||
yam pariyāyam āgamma satta bojjhaŋgā catuddasā ti|| ||

[page 112]

 

 

53. Aggi

2. Atha kho sambahulā bhikkhū pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Sāvatthiɱ piṇḍaya pavisiɱsu|| ||

3—10. Pariyāyasuttasadisaɱ|| ||

11. Evam vādino bhikkhave aññatitthiyā paribbājakā evam assu vacanīyā|| ||

Yasmim āvuso samaye līnaɱ cittaɱ hoti||
katamesaɱ tasmiɱ samaye bojjhaŋgānam akālo bhāvanāya||
katamesaɱ tasmiɱ samaye bojjhaŋgānam kālo bhāvanāya|| ||

Yasmim panāvuso samaye uddhataɱ cittaɱ hoti||
katamesaɱ tasmiɱ samaye bojjhaŋgānam akālo bhāvanāya||
katamesam tasmiɱ samaye bojjhaŋgānaɱ kālo bhāvanāyā ti|| ||

Evam puṭṭhā bhikkhave aññatitthiyā paribbājakā na ceva sampāyissanti uttariɱ ca vighātam āpajjissanti|| ||

12. Tam kissa hetu|| ||

Yathā tam bhikkhave avisayasmiɱ|| ||

Nāhaɱ tam bhikkhave passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sasamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya yo imesam pañhānaɱ veyyakāraṇena cittam ārādheyya aññatra tathāgatena vā Tathāgatasāvakena vā ito vā pana sutvā|| ||

I. Akālo

13. Yasmiɱ bhikkhave samaye līnaɱ cittaɱ hoti||
akālo tasmiɱ samaye passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya||
akālo samādhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya akālo upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

Līnam bhikkhave cittam tam etehi dhammehi dussamuṭṭhāpayaɱ hoti|| ||

14. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave puriso parittam aggim ujjāletukāmo assa||
So tattha allāni ceva tiṇāni pakkhipeyya allāni ca gomayāni pakkhipeyya allāni ca kaṭṭhani pakkhipeyya udakavātañca dadeyya paɱsukāna ca okireyya bhabbo nu kho so puriso parittam aggim ujjāletuɱ

[page 113]

No hetam bhante|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave yasmiɱ samaye līnaɱ cittam hoti||
akālo tasmiɱ samaye passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya||
akālo samādhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya||
akālo upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

līnam bhikkhave cittaɱ tam etehi dhammehi dussamuṭṭhāpayaɱ hoti|| ||

II. Kālo|| ||

15. Yasmiɱ ca kho bhikkhave samaye līnaɱ cittaɱ hoti||
kālo {tasmiɱ} samaye dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya kālo viriyasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya kālo pītisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya|| ||

Tam kissa hetu||
līnaɱ bhikkhave cittaɱ tam etehi dhammehi susamuṭṭhāpayaɱ hoti|| ||

16. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave puriso parittam aggim ujjāletukāmo assa||
so tattha sukkhāni ceva tiṇāni pakkhipeyya sukkhāni gomayāni pakkhipeyya sukkhāni kaṭṭhāni pakkhipeyya||
mukhavātañca dadeyya na ca paɱsukena okireyya||
bhabbo nu kho so puriso parittam aggim ujjāletun ti|| ||

Evam bhante|| ||

Evaɱ eva kho bhikkhave yasmiɱ samaye līnaɱ cittaɱ hoti||
kālo tasmiɱ samaye dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya||
kālo viriyasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya||
kālo pītisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

līnaɱ bhikkhave cittaɱ tam etehi dhammehi susamuṭṭhāpayaɱ hoti|| ||

III. Akālo|| ||

17. Yasmim bhikkhave samaye uddhataɱ cittaɱ hoti||
akālo tasmiɱ samaye dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya||
akālo viriyasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya||
akālo pītisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya

[page 114]

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

Uddhatam bhikkhave cittaɱ tam etehi dhammehi duvūpasamayaɱ hoti|| ||

18. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave puriso mahantam aggikhandhaɱ nibbāpetukāmo assa||
so tattha sukkhāni ceva teṇāni pakkhipeyya sukkhāni gomayāni pakkhipeyya sukkhānī ca kaṭṭhāni pakkhipeyya mukhavātañca dadeyya na ca paɱsukena okireyya||
bhabbo nu kho so puriso mahantam aggikhandhaɱ nibbāpetun ti|| ||

No hetam bhante|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave yasmiɱ samaye uddhataɱ cittaɱ hoti||
akālo tasmiɱ samaye dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya||
akālo {viriyasambojjhaŋgassa} bhāvanāya||
akālo pītisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

uddhatam bhikkhave cittaɱ tam etehi dhammehi duvūpasamayam hoti|| ||

IV. Kālo|| ||

19. Yasmiɱ ca kho bhikkhave samaye uddhataɱ cittaɱ hoti||
kālo tasmiɱ samaye passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya||
kālo samādhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya||
kālo upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

uddhatam bhikkhave cittaɱ tam etehi dhammehi suvūpasamayaɱ hoti|| ||

20. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave puriso mahantam aggikhandhaɱ nibbāpetukāmo assa||
so tattha allāni ceva tiṇāni pakkhipeyya allāni ca gomayāni pakkhipeyya- allāni ca kaṭṭhāni pakkhipeyya udakavātañ ca dadeyya||
paɱsukena ca okireyya||
bhabbo nu kho so puriso mahantam aggikhandhaɱ nibbāpetunti|| ||

Evam bhante||
Evam eva kho bhikkhave yasmim samaye uddhataɱ cittaɱ hoti

[page 115]

kālo tasmiɱ samaye passaddhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya||
kālo samādhisambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya||
kālo upekhāsambojjhaŋgassa bhāvanāya|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

uddhatam bhikkhave cittaɱ tam etehi dhammehi suvūpasamayaɱ hoti|| ||

21. Satim ca kvāham bhikkhave sabbatthikaɱ vadāmīti|| ||

 

 

54. Mettam

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Koliyesu viharati Haliddavasaṇaɱ nāma Koliyānaɱ nigamo|| ||

2. Atha kho sambahulā bhikkhū pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Haliddavasanam piṇḍāya pavisiɱsu|| ||

3. Atha kho tesam bhikkhūnam etad ahosi||
Atippago kho tāva Haliddavasane piṇḍāya carituɱ||
yaɱ nuna mayaɱ yena aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam ārāmo tenupasaŋkameyyāmā ti|| ||

4. Atha kho te bhikkhū yena aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam ārāmo tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā tehi aññatitthiyehi paribbājakehi saddhim sammodiɱsu||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārānīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinne kho te bhikkhū te aññatitthiyā paribbājakā etad avocuɱ|| ||

5. Samaṇo āvuso Gotamo sāvakānam evaɱ dhammaɱ deseti|| ||

Etha tumhe bhikkhave pañcanīvaraṇe pahāya cetaso upakkilese paññāya dubbalīkaraṇe mettāsahagatena cetasā ekaɱ disam pharitvā viharatha||
tathā dutiyaɱ tathā tatiyam tathā catutthaɱ||
iti uddham adho tīriyaɱ sabbādhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaɱ lokam mettāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjhena pharitvā viharatha

[page 116]

Karuṇāsahagatena cetasā ekaɱ disam pharitvā viharatha||
tathā dutiyam tathā tatiyaɱ tathā catutthaɱ||
iti uddhaɱ adho tiriyam sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaɱ lokam karuṇāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjhena pharitvā viharatha|| ||

Muditāsahagatena cetasā ekaɱ disam pharitvā viharatha||
tathā dutiyaɱ tathā tatiyaɱ tathā catuttham||
iti uddham adho tiriyaɱ sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaɱ lokam muditāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjhenā pharitvā viharatha|| ||

Upekhāsahagatena cetasā ekaɱ disam pharitvā viharatha||
tathā dutiyam tathā tatiyaɱ tathā catuttham iti uddham adho tiriyaɱ sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaɱ lokam upekhāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjhena pharitvā viharathā ti|| ||

6. Mayam pi kho āvuso sāvakānam evaɱ dhammaɱ desema|| ||

Etha tumhe āvuso pañca nīvaraṇe pahāya cetaso upakkilese paññāya dubbalīkaraṇe mettāsahagatena cetasā ekaɱ disam pharitvā viharatha||
... pe ...||
Karunā sahagatena cetasā||
Muditāsahagatena cetasā||
Upekhāsahagatena cetasā ekaɱ disam pharitvā viharatha||
tathā dutiyaɱ tathā tatiyaɱ tathā catutthaɱ||
iti uddham adho tiriyam sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantam lokam upekhāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjhena pharitvā viharathā ti|| ||

7. Idha no āvuso ko viseso ko adhippāyo so kiɱ nānākaraṇaɱ samaṇassa Gotamassa amhākaɱ vā yadidam dhammadesanāya vā dhammadesanam anusāsaniyā anusāsaninti

[page 117]

Atha kho te bhikkhū tesam aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānaɱ bhāsitaɱ neva abhinandiɱsu na paṭikkosiɱsu||
anabhinanditvā appaṭikkositvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkamiɱsu Bhagavato santike etassa bhāsitassa attham ājānissāmāti|| ||

8. Atha kho te bhikkhū Haliddavasane piṇḍāya caritvā pacchābhattam piṇḍapātapaṭikkantā yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū Bhagavantam etad avocuɱ|| ||

9. Idha mayam bhante pubbaṇhasamayam nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Haliddavasanam piṇḍāya pavisimha||
tesaɱ no bhante amhākam etad ahosi||
Atippago kho tāva Haliddavasane piṇḍāya carituɱ||
yan nuna mayam yena aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam ārāmo tenupasaŋkameyyāmāti|| ||

Atha kho mayam bhante yena aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam ārāmo tenupasaŋkamimha||
... pe...||
tehi aññatitthiyehi paribbājakehi saddhiɱ sammodimha||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdimha||
Eka-m-antaɱ nisinne kho amhe bhante te aññatitthiyā paribbājakā etad avocuɱ|| ||

Samaṇo āvuso Gotamo sāvakānam evaɱ dhammaɱ deseti||
Etha tumhe bhikkhave pañca nīvaraṇe pahāya cetaso upakkilese paññāya dubbalīkaraṇe mettāsahagatena cetasā ekaɱ disam pharitvā viharatha||
... pe ...||
karuṇāsahagatena cetasā||
muditāsahagatena cetasā||
upekhāsahagatena cetasā ekaɱ disam pharitvā viharatha||
tathā dutiyaɱ tathā tatiyaɱ tathā catutthaɱ||
iti uddham adho tiriyaɱ sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaɱ lokam upekhāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjhena pharitvā viharathā ti

[page 118]

Mayam pi kho āvuso sāvakānam evaɱ dhammaɱ desema||
Etha tumhe āvuso pañca nīvaraṇe pahāya cetaso upakkilese paññāya dubbalīkaraṇe mettāsahagatena cetasā ekaɱ disaɱ pharitvā viharatha ... pe ... karuṇāsahagatena cetasā||
muditāsahagatena cetasā||
upekhāsahagatena cetasā ekaɱ disam pharitvā viharatha||
tathā dutiyam tathā tatiyam tathā catutthaɱ||
iti uddham adho tiriyaɱ sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaɱ lokam upekhāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjhena pharitvā viharathā ti|| ||

Idha no āvuso ko viseso ko adhippāyo so kiɱ nānākaraṇaɱ samaṇassa vā Gotamassa amhākaɱ vā yad idaɱ dhammadesanāya vā dhammadesanam anusāsaniyā vā anusāsaninti|| ||

Atha kho mayam bhante tesam aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam bhāsitam neva abhinandimha na paṭikkosimha||
anabhinanditvā appaṭikkositvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkamimha Bhagavato santika etassa bhāsitassa attham ājānissāmāti|| ||

10. Evaɱ vādino bhikkhave aññatitthiyā paribbājakā evam assu vacanīyā|| ||

Kathambhāvitā panāvuso mettācetovimutti kiŋgātikā hoti kimparamā kimphalā kim pariyosānā|| ||

Katham bhāvitā panāvuso karuṇācetovimutti kiŋgatikā hoti kimparamā kimphalā kimpariyosānā|| ||

Katham bhāvitā panāvuso muditācetovimutti||
kimpariyosanā|| ||

Katham bhāvitā panāvuso upekhācetovimutti° °kim pariyosānā ti|| ||

Evam puṭṭhā bhikkhave aññatitthiyā paribbājakā na ceva sampāyissanti uttariñca vighātam āpajjissanti|| ||

11. Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

Yathā tam bhikkhave avisayasmim|| ||

Nāhaɱ tam bhikkhave passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sasamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya yo imesam pañhānaɱ veyyākaraṇena cittam ārādheyya aññatra Tathāgatena vā Tathāgatasāvakena vā ito vā pana sutvā|| ||

[page 119]

12. Kathambhāvitā ca bhikkhave mettācetovimutti kiŋgatikā hoti kimparamā kimphalā kimpariyosānā|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu mettāsahagataɱ satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ... mettāsahagatam upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitam vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

So sace ākaŋkhati Appatikkūle paṭikkūlasaññī vihareyyanti||
paṭikkūlasaññī tattha viharati|| ||

Sa ce ākaŋkhati Paṭikkūle appaṭikkūlasaññī vihareyyanti||
appaṭikkūlasaññī tattha viharati|| ||

Sace ākaŋkhati Appaṭikkūle ca paṭikkūle ca paṭikkūlasaññī vihareyyanti||
paṭikkūlasaññī tattha viharati|| ||

Sace ākaŋkhati Paṭikkūle ca appaṭikkūle ca appaṭikkulasaññī vihareyyanti appaṭikkūlasaññī tattha viharati|| ||

Sace ākaŋkhati Appaṭikkūlañca {paṭikkūlañca} tad ubhayam abhinivajjetvā upekha ko vihareyyaɱ sato sampajāno ti||
upekhako tattha viharati sato sampajano|| ||

Subhaɱ vā kho pana vimokkham upasampajja viharati||
subhaparamāham bhikkhave mettācetovimuttiɱ vadāmi|| ||

Idha paññassa bhikkhuno uttariɱ vimuttim apaṭivijjhato|| ||

13. Kathambhāvitā ca bhikkhave karuṇācetovimutti kiŋgatikā hoti kimparamā kimphalā kimpariyosānā|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu karuṇasahagataɱ satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti||
... pe ...||
karunāsahagatam upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

So sace ākaŋkhati Appaṭikkūle paṭikkuḷasaññī vihareyyanti||
paṭikkūlasaññī tattha viharati ... pe ...|| ||
Sace ākaŋkhati Appaṭikkūlañca paṭikkūlañca tad ubhayam abhinivajjetvā upekhako vihareyyaɱ sato sampajāno ti||
upekhako tattha viharati sato sampajāno|| ||

Sabbaso vā pana rūpasaññānaɱ samatikkamā paṭighasaññanam atthagamā nānattasaññānam amanasikārā Ananto ākāso ti ākāsanañcāyatanam upasampajja viharati||
ākāsānañcāyatanaparamāham bhikkhave karuṇācetovimuttiɱ vadāmi|| ||

[page 120]

Idha paññassa bhikkhuno uttariɱvimuttim apaṭivijjhato|| ||

14. Kathaɱbhāvitā ca bhikkhave muditācetovimutti kiŋgatikā hoti kimparamā kimpariyosānā|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu muditāsahagataɱ satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti||
... pe ...||
muditāsahagatam upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka- virāgā- nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmim|| ||

So sace ākaŋkhati Appaṭikkūle paṭikkūlasaññī vihareyyanti||
paṭikkūlasaññī tattha viharati||
... pe ...||
sa ce ākaŋkhati Appaṭikkūlañca patikkūlañca tad ubhayam abhinivajjetvā upekkhako vihareyyaɱ sato sampajāno ti||
upekkhako tattha viharati sato sampajāno|| ||

Sabbaso vā pana ākāsānañcāyatanaɱ samatikkamma Anantaɱ viññāṇanti viññāṇañcāyatanam upasampajja viharati||
viññāṇañcāyatanaparamāham bhikkhave muditācetovimuttiɱ vadāmi|| ||

Idha paññassa bhikkhuno uttariɱvimuttim apaṭivijjhato|| ||

15. Kathambhāvitā ca bhikkhave upekhācetovimutt kiŋgātikā hoti kimparamā kimphalā kimpariyosānā|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu upekhāsahagataɱ satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitam vossaggapariṇāmim||
... pe ...||
upekhāsahagatam upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇamiɱ|| ||

So sace ākaŋkhati Appaṭikūle paṭikūlasaññī vihareyyanti||
paṭikūlasaññī tattha viharati||
Sace ākaŋkhati Paṭikūle appaṭikūlasaññī vihareyyanti||
appaṭikūlasaññī tattha viharati|| ||

Sace ākaŋkhati Appaṭikkūle ca paṭikkūle ca paṭikkūlasaññī vihareyyanti||
paṭikkūlasaññī tattha viharati||
Sace ākaŋkhati Paṭikūle ca appaṭikkūle ca appatikkūlasaññī vihareyyanti||
appaṭikkūlasaññī tattha viharati||
Sace ākaŋkhati Appatikkūlañca paṭikkūlañca tad ubhayam abhinivajjetvā upekhako vihareyyaɱ sato sampajāno ti||
upekhako tattha viharati sato sampajāno|| ||

[page 121]

Sabbaso vā pana viññāṇañcāyatanaɱ samatikkamma Natthi kiñcīti akiñcaññāyatanam upasampajja viharati|| ||

Ākiñcaññāyatanaparamāham bhikkhave upekhācetovimuttiɱ vadāmi|| ||

Idha paññassa bhikkhuno uttariɱvimuttim apaṭivijjhato ti|| ||

 

 

55. Sāŋgarava

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Atha kho Saŋgāravo brāhmaṇo yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodi||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyam vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Saŋgāravo brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Ko nu kho bho Gotama hetu ko paccayo yenekadā dīgharattam sajjhāyakatā pi mantā na paṭibhanti pageva asajjhāyakatā||
ko pana bho Gotama hetu ko paccayo yenekadā dīgharattam asajjhāyakatā pi mantā paṭibhanti pageva sajjhāyakatā ti|| ||

I.|| ||

4. {Yasmiɱ} kho brāhmaṇa samaye kāmarāgapariyuṭṭhitena cetasā viharati kāmarāgaparetena||
uppannassa ca kāmarāgassa nissaraṇaɱ yathābhūtaɱ na pajānāti attattham pi tasmiɱ samaye yathābhūtam na pajānāti na passati||
parattham pi tasmiɱ samaye yathābhūtaɱ na jānāti na passati||
ubhayattham pi tasmiɱ samaye yathābhūtaɱ na jānāti na passati||
dīgharattam sajjhāyakatā pi mantā na paṭibhanti pageva asajjhāyakatā|| ||

Seyyathā pi brāhmaṇa udapatto saɱsaṭṭho lākhāya vā haliddiyā vā niliyā vā mañjeṭṭhāya va vā||
tattha cakkhumā puriso sakam mukhanimittam paccavekkhamāno yathābhūtaɱ na jāneyya na passeyya||
evam eva kho brāhmaṇa yasmiɱ samaye kāmarāgapariyuṭṭhitena cetasā viharati kāmarāgaparetena||
uppannassa ca kāmarāgassa nissaraṇam yāthābhūtaɱ nappajānati||
attattham pi tasmiɱ samaye yathābhūtaɱ na jānāti na passati

[page 122]

parattham pi||
ubhayattham pi tasmiɱ samaye yathābhūtaɱ na jānāti na passati||
dīgharattam sajjhāyakatā pi mantā na paṭibhanti pageva asajjhāyakatā|| ||

5. Puna ca param brāhmaṇa yasmiɱ samaye byāpādapariyuṭṭhitena cetasā viharati byāpādaparetena||
uppannassa ca byāpadassa nissaraṇaɱ yathābhūtaɱ na pajānāti||
attattham pi tasmiɱ samaye yathābhūtaɱ na jānāti na passati||
parattham pi||
... pe ...||
ubhayattham pi tasmiɱ samaye yathābhūtaɱ na jānāti na passati||
dīgharattaɱ sajjhāyakatā pi mantā na paṭibhanti pageva asajjhāyakatā|| ||

Seyyathā pi brāhmaṇa udapatto agginā santatto ukkaṭṭhito usmudakajāto||
tattha cakkhumā puriso sakaɱ mukhanimittam paccavekkhamāno yathābhūtaɱ na jāneyya na passeyya||
evam eva kho brāhmaṇa yasmiɱ samaye byāpādapariyuṭṭhitena cetasā viharati byāpādaparetena||
uppannassa ca byāpādassa nissaraṇam yathābhūtam nappajānāti||
attattham pi tasmiɱ samaye yathābhūtam na jānāti na passati||
parattham pi||
... pe ...||
ubhayattham pi tasmiɱ samaye yathābhūtaɱ na jānāti na passati||
dīgharattaɱ sajjhāyakatā pi mantā na paṭibhanti pageva asajjhāyakatā|| ||

attattham pi° °na jānāti na passati||
parattham pi||
... pe ...||

Seyyathā pi brāhmaṇa udapatto sevālapaṇakapariyonaddho||
tattha cakkhumā puriso sakam mukhanimittam paccavekkhamāno yathābhūtaɱ na jāneyya na passeyya

evam eva kho brāhmaṇa yasmim samaye thīnamiddhapariyuṭṭhitena cetasā viharati thīnamiddhaparetena||

tattha cakkhumā puriso sakam mukhanimittam paccavekkhamāno yathābhūtaɱ na jāneyya na passeyya||
evam eva kho brāhmaṇa yasmiɱ samaye uddhaccakukkuccapariyuṭṭhitena cetasā viharati uddhaccakukkuccaparetena||

... pe ...||
ubhayattham pi° °na jānāti na passati||

tattha cakkhumā puriso sakam mukhanimittam paccavekkhamāno yathābhūtaɱ na jāneyya na passeyya

[page 124]

evam eva kho brāhmaṇa yasmiɱ samaye vicikicchāpariyuṭṭhitena cetasā viharati vicikicchāparetena||

parattham pi tasmiɱ samaye yathābhūtaɱ na jānāti na passati||

dīgharattaɱ sajjhāyakatā pi mantā na paṭibhanti pageva asajjhāyakatā|| ||

9. Ayaɱ kho brāhmaṇa hetu ayam paccayo yenekadā dīgharattaɱ sajjhāyakatā pi mantā na paṭibhanti pageva asajjhāyakatā|| ||

II.

10. Yasmiɱ ca kho brāhmaṇa samaye na kāmarāgapariyuṭṭhena cetasā viharati na kāmarāgaparetena||

parattham pi tasmiɱ samaye yathābhūtam jānāti passati||
ubhayattam pi tasmiɱ samaye yathābhūtam jānāti passati||
dīgharattam asajjhāyakatā pi mantā paṭibhanti pageva sajjhāyakatā|| ||

Seyyathā pi brāhmaṇa udapatto asaɱsaṭṭho lākhāya vā haliddiyā vā nīliyā vā mañjeṭṭhāya vā||
tattha cakkhumā puriso sakam mukhanimittam paccavekkhamāno yathābhūtaɱ jāneyya passeyya||

... pe ...|| ||

°sajjhāyakatā|| ||

tattha cakkhumā puriso passeyya

katame satta|| ||

56. Abhayo

1. Evam me sutam Ekam samayam Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Gijjhakūṭe pabbate|| ||

2. Atha kho Abhayo rājakumāro yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Ekam antam nisinno kho Abhayo rājakumāro Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Pūraṇo bhante Kassapo evam āha|| ||

Natthi hetu natthi paccayo aññaṇāya adassanāya ahetu apaccayo aññānaɱ adassanaɱ hoti|| ||

Natthi hetu natthi paccayo ñāṇāya dassanāya ahetu apaccayo ñāṇaɱ dassanaɱ hoti|| ||

Idha Bhagavā kim āhāti|| ||

4. Atthi rājakumāra hetu atthi paccayo aññaṇāya adassanāya sahetu sapaccayo aññāṇam adassaṇam hoti|| ||

[page 127]

Atthi rājakumāra hetu atthi paccayo ñānāya dassanāya sahetu sapaccayo ñānaɱ dassanaɱ hotī ti|| ||

I.

5. Katamo pana bhante hetu katamo paccayo aññānāya adassanāya||
kathaɱ sahetu sapaccayo aññānam adassanaɱ hotī ti|| ||

6. Yasmiɱ kho rājakumāra samaye kāmarāgapariyuṭṭhitena cetasā viharati kāmarāgaparetena||
uppannassa ca kāmarāgassa nissaraṇam yathābhūtaɱ na jānāti na passati||
ayam pi kho rājakumāra hetu ayam paccayo aññāṇaya adassanāya||
evam pi sahetu sapaccayo aññānaɱ adassanaɱ hoti|| ||

7. Puna ca param rājakumāra yasmiɱ samaye byāpādapariyuṭṭhitena cetasā viharati byāpādaparetenati ... pe ...|| ||

8. Thīnamiddhapariyuṭṭhitenati ... pe ...|| ||

9. Uddhaccakukkuccapariyuṭṭhitenati ... pe ...|| ||

10. Vicikicchāpariyuṭṭhitena cetasā viharati vicikicchāparetena||
uppannāya ca vicikicchāya nissaraṇaɱ yathābhūtaɱ na jānāti na passati||
ayam pi kho rājakumāra hetu ayam paccayo aññaṇāya adassanāya|| ||

Evam pi sahetu sapaccayo aññāṇam adassanaɱ hoti|| ||

11. Ko nāmāyam bhante dhammapariyāyo ti|| ||

Nīvaraṇā nāmete rājakumārā ti|| ||

Taggha Bhagavā nīvaraṇā taggha Sugata nīvaraṇā||
eka-m-ekena pi kho bhante nīvaraṇena abhibhūto yathābhūtaɱ na jāneyya na passeyya||
ko pana vādo pañcahi nīvaraṇehi|| ||

II.|| ||

12. Katamo pana bhante hetu katamo paccayo ñāṇāya dassanāya||
kathaɱ sahetu sapaccayo nānam dassanaɱ hotī ti|| ||

[page 128]

13. Idha rājakumāra bhikkhu satisambojjaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇamiɱ||
so satisambojjhaŋgam bhāvitena cittena yathābhūtaɱ jānāti passati||
ayam pi kho rājakumāra hetu ayam paccayo ñāṇāya dassanāya||
evam pi sahetu sappaccayo ñānaɱ dassanaɱ hoti|| ||

14—18. Puna ca paraɱ rājakumāra bhikkhu||
... pe ...|| ||

19. Upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ||
so upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāvitena cittena yathābhūtaɱ jānāti passati||
ayam pi kho rājakumāra hetu ayam paccayo ñānāya dassanāya||
evaɱ sahetu sappaccayo ñāṇam dassanaɱ hotī ti|| ||

20. Ko nāmāyam bhante dhammapariyāyo ti|| ||

Bojjhaŋgānāmete rājakumārāti|| ||

Taggha Bhagavā bojjhaŋgā taggha Sugata bojjhaŋgā|| ||

eka-m-ekena pi kho bhante bojjhaŋgena samannāgato yathābhūtam jāneyya passeyya||
ko pana vādo sattahi bojjhaŋgehi|| ||

Yo pi me bhante Gijjhakūṭam pabbatam ārohantassa kāyakilamatho cittakilamatho so pi me paṭipassaddho||
dhammo ca me abhisameto ti|| ||

Uddānam bhavati|| ||

Āhāra Pariyāy-Aggi||
Mettaɱ Saŋgāravena ca||
Abhayo pucchito pañhaɱ||
Gijjhakūṭamhi pabbate ti||
Bojjhaŋgasaɱyuttassa Bojjhaŋgasākaccaɱ chaṭṭham|| ||

Chapter VII. Ānāpāna Vaggo

57. Aṭṭhika

I. Mahapphala-Mahanisaɱsā

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Aṭṭhikasaññā bhikkhave bhāvitā bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

3. Katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave aṭṭhikasaññā katham bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu aṭṭhikasaññāsahagataɱ satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ ... pe ...aṭṭhikasaññāsahagatam upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

5. Evam bhavitā kho bhikkhave aṭṭhikasannā evam bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsāti|| ||

II. Aññāsativā

2. Aṭṭhikasaññāya bhikkhave bhāvitāya bahulīkatāya dvinnam phalānam aññataram phalam pāṭikaŋkhaɱ diṭṭheva dhamme aññā||
sati vā upādisese anāgāmitā|| ||

3. Katham bhāvitāya ca kho bhikkhave aṭṭhikasaññāya katham bahulīkatāya dvinnam phalānam aññataraɱ phalam pāṭikaŋkhaɱ diṭṭheva dhamme aññā||
sati vā upādisese anāgamitā|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu aṭṭhikasaññāsahagataɱ satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ... aṭṭhikasaññāsahagatam upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

5. Evam bhāvitāya kho bhikkhave aṭṭhikasaññāya evam bahulīkatāya dvinnam phalānam aññataram phalam pāṭikaŋkham diṭṭheva dhamme aññā||
sati vā upādisese anāgāmitā|| ||

[page 130]

III. Mahato Attha

2. Aṭṭhikasaññā bhikkhave bhāvitā bahulīkatā mahato atthāya saɱvattati|| ||

3. Katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave aṭṭhikasaññā katham bahulīkatā mahato atthāya saɱvattati|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu aṭṭhikasaññāsahagatam satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ... aṭṭhikasaññāsahagatam upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggaparināmiɱ|| ||

5. Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave aṭṭhikasaññā evam bahulīkatā mahato atthāya saɱvattatī ti|| ||

IV. Mahato Yogakkhema

2. Aṭṭhikasannā bhikkhave bhāvitā bahulīkatā mahato yogakkhemāya saɱvattati|| ||

3. Katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave aṭṭhikasaññā katham bahulīkatā mahato yogakkhemāya saɱvattati|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu aṭṭhikasaññāsahagataɱ satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ... aṭṭhikasaññāsahagatam upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmim|| ||

5. Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave aṭṭhikasaññā evam bahulīkatā mahato yogakkhemāya saɱvattatī ti|| ||

V. Mahato Saɱvega

2. Aṭṭhikasaññā bhikkhave bhāvitā bahulīkatā mahato saɱvegāya saɱvattati|| ||

3. Katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave aṭṭhikasaññā katham bahulīkatā mahato saɱvegāya saɱvattati|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu aṭṭhikasaññāsahagataɱ satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ... aṭṭhikasaññāsahagatam upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

5. Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave aṭṭhikasaññā evam bahulīkatā mahato saɱvegāya {saɱvattatī} ti|| ||

[page 131]

VI. Phāsuvihāra

2. Aṭṭhikasaññā bhikkhave bhāvitā bahulīkatā mahato phāsuvihārāya saɱvattati|| ||

3. Katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave aṭṭhikasaññā katham bahulīkatā mahato phāsuvihārāya saɱvattati|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu aṭṭhikasaññāsahagataɱ satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ... aṭṭhikasaññāsahagatam upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

5. Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave aṭṭhikasaññā evam bahulīkatā mahato phāsuvihārāya {saɱvattatī} ti|| ||

76. Nirodha

I. Mahapphalaɱ Mahānisaɱsa

2. Nirodhasaññā bhikkhave bhāvitā bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

3. Katham bhavitā ca bhikkhave nirodhasaññā-|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu nirodhasaññāsahagataɱ-|| ||

5. Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave°|| ||

II. Aññā Sativā

2. Nirodhasaññāya bhikkhave bhavitāya bahulīkatāya dvinnam phalānamo|| ||

3. Katham bhāvitāya bhikkhave nirodhasaññāya|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu nirodhasaññāsahagataɱ|| ||

5. Evam bhāvitāya kho bhikkhave° °anāgāmitāti|| ||

III. IV. V. VI.
Mahato Attha - Yogakkhama - Saɱvega - Phāsuviharā

2. Nirodhasaññā bhikkhave bhāvitā bahulīkatā mahato atthāya saɱvattati||
mahato yogakkhemāya saɱvattati||
mahato saɱvegāya saɱvattati||
mahato phāsuvihārāya saɱvattati|| ||

3. Katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave nirodhasaññākatham bahulīkatā mahato atthāya saɱvattati

[page 134]

mahato yogakkhemāya saɱvattati||
mahato saɱvegāya saɱvattati||
mahato phāsuvihārāya {saɱvattati}|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu nirodhasaññāsahagataɱ satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti ... pe ... nirodhasaññasahagatam upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggaparināmiɱ|| ||

Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave nirodhasaññā evam bahulīkatā mahato atthāya saɱvattati||
mahato yogakkhemāya saɱvattati||
mahato saɱvegāya saɱvattaṭi||
mahato phāsuviharāya saɱvattati|| ||

Tatr'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Asubha-Marana-Āhāre||
Paṭikkūla Anabhiratena||
Anicca Dukkha Anatta Pahānam||
Virāgaɱ Nirodhena te dasā ti|| ||

Bojjhaŋgasaɱyuttassa Nirodhavaggo aṭṭhamo|| ||

 

 

Chapter IX Gaŋgā Peyyālo (Viveka°)

77.
