Book III

Satipaṭṭhāna Saɱyutta

Chapter I. Ambapāli Vaggo

1. Ambapāli

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekam Samayam Bhagavā Vesāliyaɱ viharati Ambapālivane|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Bhikkhavoti|| ||

Bhadante ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

3. Ekāyano ayam bhikkhave maggo sattānaɱ visuddhiyā sokaparidevānaɱ samatikkamāya dukkhadomanassānaɱ atthagamāya ñāyassa adhigamāya nibbānassa sacchikiriyāya||
yad idaɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhānā||
Katame cattāro|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyanupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam|| ||

Vedanāsu vedānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno°|| ||

Citte cittānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno-|| ||

Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vinneyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

5. Ekāya no ayam bhikkhave maggo sattānaɱ visuddhiyā sokaparidevānaɱ samatikkamāya dukkhadomanassānam atthagamāya ñāyassa adhigamāya nibbānassa sacchikiriyāya||
yad idam cattāro satipaṭṭhānā ti|| ||

6. Idam avoca Bhagavā||
attamanā te bhikkhū Bhagavato bhāsitam abhinanduɱ|| ||

[page 142]

 

 

2. Sato

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Vesāliyaɱ viharati Ambapālivane|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi||
... pe ...||
3. Sato bhikkhave bhikkhu vihareyya sampajāno||
ayam vo amhākam anusāsanī|| ||

4. Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu sato hoti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Vedanāsu||
... pe ...||
Citte||
... pe ...||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sato hoti|| ||

5. Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu sampajāno hoti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu abhikkante paṭikkante sampajānakārī hoti ālokite vilokite sampajānakārī hoti||
sammiñjite pasārite sampajānakārī hoti||
saŋghāṭi patta-cīvara-dhāraṇe sampajānakārī hoti||
asite pīte khāyite sāyite sampajānakārī hoti||
uccārapassāvakamme sampajānakārī hoti||
gate ṭhite nisinne sutte jāgarite bhāsite tunhībhāve sampajānakārī hoti|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sampajāno hoti|| ||

6. Sato bhikkhave bhikkhu vihareyya sampajāno||
ayaɱ vo amhākam anusāsanī ti|| ||

 

 

3. Bhikkhu

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā ... pe ...eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Sādhu me bhante Bhagavā saŋkhittena dhammaɱ desetu||
yam aham Bhagavato dhammaɱ sutvā eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto vihareyyaɱ ti evam eva panidhekacce moghapurisā mañceva ajjhesanti dhamme ca bhāsite mam eva anubandhitabbam maññantī ti

[page 143]

Desetu me bhante Bhagavā saŋkhittena dhammaɱ desetu Sugato saŋkhittena dhammam||
appeva nāmāham Bhagavato bhāsitassa atthaɱ jāneyyam appeva nāmāham Bhagavato bhāsitassa dāyādo assan ti|| ||

Tasmātiha tvam bhikkhu ādim eva visodehi kusalesu dhammesu||
ko cādikusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ sīlam ca suvisuddhaɱ diṭṭhi ca ujukā||
yato kho te bhikkhu sīlañ ca suvisuddham bhavissati diṭṭhi ca ujukā||
tato tvam bhikkhu sīlam nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya cattāro satipaṭṭhāne tividhena bhāveyyāsi||
kātame cattāro|| ||

5. Idha tvam bhikkhu ajjhattaɱ vā kāye kāyānupassī viharāhi||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
bahiddhā vā kāye kāyānupassī viharāhi||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||
ajjhattabahiddhā vā kāye kāyānupassī viharāhi||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjadomanassaɱ|| ||

Ajjhattaɱ vā vedanāsu||
bahiddhāvā vedanāsu||
ajjhattabahiddhā vā vedanāsu vedanānupassī viharāhi||
... pe ...||
Ajjhattaɱ citte||
bahiddhā citte||
ajjhattabahiddhā citte cittānupassī viharāhi||
... pe ...||
Ajjhattaɱ vā dhammesu||
bahiddhā vā dhammesu||
ajjhattabahiddhā vā dhammesu dhammānupassī viharāhi||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjādomanassaɱ|| ||

5. Yato kho tvam bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya ime cattāro satipaṭṭhāne evaɱ tividhena bhāvessasi||
tato tuyham bhikkhu yā ratti vā divaso vā āgamissati vuddhi yeva pāṭikaŋkhā kusalesu dhammesu no parihānīti|| ||

6. Atha kho so bhikkhu Bhagavato bhāsitam abhinanditvā anumoditvā uṭṭhāyasanā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaɱ katvā pakkāmi

[page 144]

7. Atha kho so bhikkhu eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto na cirasseva yassatthāya kulaputtā sammad eva agārasmā anagāriyam pabbajanti tad anuttaram brahmacariyapariyosānam diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sachikatvā upasampajja vihāsi|| ||

Khīṇā jāti vusitam brahmacariyaɱ kataɱ karaṇīyam nāparam itthattāyāti abhiññāsi|| ||

8. Aññataro ca pana so bhikkhu arahatam ahosīti|| ||

 

 

4. Sallam

1. Evam me sutam Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Kosalesu viharati Sālāyam brāhmaṇagāme|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi||
... pe ...||
etad avoca|| ||

3. Ye te bhikkhave bhikkhū navā acirapabbajitā adhunāgatā imaɱ dhammavinayaɱ||
te ve bhikkhave bhikkhū catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvanāya samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhāpetabbā||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

4. Etha tumhe āvuso kāye kāyānupassino viharatha||
ātāpino sampajānā ekodibhūtā vippasannacittā samāhitā ekaggacittā kāyassa yathābhūtaɱ ñāṇāya|| ||

Vedanāsu vedanānupassino viharatha||
ātāpino sampajānā ekodibhūtā vippasannacittā samāhitā ekaggacittā vedanānaɱ yathābhutaɱ ñāṇāya|| ||

Citte cittānupassino viharatha||
ātāpino sampajānā ekodibhūtā vippassannacittā samāhitā ekaggacittā cittassa yathābhūtaɱ ñāṇāya|| ||

Dammesu dhammānupassino viharatha||
ātāpino sampajānā ekodibhūtā vippasannacittā samāhitā ekaggacittā dhammānaɱ yathābhutaɱ ñāṇāya|| ||

[page 145]

5. Ye pi te bhikkhave bhikkhū sekhā appattamānasā anuttaraɱ yogakkhemam patthayamānā viharanti||
te pi kāye kāyānupassino viharanti||
ātāpino sampajānā ekodibhūtā vippasannacittā samāhitā ekaggacittā kāyassa pariññāya|| ||

Vedanāsu vedanānupassino viharanti... pe ...||
vedanānam pariññāya|| ||

Citte cittānupassino viharanti||
... pe ...||
cittassa pariññāya|| ||

Dhammesu dhammānupassino viharanti ātāpino sampajānā ekodibhūtā vippasannacittā samāhitā ekaggacittā dhammānaɱ pariññāya|| ||

6. Ye pi te bhikkhave bhikkhū arahanto khīṇāsavā vusitavanto katakaraṇīyā ohitabhārā anuppattasadatthā parikkhīṇabhavasaŋyojanā sammadaññā vimuttā||
te pi kāye kāyanupassino viharanti||
ātāpino sampajānā ekodibhūtā vippasannacittā samāhitā ekaggacittā kāyena visaɱyuttā|| ||

Vedanāsu vedanānupassino viharanti||
... pe ...||
vedanāhi visaɱyuttā|| ||

Citte ... pe ...||
cittena visaɱyuttā|| ||

Dhammesu dhammānupassino viharanti||
ātāpino sampajānā ekodibhūtā vippasannacittā samāhitā ekaggacittā dhammehi visaɱyuttā|| ||

7. Ye pi te bhikkhave bhikkhū navā acirapabbajitā adhunāgatā imaɱ dhammavinayaɱ||
te ve bhikkhave bhikkhū imesaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvanāya samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhāpetabbā ti|| ||

 

 

5. Kusalarāsi

1—2. Sāvatthi||
Tatra kho Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

3. Akusalarāsī ti bhikkhave vadamāno pañcanīvaraṇe sammāvadamāno vadeyya||
kevalo hāyam bhikkhave akusalarāsi yad idam pañcanīvaraṇā|| ||

Katame pañca?|| ||

[page 146]

4. Kāmacchandanīvaraṇaɱ||
byāpādanīvaraṇaɱ||
thīnamiddhanīvaraṇam||
uddhaccakukkuccanīvaraṇaɱ||
vicikicchānīvaraṇaɱ|| ||

Akusalarāsīti bhikkhave vadamāno ime pañca nīvaraṇe sammāvadamāno vadeyya||
kevalo hāyam bhikkhave akusalarāsi yad idam pañcanīvaraṇā|| ||

5. Kusalarāsī ti bhikkhave vadamāno cattāro satipaṭṭhāne sammāvadamāno vadeyya||
kevalo hāyam bhikkhave kusalarāsi yad idam cattāro satipaṭṭhānā||
katame cattaro|| ||

6. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Vedanāsu|| ||

Citte|| ||

Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Kusalarāsī ti bhikkhave vadamāno ime cattāro satipaṭṭhāne sammāvadamāno vadeyya||
kevalo hāyam bhikkhave kusalarāsi yad idam cattāro satipaṭṭhānā ti|| ||

 

 

6. Sakuṇagghi

3. Bhūtapubbam bhikkhave sakuṇagghi lāpam sakuṇam sahasā ajjhapattā aggahesi|| ||

4. Atha kho bhikkhave lāpo sakuṇo sakuṇagghiyā hariyamāno evam paridevasi||
Mayam evamha alakkhikā mayam appapuññā ye mayam agocare carimha paravisaye||
sacejja mayaɱ gocare careyyāma sake pettike visaye||
na myāyam sakuṇagghi alambhavissa yad idaɱ yuddhāyā ti|| ||

Ko pana te lāpa gocaro sako pettiko visayo ti|| ||

Yad idam naŋgalakaṭṭhakaraṇam leḍḍuṭṭhānanti|| ||

[page 147]

5. Atha kho bhikkhave sakuṇagghi sake bale apatthaddhā sake bale asaɱvadamānā lāpam sakuṇaɱ pamuñci|| ||

Gaccha kho tvaɱ lāpa tatra pi me gantvā na mokkhasī ti|| ||

6. Atha kho bhikkhave lāpo sakuṇo naŋgalakaṭṭhakaraṇam leḍḍuṭṭhānaɱ gantvā mahantaɱ leḍḍum abhirūhitvā sakuṇagghim vadamāno aṭṭhāsi|| ||

Ehi kho dāni me sakuṇagghi||
Ehi kho dāni me sakuṇagghī ti|| ||

7. Atha kho bhikkhave sakunagghi sake bale apatthaddhā sake bale asaɱvadamānā ubho pakkhe sannāyha lāpaɱ sakuṇaɱ sahasā ajjhapattā|| ||

Yadā kho bhikkhave aññāsi lāpo sakuṇo Bahuɱ āgatā kho myāyam sakunagghīti||
atha tasseva leḍḍussa antaram paccupādi|| ||

Atha kho bhikkhave sakuṇagghi tattheva uram paccatālesi|| ||

8. Evaɱ hi tam bhikkhave hoti yo agocare carati paravisaye|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave mā agocare carittha paravisaye||
agocare bhikkhave caratam paravisaye lacchati Māro otāraɱ lacchati Māro ārammaṇaɱ|| ||

9. Ko ca bhikkhave bhikkhuno agocaro paravisayo||
yad idam pañca kāmaguṇā||
katame pañca|| ||

10. Cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmupasaɱhitā rajanīyā||
Sotaviññeyyā saddā||
... pe ...||
Ghānaviññeyyā gandhā||
Jivhāviññeyyā rasā||
Kāyaviññeyyā poṭṭhabbā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaɱhitā rajanīyā|| ||

Ayaɱ bhikkhave bhikkhuno agocaro paravisayo|| ||

11. Gocare bhikkhave caratha sake pettike visaye||
Gocare bhikkhave carataɱ sake pettike visaye na lacchati Māro otāram na lacchati Māro ārammanaɱ|| ||

[page 148]

12. Ko ca bhikkhave bhikkhuno gocaro sako pettiko visayo||
yad idaɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhānā|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

13. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyanupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Ayam bhikkhave bhikkhuno gocaro sako pettiko visayo ti|| ||

 

 

7. Makkaṭo

3. Atthi bhikkhave Himavato pabbatarājassa duggā visamā desā||
yattha neva makkaṭānaɱ cāri na manussānaɱ|| ||

4. Atthi bhikkhave Himavato pabbatarājassa duggā visamā desā||
yattha makkaṭānaɱ hi kho cāri na manussānaɱ|| ||

5. Atthi Himavato pabbatarājassa samā bhūmibhāgā ramanīyā||
yattha makkaṭānañceva cāri manussānañ ca|| ||

Tatra bhikkhave luddā makkaṭavīthīsu lepam oḍḍenti makkaṭānam bādhanāya|| ||

Tatra bhikkhave ye te makkaṭā abālajātikā alolajātikā te taɱ lepaɱ disvā ārakā parivajjanti|| ||

Yo pana so hoti makkaṭo bālajātiko lolajātiko||
so tam lepam upasaŋkamitvā hatthena gaṇhāti||
so tattha bajjhati|| ||

Hattham mocessāmīti dutiyena hatthena gaṇhāti||
so tattha bajjhati|| ||

Ubho hatthe mocessāmīti pādena gaṇhāti so tattha bajjhati|| ||

Ubho hatthe mocessāmīti pādam cā ti dutiyena pādena gaṇhāti so tattha bajjhati|| ||

Ubho hatthe mocessāmi pāde cā ti tuṇḍena gaṇhāti so tattha bajjhati|| ||

6. Evaɱ hi so bhikkhave makkaṭo pañcoḍḍito thunam seti anayam āpanno byasanam āpanno yathākāmakaraṇīyo luddassa

[page 149]

Tam enam bhikkhave luddo vijjhitvā tasmiɱ yeva kaṭṭhakataŋgāre avasajjetvā yena kāmam pakkamati|| ||

7. Evaɱ hi tam bhikkhave hoti yo agocare carati paravisaye||
tasmā ti ha bhikkhave mā agocare carittha paravisaye||
agocare bhikkhave caratam paravisaye lacchati Māro otāraɱ lacchati Māro ārammanaɱ|| ||

8. Ko ca bhikkhave bhikkhuno agocaro paravisayo|| ||

Yad idam pañcakāmaguṇā||
katame pañca|| ||

9. Cakkhu viññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā||
... pe ...||
Kāyaviññeyyā poṭṭhabbā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā||
kāmūpasaɱhitā rajanīyā|| ||

Ayam bhikkhave bhikkhuno agocaro paravisayo|| ||

10. Gocare bhikkhave caratha sake pettike visaye||
Gocare bhikkhave carataɱ sake pettike visaye na lacchati Māro otāram na lacchati Māro ārammaṇaɱ|| ||

11. Ko ca bhikkhave bhikkhuno gocaro sako pettiko visayo|| ||

Yad idaɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhānā||
katame cattāro|| ||

12. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Ayam bhikkhave bhikkhuno gocaro sako pettiko visayo ti|| ||

 

 

8. Sūdo

I.

Seyyathā pi bhikkhave bālo avyatto akusalo sūdo rājānam vā rājamahāmattānaɱ vā nānāccayehi sūpehi paccupaṭṭhito assa||
ambilaggehi pi tittakaggehi pi kaṭukaggehi pi madhuraggehi pi khārikehi pi akhārikehi pi loṇikehi pi aloṇikehi pi|| ||

[page 150]

4. Sa kho so bhikkhave bālo avyatto akusalo sūdo sakassa bhattassa nimittaɱ na uggaṇhati||
Idam vā me ajja bhattasūpeyyaɱ ruccati||
imassa vā abhiharati||
imassa vā bahuɱ gaṇhāti||
imassa vā vaṇṇam bhāsati|| ||

Ambilaggaɱ vā me ajja bhattasūpeyyaɱ ruccati||
ambilaggassa vā abhiharati||
ambilaggassa vā bahuɱ gaṇhāti||
ambilaggassa vā vaṇṇam bhāsati|| ||

Tittakaggaɱ vā me ajja Kaṭukaggaɱ vā me ajja||
Madhuraggaɱ vā me ajja||
Khārikaɱ vā me ajja||
Akhārikaɱ vā me ajja||
Loṇikaɱ vā me ajja||
Aloṇikaɱ vā me ajja bhattasūpeyyaɱ ruccati||
aloṇikassa vā abhiharati||
aloṇikassa vā bahuɱ gaṇhāti aloṇikassa vā vaṇṇam bhāsatī ti|| ||

5. Sa kho so bhikkhave bālo avyatto akusalo sūdo na ceva lābhī hoti acchādanassa||
na lābhī vetanassa na lābhī abhihārānaɱ|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

Tathā hi so bhikkhave bālo avyatto akusalo sūdo sakassa bhattassa nimittaɱ na ugganhāti|| ||

6. Evam eva kho bhikkhave idhekacco bālo avyatto akusalo bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
tassa kāye kāyānupassino viharato cittaɱ na samādhiyati upakkilesā na pahiyyanti||
so taɱ nimittam na uggaṇhāti||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassi viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
tassa dhammesu dhammānupassino viharato cittaɱ na samādhiyati upakkilesā na pahiyyanti||
so tam nimittaɱ na uggaṇhāti|| ||

7. Sa kho so bhikkhave bālo avyatto akusalo bhikkhu na ceva lābhī diṭṭheva dhamme sukhavihārānaɱ||
na lābhī satisampajaññassa

[page 151]

Tam kissa hetu?|| ||

Tathā hi so bhikkhave bālo avyatto akusalo bhikkhu sakassa cittassa nimittaɱ na uggaṇhāti|| ||

II.

8. Seyyathā pi pi bhikkhave paṇḍito vyatto kusalo sūdo rājānaɱ vā rājamahāmattānaɱ vā nānāccayehi sūpehi paccupaṭṭhito assa||
ambilaggehi pi tittakaggehi pi kaṭukaggehi pi madhuraggehi pi khārikehi pi akhārikehi pi loṇikehi pi aloṇikehi pi|| ||

Sa kho so bhikkhave paṇḍito vyatto kusalo sūdo sakassa bhattassa nimittam uggaṇhāti||
Idam vā me ajja bhattasupeyyaɱ ruccati||
imassa vā abhiharati||
imassa vā bahuɱ gaṇhāti||
imassa vā vaṇṇaɱ bhāsati|| ||

Ambilaggaɱ vā me ajja bhattasūpeyyaɱ ruccati ambilaggassa vā abhiharati||
ambilaggassa vā bahum gaṇhāti||
ambilaggassa vā vaṇṇam bhasati||
Tittakaggaɱ vā ma ajja||
Kaṭukaggaɱ vā me ajja||
Madhuraggaɱ vā me ajja||
Khārikaɱ vā me ajja||
Akhārikaɱ vā me ajja||
Loṇikaɱ vā me ajja||
Aloṇikaɱ vā me ajja bhattasūpeyyaɱ ruccati||
aloṇikassa vā abhiharati||
aloṇikassa vā bahuɱ gaṇhāti||
aloṇikassa vā vaṇṇam bhāsatī ti|| ||

9. Sa kho bhikkhave paṇḍito vyatto kusalo sūdo lābhī ceva hoti acchādanassa lābhī vetanassa lābhi abhihārānaɱ||
taɱ kissa hetu|| ||

Tathā hi so bhikkhave paṇḍito vyatto kusalo sūdo sakassa bhattassa nimittam uggaṇhāti|| ||

10. Evam eva kho bhikkhave idhekacco paṇḍito vyatto kusalo bhikkhu kāye kāyanupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
tassa kāye kāyānupassino viharato cittaɱ samādhiyati upakkilesā pahīyanti

[page 152]

so taɱ nimittam uggaṇhāti||
Vedanāsu||
... pe ...||
Citte||
... pe ...||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
tassa dhammesu dhammānupassino viharato cittaɱ samādhiyati upakkilesā pahīyanti||
so taɱ nimittam uggaṇhāti|| ||

11. Sa kho so bhikkhave paṇḍito vyatto kusalo bhikkhu lābhī ceva hoti diṭṭheva dhamme sukhavihārānaɱ lābhī hoti satisampajaññassa||
taɱ kissa hetu|| ||

Tathā hi so bhikkhave paṇḍito vyatto kusalo bhikkhu sakassa cittassa nimittam uggaṇhātī ti|| ||

 

 

9. Gilāno

1. Ekam me sutaɱ Ekam samayam Bhagavā Vesāliyaɱ viharati Beluvagāmake|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Etha tumhe bhikkhave samantā Vesāliyā yathā mittaɱ yathā sandiṭṭhaɱ yathā sambhattaɱ vassam upetha gacchatha idhevāham Beluvagāmake vassam upagacchamīti|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho te bhikkhū Bhagavato paṭissutvā samantā Vesāliyā yathā mittam yathā sandiṭṭham yathā sambhattaɱ vassam upagañchuɱ||
Bhagavā pana tattheva Beluvagāmake vassam upagañchi|| ||

3. Atha kho Bhagavato vassupagatassa kharo ābādho uppajji||
bāḷhā vedanā vattanti māraṇantikā||
tatra sudam Bhagavā sato sampajāno adhivāsesi avihaññamāno|| ||

4. Atha kho Bhagavato etad ahosi||
Na kho pana me tam paṭirūpaɱ yo ham anāmantetvā upaṭṭhāke anapaloketvā bhikkhusaŋgham parinibbāyeyyaɱ||
yan nūnāham imam ābādham viriyena patipaṇāmetvā jīvitasaŋkhāram adhiṭṭhāya vihareyyanti

[page 153]

Atha kho Bhagavā tam ābādhaɱ viriyena patipaṇāmetvā jīvitasaŋkhāram adhiṭṭhāya vihāsi|| ||

5. Atha kho Bhagavā gilānā vuṭṭhito aciravuṭṭhito gelaññā vihārā nikkhāmitvā vihārapacchā chāyāyam paññatte āsane nisīdi|| ||

6. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nīsīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Diṭṭhā bhante khamanīyam diṭṭhā bhante Bhagavato yāpanīyaɱ||
api me bhante madhurakajāto viya kāyo||
disā pi me na pakkhāyanti||
dhammā pi maɱ na paṭibbanti Bhagavato gelāññena|| ||

Api ca me bhante ahosi kācid eva assāsamattā||
na tāva Bhagavā parinibbāyissati||
na tāva Bhagavā bhikkhusaŋgham ārabbha kiñcid eva udāharatī ti|| ||

7. Kim pana dāni Ānanda bhikkhusaŋgho mayi paccāsiɱsati||
desito Ānanda mayā dhammo anantaram abāhiraɱ katvā|| ||

Natthānanda Tathāgatassa dhammesu ācariyamuṭṭhi||
yassa nūnānanda evam assa Aham bhikkhusaŋgham pariharissāmīti vā Mamuddesiko bhikkhusaŋgho ti vā so nūnānanda bhikkhusaŋgham ārabbha kiñcid eva udāhareyya|| ||

Tathāgatassa kho Ānanda na evam hoti||
Aham bhikkhusaŋgham pariharissamī ti vā Mamuddesiko bhikkhusaŋgho ti vā sakim Ānanda Tathāgato bhikkhusaŋgham ārabbha kiñcid eva udāharissati|| ||

8. Etarahi kho panāham Ānanda jiṇṇo vuddho mahallako addhagato vayo anuppatto asītiko me vasso vattati|| ||

Seyyathā pi Ānanda jarasakaṭam vedhamissakena yāpeti||
evam eva kho Ānanda vedhamissakena maññe Tathāgatassa kāyo yāpeti|| ||

[page 154]

9. Yasmiɱ Ānanda samaye Tathāgato sabbanimittānam amanasikārā ekaccānam vedanānaɱ nirodhā animittam cetosamādhim upasampajja viharati||
phāsutaram Ānanda tasmiɱ samaye Tathāgatassa kāyo hoti|| ||

Tasmā ti hānanda attadīpā viharatha attasaraṇā anaññasaraṇā dhammadīpā dhammasaraṇā anaññasaraṇā|| ||

Kathañcānanda bhikkhu attadīpo viharati attasaraṇo anaññasaraṇo dhammadīpo dhammasaraṇo anaññasaraṇo|| ||

10. Idhānanda bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam|| ||

Evaɱ kho Ānanda bhikkhu attadīpo viharati attasaraṇo anaññāsaraṇo dhammadīpo dhammasaraṇo anaññasaraṇo|| ||

11. Ye hi keci Ānanda etarahi vā mamaccaye vā attadīpā viharissanti attasaraṇā anaññasaraṇā dhammadīpā dhammasaraṇā anaññasaraṇā||
tamatagge me te Ānanda bhikkhū bhavissanti ye keci sikkhākāmā ti|| ||

 

 

10. Bhikkhunivāsako

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya yena aññataro bhikkhunupassayo tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi|| ||

2. Atha kho sambahulā bhikkhuniyo yenāyasmā Ānando tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantam Ānandam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnā kho tā bhikkhuniyo āyasmantam Ānandam etad avocuɱ|| ||

3. Idha bhante Ānanda sambahulā bhikkhuniyo catūsu satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacittā viharantiyo uḷāram pubbenāparam visesaɱ sampajānantī ti|| ||

[page 155]

Evam etam bhaginiyo evam etam bhaginiyo||
yo hi koci bhaginiyo bhikkhu vā bhikkhunī vā catūsu satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacitto viharati||
tassetam pāṭikaŋkham uḷāram pubbenāparaɱ visesaɱ sampajānissatī ti|| ||

4. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando tā bhikkhuniyo dhammiyā kathāya sandassetvā samādapetvā samuttejetvā sampahaɱsetvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkāmi|| ||

5. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando Sāvatthiyam piṇḍāya caritvā pacchābhattam piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Idhāham bhante pubbaṇhasamayam nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya yena aññataro bhikkhunupassayo tenupasaŋkamiɱ||
upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdiɱ|| ||

Atha kho bhante sambahulā bhikkhuniyo yenāhaɱ tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā mam abhivādetvā ekam antam nisīdiɱsu||
eka-m-antaɱ nisinnā kho bhante tā bhikkhuniyo mam etad avocuɱ|| ||

Idha bhante Ānanda sambahulā bhikkhuniyo catusu satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacittā viharantiyo uḷaram pubbenāparam visesaɱ sampajānantī ti|| ||

Evam vuttāham bhante tā bhikkhuniyo etad avocuɱ||
Evam etam bhaginiyo evam etam bhaginiyo yo hi koci bhaginiyo bhikkhu va bhikkhunī vā catusu satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacitto viharati||
tassetam pāṭikaŋkham uḷāram pubbenāparaɱ visesaɱ saɱjānissatī ti|| ||

6. Evam etam Ānanda evam etaɱ||
yo hi koci Ānanda bhikkhu vā bhikkhunī vā catusu satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacitto viharati||
tassetam pāṭikaŋkham uḷāram pubbenāparam visesaɱ sañjānissatī ti|| ||

Katamesu catusu?|| ||

7. Idhānanda bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam|| ||

[page 156]

Tassa kāye kāyanupassino viharato kāyārammano vā uppajjati kāyasmim pariḷāho cetaso vā līnattam bahiddhā vā cittaɱ vikkhipati|| ||

Tenānanda bhikkhunā kismiñcid eva pasādaniye nimitta cittam paṇidahitabbam||
tassa kismiñcid eva pasādaniye nimitte cittam paṇidahato pāmujjaɱ jāyati||
pamuditassa pīti jāyati||
pītimanassa kāyo passambhati||
passaddhakāyo sukhaɱ vedayati||
sukhino cittaɱ samādhiyati|| ||

So iti paṭisañcikkhati||
Yassa khvāhaɱ atthāya cittam paṇidahiɱ so me attho abhinipphanno handa dāni paṭisaɱharāmī ti||
So paṭisaɱharati ceva na ca vitakketi na ca vicāreti||
Avitakkomhi avicāro ajjhattaɱ satimā sukhamasmī ti pajānāti|| ||

8—9. Puna ca param Ānanda vedanāsu||
citte|| ||

10. Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
tassa dhammesu dhammānupassino viharato dhammārammaṇo vā uppajjati kāyasmiɱ pariḷāho cetaso vā līnattam bahiddhā vā cittaɱ vikkhipati|| ||

Tenānanda bhikkhunā kismiñcid eva pasādaniye nimitte cittam paṇidahitabbaɱ||
tassa kimiñcid eva pasādaniye nimitte cittam paṇidahato pāmujjaɱ jāyati||
pamūditassa pīti jāyati||
pītimanassa kāyo passambhati||
passaddhakāyo sukhaɱ vedayati||
sukhino cittaɱ samādhiyati||
so iti paṭisañcikkhati||
Yassa khvāham atthāya cittam paṇidahiɱ||
so me attho abhinipphanno||
handa dāni paṭisaɱharāmīti|| ||

So paṭisaɱharati ceva na ca vitakketi na ca vicāreti||
Avitakkomhi avicāro ajjhattaɱ satimā sukhamasmī ti pajānāti|| ||

11. Evaɱ kho Ānanda paṇidhāya bhāvanā hoti|| ||

12. Kathañcānanda apaṇidhāya bhāvanā hoti|| ||

[page 157]

13. Bahiddhā Ānanda bhikkhu cittam apaṇidhāya Apaṇihitam me bahiddhā cittan ti pajānāti|| ||

Atha pacchāpure asaɱkhittaɱ vimuttam Apaṇihitan ti pajānāti|| ||

Atha ca pana kāye kāyānupassī viharāmi ātāpī sampajāno satimā sukhamasmī ti pajānāti|| ||

14. Bahiddhā Ānanda bhikkhu cittam apanidhāya Apaṇihitam me bahiddhā cittan ti pajānāti|| ||

Atha pacchāpure asaɱkhittam vimuttam Apaṇihitanti pajānāti|| ||

Atha ca pana vedanāsu vedanānupassī viharāmi ātāpī sampajāno satimā Sukham asmī ti pajānāti|| ||

15. Bahiddhā Ānanda bhikkhu cittam apaṇidhāya Apaṇihitam me bahiddhā cittan ti pajānati|| ||

Atha pacchāpure asaɱkhittam vimuttam Apaṇihitanti pajānāti|| ||

Atha pana citte cittānupassī viharāmi ātāpī sampajāno satimā sukhamasmīti pajānāti|| ||

16. Bahiddhā Ānanda bhikkhu cittam apanidhāya apaṇihitam me bahiddhā cittanti pajānāti|| ||

Atha pacchāpure asaɱkhittaɱ vimuttam Apaṇihitanti pajānāti|| ||

Atha ca pana dhammesu dhammānupassī viharāmi||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā sukhamasmīti pajānāti|| ||

17. Evaɱ kho Ānanda apaṇidhāya bhāvanā hoti|| ||

18. Iti kho Ānanda desitā mayā paṇidhāya bhāvanā desitā apaṇidhāya bhāvanā|| ||

Yam Ānanda satthārā karaṇīyam sāvakānaɱ hitesinā anukampakena anukampam upādāya||
kataɱ vo tam mayā|| ||

Etāni Ānanda rukkhamūlāni etāni suññāgārāni nijjhāyathānanda mā pamādattha ma pacchāvippatisārino ahuvattha||
ayaɱ vo amhākam anusāsanī ti|| ||

19. Idam avoca Bhagavā||
attamano āyasmā Ānando Bhagavato bhāsitam abhinandī ti|| ||

[page 158]

Tatr'uddānam:|| ||

Ambapālivaggo pathamo|| ||

Ambapāli Sato Bhikkhu||
Sāllam Kusalarāsi ca||
Sakunagghi Makkaṭo Sūdo||
Gilāno Bhikkhuni-vāsakoti|| ||

 

 

Chapter II. Nālanda Vaggo

11. Mahāpuriso

1. Sāvatthi-nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Sāriputto yena Bhagavā tenupa saŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā ... pe ...Ekam antam nisinno kho āyasmā Sāriputto Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Mahāpuriso mahāpuriso ti bhante vuccati||
Kittāvatā nu kho bhante mahāpuriso hotī ti|| ||

Vimuttacittattā kho haɱ Sāriputta Mahāpuriso ti vadāmi||
avimuttacittattā No mahāpuriso ti vadāmi|| ||

Kathañ ca Sāriputta vimuttacitto hoti|| ||

4. Idha Sāriputta bhikkhu kāye kāyanupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam||
tassa kāye kāyānupassino viharato cittaɱ virajjati vimuccati anupādāya āsavehi|| ||

Vedanāsu|| ||

Citte|| ||

Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
tassa dhammesu dhammānupassino viharato cittaɱ virajjati vimuccati anupādāya āsavehi|| ||

5. Evaɱ kho Sāriputta vimuttacitto hoti|| ||

Vimuttacittattā kho haɱ Sāriputta Mahāpuriso ti vadāmi||
avimuttacittattā No mahāpuriso ti vadāmī ti|| ||

[page 159]

 

 

12. Nālandam

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Nālandāyaɱ viharati Pāvārikambavane|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Sāriputto yena Bhagavā tenupasarikami||
upasaŋkamitvā||
... pe ...||
Ekam antam nisinno kho āyasmā Sāriputto Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Evam pasanno ham bhante Bhagavati||
Na cāhu na ca bhavissati na cetarahi vijjati añño samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā Bhagavatā bhiyyo bhiññataro yad idaɱ sambodhiyan ti|| ||

Uḷārā kho tyāyaɱ Sāriputta āsabhi vācā bhāsitā ekaɱso gahito sīhanādo nadito|| ||

Evam pasanno ham bhante Bhagavati na cāhu na ca bhavissati na cetarahi vijjati añño samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā Bhagavatā bhiyyo bhiññataro yad idaɱ sambodhiyan ti|| ||

4. Kinnu te Sāriputta ye te ahesum atītam addhānam arahanto sammāsambuddhā||
sabbe te bhagavanto cetasā cetopariccaviditā||
Evaɱsīlā te bhagavanto ahesuɱ iti vā||
Evaɱ dhammā te bhagavanto ahesuɱ iti vā||
Evam paññā te bhagavanto ahesum iti vā||
{Evaɱvihārino} te bhagavanto ahesuɱ iti vā Evaɱvimuttā te bhagavanto ahesum iti vā ti|| ||

No hetam bhante|| ||

5. Kim pana te Sāriputta ye te bhavissanti anāgatam addhānam arahanto sammāsambuddhā||
sabbe te bhagavanto cetasā cetopariccaviditā evaɱsilā te bhagavanto bhavissanti iti vā evaɱ dhammā te bhagavanto bhavissanti iti vā evampaññā te bhagavanto bhavissanti iti vā evaɱvihārino te bhagavanto bhavissanti iti vā||
evaɱvimuttā kho bhagavanto bhavissanti iti vā ti|| ||

[page 160]

No hetam bhante|| ||

6. Kim pana tyāhaɱ Sāriputta etarahi arahaɱ sammāsambuddho cetasā cetopariccavidīto||
evaɱsīlo bhagavā iti vā evaɱdhammo bhagavā iti vā evampañño bhagavā iti vā evaɱvihārī bhagavā iti vā evaɱvimutto bhagavā iti vā ti|| ||

No hetam bhante|| ||

7. Ettha ca te Sāriputta atītānāgatapaccuppannesu arahantesu sammāsambuddhesu cetopariyāyañāṇaɱ natthi||
atha kiɱcarahi tayā Sāriputta ulārā āsabhi vācā bhāsitā ekaɱso gahito sīhanādo nadito||
Evam pasannoham bhante Bhagavati na cāhu na ca bhavissati na cetarahi vijjati añño samaṇo va brāhmaṇo vā Bhagavato bhiyyo bhiññataro yadidaɱ sambodhiyan ti||
Na kho me tam bhante atītānāgatapaccuppannesu arahantesu sammāsambuddhesu cetopariyāyañāṇam atthi||
api ca dhammanvayo vidito|| ||

8. Seyyathā pi bhante rañño paccantimaɱ nagaram daḷhuddāpaɱ daḷhapākāratoraṇam ekadvāraɱ||
tatrassa dovāriko paṇḍito viyatto medhāvī aññātānaɱ nivāretvā ñātānam pavesetā|| ||

So tassa nagarassa samantā anupariyāya patham anukkamamāno na passeyya pākārasandhiɱ vā pākāravivaraɱ vā antamaso biḷāranissakkanamattam pi||
tassa evam assa||
Ye kho keci oḷarikā pāṇā imaɱ nagaram pavisanti vā nikkhamanti vā sabbe te iminā va dvārena pavisanti vā nikkhamanti vā ti|| ||

Evam eva kho me bhante dhammanvayo vidito|| ||

9. Ye pi te bhante ahesum atītam addhānaɱ arahanto sammāsambuddhā sabbe te bhagavanto pañcanīvaraṇe pahāya cetaso upakkilese paññāya dubbalīkaraṇe catusu satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacittā sattabojjhaŋge yathābhūtam bhāvetvā anuttaraɱ sammāsambodhim abhisambujjhiɱsu

[page 161]

Ye pi te bhante bhavissanti anāgatam addhānam arahanto sammāsambuddhā sabbe te bhagavanto pañcanīvaraṇe pahāya cetaso upakkilese paññāya dubbalīkaraṇe catusu satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacittā sattabojjhaŋge yathābhūtam bhāvetvā anuttaraɱ sammāsambodhim abhisambujjhissanti|| ||

Bhagavā pi bhante etarahi arahaɱ sammāsambuddho pañcanīvaraṇe pahāya cetaso uppakkilese paññāya dubbalīkaraṇe catusu satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacitto sattabojjhaŋge yathābhūtam bhāvetvā anuttaram sammāsambodhim abhisambuddhoti|| ||

10. Sādhu sādhu Sāriputta tasmā ti ha tvaɱ Sāriputta imam dhammapariyāyam abhikkhaṇam bhāseyyāsi bhikkhūnam bhikkhūnīnam upāsakānam upāsikānam||
yesam pi hi Sāriputta moghapurisānam bhavissati Tathāgate kaŋkhā vā vimati vā tesam pi mam dhammapariyāyam sutvā yā tesaɱ Tathāgate kaŋkhā vā vimati vā sā pahīyissatī ti|| ||

 

 

13. Cuṇḍo

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Sāriputto Magadhesu viharati Nālagāmake||
ābādhiko dukkhito bāḷhagilāno||
Cundo ca samaṇuddeso āyasmato Sāriputtassa upaṭṭhāko hoti|| ||

3. Atha āyasmā Sāriputto tena ābādhena parinibbāyi|| ||

4. Atha kho Cundo samaṇuddeso āyasmato Sāriputtassa pattacīvaram adāya yena Sāvatthi-Jetavanam Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāmo yenāyasmā Ānando tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantam Ānandam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Cundo samaṇuddeso āyasmantam Ānandam etad avoca

[page 162]

Āyasmā bhante Sāriputto parinibbuto idam assa pattacīvaranti|| ||

5. Atthi kho idam āvuso Cunda kathāpābhatam Bhagavantaɱ dassanāya||
āyāmāvuso Cunda yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkamissāma||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavato etam attham ārocessāmāti|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho Cundo samaṇuddeso āyasmato Ānandassa paccassosi|| ||

6. Atha kho āyasmā ca Ānando Cundo ca samaṇuddeso yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nīsīdiɱsu|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Ayam bhante Cundo samaṇuddeso evam āha||
Āyasmā bhante Sāriputto parinibbuto idam assa pattacīvaran ti|| ||

Api ca me bhante madhurakajāto viya kāyo||
disā pi me na pakkhāyanti dhammā pi me na paṭibhanti āyasmā Sāriputto parinibbuto ti sutvā ti|| ||

7. Kinnu te Ānanda Sāriputto sīlakkhandhaɱ vā ādāya parinibbuto||
samādhikkhandhaɱ vā ādāya parinibbuto||
paññakkhandhaɱ vā ādāya parinibbuto||
vimuttikkhandhaɱ vā ādāya parinibbuto||
vimuttiññanadassanakkhandhaɱ vā ādāya parinibbuto ti|| ||

Na ca kho me tam bhante āyasmā Sāriputto sīlakkhandhaɱ vā ādāya parinibbuto ... pe ...vimuttiññāṇadassanakkhandhaɱ vā ādāya parinibbuto||
Api ca me bhante āyasmā Sāriputto ovādako ahosi otiṇṇo viññāpako sandassako samādapako samuttejako sampahaɱsako akilāsu dhammadesanāya anuggāhako sabrahmacārīnaɱ tam mayam āyasmato Sāriputtassa dhammojaɱ dhammabhogaɱ dhammānuggaham anussarāmāti|| ||

8. Nanu tam Ānanda mayā paṭigacceva akkhātaɱ sabbehi piyehi manāpehi nānābhāvo vinābhāvo aññathābhāvo

[page 163]

tam kutettha Ānanda labbhā||
Yan taɱ jātam bhūtaɱ saŋkhatam palokadhammaɱ taɱ vata mā palujjīti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

9. Seyyathā pi Ānanda mahato rukkhassa tiṭṭhato sāravato yo mahantataro khandho so palujjeyya||
evam eva kho Ānanda mahato bhikkhusaŋghassa tiṭṭhato sāravato Sāriputto parinibbuto taɱ kutettha Ānanda labbhā yan taɱ jātam bhūtaɱ saŋkhataɱ palokadhammaɱ taɱ vata mā palujjīti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

10. Tasmā ti hānanda attadīpā viharatha attasaraṇā anaññasaraṇā dhammadīpā dhammasaraṇā anaññasaraṇā|| ||

Kathañcānanda bhikkhu attadīpo viharati attasaraṇo anaññasaraṇo dhammadīpo dhammasaraṇo anaññasaraṇo|| ||

11. Idhānanda bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Evaɱ kho Ānanda bhikkhu attadīpo viharati attasaraṇo anaññasaraṇo dhammadīpo dhammasaraṇo anaññasaraṇo|| ||

12. Ye hi keci Ānanda etarahi vā mamaccaye vā attadipā viharissanti attasaraṇā anaññasaraṇā dhammadīpā dhammasaraṇā anaññasaraṇā||
tamatagge pete Ānanda bhikkhū bhavissanti ye keci sikkhākāmā ti|| ||

 

 

14. Ceḷam

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Vajjīsu viharati Ukkacelāyaɱ Gaŋgāya nadiyā tīre mahatā bhikkhusaŋghena saddhim aciraparinibbutesu Sāriputta-Moggalānesu|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Bhagavā bhikkhu-saŋghaparivuto ajjhokāse nisinno hoti|| ||

Atha kho Bhagavā tunhībhūtam bhikkhusaŋgham anuviloketvā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

[page 164]

3. Api myāyam bhikkhave parisā suññā viya khāyati||
parinibbutesu Sāriputta-Moggalānesu suññā me bhikkhave parisā hoti||
anapekkhā tassam disāyam hoti yassaɱ dīsāyaɱ Sāriputta-Moggalānā viharanti|| ||

4. Ye hi te bhikkhave ahesum atītamadhānam arahanto sammāsambuddhā||
tesam pi bhagavantānam etaparamam yeva sāvakayugam ahosi||
seyyathāpi mayhaɱ SāriputtaMoggalānā|| ||

Ye pi te bhikkhave bhavissanti anāgatam addhānam arahanto sammāsambuddhā||
tesam pi bhagavantānam etaparamaɱ yeva sāvakayugam bhavissati||
seyyathāpi mayhaɱ Sāriputta-Moggalānā|| ||

5. Acchariyam bhikkhave sāvakānam abbhutam bhikkhave sāvakānam satthu ca nāma sāsanakarā bhavissanti ovādapatikarā||
catunnaɱ ca parisānam piyā bhavissanti manāpā garū ca bhāvaniyā ca|| ||

Acchariyam bhikkhave Tathāgatassa abbhutam bhikkhave Tathāgatassa||
evarūpe pi nāma sāvakayuge parinibbute natthi Tathāgatassa soko vā paridevo vā||
tam kutettha bhikkhave labbhā||
yantaɱ jātaɱ bhūtaɱ saŋkhataɱ palokadhammaɱ taɱ vata ma palujjīti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

6. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave mahato rukkhassa tiṭṭhato sāravato ye mahantatarā khandhā te palujjeyyuɱ||
Evam eva kho bhikkhave mahato bhikkhusaŋghassa tiṭṭhato sāravato Sāriputta-Moggalānā parinibbutā||
taɱ kutettha bhikkhave labbhā||
yan taɱ jātam bhūtam saŋkhatam palokadhammaɱ taɱ vata mā palujjīti||
netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

7. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave attadīpā viharathā- -anaññasaraṇā|| ||

8. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī- -anaññasaraṇo|| ||

[page 165]

9. Ye hi keci bhikkhave etarahi vā mamaccaye vā attadīpā viharissanti- -tamatagge bhikkhave bhikkhu bhavissanti ye keci sikkhākāmā ti|| ||

 

 

15. Bāhiyo (or Bāhiko)

1. Sāvatthi nidanaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Bāhiyo yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā||
... pe ...||
eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Bāhiyo Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Sādhu me bhante saŋkhittena dhammaɱ desetu||
yaɱ aham Bhagavato dhammaɱ sutvā eko vūpakaṭṭho apamatto ātāpī pahitatto vihareyyanti||
Tasmā ti ha tvam Bāhiya ādim eva visodhehi kusalesu dhammesu|| ||

Ko cādi kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ||
sīlañca suvisuddhaɱ diṭṭhi ca ujukā|| ||

3. Yato ca kho te Bāhiya sīlañca suvisuddham bhavissati diṭṭhi ca ujukā||
tato tvam Bāhiya sīlam nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya cattāro satipaṭṭhāne bhāveyyāsi||
katame cattāro|| ||

4. Idha tvam Bāhiya kāye kāyānupassī viharāhi||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharāhi||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Yato kho tvam Bāhiya sīlam nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya ime cattāro satipaṭṭhāne evam bhāvessasi||
tato {tuyham} Bāhiya yā ratti vā divaso vā āgamissasi||
vuddhi yeva paṭikaŋkhā kusalesu dhammesu no parihānī ti|| ||

[page 166]

5. Atha kho āyasmā Bāhiyo Bhagavato bhāsitam abhinanditvā anumoditvā uṭṭhāyāsanā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaɱ katvā pakkāmi|| ||

6. Atha kho āyasmā Bāhiyo eko vupakaṭṭho apamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto na cirasseva yassatthāya kulaputtā sammadeva agārasmā anagāriyam pabbajanti tad anuttaram brahmacariyapariyosānaɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi||
Khīnā jāti vusitam brahmacariyam kataɱ karaṇīyaɱ nāparam ittatthāyā ti abbhaññāsi|| ||

7. Aññataro ca panāyasmā Bāhiyo arahatam ahosī ti|| ||

 

 

16. Uttiyo

1. Sāvatthi nīdānam|| ||

2—4. Atha kho āyasmā Uttiyo yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
... pe ...||
tato tvam Uttiya gamissasi maccudheyyassa pāranti ... pe ...|| ||

5.6.7. Aññataro ca panāyasmā Uttiyo arahatam ahosī ti|| ||

 

 

17. Ariyo

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānā bhāvitā bahulīkatā ariyā niyyānikā niyyanti takkarassa sammādukkhākkhayāya||
katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhadomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

[page 167]

4. Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro satipaṭṭhānā bhāvitā bahulīkatā ariyā niyyānikā niyyanti takkarassa sammādukkhakkhayāyā ti|| ||

 

 

18. Brahmā

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Uruvelāyaɱ viharati najjā Nerañjarāya tīre Ajapālanigrodhe pathamābhisambuddho|| ||

2. Atha kho Bhagavato rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaɱ cetaso parivitakko udapādi|| ||

Ekāyano yam maggo sattānam visuddhiyā sokaparidevānam samatikkamāya dukkhadomanassānam atthagamāya ñāyassa adhigamāya nibbānassa sacchikiriyāya yad idaɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhānā||
katame cattāro|| ||

3. Kāye vā bhikkhu kāyānupassī vihareyya||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vinneyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu vā bhikkhu||
Citte vā bhikkhu|| ||

Dhammesu vā bhikkhu dhammānupassī vihareyya||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Ekāyano yam maggo sattānaɱ visuddhiyā sokaparidevānaɱ samatikkamāya dukkhadomanassānam atthagamāya ñāyassa adhigamāya nibbānassa sacchikiriyāya yadidaɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhānā ti|| ||

4. Atha kho Brahmā sahampati Bhagavato cetasā cetoparivitakkam aññāya seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaɱ vā bāham pasāreyya pasāritaɱ vā bāhaɱ sammiñjeyya||
evam eva kho Brahmaloke antarahito Bhagavato purato pāturahosi|| ||

Atha kho Brahmā sahampati ekaɱsam uttarāsaŋgaɱ karitvā yena Bhagavā tenañjalim paṇāmetvā Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

5. Evam etam Bhagavā evam etaɱ Sugata||
ekāyano yam bhante maggo sattānaɱ visuddhiyā sokaparidevānam samatikkamāya dukkhadomanassānam atthagamāya ñāyassa adhigamāya nibbānassa sacchikiriyāya yadidaɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhānā

[page 168]

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Kāye vā bhante bhikkhu kāyanupassī vihareyya||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā||
vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu vā bhante bhikkhu||
Citte vā bhante bhikkhu||
Dhammesu vā bhante dhammānupassī vihareyya||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Ekāyano yam bhante maggo sattānaɱ visuddhiyā sokaparidevānam samatikkamāya dukkhadomanassānam atthagamāya ñāyassa adhigamāya nibbānassa sacchikiriyāya yad idam cattāro satipaṭṭhānāti|| ||

6. Idam avoca Brahmā sahampati||
idaɱ vatvā Brahmā sahampati athāparam etad avoca|| ||

Ekāyanaɱ jātikhayantadassī||
Maggam pajānāti hitānukampi||
Etena maggena atariɱsu pubbe||
Tarissanti ye taranti ca oghan ti|| ||

 

 

19. Sedakam or Ekantaka(?)

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sumbhesu viharati Sedakaɱ nāma Sumbhānaɱ nigamo|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Bhūtapubbam bhikkhave caṇḍālavaɱsiko caṇḍālavaɱsam ussāpetvā Medakathālikam antevāsim āmantesi||
Ehi tvaɱ samma Medakathālike Caṇḍālavaɱsam abhirūhitvā mama uparikhandhe titthāhī ti||
Evam ācariyā ti kho bhikkhave Medakathālikā antevāsī Caṇḍālavaɱsikassa paṭissutvā Caṇḍālavaɱsam abhirūhitvā ācariyassa uparikhandhe aṭṭhāsi|| ||

3. Atha kho bhikkhave Caṇḍālavaɱsiko Medakathālikam antevāsim etad avoca||
Tvaɱ samma Medakathālike mamaɱ rakkha aham tvaɱ rakkhissāmi evaɱ mayam aññamaññaguttā aññamaññarakkhitā sippāni ceva dassessāma lābhañ ca lacchāma sotthinā ca caṇḍālavaɱsam orohissāmā ti

[page 169]

4. Evaɱ vutte bhikkhave Medakathālikā antevāsī Caṇḍālavaɱsikam etad avoca|| ||

Na kho panetam ācariya evam bhavissati||
tvam ācariya attānaɱ rakkha aham attanaɱ rakkhissāmi|| ||

Evam mayam attaguttā attarakkhitā sippāni ceva dassessāma lābhañca lacchāma sotthinā ca caṇḍalavaɱsā orohissāmā ti|| ||

So tattha ñāyo ti|| ||

5. Bhagavā avoca|| ||

Yathā Medakathālikā antevāsī ācariyam avoca||
Attānam bhikkhave rakkhissāmī ti satipaṭṭhānaɱ sevitabbaɱ||
Param rakkhissamā ti satipaṭṭhānaɱ sevitabbaɱ|| ||

Attānam bhikkhave rakkhanto paraɱ rakkhati||
paraɱ rakkhanto attānaɱ rakkhati|| ||

6. Kathañca bhikkhave attānam rakkhanto param rakkhati||
āsevanāya bhāvanāya bahulīkammena|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave attānaɱ rakkhanto paraɱ rakkhati|| ||

7. Kathañca bhikkhave paraɱ rakkhanto attānaɱ rakkhati||
khantiyā avihiɱsāya mettatāya anudayatāya|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave paraɱ rakkhanto attānaɱ rakkhati|| ||

8. Attānaɱ bhikkhave rakkhissāmī ti satipaṭṭhānaɱ sevitabbam||
Paraɱ rakkhissāmī ti satipaṭṭhānaɱ sevitabbaɱ||
attānam bhikkhave rakkhanto paraɱ rakkhati||
paraɱ rakkhanto attānaɱ rakkhatī ti|| ||

 

 

20. Janapada or Ekantaka(?)

1. Evam me sutam Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sumbhesu viharati Sedakam nāma Sumbhānaɱ nigamo|| ||

[page 170]

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi||
... pe ...||
3. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave Janapadakalyāṇī janapadakalyāṇī ti kho bhikkhave mahājanakāyo sannipateyya||
Sā kho panassa janapadakalyāṇī paramapāsāvinī nacce paramapāsāvinī gīte||
Janapadakalyāṇī naccati gāyatīti kho bhikkhave bhiyyosomattāya mahā janakāyo sannipateyya|| ||

Atha puriso āgaccheyya jīvitukāmo amaritukāmo sukhakāmo dukkhapaṭikūlo tam enaɱ evaɱ vadeyyum||
Ayan te ambho purisa samatittiko telapatto antarena ca mahāsamajjam antarena ca janapadakalyāṇiɱ parihātabbo||
puriso ca te ukkhitāsiko piṭṭhito piṭṭhito anubandhissati yattheva naɱ thokam pi chaddessati tattheva te siro pātessatī ti|| ||

Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
api nu so puriso amum telapattam amanasikaritvā bahiddhā pamādam āhareyyāti|| ||

No hetam bhante|| ||

4. Upamā kho myāyam bhikkhave katā atthassa viññāpanāya||
ayaɱ cevettha attho||
Samatittiko telapatto ti kho bhikkhave kāyagatāya etaɱ satiyā adhivacanaɱ|| ||

5. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave evam sikkhitabbaɱ|| ||

Kāyagatā sati no bhāvitā bhavissati bahulīkatā yānikatā vatthukatā anuṭṭhitā paricitā susamāraddhā ti||
Evaɱ hi vo bhikkhave sikkhitabbanti|| ||

Nāḷandavaggo dutiyo

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

[page 171]

Mahāpuriso Nāḷandam||
Cundo Celañca Bāhiyo||
Uttiyo Ariyo Brahmā||
Sedakaɱ Janapadena cā ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter III. Sīlaṭṭhiti Vaggo

21. Sīlam

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā ca Ānando āyasmā ca Bhaddo Pāṭaliputte viharanti Kukkuṭārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Bhaddo sāyaṇhasamayam paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito yenāyasmā Ānando tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmatā Ānandena saddhiɱ sammodi... pe ...||
āyasmantam Ānandam etad avoca|| ||

3. Yānimani āvuso Ānanda kusalāni sīlāni vuttāni Bhagavatā||
imāni kusalāni sīlāni kimatthiyāni vuttāni Bhagavatā ti||
Sādhu sādhu āvuso Bhadda||
bhaddako kho te āvuso Bhadda ummaggo bhaddakam paṭibhānam kalyāṇī paripucchā|| ||

Evaɱ hi tvam avuso Bhadda pucchasi||
Yānimāni āvuso Ānanda kusalāni sīlāni vuttāni Bhagavatā||
imāni kusalāni sīlāni kimatthiyāni vuttāni Bhagavatā ti|| ||

Evam āvuso ti|| ||

4. Yānimani āvuso Bhadda kusalāni sīlāni vuttāni Bhagavatā imāni kusalāni sīlāni yāvad eva catunnam satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvanāya vuttāni Bhagavatā||
katamesam catunnaɱ|| ||

5. Idhāvuso bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhadomanassaɱ|| ||

[page 172]

Yānimanī āvuso Bhadda kusalāni sīlāni vuttāni Bhagavatā||
imani kusalāni sīlāni yāvad eva imesaɱ catunaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvanāya vuttāni Bhagavatā ti|| ||

 

 

22. Ṭhiti

1. Taɱ yeva nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Ekam antam nisinnam° °etad avoca|| ||

3. Ko nu kho āvuso Ānanda hetu ko paccayo yena tathāgate parinibbute saddhammo na ciraṭṭhitiko hoti||
ko panāvuso hetu ko paccayo yena tathāgate parinibbute saddhammo ciraṭṭhitiko hotī ti|| ||

Sādhu sādhu āvuso Bhadda||
bhaddako kho te āvuso Bhadda ummaggo bhaddakam paṭibhānaɱ kalyaṇī paripucchā||
evaɱ hi tvam āvuso Bhadda pucchasi||
Ko nu kho āvuso Ānanda hetu ko paccayo yena tathāgate parinibbute saddhammo na ciraṭṭhitiko hoti||
ko panāvuso Ānanda hetu ko paccayo yena tathāgate parinibbute saddhammo ciraṭṭhitiko hotī ti|| ||

Evam āvuso ti|| ||

4. Catunnaɱ kho āvuso satipaṭṭhānānam abhāvitattā abahulīkatattā Tathāgate parinibbute saddhammo na ciraṭṭhitiko hoti||
Catunnaɱ ca kho āvuso satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā Tathāgate parinibbute saddhammo ciraṭṭhitiko hoti||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

5. Idhāvuso bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Imesaɱ kho āvuso catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam abhāvitattā abahulīkatattā tathāgate parinibbute saddhammo na ciraṭṭhitiko hoti||
imesaɱ ca kho āvuso catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā tathāgate parinibbute saddhammo ciraṭṭhitiko hotī ti|| ||

[page 173]

 

 

23. Parihānaɱ

1—2. Pāṭaliputte viharanti Kukkuṭārāme|| ||

3. Ko nu kho āvuso Ānanda hetu ko paccayo yena saddhammaparihānaɱ hoti||
ko nu kho āvuso Ānanda hetu ko paccayo yena saddhamma-aparihānaɱ hetu|| ||

Sādhu sādhu āvuso Bhadda||
bhaddhako kho te āvuso Bhadda ummaggo bhaddakam paṭibhānaɱ kalyāṇī paripucchā||
evaɱ hi tvam āvuso Bhadda pucchasi||
Ko nu āvuso hetu ko paccayo yena saddhammaparihānaɱ hoti||
ko panāvuso Ānanda hetu ko paccayo yena saddhammaaparihānaɱ hoti ti|| ||

Evam āvuso ti|| ||

4. Catunnaɱ kho āvuso satipaṭṭhānānam abhāvitattā abahulīkatattā saddhammaparihānaɱ hoti||
catunnaɱ ca kho āvuso satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā saddhamma-aparihānaɱ hoti||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

5. Idhāvuso bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Imesaɱ kho āvuso catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam abhāvitattā abahulīkatattā saddhammaparihānaɱ hoti||
imesaɱ kho āvuso catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā saddhamma-aparihānaɱ hotī ti|| ||

 

 

24. Suddhakam

1. Sāvatthinidānam|| ||

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānā||
katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
ātāpi sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||

[page 174]

Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro satipaṭṭhānā ti|| ||

 

 

25. Brāhmaṇa

1. Evam me sutaɱ ekam samayam Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho aññataro brāhmaṇo yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodi||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Ko nu kho bho Gotama hetu ko paccayo yena Tathāgate parinibbute saddhammo na ciraṭṭhitiko hoti||
ko pana bho Gotama hetu ko paccayo yena tathāgate parinibbute saddhammo ciraṭṭhitiko hotī ti|| ||

4. Catunnaɱ kho brāhmaṇa satipatthānānam abhāvitattā. Idha brāhmaṇa bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī- -domanassaɱ||
Imesaɱ kho brāhmaṇa catunnaɱ- -ciraṭṭhitiko hotī ti|| ||

6. Evaɱ vutte so brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Abhikkantam bho Gotama ... pe ... upāsakam mam bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatan ti|| ||

 

 

26. Padesam

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā ca Sāriputto āyasmā ca Mahā-Moggalāno āyasmā ca Anuruddho Sākete viharanti Kanṭakīvane|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā ca Sāriputto āyasmā ca MahāMoggalāno sāyaṇhasamayam patisallāṇā vuṭṭhito yenāyasmā Anuruddho tenupasaŋkamiɱsa||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmatā Anuruddhena saddhiɱ sammodiɱsu||
sammodanīyaɱ Kathaɱ sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu

[page 175]

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Sāriputto āyasmantam Anuruddham etad avoca|| ||

3. Sekho sekho ti āvuso Anuruddha vuccati||
kittāvatā nu kho āvuso Sekho ti hotī ti|| ||

Catunnam kho āvuso satipaṭṭhānānam padesaɱ bhāvitattā sekho hoti||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

4. Idhāvuso bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyyyaloke abhijjhadomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Imesaɱ kho āvuso catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam padesam bhāvitattā sekho hotī ti|| ||

 

 

27. Samattam

1—2. Taɱ yeva nidānaɱ|| ||

Ekam antam- -Anuruddham etad avoca|| ||

3. Asekho asekho ti āvuso Anuruddha vuccati||
kittāvatā nu kho āvuso Asekho hotī ti|| ||

Catunnaɱ kho āvuso satipaṭṭhānānam samattam bhāvitattā asekho hoti|| ||

Katamesaɱ catunnaɱ?|| ||

4. Idhāvuso bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam|| ||

Imesaɱ kho āvuso catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānaɱ samattā bhāvitattā asekho hotī ti|| ||

 

 

28. Loko

1—2. Taɱ yeva nidānaɱ|| ||

Ekam antam nisinno-Anuruddham etad avoca|| ||

3. Katamesam āyasmā Anuruddha dhammānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā mahābhiññatam patto ti|| ||

[page 176]

Catunnaɱ āvuso satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā mahābhiññatam patto||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

4. Idhāham āvuso kāye kāyanupassī viharāmi ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhadomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammanupassī viharāmi ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Imesaɱ khvāham āvuso catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā mahabhiññatam patto|| ||

5. Imesaɱ ca panāham āvuso catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā sahassaɱ lokam abhijānāmīti|| ||

 

 

29. Sirivaḍḍho

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Ānando Rājagahe viharati Veḷuvane Kalandakanivāpe|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Sirivaḍḍho gahapati ābādhiko hoti||
dukkhito bāḷhagilāno|| ||

3. Atha kho Sirivaḍḍho gahapati aññataram purisam āmantesi||
Ehi tvam ambho purisa yenāyasmā Ānando tenupasaŋkama||
upasaŋkamitvā mama vacanena āyasmato Ānandassa pāde sirasā vanda||
Sirivaḍḍho bhante gahapati ābādhiko dukkhito bāḷhagilāno||
so āyasmato Ānandassa pāde sirasā vandatī ti evañca vadeti||
Sādhu kira bhante āyasmā Ānando yena Sirivaḍḍhassa gahapatissa nivesanaɱ||
tenupasaŋkamatu anukampam upādāyāti|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho so puriso Sirivaḍḍhassa gahapatissa paṭissutvā yenāyasmā Ānando tenupasaŋkami|| ||

4. Upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantaɱ Ānandam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi||
eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so puriso āyasmantam Ānandam etad avoca||
Sirivaḍḍho bhante gahapati ābādhiko dukkhito bāḷhagilāno||
so āyasmato Ānandassa pāde sirasā vandati||
evañca vadeti||
Sādhu kira bhante āyasmā Ānando yena Sirivaḍḍhassa gahapatissa nivesanaɱ tenupasaŋkamatu anukampam upādāyā ti|| ||

[page 177]

Adhivāsesi kho āyasmā Ānando tuṇhībhāvena|| ||

5. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya yena Sirivaḍḍhassa gahapatissa nivesanam upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi|| ||

Nisajja kho āyasmā Ānando Sirivaḍḍham gahapatim etad avoca|| ||

6. Kacci te gahapati khamanīyaɱ kacci yāpanīyaɱ kacci dukkhā vedanā paṭikkamanti no abhikkamanti paṭikkamosānam paññāyati no abhikkamo ti|| ||

Na me bhante khamanīyaɱ na yāpanīyam bāḷhā me dukkhā vedanā abhikkamanti no paṭikkammanti abhikkamo sānam paññāyati no paṭikkamo ti|| ||

7. Tasmā ti ha te gahapati evaɱ sikkhitabbaɱ|| ||

Kāye kāyānupassī viharissāmi ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharissāmi ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassan ti|| ||

Evaɱ hi te gahapati sikkhitabban ti|| ||

8. Ye me bhante Bhagavatā cattāro satipaṭṭhānā desitā saɱvijjanti te dhammā mayi ahaɱ ca tesu dhammesu sandissāmi||
ahaɱ hi bhante kāye kāyānupassī viharāmi ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharāmi ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

9. Yāni cimāni bhante Bhagavatā pañcorambhāgiyāni saŋyojanāni desitāni||
nāhaɱ tesaɱ kiñci attani appahīnaɱ samanupassāmī ti|| ||

10. Lādhā te gahapati||
suladdhaɱ te gahapati||
anāgāmiphalaɱ tayā gahapati vyākatan ti|| ||

[page 178]

 

 

30. Mānadinna

1. Taɱ yeva nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Mānadinno gahapati ābādhiko hoti dukkhito bāḷhagilāno|| ||

3—6. Atha kho Mānadinno gahapati aññataram purisam āmantesi ... pe ...|| ||

7. Evarūpāya cāham bhante dukkhāya vedanāya puṭṭho samāno kāye kāyānupassī viharāmi ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharāmi ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

8. Yānicimāni bhante Bhagavatā pañcorambhāgiyani saŋyojanāni desitāni||
nāham bhante yaɱ kiñci attani appahīnaɱ samanupassāmīti|| ||

9. Lābhā te gahapati||
suladdhan te gahapati||
anāgāmiphalaɱ tayā gahapati vyākatan ti|| ||

Sīlavaggo tatiyo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Sīlaɱ Ṭhiti Parihānam Suddhakaɱ||
Brāhmaṇena ca Padesam||
Samattam Loko ca Sirivaḍḍho||
Mānadinnena te dasā ti|| ||

Satipaṭṭhāna-saɱyuttassa Sīlaṭṭhitivaggo tatiyo|| ||

 

 

Chapter IV. Anussuta Vaggo

31. Anussutam

1—2. Sāvatthi nidānam|| ||

3. Ayaɱ kāye kāyānupassanā ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ñāṇam udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādi

[page 179]

Sā kho panāyam kāye kāyanupassanā bhāvetabbā ti me bhikkhave||
bhavitā ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ñāṇam udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādi|| ||

4. Ayam vedanānupassanā ti-||
5. Ayaɱ citte cittānupassanā ti. Ayaɱ dhammesu dhammānupassanā ti-||
sā kho panāyaɱ dhammesu dhammānupassanā bhāvetabbā ti me bhikkhave||
bhāvitā ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ñāṇam udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādīti|| ||

 

 

32. Virāgo

1—2. Sāvatthiyaɱ|| ||

3. Cattāro me bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānā bhāvitā bahulīkatā ekantanibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya {saɱvattanti}||
katame cattāro|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro satipaṭṭhānā bhāvitā bahulīkatā ekantanibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

 

 

33. Viraddho

3. Yesaɱ kesañci bhikkhave cattāro satipaṭṭhānā viraddhā||
viraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī|| ||

[page 180]

4. Yesaɱ kesañci bhikkhave cattāro satipaṭṭhānā āraddhā||
āraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

5. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
... pe ...||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Yesaɱ kesañci bhikkhave ime cattāro satipaṭṭhānā viraddhā||
viraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī|| ||

Yesaɱ kesañci bhikkhave ime cattāro satipaṭṭhānā āraddhā||
āraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī ti|| ||

 

 

34. Bhāvanā

1—2. Sāvatthiyam|| ||

3. Cattāro me bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānā bhāvitā bahulīkatā aparāparaŋgamanāya saɱvattanti||
katame cattāro|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
... pe ...||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro satipaṭṭhānā bhāvitā bahulīkatā aparāparaŋgamanāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

 

 

35. Sato

1—2. Sāvatthi|| ||

3. Sato bhikkhave bhikkhu vihareyya sampajāno||
ayaɱ vo amhākam anusāsanī|| ||

4. Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu sato hoti||
Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyanupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam||
[pe]|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sato hoti|| ||

5. Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu sampajāno hoti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhuno viditā vedanā uppajjanti||
viditā upaṭṭhahanti

[page 181]

viditā abbhatthaɱ gacchanti|| ||

Viditā vitakkā uppajjanti||
viditā upaṭṭhahanti||
viditā abbhattham gacchanti|| ||

Viditā saññā uppajjanti||
viditā upaṭṭhahanti||
viditā abbhatthaɱ gacchanti|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sampajāno hoti|| ||

6. Sato bhikkhave bhikkhu vihareyya sampajāno||
ayaɱ vo amhākam anusāsanīti|| ||

 

 

36. Aññam

1—2. Sāvatthiyaɱ|| ||

3. Cattāro me bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānā||
katame cattāro|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
... pe ...||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammanupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro satipaṭṭhānā|| ||

4. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam bhavitattā bahulīkatattā dvinnam phalānam aññataram phalam pāṭikaŋkhaɱ diṭṭheva dhamme aññā sati vā upādisese anāgāmitā ti|| ||

 

 

37. Chandam

1. Sāvatthiyaɱ|| ||

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānā||
katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpi sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Tassa kāye kāyānupassino viharato yo kāyasmiɱ chando so pahīyati||
chandassa pahānāya amataɱ sacchikataɱ hoti|| ||

4. Vedanāsu° °yo vedanāsu chando so pahīyati||
chandassa pahānā amataɱ sacchikataɱ hoti|| ||

[page 182]

5. Citte- -yo cittamhi chando so pahīyati||
chandassa pahānā amataɱ sacchikataɱ hoti|| ||

6. Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
tassa dhammesu dhammānupassino viharato yo dhammesu chando so pahīyati||
chandassa pahānā amatam sacchikataɱ hotī ti|| ||

 

 

38. Pariññāya

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānā||
katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
tassa kāye kāyānupassino viharato kāyo pariññāto hoti||
kāyassa pariññātattā amataɱ sacchikataɱ hoti|| ||

4. Vedanāsu° vedanā pariññātā honti vedanānam pariññātattā amatam sacchikataɱ hoti|| ||

5. Citte° °cittam pariññātām hoti||
cittassa pariññātattā amataɱ sacchikataɱ hoti|| ||

6. Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ.||
tassa dhammesu dhammānupassino viharato dhammā pariññātā honti||
dhammānam pariññātattā amataɱ sacchikatam hotī ti|| ||

 

 

39. Bhāvanā

2. Catunnam bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvanaɱ desissāmi||
taɱ suṇātha|| ||

Katamā ca bhikkhave catunnam satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvanā|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyanupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ

[page 183]

4 Ayam bhikkhave catunnam satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvanā ti|| ||

 

 

40. Vibhaŋga

2. Satipaṭṭhānañca vo bhikkhave desissāmi satipaṭṭhānabhāvanañca satipaṭṭhānabhāvanāgaminiñca paṭipadaɱ||
tam suṇātha|| ||

3. Katamañ ca bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānaɱ|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyanupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānaɱ|| ||

4. Katamā ca bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānabhāvanā|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu samudayadhammānupassī kāyasmiɱ viharati||
vayadhammānupassī kāyasmiɱ viharati||
samudayavayadhammānupassī kāyasmim viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam|| ||

Samudayadhammānupassī vedanāsu viharati vayadhammānupassī vedanāsu viharati||
samudayavayadhammanupassī vedanāsu viharati|| ||

Tathā citte||
Dhammesu viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānabhāvanā|| ||

5. Katamā ca bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānabhāvanāgāminī patipādā|| ||

Ayam eva ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo||
seyyathīdaɱ sammādiṭṭhi||
... pe ...||
sammāsamādhi|| ||

Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave satipaṭṭhāna bhāvanāgāminī patipadā ti|| ||

Ananussuta-vaggo catuttho|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

[page 184]

Ananussutaɱ Virāgo ca||
Viraddho Bhāvanā Sato||
Aññam Chandam Pariññāya||
Bhāvanā {Vibhaŋgena} te dasāti|| ||

 

 

Chapter V. Amata Vaggo

41. Amatam

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Catusu bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacittā viharatha||
mā vo amatam panassa||
katamesu catusu|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam|| ||

4. Imesu bhikkhave catusu satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacittā viharatha||
mā vo amatam panassā ti|| ||

 

 

42. Samudayo

2. Catunnam bhikkhave satipaṭṭhānānam samudayañca atthagamañca desissāmi||
taɱ suṇātha|| ||

3. Ko ca bhikkhave kāyassa samudayo|| ||

Āhārasamudayā kāyassa samudayo||
āhāranirodhā kāyassa atthagamo|| ||

4. Phassasamudayā vedanānaɱ samudayo||
phassanirodhā vedanānam atthagamo|| ||

5. Nāmarūpasamudayā cittassa samudayo||
nāmarūpanirodhā cittassa atthagamo|| ||

6. Manasikārasamudayā dhammānam samudayo||
manasikāranirodhā dhammānam atthagamo ti|| ||

[page 185]

 

 

43. Maggo

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū amantesi|| ||

Ekam idāham bhikkhave samayam Uruvelāyaɱ viharāmi najjā Nerañjarāya tīre Ajapālanigrodhe pathamābhisambuddho|| ||

3. Tassa mayham bhikkhave rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaɱ cetaso parivitakko udapādi||
Ekāyanvāyam maggo sattānaɱ visuddhiyā sokaparidevānam samatikkamāya dukkhadomanassānam atthagamāya ñāyassa adhigamāya nibbānassa sacchikiriyāya yad idaɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhānā||
katame cattāro|| ||

Kāye vā bhikkhu kāyānupassī vihareyya Vedanāsu vā bhikkhu vedanānupassī vihareyya||
Citte vā bhikkhu cittānupassī vihareyya||
Dhammesu vā bhikkhu dhammānupassī vihareyya||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
Ekāyanvāyam maggo sattānam visuddhiyā sokaparidevānaɱ samatikkamāya dukkhadomanassānam atthagamāya ñāyassa adhigamāya nibbānassa sacchikiriyāya yad idaɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhānā ti|| ||

4. Atha kho bhikkhave Brahmā sahampati mama cetasā ceto parivitakkam aññāya||
seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjītaɱ vā bāham pasāreyya pasāritaɱ vā bāham sammiñjeyya||
evam eva Brahmaloke antarahito pi mama purato pātur ahosi|| ||

5. Atha kho bhikkhave Brahmā sahampati ekaɱsam uttarāsaŋgaɱ karitvā yenāham tenañjalim paṇametvā mam etad avoca||
Evam etam Bhagavā evam etaɱ Sugata||
ekāyanvāyam maggo sattānaɱ visuddhiyā sokaparidevānam samatikkamāya dukkhadomanassānam atthagamāya ñāyassa adhigamāya nibbānassa sacchikiriyāya yad idaɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhānā

[page 186]

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Kāye vā bhante bhikkhu kāyānupassī vihareyya||
Vedanāsu vā||
Citte vā||
Dhammesu vā bhante {bhikkhu} dhammānupassī vihareyya||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Ekāyanvāyam bhante maggo sattānam visuddhiyā sokaparidavānaɱ samatikkamāya dukkhadomanassānaɱ atthagamāya ñāyassa adhigamāya nibbānassa sacchikiriyāya yad idaɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhānā ti|| ||

6. Idam avoca bhikkhave Brahmā sahampati||
idaɱ vatvā athāparam etad avoca|| ||

Ekāyanaɱ jātikhayantadassī||
maggam pajānāti hitānukampī||
Etena maggena ataɱsu pubbe||
tarissanti ye ca taranti oghan ti|| ||

 

 

44. Sato

1. Sāvatthiyaɱ|| ||

2. Sato bhikkhave bhikkhu vihareyya||
ayam vo amhākam anusāsanī|| ||

3. Kathañca bhikkhave {bhikkhu} sato hoti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sato hoti|| ||

4. Sato bhikkhave bhikkhu vihareyya||
ayaɱ vo amhākam anusāsanī ti|| ||

 

 

45. Kusalarāsi

2. Kusalarāsī ti bhikkhave vadamāno cattāro satipaṭṭhāne sammāvadamāno vadeyya|| ||

Kevalo hāyam bhikkhave kusalarāsī yad idaɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhānā||
katame cattāro|| ||

[page 187]

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

4. Kusalarāsī ti bhikkhave vadamāno ime cattāro satipaṭṭhāne sammāvadamāno vadeyya|| ||

Kevalo hāyam bhikkhave kusalarāsī yad idaɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhānā ti|| ||

 

 

46. Pātimokkha

2. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami ... pe ... Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Sādhu me bhante saŋkhittena dhammaɱ desetu yam aham Bhagavato dhammaɱ sutvā eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto vihareyyanti||
Tasmā ti ha tvam bhikkhu ādim eva visodhehi kusalesu dhammesu|| ||

Ko cādi kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ|| ||

4. Idha tvam bhikkhu pātimokkhasaɱvarasaɱvuto viharāhi ācāragocarasampanno anumattesu vajjesu bhayadassāvī samādāya sikkhasu sikkhāpadesu|| ||

Yato kho tvam bhikkhu pātimokkhasaɱvarasaɱvuto viharissasi ācāragocarasampanno anumattesu vajjesu bhayadassāvī samādāya sikkhissasi sikkhāpadesu||
tato tvam bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya cattāro satipaṭṭhāne bhāveyyāsi||
katame cattāro|| ||

5. Idha tvam bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharāhi||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharāhi ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

6. Yato kho tvam bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya ime cattāro satipaṭṭhāne evam bhāvessasi||
tato tuyham bhikkhu yā ratti vā divāso vā āgamissati vuddhi yeva pāṭikaŋkhā kusalesu dhammesu no parihānīti|| ||

7. Atha kho so bhikkhu Bhagavato bhāsitaɱ-|| ||

[page 188]

8. Atha kho so bhikkhu eko vūpakattho- -abbhaññāsi|| ||

9. Aññataro capana so bhikkhu arahatam ahosī ti|| ||

ko cādi kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ|| ||

vacī-||
mano- sucaritam bhāvessasi|| ||

vacī-||
mano- -sucaritam bhāvessasi||
tato tvam bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya cattāro satipaṭṭhāne bhāvessasi||

48. Mittā

1. Sāvatthiyam|| ||

2. Ye bhikkhave anukampeyyātha||
ye ca sotabbam maññeyyuɱ mittā vā amaccā vā ñāti vā sālohitā vā||
te vo bhikkhave catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvanāya samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhāpetabbā||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

4. Ye bhikkhave anukampeyyātha ye ca sotabbam maññeyyum mittā va amaccā vā ñati vā sālohitā vā||
te vo bhikkhave imesaɱ catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvanāya samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhāpetabbā ti|| ||

 

 

49. Vedanā

1. Sāvatthiyam|| ||

2. Tisso imā bhikkhave vedanā||
katamā tisso|| ||

Sukhā vedanā dukkhā vedanā adukkhamasukhāvedanā|| ||

Imā kho bhikkhave tisso vedanā|| ||

3. Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannaɱ vedanānaɱ pariññāya cattāro satipaṭṭhānā bhāvetabbā||
katame cattāro|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

5. Imāsaɱ kho bhikkhave tissannaɱ vedanānam pariññāya ime cattāro satipaṭṭhānā bhāvetabbā ti|| ||

51-62.

Vatthena dasamam padam|| ||

Satipaṭṭhānavasena appamādavaggo satipaṭṭhāna-vitthāretabbo vaggo

Chapter X. Ogha Vaggo

93-102.

103. Uddhambhāgiyāni

2. Pañcimani bhikkhave uddhambhāgiyāni saŋyojanāni||
katamāni pañca||
Rūparāgo arūparāgo māno uddhaccam avijjā

[page 192]

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcuddhambhāgiyāni saŋyojanāni|| ||

3. Imesam kho bhikkhave pañcannam uddhambhāgiyānam saŋyojanānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya cattāro satipaṭṭhānā bhāvetabbā ||katame cattāro|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam||
Vedanāsu||
Citte||
Dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

5. Imesam kho bhikkhave pañcannam uddhambhāgiyānam saŋyojanānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya ime cattāro satipatthānā bhāvetabbāti|| ||

[Uddānam]|| ||

Ogho Yogo Upādānaɱ||
Gantha-Anusayena ca||
Kāmaguṇā Nīvaranaɱ||
Khandham Oruddhabhāgiyāni|| ||

Oghavaggo||

evam Satipaṭṭhānasamyuttaɱ vitthāretabbaɱ|| ||
