Book IV

Indriya Saɱyutta

Chapter I. Suddhika Vaggo

1. Suddhikam

1—2. Sāvatthi|| ||

Tatra kho Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

3. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ viriyindriyaɱ satindriyaɱ samādhindriyaɱ paññindriyam|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyānī ti|| ||

 

 

2. Sota 1

3. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyam viriyindriyaɱ satindriyaɱ samādhindriyaɱ paññindriyaɱ|| ||

4. Yato kho bhikkhave ariyasāvako imesaɱ pañcannam indriyānam assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇaɱ ca yathābhūtam pajānati||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave ariyasāvako sotāpanno avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

 

 

3. Sota 2

3. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyam ... pe ...paññindriyaɱ|| ||

4. Yato kho bhikkhave ariyasāvako imesam pañcannam indriyānaɱ samudayañca atthagamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtam pajānāti

[page 194]

ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave ariyasāvako sotāpanno avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

 

 

4. Araham 1

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ...paññindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Yato kho bhikkhave ariyasāvako imesam pañcannam indriyānam assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtam viditvā anupādā vimutto hoti||
ayam vuccati bhikkhave arahaɱ khīṇāsavo vusitavā katakaraṇīyo ohītabhāro anuppattasadattho parikkhīṇabhavasaŋyojano sammadaññā vimutto ti|| ||

 

 

5. Araham 2

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ...paññindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Yato kho bhikkhave bhikkhu imesam pañcannam indriyānam Samudayañca atthagamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtam viditvā anupādā vimutto hoti||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave bhikkhu arahaɱ khīṇāsavo-samadaññā vimutto ti|| ||

 

 

6. Samaṇabrāhmaṇā 1

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ||... pe ...||
paññindriyam|| ||

3. Ye hi keci bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā imesam pañcannam indriyānaɱ samudayañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtaɱ nappajānanti na me te bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samaṇesu vā samaṇasammatā brāhmaṇesu vā brāhmaṇasammatā na ca panete āyasmanto sāmaññatthaɱ vā brahmaññatthaɱ vā diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharanti

[page 195]

4. Ye ca kho keci bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā imesam pañcannam indriyānam {samudayañca} attha{gamañca} {assādañca} {ādinavañca} nissaranaɱ ca yathābhūtam pajānanti||
te kho me bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samaṇesu ceva samaṇasammatā brāhmaṇesu ca brāhmaṇasammatā te ca panāyasmanto sāmaññatthaɱ ca brahmaññatthaɱ ca diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharantī ti|| ||

 

 

7. {Samaṇabrāhmaṇā} 2

3. Ye hi keci bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā saddhindriyaɱ nappajānanti saddhindriyasamudayaɱ nappajānanti saddhindriyanirodhaɱ nappajānanti saddhindriyanirodhagāminipaṭipadam nappajānanti ... pe ...Viriyindriyaɱ nappajānanti ... pe ...Satindriyam nappajānanti||
Samādhindriyaɱ nappajānanti||
Paññindriyaɱ nappajānanti paññindriyasamudayaɱ nappajānanti||
paññindriyanirodhaɱ nappajānanti paññindriyanirodhagāminipaṭipadam nappajānanti||
na me te bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samaṇesu ceva samaṇasammatā {brāhmaṇesu} ca brāhmaṇasammatā||
na ca panete āyasmantā sāmaññatthaɱ vā brahmaññatthaɱ vā diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharanti|| ||

4. Ye hi keci bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā saddhindriyam pajānanti saddhindriyasamudayam pajānanti saddhindriyanirodham pajānanti saddhindriyanirodhagāminipaṭipadam pajānanti||
{Viriyindriyam} pajānanti ... pe ...Satindriyam pajānanti||
samādhindriyam pajānanti ... pe ...||

[page 196]

paññindriyam pajānanti paññindriyasamudayam pajānanti||
paññindriyanirodham pajānanti||
paññindriyanirodhagāminipatipadam pajānanti||
te kho pana me bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samaṇesu ceva samaṇasammatā brāhmaṇesu ca brāhmaṇasammatā||
te ca panāyasmanto sāmaññatthaɱ ca brahmaññatthaɱ ca diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharantī ti|| ||

 

 

8. Daṭṭhabbam

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyam|| ||

3. Kattha ca bhikkhave saddhindriyaɱ daṭṭhabbaɱ|| ||

Catusu sotāpattiyaŋgesu||
ettha saddhindriyaɱ daṭṭhabbaɱ|| ||

4. Kattha ca bhikkhave viriyindriyaɱ daṭṭhabbaɱ|| ||

Catusu sammapadhānesu||
ettha viriyindriyaɱ daṭṭhabbaɱ|| ||

5. Kattha ca bhikkhave satindriyaɱ daṭṭhabbaɱ|| ||

Catusu satipaṭṭhānesu||
ettha satindriyaɱ daṭṭhabbaɱ|| ||

6. Kattha ca bhikkhave samādhindriyaɱ daṭṭhabbaɱ|| ||

Catusu jhānesu||
ettha samādhindriyaɱ daṭṭhabbam|| ||

7. Kattha ca bhikkhave paññindriyaɱ daṭṭhabbaɱ|| ||

Catusu ariyasaccesu||
ettha paññindriyaɱ daṭṭhabbaɱ|| ||

8. Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyānī ti|| ||

 

 

9. Vibhaŋga 1

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Katamañ ca bhikkhave saddhindriyaɱ|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako saddho hoti||
saddahati Tathāgatassa bodhiɱ

[page 197]

Iti pi so Bhagavā arahaɱ sammāsambuddho vijjācaraṇasampanno sugato lokavidū anuttaro purisadhammasārathi satthā devamanussānaɱ buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Idam vuccati bhikkhave saddhindriyam|| ||

4. Katamañ ca bhikkhave viriyindriyaɱ|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako āraddhaviriyo viharati||
akusalānaɱ dhammānam pahānāya kusalānaɱ dhammānam upasampadāya thāmavā daḷhaparakkamo anikkhittadhuro kusalesu dhammesu|| ||

Idam vuccati viriyindriyaɱ|| ||

5. Katamañ ca bhikkhave satindriyam|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako satimā hoti paramena satinepakkena samannāgato cirakataɱ cirabhāsitam pi saritā anussaritā|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave satindriyaɱ|| ||

6. Katamañ ca bhikkhave samādhindriyam|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako vossaggārammanaɱ karitvā labhati samādhiɱ labhati cittassa ekaggataɱ|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave samādhindriyaɱ|| ||

7. Katamañ ca bhikkhave paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako paññavā hoti||
Udayatthagāminiyā paññāya samannāgato ariyāya nibbedhikāya sammādukkhakhayagāminiyā|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave paññindriyam|| ||

8. Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyānī ti|| ||

 

 

10. Vibhaŋga 2

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni||
katamāni pañca||
saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Katamañ ca bhikkhave saddhindriyaɱ|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako saddho hoti saddahati Tathāgatassa bodhiɱ||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave samādhindriyaɱ|| ||

[page 198]

4. Katamañ ca bhikkhave viriyindriyam?|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako āraddhaviriyo viharati||
akusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ pahānāya kusalānaɱ dhammānam upasampadāya thāmavā daḷhaparakkamo anikkhittadhuro kusalesu dhammesu||
so anuppannānam pāpakānam akusalānam dhammānam anuppādāya chandam janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati||
uppannānam pāpakānam akusalānam pahānāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati anuppannānaɱ kusalānam dhammānam uppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati||
uppannānaɱ kusalānam dhammānam ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave viriyindriyaɱ|| ||

5. Katamañ ca bhikkhave satindriyaɱ|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako satimā hoti paramena satinepakkena samannāgato cirakatam pi cirabhāsitam pi saritā anussaritā||
so kāye kāyānupassī viharati ... pe ...vedanāsu||
citte||
dhammesu dhammanupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave satindriyaɱ|| ||

6. Katamañ ca bhikkhave samādhindriyaɱ|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako vossaggārammaṇaɱ karitvā labhati samādhim labhati cittassa ekaggataɱ||
So vivicceva kāmehi vivicca akusalehi dhammehi savitakkaɱ savicāram vivekajam pītisukham pathamajjhānam upasampajja viharati||
vitakkavicārānaɱ vūpasamā ... pe ... dutiyaɱ jhānaɱ||
tatiyaɱ jhānaɱ||
upasampajja viharati|| ||

Sukhassa ca pahānā dukkhassa ca pahānā pubbeva somanassadomanassānam atthagamā adukkham asukham upekhāsatipārisuddhiɱ catutthaɱ jhānaɱ upasampajja viharati|| ||

Idam vuccati bhikkhave samādhindriyaɱ|| ||

[page 199]

7. Katannaɱ ca bhikkhave paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyāsāvako paññavā hoti udayatthagāminiyā paññāya samannāgato ariyāya nibbedhikāya sammādukkhakkhayagāminiyā||
so Idaɱ dukkhanti yathābhūtam pajānāti||
Ayaɱ dukkhasamudayo ti yathābhūtam pajānāti ... pe ...Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminipatipadā ti yathā bhūtam pajānāti|| ||

8. Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave paññindriyaɱ||
imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyānī ti|| ||

Suddhikavaggo pathamo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Suddhikañ ceva dve Sotā||
Arahantā apare duve||
Samaṇabrāhmaṇā Daṭṭhabbam||
Vibhaŋgā apare duve ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter II. Mudatara Vaggo

11. Paṭilābho

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyam ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Katamañ ca bhikkhave saddhindriyam||
Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako saddho hoti||
saddahati Tathāgatassa bodhim||
Iti pi so Bhagavā arahaɱ sammāsambuddho ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave saddhindriyaɱ|| ||

4. Katamañ ca bhikkhave viriyindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave cattāro sammappadhāne ārabbha viriyam paṭilabhati|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave viriyindriyaɱ|| ||

[page 200]

5. Katamañ ca bhikkhave satindriyaɱ?|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave cattaro satipaṭṭhāne ārabbha satim paṭilabhati|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave satindriyaɱ|| ||

6. Katamañ ca bhikkhave samādhindriyaɱ?|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako vossaggārammaṇaɱ karitvā labhati samādhiɱ labhati cittassa ekaggataɱ|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave samādhindriyaɱ|| ||

7. Katamañ ca bhikkhave paññindriyaɱ?|| ||

Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako paññavā hoti udayatthagāminiyā paññaya samannāgato ariyāya nibbedhikāya sammādukkhakkhayagāminiyā|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave paññindriyaɱ|| ||

8. Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyānī ti|| ||

 

 

12. Saŋkhitta 1

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyam|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyāni|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcindriyānaɱ samattā paripūrattā arahaɱ hoti||
tato mudutarehi anāgāmī hoti||
tato mudutarehi sakadāgāmī hoti||
tato mudutarehi sotāpanno hoti||
tato mudutarehi dhammānusārī hoti||
tato mudutarehi saddhānusārī hoti|| ||

 

 

13. Saŋkhitta 2

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave {indriyāni}|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyāni|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam indriyānaɱ samattā paripūrattā arahaɱ hoti-||
osaddhānusari hoti|| ||

4. Iti kho bhikkhave indriyavemattatā phalavemattatā hoti||
balavemattatā puggalavemattatā hoti|| ||

[page 201]

 

 

14. Saŋkhitta 3

2. Pañcimani bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyāni|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam indriyānaɱ samattā paripūrattā arahaɱ hoti- -saddhānusārī hoti|| ||

4. Iti kho bhikkhave paripūram paripūrakārī ārādheti||
padesaɱ padesakārī ārādheti||
avañjhānitvevāham bhikkhave pañcindriyāni vadāmīti|| ||

 

 

15. Vitthāro 1

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyāni|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam indriyānaɱ samattā paripūrattā arahaɱ hoti||
tato mudutarehi antarāparinibbāyī hoti||
tato mudutarehi upahacca parinibbāyī hoti||
tato mudutarehi asaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti||
tato mudutarehi sasaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti||
tato mudutarehi uddhaɱsoto hoti akaniṭṭhagāmī||
tato mudutarehi sakadāgāmī hoti||
tato mudutarehi sotāpanno hoti||
tato mudutarehi dammānusārī hoti||
tato mudutarehi saddhānusārī hotīti|| ||

 

 

16. Vitthāro 2

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni||
Katamāni pañca|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyāni|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam indriyānaɱ samattā paripūrattā arahaɱ hoti||
tato mudutarehi antarāparinibbāyī- -saddhānusārī hoti|| ||

4. Iti kho bhikkhave indriyavemattatā phaḷavemattatā hoti||
phalavemattatā puggalavemattatā hoti|| ||

[page 202]

 

 

17. Vitthāro 3

2. pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyāni|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam indriyānaɱ samattā paripūrattā arahaɱ hoti||
tato mudatarehi antarāparinibbāyī- -saddhānusārī hoti|| ||

4. Iti kho bhikkhave paripūraɱ paripūrakārī ārādheti||
padesam padesakārī ārādheti avañjhānitvevāham bhikkhave pañcindriyāni vadamīti|| ||

 

 

18. Paṭipanno

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyāni|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam indriyānaɱ samattā paripūrattā arahaɱ hoti||
tato mudutarehi arahattaphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno hoti||
tato mudutarehi anāgāmī hoti||
tato mudutarehi anāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno hoti||
tato mudutarehi sakadāgāmī hoti||
tato mudutarehi sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno hoti||
tato mudutarehi sotāpanno hoti||
tato mudutarehi sotāpattiphala sacchikiriyāya paṭipanno hoti|| ||

4. Yassa kho bhikkhave imāni pañcindriyāni sabbena sabbaɱ sabbathā sabbaɱ natthi||
tam aham Bāhiro puthujjanapakkhe ṭhito ti vadāmī ti|| ||

 

 

19. Upasanno

2. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami ... pe ...Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Indriyasampanno indriyasampanno ti bhante vuccati||
kittāvatā nu kho bhante indriyasampanno hotīti|| ||

[page 203]

4. Idha bhikkhu bhikkhu saddhindriyam bhāveti upasamagāmiɱ sambodhagāmiɱ ... pe ...paññindriyam bhāveti upasamagāmiɱ sambodhagāmiɱ|| ||

5. Ettāvatā kho bhikkhu bhikkhu indriyasampanno hotīti|| ||

 

 

20. Āsavānaɱ khayo

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyām|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyāni|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam indriyānam bhavitattā bahulīkatattā bhikkhu āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim paññāvimuttiɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharatī ti|| ||

Mudutaravaggo dutiyo

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Paṭilābho ca tayo Saŋkhittā||
Vitthārā apare tayo||
Paṭipanno cupasamo||
Āsavānaɱ khayo cime ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter III. Chaḷindriya Vaggo

21. Nabbhavo (or Ñānavā)

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyam ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Yāva kīvañcāham bhikkhave imesam pañcannam indriyānaɱ samudayañca atthagamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtaɱ na abbhaññāsiɱ||

[page 204]

neva tāvāham bhikkhave sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya anuttaraɱ sammāsambodhim abhisambuddho ti paccaññāsiɱ|| ||

4. Yato ca khvāham bhikkhave imesam pañcannam indriyānam samudayañca atthagamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtam abbhaññāsiɱ||
atha khvāham bhikkhave sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake {sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā} pajāya sadevamanussāya anuttaraɱ sammāsambodhim abhisambuddho ti paccaññāsiɱ||
ñāṇañca pana me dassanam udapādi||
Akuppā me cetovimutti||
ayam antimā jāti natthidāni punabbhavo ti|| ||

 

 

22. Jīvita

2. Tīṇimāni bhikkhave indriyāni||
katamāni {tīṇi}|| ||

Itthindriyam purisindriyaɱ jīvitindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Imāni kho bhikkhave tīṇi indriyānī ti|| ||

 

 

23. Ñāya

2. Tīṇimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni {tīṇi}?|| ||

Anaññātaññassāmītindriyaɱ aññindriyam aññātāvindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Imāni kho bhikkhave tīṇi indriyānīti|| ||

 

 

24. Ekābhiññam (or Ekabījī)

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyam ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyani|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam indriyānaɱ samattā paripūrattā arahaɱ hoti||
tato mudutarehi antarāparinibbāyī hoti||
tato mudutarehi upahaccaparinibbāyī hoti||
tato mudutarehi asaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti||
tato mudutarehi sasaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti

[page 205]

tato mudutarehi uddhaɱsoto hoti akaniṭṭhagāmī||
tato mudutarehi sakadāgāmī hoti||
tato mudutarehi ekabījī hoti||
tato mudutarehi kolaŋkolo hoti||
tato mudutarehi sattakkhattuparamo hoti||
tato mudutarehi dhammānusārī hoti||
tato mudutarehi saddhānusārī hotī ti|| ||

 

 

25. Suddhakam

2. Chayimāni bhikkhave indriyāni||
katamāni cha|| ||

Cakkhundriyaɱ sotindriyaɱ ghānindriyaɱ jivhindriyaɱ kāyindriyam manindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Imāni kho bhikkhave cha indriyānī ti|| ||

 

 

26. Soto or Sotāpanno

2. Cha yimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni cha?|| ||

Cakkhundriyaɱ||
... pe ...||
manindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Yato kho bhikkhave ariyasāvako imesaɱ channam indriyānaɱ samudayañca atthagamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtam pajānāti||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave ariyasāvako sotāpanno avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

 

 

27. Arahatā 1

2. Cha yimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni cha?|| ||

Cakkhundriyam ... pe ... manindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Yato kho bhikkhave bhikkhu imesaɱ channam indriyānaɱ samudayañca atthagamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtaɱ viditvā anupādā vimutto hoti ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave bhikkhu arahaɱ khīṇāsavo vusitavā katakaraṇīyo ohitabhāro anuppattasadattho parikkhīṇabhavasaŋyojano samadaññā vimutto ti|| ||

 

 

28. Arahatā 2 or Buddho

2. Chayimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni cha?|| ||

Cakkhundriyam ... pe ... manindriyaɱ|| ||

[page 206]

3. Yāva kīvañcāham bhikkhave imesaɱ channam indriyānaɱ samudayañca atthagamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtam na abbhaññāsiɱ||
neva- -abhisambuddhoti paccaññāsiɱ|| ||

Yato ca° °abbhaññasiɱ °abhisaɱbuddho ti paccaññāsiɱ||
ñaṇañca pana me dassanaɱ udapādi||
Akuppā me cetovimutti||
ayam antimājāti natthidāni punabbhavo ti|| ||

 

 

29. Samaṇabrāhmaṇā 1

2. Cha yimāni bhikkhave indriyāni||
katamāni cha|| ||

Cakkhundriyaɱ||
... pe ...||
manindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Ye hi keci bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā imesaɱ channam indriyānaɱ samudayañca atthagamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtaɱ nappajānanti||
na me te bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā-upasampajja viharanti|| ||

4. Ye hi keci bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā° pajānanti||
te kho me bhikkhave° °sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharantīti|| ||

 

 

30. Samaṇabrāhmaṇā 2

cakkhundriyasamudayaɱ nappajānanti ... pe ...cakkhundriyanirodhagāminipaṭipadaɱ nappajānanti||

te bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā- -sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharantīti|| ||

Chaḷindriyavaggo tatiyo

Chapter IV. Sukhindriya (or Uppaṭi) Vaggo

31. Suddhikam

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni||
katamani pañca|| ||

Sukhindriyam dukkhindriyam somanassindriyaɱ domanassindriyam upekhindriyam|| ||

3. Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyānī ti|| ||

 

 

32. Soto

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Sukhindriyaɱ dukkhindriyaɱ somanassindriyaɱ domanassindriyaɱ upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Yato kho bhikkhave ariyasāvako imesam pañcannam indriyānaɱ samudayañca atthagamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathabhūtam pajānāti||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave ariyasāvako sotāpanno avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

[page 208]

 

 

33. Arahā

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Sukhindriyaɱ dukkhindriyaɱ somanassindriyaɱ domanassindriyam upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Yato kho bhikkhave bhikkhu imesam pañcannam indriyānam samudayañca atthagamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtaɱ viditvā anupādā vimutto hoti||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave bhikkhu arahaɱ khīṇāsavo vusitavā katakaraṇīyo ohitabhāro anuppattasadattho parikkhīṇabhavasaŋyojano sammadaññā vimutto ti|| ||

 

 

34. Samaṇabrāhmaṇa 1

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Sukhindriyaɱ ... pe ...upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Ye hi keci bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā imesaɱ pañcannam indriyānaɱ samudayañca atthagamañca assādañca- -yathābhūtam nappajānanti- na ca panete- -viharanti|| ||

4. Ye hi keci- -pajjānanti||
te kho- -sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharantīti|| ||

 

 

35. Samaṇabrāhmaṇa 2

2. {Pañcimāni} bhikkhave indriyāni- -upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

3. ye hi keci bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā sukhindriyaɱ nappajānanti sukhindriyasamudayaɱ nappajānanti||
sukhindriyanirodham nappajānanti||
sukhindriyanirodhagāminipaṭipadaɱ nappajānanti||
... pe ...||
upekhindriyaɱ nappajānanti||
upekhindriyasamudayaɱ nappajānanti||

[page 209]

upekhindriyanirodhagāminipatipadaɱ nappajānanti||
na me te- viharanti|| ||

4. Ye ca keci||
°pajānananti° te ca kho° °sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharantī ti|| ||

 

 

36. Vibhaŋga 1

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Sukhindriyaɱ ... pe ...upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Katamañ ca bhikkhave sukhindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave kāyikaɱ sukhaɱ kāyikaɱ sātaɱ kāyasamphassajaɱ sukhaɱ sātaɱ vedayitaɱ||
idam vuccati bhikkhave sukhindriyaɱ|| ||

4. Katamañ ca bhikkhave dukkhindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave kāyikaɱ dukkhaɱ kāyikam asātaɱ kāyasamphassajaɱ dukkham asātaɱ vedayitaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave dukkhindriyaɱ|| ||

5. Katamañ ca bhikkhave somanassindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhu cetasikaɱ sukhaɱ cetasikaɱ sātam manosamphassajaɱ sukhaɱ sātaɱ vedayitaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave somanassindriyaɱ|| ||

6. Katamañ ca bhikkhave domanassindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave cetasikaɱ dukkhaɱ cetasikaɱ asātam manosamphassajaɱ dukkham asātaɱ vedayitaɱ||
idam vuccati bhikkhave domanassindriyaɱ|| ||

7. Katamañ ca bhikkhave upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave kāyikaɱ vā cetasikaɱ vā neva sātaɱ nāsātaɱ vedayitaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

8. Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyānīti|| ||

 

 

37. Vibhaŋga 2

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Sukhindriyaɱ ... pe ...||
upekhindriyam|| ||

[page 210]

3. Katamañ ca bhikkhave sukhindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave kāyikaɱ sukhaɱ kāyikaɱ sātaɱ kāyasamphassajaɱ sukhaɱ sātaɱ vedayitaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave sukhindriyaɱ|| ||

4.5.6. Katamañ ca bhikkhave dukkhindriyaɱ ... pe ...|| ||

7. Katamañ ca bhikkhave upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave kāyikaɱ vā cetasikaɱ vā neva sātaɱ nāsātaɱ vedayitaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

8. Tatra bhikkhave yaɱ ca sukhindriyaɱ yaɱ ca somanassindriyaɱ sukhā sā vedanā daṭṭhabbā|| ||

Tatra bhikkhave yaɱ ca dukkhindriyam yaɱ ca domanassindriyaɱ dukkhā sā vedanā daṭṭhabbā|| ||

Tatra bhikkhave yadidam upekhindriyam adukkhamasukhā sā vedanā daṭṭhabbā|| ||

9. Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyānīti|| ||

 

 

38. Vibhaŋga 3

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Sukhindriyam ... pe ...upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Katamañ ca bhikkhave sukhindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave kāyikaɱ sukhaɱ kāyikaɱ sātaɱ kāyasamphassajaɱ sukhaɱ sātaɱ vedāyitaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave sukhindriyaɱ|| ||

4. Katamañ ca bhikkhave dukkhindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave kāyikaɱ dukkhaɱ kāyikam asātaɱ kāyasamphassajaɱ dukkham asātaɱ vedayitaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave dukkhindriyaɱ|| ||

5. Katamañ ca bhikkhave somanassindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave cetasikaɱ sukhaɱ cetasikaɱ sātaɱ manosamphassajaɱ sukhaɱ sātaɱ vedayitaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave somanassindriyaɱ|| ||

[page 211]

6. Katamañ ca bhikkhave domanassindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave cetasikaɱ dukkhaɱ cetasikaɱ asātam manosamphassajaɱ dukkham asātaɱ vedayitaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave domanassindriyaɱ|| ||

7. Katamañ ca bhikkhave upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

Yaɱ kho bhikkhave kāyikaɱ vā cetasikaɱ vā neva sātaɱ nāsātaɱ vedayitaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

8. Tatra bhikkhave yaɱ ca sukhindriyaɱ yaɱ ca somanassindriyaɱ sukhā sā vedanā daṭṭhabbā|| ||

Tatra bhikkhave yaɱ ca dukkhindriyaɱ yaɱ ca domanassindriyaɱ dukkhā sā vedanā daṭṭhabbā|| ||

Tatra bhikkhave yadidam upekhindriyaɱ adukkhamasukhā sā vedanā daṭṭhabbā|| ||

9. Iti kho bhikkhave imāni pañcindriyāni pañca hutvā tīni honti||
tīni hutvā pañca honti pariyāyenā ti|| ||

 

 

39. Araṇi

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Sukhindriyaɱ dukkhindriyaɱ somanassindriyaɱ domanassindriyaɱ upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Sukhavedaniyam bhikkhave phassam paṭicca uppajjati sukhindriyaɱ||
so sukhito va samāno Sukhito smīti pajānāti|| ||
tasseva sukhavedaniyassa phassassa nirodhā yaɱ tajjaɱ vedayitaɱ sukhavedaniyam phassam paṭicca Uppannaɱ sukhindriyaɱ taɱ nirujjhati taɱ vūpasammatīti pajānātīti|| ||

4. Dukkhavedaniyam bhikkhave phassam paṭicca uppajjati dukkhindriyam so dukkhito va samāno Dukkhito smīti pajānāti||
tasseva dukkhavedaniyassa phassassa nirodhā yaɱ tajjaɱ vedayitaɱ taɱ dukkhavedaniyam phassam paṭicca Uppannaɱ dukkhindriyaɱ tam nirujjhati taɱ vūpasammatīti pajānāti

[page 212]

5. Somanassavedaniyaɱ bhikkhave phassam paṭicca uppajjati somanassindriyaɱ||
so sumano va samāno Sumano smīti pajānāti||
tasseva somanassa vedaniyassa phassassa nirodhā yaɱ tajjaɱ vedayitaɱ somanassavedaniyaɱ phassam paṭicca Uppannaɱ somanassindriyaɱ taɱ nirujjhati taɱ vūpasammatīti pajānāti|| ||

6. Domanassavedaniyam bhikkhave phassam paṭicca uppajjati domanassindriyaɱ||
so dummano va samāno dummano smīti pajānāti||
tasseva domanassavedaniyassa phassassa nirodhāyaɱ tajjaɱ vedayitam domanassavedaniyam phassam paṭicca Uppannam domanassindriyaɱ taɱ nirujjhati taɱ vūpasammatīti pajānāti|| ||

7. Upekhāvedaniyam bhikkhave phassam paṭicca uppajjati upekhindriyaɱ||
so upekhako va samāno Upekhako smīti pajānāti ||tasseva upekhāvedaniyassa phassassa nirodhā yaɱ tajjaɱ vedayitaɱ upekhāvedaniyam phassa paṭicca uppannam upekhindriyaɱ taɱ nirujjhati taɱ vūpasammatīti pajānāti|| ||

8. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave dvinnam kaṭṭhānaɱ saŋghaṭṭanā samodhānā usmā jāyati||
tejo abhinibbattati||
tesaɱ yeva kaṭṭhānaɱ nānābhāvā nikkhepā yā tajjā usmā sā nirujjhati sā vūpasammati|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave sukhavedaniyam phassam paṭicca uppajjati sukhindriyaɱ||
so sukhito va samāno Sukhito smīti pajānāti||
tasseva sukhavedaniyassa phassassa nirodhā yaɱ tajjaɱ vedayitam sukhavedaniyam phassam paṭicca uppannami sukhindriyaɱ taɱ nirujjhati taɱ vūpasammatīti pajānāti

[page 213]

Dukkavedaniyam bhikkhave phassam paṭicca ... pe ... Somanassavedaniyaɱ||
Domanassavedaniyaɱ||
Upekhāvedaniyam bhikkhave phassam paṭicca uppajjati upekhindriyaɱ||
so upekhako va samāno Upekhako smīti pajānāti||
tasseva upekhāvedaniyassa phassassa nirodhā yaɱ tajjaɱ vedayitam upekhāvedaniyaɱ phassam paṭicca uppannam upekhindriyaɱ||
taɱ nirujjhati taɱ vūpasammatīti pajānātīti|| ||

 

 

40. Uppatika

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Dukkhindriyam domanassindriyam sukhindriyaɱ somanassindriyam upekhindriyaɱ|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpino pahitattassa viharato uppajjati dukkhindriyaɱ||
so evam pajānāti Uppannaɱ kho me idam dukkhindriyaɱ||
taɱ ca kho sanimittaɱ sanidānaɱ sasaŋkhāraɱ sappaccayaɱ||
tañca animittam anidānaɱ asaŋkhāram appaccayaɱ dukkhindriyaɱ uppajjissatīti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati||
so dukkhindriyañ ca pajānāti dukkhindriyasamudayañca pajānāti dukkhindriyanirodhañca pajānāti||
yattha cuppannaɱ dukkhindriyaɱ aparisesam nirujjhati||
tañca pajānāti|| ||

Kattha cuppannaɱ dukkhindriyam aparisesaɱ nirujjhati|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu vivicceva kāmehi vivicca akusalehi dhammehi savitakkaɱ savicāraɱ vivekajaɱ pītisukham pathamam jhānam upasampajja viharati||
ettha cuppannaɱ dukkhindriyam aparisesaɱ nirujjhati|| ||

Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave bhikkhu aññāsi dukkhindriyassa nirodhaɱ tathattāya cittam upasaɱhāsi|| ||

4. Idha pana bhikkhave bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpino pahitattassa viharato uppajjati domanassindriyaɱ||

[page 214]

So evam pajānāti||
Uppannaɱ kho me idaɱ domanassindriyam||
tañca kho sanimittaɱ sanidānam sasaŋkhāraɱ sappaccayaɱ||
taɱ vata animittam anidānam asaŋkhāram appaccayaɱ domanassindriyam uppajjissatīti netaɱ thānaɱ vijjati||
so domanassindriyaɱ ca pajānāti domanassindriyasamudayañca pajānāti||
domanassindriyanirodhaɱ ca pajānāti||
yattha cuppannaɱ domanassindriyam aparisesaɱ nirujjhati tañca pajānāti|| ||

Kattha cuppannaɱ domanassindriyam aparisesaɱ nirujjhati|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu vitakkavicārānaɱ vūpasamā ajjhattaɱ sampasādanaɱ cetaso ekodibhāvam avitakkam avicāraɱ samādhijam pītisukhaɱ dutiyaɱ jhānam upasampajja viharati||
ettha cuppannaɱ domanassindriyaɱ aparisesaɱ nirujjhati|| ||

Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave bhikkhu aññāsi domanassindriyassa nirodhaɱ tathattāya cittam upasaɱhāsi|| ||

5. Idha pana bhikkhave bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpino pahitattassa viharato uppajjati sukhindriyaɱ||
so evam pajānāti||
Uppannaɱ kho me idam sukhindriyaɱ||
taɱ ca kho sanimittam sanidānaɱ sasaŋkhāraɱ sappaccayaɱ||
taɱ ca animittaɱ anidānam asaŋkhāram appaccayaɱ sukhindriyam uppajjissatīti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati||
so sukhindriyaɱ ca pajānāti||
sukhindriyasamudayañca pajānāti||
sukhindriyanirodhañca pajānāti||
yattha cuppannaɱ sukhindriyaɱ aparisesam nirujjhati taɱ ca pajānāti|| ||

Kattha cuppannaɱ sukhindriyam aparisesaɱ nirujjhati|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu pītiyā ca virāgā upekhako ca viharati sato ca sampajāno||
sukhaɱ ca kāyena paṭisaɱvedeti||
yan tam ariyā ācikkhanti upekhako satimā sukhavihārīti||
tatiyaɱ jhānaɱ upasampajja viharati|| ||

Ettha cuppannaɱ sukhindriyam aparisesaɱ nirujjhati|| ||

Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave bhikkhu aññāsi sukhindriyassa nirodhaɱ tathattāya cittam upasaɱhāsi|| ||

[page 215]

6. Idha pana bhikkhave bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpino pahitattassa viharato uppajjati somanassindriyaɱ||
so evam pajānāti||
Uppannaɱ kho me idam somanassindriyaɱ||
taɱ ca kho sanimittaɱ sanidānaɱ sasaŋkhāraɱ sappaccayaɱ||
taɱ ca animittam anidānam asaŋkhāram appaccayaɱ somanassindriyam uppajjissatīti netaɱ ṭhānam vijjati||
so somanassindriyam pajānāti||
somanassindriyasamudayañca pajānāti||
somanassindriyanirodhañ ca pajānāti||
yattha cuppannaɱ somanassindriyam aparisesaɱ nirujjhati tañca pajānāti|| ||

Kattha cuppannam somanassindriyam aparisesaɱ nirujjhati|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sukhassa ca pahānā dukkhassa ca pahānā pubbeva somanassadomanassānam atthagamā adukkhamasukham upekhāsatipārisuddhiɱ catutthaɱ jhānam upasampajja viharati||
ettha cuppannaɱ somanassindriyam aparisesaɱ nirujjhati|| ||

Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave bhikkhu aññāsi somanassindriyassa nirodhaɱ tathattāya cittam upasaɱhāsi|| ||

7. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpino pahitattassa viharato uppajjati upekhindriyam||
so evam pajānāti||
Uppannaɱ kho me idam upekhindriyaɱ||
tañca kho sanimittam sanidānaɱ sasaŋkhāraɱ sappaccayaɱ||
tañca kho animittam anidānam asaŋkhāram appaccayam upekhindriyam uppajjissatīti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati||
so upekhindriyaɱ ca pajānāti upekhindriyasamudayañca pajānāti||
upekhindriyanirodhañca pajānāti||
yattha cuppannam upekhindriyam aparisesam nirujjhati tañca pajānāti|| ||

Kattha cuppannam upekhindriyam aparisesaɱ nirujjhati|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu sabbaso nevasaññānāsaññāyatanaɱ samatikkamma saññāvedayitanirodham upasampajja viharati||
ettha cuppannam upekhindriyam aparisesam nirujjhati|| ||

Āhaɱ vuccati bhikkhave bhikkhu aññāsi upekhindriyassa nirodhaɱ tathattāya cittam upasaɱhāsīti

[page 216]

Sukhindriyavaggo catuttho

Tassa uddānaɱ:|| ||

Suddhikañca Soto Arahaɱ||
Dve Samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca||
Vibhaŋgena tayo vuttā||
Araṇi Uppaṭikena cā ti|| ||

 

 

Jarā Vaggo

41. Jarā

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekam samayam Bhagavā Sāvatthivaɱ viharati Pubbārāme Migāramātupāsāde|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Bhagavā sāyaṇhasamayam paṭisallāṇā vuṭṭhito pacchātape nisinno hoti piṭṭhim otāpayamāno|| ||

3. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā Bhagavato gattāni pāṇinā anomajjanto Bhagavantam etad avoca||
Acchariyam bhante abbhutam bhante na ceva dāni bhante Bhagavato tāva parisuddho chavivaṇṇo pariyodāto sithilāni ca gattāni sabbāni baliyajātāni purato pabbhāro ca kāyo dissati ca indriyānam aññathattaɱ cakkhundriyassa sotindriyassa ghānindriyassa jivhindriyassa kāyindriyassā ti|| ||

[page 217]

4. Evaɱ hetam Ānanda hoti jarādhammo yobbaññe vyādhidhammo ārogye maraṇadhammo jīvite na ceva tāva parisuddho hoti chavivaṇṇo pariyodāto sithilāni ca honti gattāni sabbāni baliyajātāni purato pabbhāro ca kāyo||
dissati ca indriyānam aññathattaɱ cakkhundriyassa sotindriyassa ghānindriyassa ... pe ...kāyindriyassā ti|| ||

5. Idam avoca Bhagavā||
idaɱ vatvā ca sugato athāparam etad avoca satthā|| ||

Dhītaɱ jammī jare atthu||
dubbaṇṇakaraṇī jare||
tāva manoramaɱ vimbaɱ||
jarāya abhimadditaɱ|| ||

Yo pi vassasataɱ jīve||
so pi maccuparāyaṇo||
na kiñci parivajjeti||
sabbam evābhimaddatī ti|| ||

 

 

42. Uṇṇābho brāhmaṇo

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Atha kho Uṇṇābho brāhmaṇo yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodi||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi||
eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Uṇṇābho brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Pañcimāni bho Gotama indriyāni nānāvisayāni nānāgocarāni na aññam aññassa gocaravisayam paccanubhonti|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Cakkhundriyaɱ sotindriyaɱ ... pe ...||
kāyindriyaɱ

[page 218]

Imesaɱ nu kho bho Gotama pañcannam indriyānaɱ nānāvisayānaɱ nānāgocarānaɱ na aññamaññassa gocaravisayam paccanubhontānam kim patisaraṇam ko ca nesaɱ gocaravisayam paccanubhotī ti|| ||

4. Pañcimāni brāhmaṇa indriyāni nānāvisayāni nānāgocarāni na aññamaññassa gocaravisayaɱ paccanubhonti|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Cakkhundriyaɱ ... pe ...kāyindriyaɱ|| ||

Imesaɱ kho brāhmaṇa pañcannam indriyānam nānāvisayānaɱ nānāgocarānaɱ na aññamaññassa gocaravisayam paccanubhontānam mano paṭisaraṇam mano ca nesaɱ gocaravisayam paccanubhotī ti|| ||

5. Manassa pana bho Gotama kim paṭisaraṇanti|| ||

Manassa kho brāhmaṇa sati paṭisaraṇanti|| ||

6. Satiyā pana bho Gotama kim paṭisaraṇanti|| ||

Satiyā pana kho brāhmaṇa vimutti paṭisaraṇanti|| ||

7. Vimuttiyā pana bho Gotama kim paṭisaraṇanti|| ||

Vimuttiyā kho brāhmaṇa nibbānam paṭisaraṇanti|| ||

8. Nibbānassa pana bho Gotama kim paṭisaraṇanti|| ||

Ajjhaparam brāhmaṇa pañhaɱ nāsakkhi pañhassa pariyantaɱ gahetuɱ||
nibbānogadam hi brāhmaṇa brahmacariyaɱ vussati nibbānaparāyanaɱ nibbānapariyosānanti|| ||

9. Atha kho Uṇṇābho brāhmaṇo Bhagavato bhāsitam abhinanditvā anumoditvā uṭṭhāyāsanā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaɱ katvā pakkāmi|| ||

10. Atha kho Bhagavā acirapakkante Uṇṇābhe brāhmaṇe bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

11. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave kuṭāgāre vā kuṭāgārasālāyaɱ vā pācīnavātapānā suriye uggacchante vātapānena rasmiyo pavisitvā kāya patiṭṭhitā ti|| ||

Pacchimāyam bhante bhittiyanti|| ||

[page 219]

12. Evam eva kho bhikkhave Uṇṇābhassa brāhmaṇassa Tathāgate saddhā niviṭṭhā mūlajātā patiṭṭhitā daḷhā asaɱhāriyā sāmaṇena vā brāhmaṇena vā devena vā Mārena vā Brahmunā vā kenaci vā lokasmiɱ|| ||

Imamhi ce bhikkhave samaye Uṇṇābho brāhmaṇo kālaɱ kareyya natthi taɱ saŋyojanaɱ yena saŋyojanena saɱyutto Uṇṇābho brāhmaṇo puna imaɱ lokam āgaccheyyāti|| ||

 

 

43. Sāketo

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sākete viharati Añjanavane Migadāye|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi||
Atthi nu kho bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma yāni pañcindriyāni tāni pañcabalāni honti||
yāni pañcabalāni tāni pañcindriyāni hontī ti|| ||

Bhagavaɱmūlakā no bhante dhammā ... pe ...|| ||

3. Atthi bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma yāni pañcindriyāni tāni pañcabalāni honti||
yāni pañcabalāni tāni pañcindriyāni honti|| ||

Katamo ca bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma yāni pañcindriyāni tāni pañcabalāni honti||
yāni pañcabalāni tāni pañcindriyāni honti|| ||

4. Yam bhikkhave saddhindriyam taɱ saddhābalaɱ||
yaɱ saddhābalaɱ taɱ saddhindriyaɱ|| ||

Yam viriyindriyaɱ taɱ viriyabalaɱ||
yaɱ viriyabalaɱ taɱ viriyindriyaɱ||
... pe ...||
Yam paññindriyam taɱ paññābalaɱ||
yam paññābalaɱ tam paññindriyaɱ|| ||

5. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave nadī pācīnaninnā pācīnapoṇā pācīnapabbharā||
tassā majjhe dīpo||
Atthi bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma tassā nadiyā eko soto tv eva saŋkhyaɱ gacchati|| ||

Atthi pana bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma tassā nadiyā dve sotāni tv eva {saŋkhyaɱ} gacchanti|| ||

[page 220]

6. Katamo ca bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma tassā nadiyā eko soto tv eva saŋkhyaɱ gacchati|| ||

Yaɱ ca bhikkhave tassa dīpassa puratthimante udakaɱ yaɱ ca pacchimante udakaɱ|| ||

Ayaɱ kho bhikkhave||
... pe ...||
gacchati|| ||

7. Katamo ca bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma tassā nadiyā dve sotāni tv eva saŋkhyaɱ gacchanti||
yaɱ ca bhikkhave tassa dīpassa uttarante udakaɱ yañca dakkhiṇante udakaɱ|| ||

Ayaɱ kho bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma tassā nadiyā dve sotāni tv eva saŋkhyaɱ gacchanti|| ||

8. Evam eva kho bhikkhave||
yaɱ saddhindriyaɱ taɱ saddhābalaɱ||
yaɱ saddhābalaɱ taɱ saddhindriyaɱ||
... pe ...||
yam paññindriyaɱ tam paññābalaɱ||
yam paññābalaɱ tam paññindriyaɱ|| ||

9. Pañcannam bhikkhave indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā bhikkhu āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim paññāvimuttiɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharatī ti|| ||

 

 

44. Pubbakoṭṭhako

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Pubbakoṭṭhake|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā āyasmantam Sāriputtam āmantesi|| ||

3. Saddahāsi tvaɱ Sāriputta||
Saddhindriyam bhāvitaɱ bahulīkatam amatogadhaɱ hoti amataparāyanaɱ amatapariyosānaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyam bhāvitam bahulīkatam amatogadhaɱ hoti amataparāyanam amatapariyosānanti|| ||

[page 221]

4. Na khvāham ettha bhante Bhagavato saddhāya gacchāmi saddhindriyam ||... pe ...
paññindriyam bhāvitaɱ bahulīkatam amatogadham hoti||
amataparāyanam amatapariyosānaɱ|| ||

Yesaɱ hi tam bhante aññātam assa adiṭṭham aviditam asacchikatam aphusitam paññaya te tattha paresam saddhāya gaccheyyuɱ||
Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyam bhavitam bahulīkatam amatogadhaɱ hoti amataparāyanam amatapariyosānaɱ|| ||

Yesañca kho etam bhante ñātaɱ diṭṭhaɱ viditaɱ sacchikatam phusitam paññāya nikkaŋkhā te tattha nibbicikiccā Saddhindriyaɱ||
... pe ...||
paññindriyam bhāvitam bahulīkatam amatogadham hoti amataparāyanam amatapariyosānaɱ|| ||

Mayhañca kho etam bhante ñātaɱ diṭṭhaɱ viditaɱ sacchikatam phusitam paññāya nikkaŋkhāham tattha paresaɱ nibbicikiccho||
Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ bhāvitam bahulīkatam amatogadhaɱ hoti amataparāyanam amatapariyosānan ti|| ||

5. Sādhu sādhu Sāriputta||
Yesaɱ hi taɱ Sāriputta aññātam assa adiṭṭham aviditam asacchikatam aphussitam paññāya te tattha paresaɱ saddhāya gaccheyyuɱ||
Saddhindriyam bhāvitam bahulīkatam amatogadhaɱ hoti amataparāyanam amatapariyosānaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyam bhāvitam bahulīkatam amatogadhaɱ hoti amataparāyanam amatapariyosānaɱ||
Yesaɱ ca kho etaɱ Sāriputta ñataɱ diṭṭhaɱ viditaɱ sacchikatam phusitam paññāya nikkaŋkhā te tattha nibbicikicchā Saddhindriyam bhāvitam bahulīkatam amatogadhaɱ hoti amataparayānam amatapariyosānaɱ

[page 222]

... pe ...paññindriyam bhāvitam bahulīkatam amatogadhaɱ hoti amatapariyosānan ti|| ||

 

 

45. Pubbārāma 1

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Pubbārāme Migāramātupāsāde|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Katinnaɱ nu kho bhikkhave indriyānam bhavitattā bahulīkatattā khīnāsavo bhikkhu aññaɱ vyākaroti|| ||

Khīṇā jāti vusitam brahmacariyaɱ kataɱ karaṇīyaɱ nāparam itthattāyā ti pajānāmī ti|| ||

Bhagavaɱmūlakā no bhante dhammā||
... pe ...|| ||

3. Ekassa kho bhikkhave indriyassa bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā khīṇāsavo bhikkhu aññaɱ vyākaroti||
Khīnājāti-nāparam itthattāyā ti pajānāmī ti|| ||

Katamassa ekassa indriyassa|| ||

4. Paññāvato bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa tadanvayā saddhā saṇṭhāti||
tadanvayaɱ viriyaɱ saṇṭhāti||
tadanvayā sati saṇṭhāti||
tadanvayo samādhi saṇṭhāti|| ||

5. Imassa kho bhikkhave ekassa indriyassa bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā khīnāsavo bhikkhu aññaɱ vyākaroti|| ||

Khīnā jāti vusitam brahmacariyaɱ kataɱ karaṇīyaɱ nāparam itthattāyāti pajānāmī ti|| ||

 

 

46. Pubbārāma 2

1. Taɱ yeva nidānam|| ||

2. Katinnaɱ nu kho bhikkhave indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulikatattā khīnāsavo bhikkhu aññam vyākaroti||
Khīnā jāti nāparam itthattāyāti pajānāmī ti|| ||

Bhagavaɱmūlakā no bhante dhammā||
... pe ...|| ||

[page 223]

3. Dvinnaɱ kho bhikkhave indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā khīṇāsavo bhikkhu aññaɱ vyākaroti||
Khīṇājāti-nāparam itthattāyati pajānāmīti||
katamesaɱ dvinnaɱ|| ||

4. Ariyāya ca paññāya ariyāya ca vimuttiyā|| ||

Yā hissa bhikkhave ariyā paññā tad assa pāññindriyaɱ||
yā hissa bhikkhave ariyā vimutti tad assa samādhindriyaɱ|| ||

5. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave dvinnam indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā khīnāsavo bhikkhu aññaɱ vyākaroti||
Khīṇā jāti° °nāparam itthattāyāti pajānāmī ti|| ||

 

 

47. Pubbārāma 3

1. Tam eva nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Katinnam nu kho bhikkhave indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā khīṇāsavo bhikkhu aññaɱ vyākaroti||
Khīṇā jāti° °nāparam itthattāyā ti pajānāmī ti|| ||

Bhagavaɱmūlakā no bhante dhammā||
... pe ...|| ||

3. Catunnaɱ kho bhikkhave indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā khīṇāsavo bhikkhu aññaɱ vyakaroti||
Khīnā jāti° °nāparam itthattāyāti pajānāmīti|| ||

Katamesaɱ catunnaɱ?|| ||

4. Viriyindriyassa satindriyassa samādhindriyassa paññindriyassa|| ||

5. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā khīṇāsavo bhikkhu aññaɱ vyākaroti||
Khīnā jāti° °nāparam itthattāyā ti pajānāmī ti|| ||

 

 

48. Pubbārāma 4

1. Taɱ yeva nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Katinnaɱ kho bhikkhave indriyānam bhāvitattā- onāparam itthattāyāti pajānāmīti|| ||

Bhagavaɱmūlakā no bhante dhammā||
... pe ...|| ||

3. Pañcannaɱ kho bhikkhave indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā khīnāsavo bhikkhu aññaɱ vyākaroti||
Khīṇā jāti° °nāparam itthattāyāti pajānāmī ti|| ||

Katamesam pañcannaɱ/|| ||

[page 224]

4. Saddhindriyassa viriyindriyassa satindriyassa samādhindriyassa paññindriyassa|| ||

5. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā khīnāsavo bhikkhu aññaɱ vyākaroti||
Khīṇā jāti vusitam brahmacariyaɱ kataɱ karaṇīyaɱ nāparam itthattāyāti pajānāmī ti|| ||

 

 

49. Piṇḍolo

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Kosambīyaɱ viharati Ghositārāme|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmatā Piṇḍolabharadvājena aññā vyākatā hoti||
Khīṇā jāti vusitam brahmacariyaɱ kataɱ karaṇīyaɱ nāparam itthattāyāti pajānāmī ti|| ||

3. Atha kho sambahulā bhikkhū yena Bhagavā tenupa.||
saŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu||
eka-m-antaɱ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū Bhagavantam etad avocuɱ|| ||

Āyasmatā bhante Piṇḍolabhāradvājena aññā vyākatā Khīnā jāti° °nāparam itthattāyāti pajānāmītī|| ||

Kiɱ nu kho bhante atthavasaɱ sampassamānena āyasmatā Piṇḍolabhāradvājena aññā vyākatā Khīṇā jāti° °nāparam itthattāyāti pajānāmī ti|| ||

4. Tiṇṇannam kho pana bhikkhave indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā Piṇḍolabhāradvājena bhikkhunā aññā vyākatā Khīṇā jāti° °nāparam itthattāyāti pajānāmī ti|| ||

Katamesaɱ tiṇṇānaɱ?|| ||

5. Satindriyassa samādhindriyassa paññindriyassa|| ||

6. Imesaɱ kho bhante tiṇṇannam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā Piṇḍolabhāradvājena bhikkhunā aññā vyākatā||
Khīnā jāti° °nāparam itthattāyā ti pajānāmī ti|| ||

7. Imāni ca bhikkhave tīṇi indriyāni|| ||

Kiɱnantāni||
khayantāni|| ||

Kissa khayantāni||
jātijarāmaraṇassa|| ||

Jātijarāmaraṇaɱ khayan ti kho bhikkhave sampassamānena Piṇḍolabhāradvājena bhikkhunā aññā vyākatā

[page 225]

Khīṇā jāti vusitam brahmacariyaɱ kataɱ karāṇīyaɱ||
nāparam itthattāyā ti pajānāmī ti|| ||

 

 

50. Saddha or Āpaṇa

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Aŋgesu viharati Āpanaɱ nāma Aŋgānaɱ nigamo|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā āyasmantam Sāriputtam āmantesi|| ||

Yo so Sāriputta ariyasāvako Tathāgate ekantagato abhippasanno||
api nu so Tathāgate vā Tathāgatasāsane vā khaŋkheyya vā vicikiccheyya vā ti|| ||

3. Yoso bhante ariyasāvako Tathāgate ekantagato abhippasanno||
na so Tathāgate vā Tathāgatasāsane vā kaŋkheyya vā vicikiccheyya vā|| ||

Saddhassa hi bhante ariyasāvakassa etam pāṭikaŋkhaɱ||
yam āraddhaviriyo viharissati akusalānaɱ dhammānam pahānāya kusalānaɱ dhammānam upasampadāya thāmavā daḷhaparakkamo anikkhittadhuro kusalesu dhammesu|| ||

4. Yaɱ hissa bhante viriyaɱ tad assa viriyindriyam|| ||

Saddhassa hi bhante ariyasāvakassa āraddhaviriyassa etam pāṭikaŋkhaɱ||
yaɱ satimā bhavissati paramena satinepakkena samannāgato cirakatam pi cirabhāsitam pi saritā anussaritā|| ||

5. Yā hissa bhante sati tad assa satindriyaɱ|| ||

Saddhassa hi bhante ariyasāvakassa āraddhaviriyassa upaṭṭhitasatino etam pātikaŋkhaɱ||
yaɱ vossaggārammaṇaɱ karitvā labhissati samādhim labhissati cittassa ekaggataɱ|| ||

6. Yo hissa bhante samādhi tad assa samādhindriyaɱ|| ||

Saddhassa hi bhante ariyasāvakassa upaṭṭhitasatino samāhitacittassa etam pāṭikaŋkhaɱ

[page 226]

yam evam pajānissati Anamataggo kho saɱsāro pubbā koṭi na paññāyati||
avijjānīvaraṇānaɱ sattānaɱ taṇhāsaŋyojanānaɱ sandhāvatam saɱsarataɱ avijjāya tv eva tamokāyassa asesavirāganirodho santam etam padam phanitam etam padam yad idaɱ sabbasaŋkhārasamatho sabbupadhipaṭinissaggo taṇhakkhayo virāgo nirodho nibbānaɱ|| ||

7. Yā hissa bhante paññā tad assa paññindriyaɱ||
Saddho so bhante ariyasāvako evam padahitvā padahitvā evaɱ saritvā saritvā evaɱ samādahitvā samādahitvā evam pajānitvā pajānitvā evam abhisaddahati||
Ime kho te dhammā ye me pubbe sutavā ahesuɱ||
te dānāham etarahi kāyena ca phusitvā viharāmi||
paññāyaca ativijjha passāmīti|| ||

8. Yā hissa bhante saddhā tad assa saddhindriyan ti|| ||

9. Sādhu sādhu Sāriputta|| ||

Yo so Sāriputta ariyasāvako Tathāgate ekantagato abhippasanno na so Tathāgate vā Tathāgatasāsane vā kaŋkheyya vā vicikiccheyya vā|| ||

Saddhassa hi Sāriputta ariyasāvakassa etam pātikaŋkhaɱ||
yaɱ āraddhaviriyo viharissati akusalānaɱ dhammānam pahānāya kusalānam dhammānam upasampadāya thāmavā daḷhaparakkamo anikkhittadhuro kusalesu dhammesu|| ||

10—13. Yaɱ hissa Sāriputta viriyam tad assa viriyindriyaɱ|| ||

Saddhassa hi Sāriputta ariyasāvakassa ... pe ...||
Saddho so Sāriputta ariyasāvako evam padahitvā padahitvā evam saritvā saritvā evaɱ samādahitvā samādahitvā evam pajānitvā pajānitvā evam abhisaddahati|| ||

Ime kho te dhammā ye me pubbe sutavā ahesuɱ||
te dānāham etarahi kāyena ca phusitvā viharāmi paññāya ca ativijjha passāmī ti

[page 227]

14. Yā hissa Sāriputta saddhā tad assa saddhindriyanti|| ||

Jarāvaggo pañcamo

Tassa uddānaɱ:|| ||

Jarā Uṇṇābho brāhmaṇo||
Sāketo Pubbakoṭṭhako||
Pubbārāme ca cattāri||
Piṇḍolo Saddhena te dasāti|| ||

 

 

Chapter VI. Vaggo Chaṭṭho

51. Sālam

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekam samayam Bhagavā Kosalesu viharati sālāyaɱ brāhmaṇagāme|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi||
pe [pa]|| ||

3. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci tiracchānagatā pāṇā sīho migarājā tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idaɱ thāmena javena sūrena||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ye keci bodhapakkhiyā dhammā paññindriyaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam bodhāya|| ||

Katame ca bhikkhave bodhipakkhiyā dhammā|| ||

4. Saddhiyindriyam bhikkhave bodhapakkhiyo dhammo tam bodhāya saɱvattati||
Viriyindriyam bodhapakkhiyo dhammo tam bodhāya saɱvattati|| ||

Satindriyam bodhapakkhiyo dhammo tam bodhāya saɱvattati||
Samādhindriyam bodhapakkhiyo dhammo tam bodhāya saɱvattati|| ||

Paññindriyam bodhapakkhiyo dhammo tam bodhāya saɱvattati|| ||

[page 228]

5. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci tiracchānagatā pāṇā sīho migarājā tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idaɱ thāmena javena sūrena||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ye keci bodhapakkhiyā dhammā paññindriyaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam bodhāyāti|| ||

 

 

52. Mallikam

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Mallikesu viharati Uruvelakappaɱ nāma Mallikānaɱ nigamo|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

3. Yāva kīvañca bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa ariyañāṇaɱ na uppannaɱ hoti||
neva tāva catunnam indriyānam saṇṭhiti hoti||
neva tāva catunnam indriyānaɱ avaṭṭhiti hoti|| ||

Yato ca kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa ariyañāṇaɱ uppannaɱ hoti||
atha catunnam indriyānaɱ saṇṭhiti hoti||
atha catunnam indriyānam avaṭṭhiti hoti|| ||

4. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave yāva kīvañca kūṭāgārassa kūṭam na ussitaɱ hoti||
neva tāva gopānasīnaɱ saṇṭhiti hoti||
neva tāva gopānasīnam avaṭṭhiti hoti|| ||

Yato ca kho bhikkhave kūṭāgārassa kūṭam ussitaɱ hoti||
atha kho gopānasīnam saṇṭhiti hoti||
atha kho gopānasīnam avaṭṭhiti hoti|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave yāva kīvañca ariyasāvakassa ariyaññāṇaɱ na uppannaɱ hoti||
neva tāva catunnam indriyānaɱ saṇṭhiti hoti||
neva tāva catunnam indriyānam avaṭṭhiti hoti|| ||

Yato ca kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa ariyañānam uppannaɱ hoti||
atha catunnam indriyānam ... pe ...avaṭṭhiti hoti|| ||

Katamesaɱ catunnaɱ?||

[page 229]

Saddhindriyassa viriyindriyassa satindriyassa samādhindriyassa|| ||

5. Paññāvato bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa tadanvayā saddhā saṇṭhāti||
tadanvayaɱ viriyaɱ saṇṭhāti||
tadanvayā sati saṇṭhāti||
tadanvayo samādhi saṇṭhātīti|| ||

 

 

53. Sekho

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekam samayam Bhagavā Kosambīyaɱ viharati Ghositārāme|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Atthi nu kho bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma sekho bhikkhu sekhabhūmiyaɱ ṭhito Sekhosmī ti pajāneyya||
asekho bhikkhu asekhabhūmiyaɱ ṭhito Asekhosmīti pajāneyyāti|| ||

Bhagavaɱmūlakā no bhante dhammā||
... pe ...|| ||

3. Atthi bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma sekho bhikkhu sekhabhūmiyaɱ ṭhito Sekhosmīti pajāneyya||
asekho bhikkhu asekhabhūmiyaɱ ṭhito Asekhosmīti pajāneyya|| ||

4. Katamo ca bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma sekho bhikkhu sekhabhūmiyaɱ ṭhito Sekho smīti pajānāti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave sekho bhikkhu Idaɱ dukkhan ti yathābhūtam pajānāti||
Ayam dukkhasamudayo ti ya° pa°||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodho ti ya° pa°||
Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti ya° pa°|| ||

Ayam pi kho bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma sekho bhikkhu sekhabhumiyaɱ ṭhito Sekhosmīti pajānāti|| ||

5. Puna ca param bhikkhave sekho bhikkhu iti paṭisañcikkhati|| ||

Atthi nu kho ito bahiddhā añño samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā yo evam bhūtaɱ tacchaɱ tathā dhammaɱ deseti yathā Bhagavā ti

[page 230]

so evam pajānāti||
Natthi kho ito bahiddhā añño samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā yo evam bhūtam taccham tathā dhammam deseti yathā Bhagavā ti|| ||

Ayam pi kho bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma sekho bhikkhu sekhabhūmiyaɱ ṭhito Sekhosmī ti pajānāti|| ||

6. Puna ca param bhikkhave sekho bhikkhu pañcindriyāni pajānāti||
saddhindriyam||
viriyo||
sati-||
samādhi-||
paññindriyam||
yaɱ gatikāni yam paramāni yam phalāni yam pariyosanāni na heva kho kāyena phusitvā viharati paññāya ca ativijjha passati|| ||

Ayam pi kho bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma sekho bhikkhu sekhabhūmiyaɱ ṭhito Sekhosmī ti pajānāti|| ||

7. Katamo ca bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma asekho bhikkhu asekhabhūmiyaɱ ṭhito Asekhosmīti pajānāti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave asekho bhikkhu pañcindriyāni pajānāti||
saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ...paññindriyaɱ||
yaŋgatikāni yamparamāni yamphalāni yampariyosanāni||
Kāyena ca phusitvā viharati paññāya ca ativijjha passati|| ||

Ayam pi kho bhikkhave pariyāyo yam pariyāyam āgamma asekho bhikkhu asekhabhūmiyaɱ ṭhito Asekho smīti pajānāti|| ||

8. Puna ca param bhikkhave asekho bhikkhu cha indriyāni pajānāti||
cakkhundriyaɱ sotindriyaɱ ghānindriyaɱ jivhindriyam kāyindriyam manindiyaɱ||
imāni kho cha indriyāni sabbena sabbam sabbathā sabbam aparisesā nirujjhissanti||
aññāni ca cha indriyāni na kuhiñci kismiñci uppajjissantī ti pajānāti|| ||

Ayam pi kho bhikkhave pariyāyo||
yam pariyāyam āgamma asekho bhikkhu asekhabhūmiyaɱ ṭhito Asekhosmī ti pajānātī ti|| ||

[page 231]

 

 

54. Pade

2. Seyyathāpī bhikkhave yāni kānici jaŋgalānam pāṇānam padajatāni sabbāni tāni hatthipade samodhānaɱ gacchanti||
hatthipadaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam mahantattena||
evam eva kho bhikkhave yāni kānici padāni bodhāya saɱvattanti paññindriyaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yadidam bodhāya|| ||

3. Katamāni ca bhikkhave padāya bodhāya saɱvattanti|| ||

Saddhindriyam bhikkhave padaɱ tam bodhāya saɱvattati||
viriyindriyam-||
satindriyaɱ-||
samādhindriyaɱ-||
paññindriyam padaɱ tam bodhaya {saɱvattati}|| ||

4. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave yāni kānici jaŋgalānam pāṇānam padajatāni sabbāni tāni hatthipade samodhānam gacchanti||
hatthipadaɱ tesam aggam akkhayati yad idam mahantattena||
evam eva kho bhikkhave yāni kānici pādāni bodhāya saɱvattanti||
paññindriyam padaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam bodhāyā ti|| ||

 

 

55. Sāre

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci sāragandhā lohitacandanaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ye keci bodhapakkhiyā dhammā paññindriyaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam bodhāyā ti|| ||

3. Katame ca bhikkhave bodhapakkhiyā dhammā|| ||

Saddhindriyam bhikkhave bodhipakkhiyo dhammo tam bodhāya saɱvattati ... pe ...paññindriyaɱ bodhipakkhiyo dhammo tam bodhāya saɱvattati|| ||

4. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci sāragandhā lohitacandanamo -paññindriyaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam bodhāyā ti|| ||

[page 232]

 

 

56. Patiṭṭhito

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Ekadhamme patiṭṭhitassa bhikkhave bhikkhuno pañcindriyāni bhāvitāni honti subhāvitāni|| ||

Katamasmim ekadhamme||
Appamāde|| ||

3. Katamo ca bhikkhave appamādo|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu cittaɱ rakkhati āsavesu ca sāsavesu ca dhammesu||
tassa cittaɱ rakkhato āsavesu ca sāsavesu ca dhammesu saddhindriyam pi bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati... pe ...||
paññindriyam pi bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati|| ||

4. Evam kho bhikkhave ekadhamme patiṭṭhitassa bhikkhuno pañcindriyāni bhāvitāni honti subhāvitānī ti|| ||

 

 

57. Brahmā

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Uruvelāyaɱ viharati najjā Nerañjarāya tīre Ajapālanigrodhe pathamābhisambuddho|| ||

2. Atha kho Bhagavato rahogatassa patisallīnassa evam cetaso parivitakko udapādi||
Pañcindriyāni bhāvitāni bahulīkatāni amatogadhāni honti amataparāyanāni amatapariyosānāni||
Katamāni pañca||
saddhindriyam bhāvitam bahulīkatam amatogadhaɱ hoti amataparāyanam amatapariyosānaɱ||
viriyindriyaɱ||
satindriyaɱ||
samādhindriyam||
paññindriyam bhāvitam bahulīkatam amatogadhaɱ hoti amataparāyanam amatapariyosānam||
imani pañcindriyāni bhāvitāni bahulīkatāni amatogadhāni honti amataparāyanāni amatapariyosānānī ti|| ||

3. Atha kho Brahmā sahampati Bhagavato cetasā cetoparivitakkam aññāya seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaɱ vā bāham pasāreyya pasāritaɱ vā bāhaɱ sammiñjeyya||
evam eva Brahmaloke antarahito Bhagavato purato pātur ahosi|| ||

[page 233]

4. Atha kho Brahmā sahampati ekaɱsam uttarāsaŋgaɱ karitvā yena Bhagavā tenāñjalim paṇāmetvā Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Evam etam Bhagavā evam etaɱ Sugata pañcindriyāni bhāvitāni bahulīkatāni amatogadhāni honti amataparāyanāni amatapariyosānāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyam bhāvitam bahulīkatam amatogadhaɱ hoti amataparāyanam amatapariyosānaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyam bhāvitamo -amatapariyosānaɱ|| ||

Imāni pañcindriyāni bhāvitāni bahulīkatāni amatogadhāni honti amataparāyanāni amatapariyosānāni|| ||

5. Bhūtapubbāham bhante Kassape {sammāsambuddhe} brahmacariyam acariɱ|| ||

Tatra pi mam evaɱ jānanti Sahako bhikkhu sahako bhikkhūti||
so khvāham bhante imesaɱ yeva pañcannam indriyānam bhavitattā bahulīkatattā kāmesu kāmacchandam virājetvā kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā sugatim brahmalokam upapanno||
tatra pi mam evaɱ jānanti Brahmā sahampati Brahmāsahampatī ti|| ||

6. Evam etam Bhagavā evam etaɱ Sugata aham etaɱ jānāmi aham etam passāmi yathā imāni pañcindriyāni bhāvitāni bahulīkatāni amatogadhāni honti amataparāyanāni amatapariyosanānī ti|| ||

 

 

58. Sūkarakhatā

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Gijjhakūṭe pabbate Sūkarakhatāyaɱ|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā āyasmantaɱ Sāriputtam āmantesi||
kiɱ nu kho Sāriputta atthavasaɱ sampassamāno khīṇāsavo bhikkhu Tathāgate vā Tathāgatasāsane vā paramanipaccākāraɱ pavattamāno pavatteti|| ||

[page 234]

Anuttaraɱ hi bhante yogakkhemaɱ sampassamāno khīṇāsavo bhikkhu Tathāgate vā Tathāgatasāsane vā paramanipaccākāram pavattamāno pavattetī ti|| ||

3. Sādhu sādhu Sāriputta anuttaraɱ hi Sāriputta yoyakkhemam sampassamāno khīṇāsavo bhikkhu Tathāgate vā Tathāgatasāsane vā paramanipaccākāram pavattamāno pavattetī ti|| ||

4. Katamo ca Sāriputta anuttaro yogakkhemo yaɱ sampassamāno khīṇāsavo bhikkhu Tathāgate vā Tathāgatasāsane vā paramanipaccākāram pavattamāno pavattetī ti|| ||

5. Idha bhante khīṇāsavo bhikkhu saddhindriyam bhāveti upasamagāmiɱ sambodhagāmim||
viriyindriyam||
satindriyaɱ||
samādhindriyam||
paññindriyam bhāveti upasamagāmiɱ sambodhagāmiɱ|| ||

Ayaɱ kho bhante anuttaro yogakkhemo yaɱ sampassamāno khīṇāsavo bhikkhu Tathāgate vā Tathāgatasāsane vā paramanipaccākāram pavattamāno pavattetī ti|| ||

6. Sādhu sādhu Sāriputta||
eso hi Sāriputta anuttaro yogakkhemo yam sampassamāno khīnāsavo bhikkhu Tathāgate vā Tathāgatasāsane vā paramanipaccākāram pavattamāno pavatteti|| ||

7. Katamo ca Sāriputta paramanipaccākāro yaɱ khīṇāsavo bhikkhu Tathāgate vā Tathāgatasāsane vā paramanipaccākāram pavattamāno pavattetī ti|| ||

8. Idha bhante khīṇāsavo bhikkhu satthari sagāravo viharati sappatisso||
dhamme sagāravo viharati sappatisso||
saŋghe-||
sikkhāya-||
samādhismiɱ sagāravo viharati sappatisso|| ||

Ayaɱ kho bhante paramanipaccākāro yaɱ khīṇāsavo bhikkhu Tathāgate vā Tathāgatasāsane vā paramanipaccākāram pavattamāno pavattetī ti|| ||

[page 235]

9. Sādhu sādhu Sāriputta||
eso hi Sāriputta paramanipaccākāro yaɱ khīṇāsavo bhikkhu Tathāgate vā Tathāgatasāsane vā paramanipaccākāram pavattamāno pavattetī ti|| ||

 

 

59. Uppāde 1

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni bhāvitāni bahulīkatāni anuppannāni uppajjanti nāññatra Tathāgatassa pātubhāvā arahato sammāsambuddhassa|| ||

3. Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ viriyindriyaɱ satindriyaɱ samādhindriyam paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyani bhāvitāni bahulīkatāni anuppannāni uppajjanti nāññatra Tathāgatassa pātubhāvā arahato sammāsambuddhassāti|| ||

 

 

60. Uppāde 2

Tatravoca|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ viriyindriyaɱ satindriyaɱ. samādhindriyam paññindriyam|| ||

Chapter VII. Bodhipakkhiya Vaggo

61. Saɱyojana

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni bhāvitāni bahulīkatāni saŋyojanānam pahānāya {saɱvattanti}|| ||

 

 

62. Anusaya

2. °anusayasamugghātāya saɱvattanti|| ||

 

 

63. Pariññā or Addhāna

2. °addhānapariññaya {saɱvattanti}|| ||

 

 

64. Āsavakkhaya

2. °āsavānaɱ khayāya {saɱvattanti}|| ||

3. Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyāni bhāvitāni bahulīkatāni saŋyojanānam pahānāya saɱvattanti anusayasamugghātāya saɱvattanti||
addhānapariññāya saɱvattantī ti||
āsavānaɱ khayāya saɱvattanti|| ||

 

 

65. Dve phalā

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyāni|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā dvinnam phalānam aññataram phalam pāṭikaŋkham diṭṭheva dhamme aññā sati vā upādisese anāgāmitā ti|| ||

[page 237]

 

 

66. Sattānisaɱsā

2. Pañcimani bhikkhave indriyāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Saddhindriyam ... pe ... paññindriyaɱ|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcindriyāni|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā satta phalā sattānisaɱsā patikaŋkhā||
katame satta phalā sattānisaɱsā|| ||

4. Diṭṭheva dhamme paṭihacca aññam ārādheti|| ||

No ce diṭṭheva dhamme paṭihacca aññam ārādheti||
atha maraṇakāle aññam ārādheti|| ||

No ce diṭṭheva dhamme paṭihacca aññam ārādheti|| ||

no ce maraṇa kāle aññam ārādheti||
atha pañcannam orambhāgiyānam saŋyojanānam parikkhayā antarāparinibbāyī hoti||
upahacca parinibbāyī hoti||
asaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti||
sasaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti||
uddhaɱsoto hoti akaniṭṭhagāmī|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam indriyānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā ime satta phalā sattanisaɱsā paṭikaŋkhā ti|| ||

 

 

67. Rukkha 1

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci jambudīpakā rukkhā Jambu tesam aggam akkhāyati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ye keci bodhapakkhikā dhammā paññindriyaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam bodhāya|| ||

3. Katame ca bhikkhave bodhapakkhikā dhammā|| ||

Saddindriyam bhikkhave bodhapakkhiko dhammo tam bodhāya saɱvattati||
viriyindriyaɱ||
satindriyaɱ||
samādhindriyaɱ||
paññindriyam bodhapakkhiko dhammo tam bodhāya saɱvattati|| ||

Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci jambūdīpakā rukkhā jambu tesam aggam akkhāyati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ye keci bodhipakkhikā dhammā paññindriyaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam bodhāyā ti|| ||

[page 238]

 

 

68. Rukkha 2

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci devānaɱ Tāvatiɱsānam rukkhā Pāricchattako tesam aggam akkhāyati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ye keci bodhapakkhikā dhammā paññindriyaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam bodhāya|| ||

3. Katame ca bhikkhave bodhapakkhikā dhammā?|| ||

Saddhindriyam bhikkhave bodhapakkhiko dhammo tam bodhāya saɱvattati ... pe ...paññindriyam bodhapakkhiko dhammo tam bodhāya saɱvattati|| ||

Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci devānaɱ Tāvatiɱsānaɱ rukkhā Pāricchattako tesam aggam akkhāyati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ye keci bodhapakkhikā dhammā paññindriyaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam bodhāyā ti|| ||

 

 

69. Rukkha 3

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci Asurānam rukkhā Cittapāṭali tesam aggam akkhāyati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave ye keci bodhapakkhikā dhammā paññindriyaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam bodhāya|| ||

3. Katame ca bhikkhave bodhapakkhikā dhammā||
Saddhindriyam bhikkhave- -tam bodhāya saɱvattati ... pe ...paññindriyaɱ- -tam bodhāya saɱvattati|| ||

Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci asurānam rukkhā Cittapāṭali tesam aggam akkhāyati||
evam eva- -paññindriyaɱ tesam aggam akkhāyati yad idam bodhāyā ti|| ||

Chapter VIII. Gaŋgā Peyyāli (viveka°)

Book V

Sammappadhāna Saɱyutta

Chapter I. Gaŋga Peyyalī

1-12.

1—2. Sāvatthi|| ||

Tatra kho Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

Cattāro me bhikkhave sammappadhānā||
katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu anuppannānam pāpakānam akusalānaɱ dhammānam anuppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

4. Uppannānam pāpakānam akusalānaɱ dhammānam pahānāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

5. Anuppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānam uppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

6. uppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

7. Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro sammappadhānāti|| ||

8. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave Gaŋgā nadī pācīnaninnā pācinapoṇā pācīnapabbharā||
evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu cattāro samappadhāne bhāvento cattāro sammappadhāne bahulīkaronto nibbānaninno hoti nibbānapoṇo nibbānapabbhāro|| ||

Kathañ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu cattāro sammappadhāne bhāvento- -bahulīkaronto nibbānaninno hoti-nibbānapabbhāro|| ||

[page 245]

9. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu anuppannānam pāpakānaɱ akusalānaɱ dhammānam anuppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

Uppannānam pāpakānam akusalānam dhammānam pahānāya chandam janeti- -padahati|| ||

Anuppannānaɱ kusalānam dhammānam uppādāya chandaɱ janeti- -padahati|| ||

Uppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

10. Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu cattāro sammappadhāne bhāvento- -bahulīkaronto nibbānaninno hoti nibbānapoṇo nibbānapabbhāro ti|| ||

[Uddānaɱ]|| ||

Cha pācinato ninnā||
Cha ninnā ca samuddato||
ete dve cha dvādasa honti||
vaggo tena pavuccatīti|| ||

Sammappadhānasaɱyuttassa Gaŋgāpeyyālī sammappadhānavasena vitthāretabbā|| || vaggo|| ||

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ye keci balakaraṇīyā kammantā kayiranti||
sabbe te pathaviɱ nissāya pathaviyam patiṭṭhāya||
evam ete balakaraṇīyā kammantā kayiranti|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya cattāro sammappadhāne bhāveti cattāro sammappadhāne bahulī karoti|| ||

3. Kathaɱ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya cattāro samappadhāne bhāveti cattāro sammappadhāne bahulīkaroti|| ||

4—7. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu anuppannānam pāpakānam akusalānaɱ dhammānam anuppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati ... pe ...||
Uppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānam ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

8. Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu sīlaɱ nissāya sīle patiṭṭhāya cattāro samappadhāne bhāveti cattāro sammappadhāne bahulīkarotī ti|| ||
