Chapter IX. Esanā Vaggo (Rāga°)

91-100.

Esanā Vidhā Āsavo Bhavo Dukkhā ca Tisso ca||
Khila-Malañca Nīgho ca Vedanaɱ Taṇhāyena ca ti|| ||

Esanavaggo balasaɱyuttassa vasena vitthāretabbo vaggo|| ||

[page 253]

 

 

Chapter X. Ogha Vaggo (Rāga°)

101-109.

110. Uddhambhāgiyāni

2. Pañcimāni bhikkhave uddhambhāgiyāni saŋyojanāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

Rūparāgo arūparāgo māno uddhaccam avijjā|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave pañcuddhambhāgiyāni saŋyojanāni|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave- -abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya pañcabalāni bhāvetabbāni|| ||

Katamāni pañca?|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu saddhābalam bhāveti ... pe ...|| ||
paññābalam bhāveti rāgavinaya- dosavinaya- mohavinayapariyosānaɱ|| ||

4. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave pañcannam uddhambhāgiyānam saŋyojanānam abhiññāya pariññāya parikkhayāya pahānāya imāni pañcabalāni bhāvetabbānī ti|| ||

[Uddānaɱ]|| ||

Ogho Yogo Upādānaɱ Ganthā Anusayena ca||
Kāmaguṇā Nīvarana-Khandhā Oruddhabhāgiyāni|| ||

Oghavaggo balasaɱyuttassa vasena vitthāretabbo vaggo dasamo|| ||

Balasaɱyuttaɱ chaṭṭhaɱ|| ||

[page 254]

 

 

Book VII

Iddhipāda Saɱyutta

Chapter I. Cālāla Vaggo

1. Aparā

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave iddhipādā bhāvitā bahulīkatā aparāparaɱ gamanāya {saɱvattanti}||
Katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhipadhānasaŋkharasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
cittasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
vīmaɱsasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgataɱ iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro iddhipādā bhāvitā bahulīkatā aparāparaŋgamanāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

 

 

2. Viraddho

2. Yesaɱ kesañci bhikkhave cattāro iddhipadā viraddhā viraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī||
yesaɱ kesañci bhikkhave cattāro iddhipādā āraddhā āraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī|| ||

Katama cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

[page 255]

4. Yesaɱ kesañci bhikkhave ime cattāro iddhipādā viraddhā viraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī||
yesaɱ kesañci bhikkhave ime cattāro iddhipādā āraddhā||
āraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī|| ||

 

 

3. Ariyā

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave iddhipādā bhāvitā bahulīkatā ariyā niyyānikā niyyanti takkarassa sammādukkhakkhayāya||
katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

4. Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro iddhipādā bhāvitā bahulīkatā ariyā niyyānikā niyyanti takkarassa sammādukkhakkhayāyā ti|| ||

 

 

4. Nibbidā

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave iddhipādā bhāvitā bahulīkatā ekantanibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abbhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattanti||
katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipadaɱ bhāveti ||viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vīmaɱsasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

4. Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro iddhipādā bhāvitā bahulīkatā ekantanibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

 

 

5. Padesam

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā iddhipadesam abhinipphādesuɱ||
sabbe te catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā||
Ye hi keci bhikkhave anāgatam addhānam samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā iddhipadesam abhinipphādessanti

[page 256]

sabbe te catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

Ye hi keci bhikkhave etarahi samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā iddhipadesam abhinipphādenti||
sabbe te catunnam iddhipadānam bhavitattā bahulīkatattā||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

4. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā iddhipadesam abhipphādesuɱ ... pe ...||
abhinipphādessanti||
abhinipphādenti||
sabbe te imesaɱ yeva catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā ti|| ||

 

 

6. Samatta

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samattam iddhim abhinipphādesuɱ sabbe te catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

Ye hi keci bhikkhave anāgatam addhānam samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samattam iddhim abhinipphādessanti||
sabbe te catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

Ye hi keci bhikkhave etarahi samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samattam iddhim abhinipphādenti sabbe te catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vīmaɱsasamādhipadhānasaŋkharasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

4. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samattaɱ iddhiɱ abhinipphādesuɱ... pe ...
abhinipphādessanti||
abhinipphādenti||
sabbe te imesaɱ yeva catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā ti|| ||

[page 257]

 

 

7. Bhikkhū

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānam bhikkhū āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim paññāvimuttiɱ diṭṭhevadhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihariɱsu||
sabbe te catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

Ye hi keci bhikkhave anāgatam addhānam bhikkhū āsavānam khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttiɱ paññavimuttiɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharissanti||
sabbe te catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

Ye hi keci bhikkhave etarahi bhikkhū āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim paññāvimuttiɱ diṭṭhevadhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharanti||
sabbe te catunnam iddhippādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

Katamesaɱ catunnaɱ?|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

4. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānam bhikkhū āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim paññāvimuttiɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihariɱsu ... pe ...||
viharissanti||
viharanti sabbe te imesaɱ catunnaɱ iddhipādānaɱ bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā ti|| ||

 

 

8. Buddha or Arahaɱ

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave iddhipādā||
katame cattāro|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro iddhipādā|| ||

3. Imesam kho bhikkhave catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā tathāgato arahaɱ {sammāsambuddho} ti vuccatī ti|| ||

[page 258]

 

 

9. Ñāṇa

4. Ayam chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgato iddhipādo ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi||
ñānam udapādi||
paññā udapādi||
vijjā udapādi||
āloko udapādi|| ||

So kho panāyam chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgato iddhipādo bhāvetabbo ti me bhikkhave||
bhāvito ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ...āloko udapādi|| ||

5. Ayaɱ viriyasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgato iddhipādo ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ...āloko udapādi||
so kho panāyam viriyasamādhi° °samannāgato iddhipādo bhāvetabbo ti me bhikkhave pubbe ... pe ... bhāvito ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ... āloko udapādi|| ||

6. Ayam cittasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgato iddhipādo ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ...aloko udapādi|| ||

So kho panāyaɱ cittasamadhi- -samannāgato iddhipādo bhāvetabbo ti me bhikkhave pubbe ... pe ... bhāvito ti me bhikkhave pubbe ... pe ... cakkhum udapādi ... pe ... āloko udapādi|| ||

7. Ayaɱ vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgato iddhipādo ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ...||
āloko udapādi|| ||

So kho panāyaɱ vīmaɱsāsamādhi- -samannāgato iddhipādo bhāvetabbo ti me bhikkhave||
... pe...||
bhāvito ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ...||
āloko udapādī ti|| ||

 

 

10. Cetiya

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Vesāliyaɱ viharati Mahāvane Kūṭāgārasālāyaɱ|| ||

[page 259]

2. Atha kho Bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Vesāliyaɱ piṇḍāya pāvisi||
Vesāliyam piṇḍāya caritvā pacchābhattam piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto āyasmantam Ānandam āmantesi||
Gaṇhāhi Ānanda nisīdanaɱ yena Cāpālacetiyam tenupasaŋkamissāmi divāvihārāyati|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavato paṭissutvā nisīdanam ādāya Bhagavantam piṭṭhito piṭṭhito anubandhi|| ||

3. Atha kho Bhagavā yena Cāpālacetiyaɱ tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi|| ||

Āyasmā pi kho Ānando Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

4. Ekam antam nisinnaɱ kho āyasmantam Ānandam Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

Ramaṇiyā Ānanda Vesālī ramaṇiyam Udenacetiyam ramaṇiyaɱ Gotamakacetiyaɱ ramaṇiyaɱ Sattambacetiyaɱ ramaṇiyam Bahuputtakacetiyaɱ ramaṇiyaɱ Sārandadam cetiyaɱ ramaṇiyaɱ Cāpālacetiyaɱ|| ||

Yassa kassaci Ānanda cattāro iddhipādā bhāvitā bahulīkatā yānikatā vatthukatā anuṭṭhitā paricitā susamāraddhā||
so ākaŋkhamāno kappaɱ vā tiṭṭheyya kappāvasesaɱ vā|| ||

Tathāgatassa kho Ānanda cattāro iddhipādā bhāvitā bahulīkatā yānikatā vatthukatā anuṭṭhitā paricitā susamāraddhā||
ākaŋkhamāno Ānanda Tathāgato kappaɱ vā tiṭṭheyya kappāvasesaɱ vā ti|| ||

5. Evam pi kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavatā oḷārike nimitte kayiramāne oḷārike obhāse kayiramāne nāsakkhi paṭivijjhituɱ||
na Bhagavantam yāci Tiṭṭhatu bhante Bhagavā kappam tiṭṭhatu Sugato kappāvasesaɱ bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāya atthāya hitāya sukhāya devamanussānan ti||
yathā tam Mārena pariyuṭṭhitacitto|| ||

6—7. Dutiyam pi kho bhagavā|| ||

[page 260]

8. Tatiyam pi kho Bhagavā āyasmantam Ānandam āmantesi||
Ramaṇiyā Ānanda Vesālī ramaṇiyam Udeṇacetiyaɱ ramaṇiyaɱ Gotamakacetiyam ramaṇiyaɱ Sattambacetiyaɱ ramaṇiyam Bahuputtakacetiyaɱ ramaniyaɱ Sārandadam cetiyam ramaṇiyaɱ Cāpālacetiyaɱ|| ||

Yassa kassaci Ānanda cattāro iddhipadā bhāvitā bahulīkatā yānikatā vatthukatā anuṭṭhitā paricitā susamāraddhā||
so ākaŋkhamāno kappaɱ vā tiṭṭheyya kappāvasesaɱ vā||
Tathāgatassa kho Ānanda cattāro iddhipādā bhāvitā bahulīkatā yānikatā vatthukatā anuṭṭhitā paricitā susamāraddhā||
so ākaŋkhamāno Ānanda Tathāgato kappaɱ vā tiṭṭheyya kappāvasesaɱ vā ti|| ||

9. Evam pi kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavatā oḷārike nimitte kayiramāne oḷārike obhāse kayiramāne nāsakkhi paṭivijjhituɱ||
na Bhagavantaɱ yāci Tiṭṭhatu Bhagavā kappaɱ tiṭṭhatu Sugato kappāvasesaɱ bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokanukampāya atthāya hitāya sukhāya devamanussānan ti||
yathā tam Mārena pariyuṭṭhitacitto|| ||

10. Atha kho Bhagavā āyasmantam Ānandam āmantesi||
Gaccha kho tvam Ānanda yassa dāni tvaɱ kālam maññasī ti|| ||

Evam bhante ti āyasmā Ānando Bhagavato paṭissutvā uṭṭhāyāsanā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaɱ katvā avidūre aññatarasmiɱ rukkhamūle nisīdi|| ||

11. Atha kho Māro pāpimā acīrapakkante āyasmante Ānande yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā etad avoca||
Parinibbātu dāni bhante Bhagavā parinibbātu dāni Sugato parinibbānakālo dāni bhante Bhagavato|| ||

Bhāsitā kho panesā bhante Bhagavatā vācā||
na tāvāham Pāpima parinibbāyissāmi yāva me bhikkhū na sāvakā bhavissanti viyattā vinītā visāradā pattayogakkhemā bahussutā dhammadharā dhammānudhammapaṭipannā sāmīcipaṭipannā anudhammacārino sakam ācariyakam uggahetvā ācikkhissanti desissanti paññāpessanti paṭṭhapessanti vivarissanti vibhajissanti uttanīkarissanti

[page 261]

uppannam parappavādam sahadhammena suniggahītaɱ niggahetvā sappāṭihāriyaɱ dhammam desissantī ti|| ||

Santi kho pana bhante etarahi bhikkhū Bhagavato sāvakā viyattā vinītā visāradā pattayogakkhemā bahussutā dhammadharā dhammānudhammapaṭipannā sāmīcipaṭipannā anudhammacārino sakam ācariyakam uggahetvā ācikkhanti desenti paññāpenti vivaranti vibhajanti uttānīkaronti||
uppannam parappavādaɱ sahadhammena suniggahītaɱ niggahetvā sappāṭihāriyaɱ dhammaɱ desenti|| ||

12. Parinibbātu dāni bhante Bhagavā parinibbātu dāni Sugato parinibbanakālo dāni bhante Bhagavato|| ||

Bhāsitā kho panesā bhante Bhagavatā vācā||
Na tāvāham Pāpima parinibbāyissami yāva me bhikkhuniyo na sāvikā bhavissanti||
pe|| ||

13. Yāva me upāsakā na sāvakā bhavissanti||
yāva me upāsikā na sāvikā bhavissanti viyattā vinītā visāradā pattayogakkhemā bahussutā dhammadharā dhammānudhammapaṭipannā sāmīcipaṭipannā anudhammacāriniyo||
sakam ācariyakam uggahetvā ācikkhissanti desissanti paññāpessanti paṭṭhapessanti vivarissanti vibhajissanti uttānīkarissanti uppannam parappavādaɱ sahadhammena suniggahītam niggahetvā sappāṭihāriyaɱ dhammaɱ desissantī ti|| ||

Santi kho pana bhante etarahi upāsakā||
upāsikā Bhagavato sāvikā viyattā vinītā vīsāradā pattayogakkhemā bahussutā dhammadharā dhammānudhammapaṭipannā sāmīcipaṭipannā anudhammacāriniyo sakam ācariyakam uggahetvā ācikkhanti desenti paññāpenti paṭṭhapenti vivaranti vibhajanti uttānīkaronti

[page 262]

uppannam parappavādaɱ sahadhammena suniggahītaɱ niggahetvā sappāṭihāriyaɱ dhammaɱ desenti|| ||

14. Parinibbātu dāni bhante Bhagavā parinibbātu dāni Sugato||
parinibbānakālo dāni bhante Bhagavato|| ||

Bhāsitā kho panesā Bhagavatā vācā||
Na tāvāham Pāpima parinibbāyissāmi yāva me idam brahmacariyam na iddhaɱ ceva bhavissati||
phītaɱ ca vitthāritaɱ bāhujāññaɱ puthubhutaɱ yāvad eva manussehi supakāsitan ti|| ||

Tayidam bhante Bhagavato brahmacariyam iddham ceva phitañca vitthāritam bahujaññam puthubhūtam yāvad eva manussehi supakāsitaɱ|| ||

Parinibbātu dāni bhante Bhagavā parinibbātu dāni Sugato parinibbānakālo dāni bhante Bhagavato ti|| ||

15. Evaɱ vutte Bhagavā Māram pāpimantam etad avoca|| ||

Apossukko tvam Pāpima hohi||
na ciraɱ Tathāgatassa parinibbānam bhavissati||
ito tiṇṇam māsānam accayena Tathāgato parinibbāyissatī ti|| ||

16. Atha kho Bhagavā Cāpāle cetiye sato sampajāno āyusaŋkhāram ossaji|| ||

Ossaṭṭhe pana Bhagavatā āyusaŋkhāre mahābhūmicālo ahosi bhiɱsanako lomahaɱso||
devadundubhiyo ca caliɱsu|| ||

17. Atha kho Bhagavā etam atthaɱ viditvā tāyaɱ velāyam imam udānam udānesi|| ||

[page 263]

Tulam atulañca sambhavam||
bhavasaŋkhāram avassaji muni||
ajjhattarato samāhito||
abhindi kavacam ivattasambhavan ti|| ||

Cāpālavaggo pathamo|| ||

Tatr'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Apārāpi Viraddho ca||
Ariyā Nibbidā yathā||
Padesaɱ Sammattā Bhikkhu||
Buddha-Ñāṇena Cetiyā ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter II. Pāsādakampana Vaggo

11. Pubbe or Hetu

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Pubbeva me bhikkhave sambodhāya anabhisambuddhassa bodhisattasseva sato etad ahosi||
Ko nu kho hetu ko paccayo iddhipādabhāvanāyā ti|| ||

Tassa mayham bhikkhave etad ahosi|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipadam bhāveti|| ||

Iti me chando na ca atilīno bhavissati||
na ca atipaggahīto bhavissati||
na ca ajjhattaɱ saŋkhitto bhavissati||
na ca bahiddhā vikkhitto bhavissati||
paccāpuresaññi ca viharati||
yathā pure tathā pacchā yathā pacchā tathā pūre||
yathā adho tathā uddhaɱ yathā uddhaɱ tathā adho||
yathā divā tathā rattiɱ yathā rattiɱ tathā divā|| ||

Iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena cetasā sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

[page 264]

4. Viriyasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Iti me viriyaɱ na ca atilīnam bhavissati||
na ca atipaggahītam bhavissati||
na ca ajjhattaɱ saŋkhittam bhavissati||
na ca bahiddhā vikkhittam bhavissati||
pacchāpuresaññī ca viharati yathā pure tathā pacchā yathā pacchā tatthā pure||
yathā adho tathā uddhaɱ||
yathā uddhaɱ tathā adho||
yathā divā tathā rattiɱ||
yathā rattiɱ tathā divā|| ||

Iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

5. Cittasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Iti me cittam na ca atilīnam bhavissati na ca atipaggahītam bhavissati||
na ca ajjhattaɱ saŋkhittam bhavissati||
na ca bahiddhā vikkhittam bhavissati||
pacchāpuresaññī ca viharati yathā pure tathā pacchā yathā pacchā tathāpure||
yatha adho tathā uddhaɱ yathā uddhaɱ tathā adho||
yathā divā tathā rattiɱ yathā rattiɱ tathā divā|| ||

Iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

6. Vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Iti me vīmaɱsā na ca atilīnā bhavissati||
na ca atipaggahitā bhavissati||
na ca ajjhattaɱ saŋkhittā bhavissati||
na ca bahiddhā vikkhittā bhavissati||
pacchāpuresaññī ca viharati yathā pure tathā pacchā yathā pacchā tathā pure||
yathā adho tathā uddhaɱ yathā uddhaɱ tathā adho||
yathā divā tathā rattiɱ yathā rattiɱ tathā divā|| ||

Iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

7. Evam bhāvitesu kho bhikkhu catusu iddhipādesu evam bahulīkatesu anekavihitam iddhividham paccanubhoti||
eko pi hutvā bahudhā hoti bahudhā pi hutvā eko hoti||
āvibhāvam tirobhāvam tirokuḍḍam tiropākāraɱ tiropabbatam asajjamāno gacchati seyyathāpi ākāse||
pathaviyam pi ummujja nimujjaɱ karoti seyyathāpi udake||
udake abhijjamāno gacchati seyyathāpi pathaviyaɱ ||ākāsepi pallaŋkena caŋkamati seyyathāpi pakkhī sakuṇo

[page 265]

ime pi candimasuriye evam mahiddhike evam mahānubhāve pāṇinā parimasati parimajjati||
yāva brahmalokā pi kāyena vasam pavatteti|| ||

8. Evam bhāvitesu kho bhikkhu catusu iddhipādesu evam bahulīkatesu dibbāya sotadhātuyā visuddhāya atikkantamanussakāya ubho sadde suṇāti dibbe ca mānusse ca ye dūre santike vā ti|| ||

9. Evam bhāvitesu kho bhikkhu catusu iddhipādesu evam bahulīkatesu parasattānam parapuggalānam cetasā ceto paricca pajānāti|| ||

Sarāgaɱ vā cittaɱ Sarāgaɱ cittanti pajānāti||
vītarāgaɱ vā cittaɱ Vītarāgaɱ cittanti pajānāti|| ||

Sadosaɱ vā cittaɱ Sadosaɱ cittanti pajānāti||
vītadosaɱ vā cittaɱ Vītadosaɱ cittan ti pajānāti|| ||

Samohaɱ vā cittaɱ Samohaɱ cittan ti pajānāti||
vītamohaɱ vā cittam Vītamohaɱ cittan ti pajānāti|| ||

Saŋkhittaɱ vā cittaɱ Saŋkhittaɱ cittan ti pajānāti||
vikkhittaɱ vā cittaɱ Vikkhittaɱ cittan ti pajānāti|| ||

Mahaggataɱ vā cittaɱ Mahaggataɱ cittan ti pajānāti||
amahaggataɱ vā cittam Amahaggataɱ cittan ti pajānāti|| ||

Sauttaraɱ vā cittaɱ Sauttaraɱ cittan ti pajānāti||
anuttaraɱ vā cittaɱ Anuttaraɱ cittan ti pajānāti|| ||

Asamāhitaɱ vā cittaɱ Asamāhitaɱ cittan ti pajānāti||
samāhitaɱ vā cittaɱ Samāhitaɱ cittan ti pajānāti|| ||

Avimuttam vā cittaɱ Avimuttaɱ cittanti pajānāti||
vimuttaɱ vā cittaɱ Vimuttaɱ cittan ti pajānāti|| ||

10. Evam bhāvitesu kho bhikkhu catusu iddhipādesu evam bahulīkatesu anekavihitam pubbenivāsam anussarati||
seyyathīdam ekam pi jātim dve pi jātiyo tisso pi jātiyo catasso pi jātiyo pañca pi jātiyo dasa pi jātiyo vīsam pi jātiyo tiɱsam pi jātiyo cattālisam pi jātiyo paññāsam pi jātiyo jātisatam pi jātisahassam pi jātisatasahassam pi aneke pi saɱvaṭṭakappe aneke pi vivaṭṭakappe aneke pi saɱvaṭṭavivaṭṭakappe amutrāsiɱ evam nāmo

[page 266]

evaŋgotto||
evaɱvaṇṇo evamāhāro evaɱsukhadukkhapaṭisaɱvedī evam āyupariyanto||
so tato cuto amutra uppādiɱ||
tatravāsim evaɱnāmo evaŋgotto evaɱvaṇṇo evamāhāro evaɱsukhadukkhapaṭisaɱvedī evam āyupariyanto||
so tato cuto idhupapanno ti||
iti sākāraɱ sauddesam anekavihitaɱ pubbenivāsam anussarati|| ||

11. Evam bhāvitesu kho bhikkhu catusu iddhipādesu evam bahulīkatesu dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānussakena satte passati||
cavamāne upapajjamāne hīne paṇīte suvaṇṇe dubbaṇṇe sugate duggate yathākammupage satte pajānāti||
Ime vata bhonto sattā kāyaduccaritena samannāgatā vacīducaritena samannāgatā manoduccaritena samannāgatā ariyānam upavādakā micchādiṭṭhikā micchādiṭṭhikammasamādānā||
te kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā apāyaɱ duggatim vinipātaɱ nirayam upapannā|| ||

Ime kho pana bhonto sattā kāyasucaritena sammannāgatā vacīsucaritena samannāgatā manosucaritena samannāgatā ariyānam anupavādakā sammādiṭṭhikā sammādiṭṭhikammasamādānā||
te kāyassa bhedā parammaraṇā sugatiɱ saggam lokam upapannā ti|| ||

Iti dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānussakena satte passati||
cavamāne upapajjamāne hīne paṇīte suvaṇṇe dubbaṇṇe||
sugate duggate yathākammupage satte pajānāti|| ||

12. Evam bhāvitesu kho bhikkhu catusu iddhipādesu evam bahulīkatesu āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim paññāvimuttim diṭṭhevadhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharatī ti|| ||

[page 267]

 

 

12. Mahapphala

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave iddhipādā bhāvitā bahulīkatā mahapphalā honti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

Katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave cattāro iddhipādā katham bahulīkatā mahapphalā honti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
Iti kho me chando na ca atilīno bhavissati||
na ca atipaggahīto bhavissati||
na ca ajjhattaɱ saŋkhitto bhavissati||
na ca bahiddhā vikkhitto bhavissati||
pacchāpuresaññī ca viharati yathāpure tathā pacchā yathā pacchā tathāpure||
yathā adho tathā uddhaɱ yathā uddhaɱ tathā adho||
yathā divā tathā rattiɱ yathā rattiɱ tathā divā||
iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

4—5. Viriyasamādhi||
... pe ...||
Cittasamādhi|| ||

6. Vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkharasamannāgatam iddhipādham bhāveti||
Iti kho me vīmaɱsā na ca atilīnā bhavissati||
na ca atipaggahitā bhavissati||
na ca ajjhattaɱsaŋkhittā bhavissati||
na ca bahiddhā vikkhittā bhavissati||
pacchāpure saññī ca viharati yathāpure tathā pacchā yathā pacchā tathāpure||
yathā adho tathā uddhaɱ yathā uddhaɱ tathā adho||
yathā divā tathā rattiɱ yathā rattiɱ tathā divā|| ||

Iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave cattāro iddhipādā evam bahulīkatā mahapphalā honti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

7—11. Evam bhāvitesu kho bhikkhave bhikkhu catusu iddhipādesu evam bahulīkatesu anekavihitam iddhividham paccanubhoti||
eko pi hutvā bahudhā hoti ... pe ... yāva brahmalokā pi kāyena vasaɱ vatteti... pe ...|| ||

[page 268]

12. Evam bhāvitesu kho bhikkhave bhikkhu catusu iddhipādesu evam bahulīkatesu āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavam cetovimuttim paññāvimuttiɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharatī ti|| ||

 

 

13. Chando

2. Chandaɱ ce bhikkhave bhikkhu nissāya labhati samādhiɱ labhati cittassa ekaggataɱ||
ayam vuccati chandasamādhi|| ||

So anuppannānam pāpakānam akusalānaɱ dhammānam anuppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

Uppannānaɱ pāpakānam akusalānam dhammānam pahānāya chandam janeti vāyamati viriyam āravhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati||
Anuppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānam uppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

Uppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

Ime vuccanti padhānasaŋkhārā|| ||

Iti ayaɱ ca chando ayaɱ ca chandasamādhi ime ca padhānasaŋkhārā||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgato iddhipādo|| ||

3. Viriyaɱ ce bhikkhave bhikkhu nissāya labhati samādhim labhati cittassa ekaggatam||
ayaɱ vuccati viriyasamādhi|| ||

So anuppannānaɱ ... pe ... Uppannānaɱ kusalānam dhammānaɱ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

Ime vuccanti padhānasaŋkharā|| ||

Iti idaɱ ca viriyam ayañca viriyasamādhi ime ca padhānasaŋkhārā||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave viriyasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgato iddhipādo|| ||

[page 269]

4. Cittaɱ ce bhikkhave bhikkhu nissāya labhati samādhiɱ labhati cittassa ekaggatam||
ayaɱ vuccati cittasamādhi|| ||

So anuppannānam pāpakānaɱ ... pe ... uppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānam ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandam janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

Ime vuccanti padhānasaŋkhārā ti|| ||

Iti idaɱ ca cittaɱ ayaɱ ca cittasamādhi ime ca padhānasaŋkharā||
ayam vuccati bhikkhave cittasamādhi padhānasaŋkhārasamannāgato iddhipādo|| ||

5. Vīmaɱsaɱ ce bhikkhave bhikkhu nissāya labhati samādhiɱ labhati cittassa ekaggataɱ||
ayam vuccati vīmaɱsāsamādhi|| ||

So anuppannānam pāpakānam akusalānaɱ dhammānam anuppādāya ... pe ...uppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya paripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyam ārabhati cittam paggaṇhāti padahati|| ||

Ime vuccanti padhānasaŋkhārā|| ||

Iti ayaɱ ca vīmaɱsā ayaɱ ca vīmaɱsāsamādhi ime ca padhānasaŋkhārā||
Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgato iddhipādoti|| ||

 

 

14. Moggalāno

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Pubbārāme Migāramātupāsāde|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena sambahulā bhikkhū heṭṭhā Migāramātupāsāde viharanti uddhatā unnaḷā capalā mukharā vikiṇṇavācā muṭṭhassatino asampajānā asamāhitā vibbhantacittā pākatindriyā|| ||

3. Atha kho Bhagavā āyasmantam Mahā-Moggalānam āmantesi|| ||

Ete kho Moggalāna sabrahmacāriyā heṭṭhā Migāramātupāsāde viharanti uddhatā unnaḷā capalā mukharā vikiṇṇavācā muṭṭhassatino asampajānā asamāhitā vibbhantacittā pākatindriyā

[page 270]

gaccha Moggalāna te bhikkhū saɱvejehīti|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho āyasmā Mahā-Moggalāno Bhagavato paṭissutvā tathārūpam iddhābhisaŋkhāram abhisaŋkhāresi||
yathā pādaŋguṭṭhakena Migāramātupāsādam saŋkampesi sampakampesi sampacālesi|| ||

4. Atha kho te bhikkhū {saɱviggā} lomahaṭṭhajātā ekam antam aṭṭhaɱsu||
Acchariyaɱ vata bho abbhutaɱ vata bho nivātañca vata ayaɱ ca Migaramatupāsādo gambhiranamo sunikhāto acalo asampakampi||
atha ca pana saŋkampito sampakampito sampacālitoti|| ||

5. Atha kho Bhagavā yena te bhikkhū tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā te bhikkhū Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

Kiɱ nu tumhe bhikkhave {saɱviggā} lomahaṭṭhajātā eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitā ti|| ||

Acchariyam bhante abbhutam bhante nivātañca vata ayaɱ ca Migāramātupāsādo gambhīranemo sunikhāto acalo asampakampi||
atha ca pana saŋkampito sampakampito sampacālito ti|| ||

6. Tumheva kho bhikkhave saɱvejetukāmena Moggalānena bhikkhunā pādaŋguṭṭhakena Migāramātupāsādo saŋkampito sampakampito sampacālito|| ||

Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamesaɱ dhammānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā Moggalāno bhikkhu evam mahiddhiko evam mahānubhāvo ti|| ||

Bhagavaɱmūlakā no bhante dhammā Bhagavaɱnettikā-Bhagavato sutvā bhikkhū dhāressantī ti|| ||

[page 271]

7. Tena bhikkhave suṇātha|| ||

Catunnaɱ kho bhikkhave iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā Moggalāno bhikkhu evam mahiddhiko evam mahānubhāvo||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

8. Idha bhikkhave Moggalano bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Iti me vīmaɱsā na ca atilīnā bhavissati na ca atipaggahītā bhavissati||
na ca ajjhattaɱsaŋkhittā bhavissati||
na ca bahiddhā vikkhittā bhavissati||
pacchāpuresaññī ca viharati yathā pure tathā pacchā yathā pacchā tathā pure||
yathā adho tathā uddhaɱ yathā uddhaɱ tathā adho||
yathā divā tathā rattiɱ yathā rattiɱ tathā divā|| ||

Iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

9. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā Moggalāno bhikkhu evam mahiddhiko evam mahānubhāvo|| ||

10. Imesaɱ ca pana bhikkhave catunnam iddhipādānam bhavitattā bahulīkatattā Moggalāno bhikkhu anekavihitam iddhividham paccanubhoti ... pe ... yāva brahmalokā pi kāyena vasaɱ vatteti|| ||

11. imesaɱ ca pana bhikkhave catunnam iddhipadānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā Moggalāno bhikkhu āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim ... pe ...||
upasampajja viharatīti|| ||

12. Evaɱ cāpi abhiññā vitthāretabbā|| ||

 

 

15. Brāhmaṇa

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Ānando Kosambīyaɱ viharati Ghositārāme|| ||

[page 272]

2. Atha kho Uṇṇābho brāhmaṇo yenāyasmā Ānando tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmatā Ānandena saddhim sammodi||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Uṇṇābho brāhmaṇo āyasmantaɱ Ānandam etad avoca|| ||

3. Kim atthi yaɱ nu kho bho Ānanda samaṇe Gotame brahmacariyaɱ vussatī ti|| ||

Chandapahānatthaɱ kho brāhmaṇa Bhagavati brahmacariyaɱ vussatī ti|| ||

4. Atthi pana bho Ānanda maggo atthi paṭipadā etassa chandassa pahānāyā ti|| ||

Atthi kho brāhmaṇa maggo atthi paṭipadā etassa chandassa pahānāyā ti|| ||

5. Katamo pana bho Ānanda maggo katamā paṭipadā etassa chandassa pahānāyā ti|| ||

Idha brāhmaṇa bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
ayaɱ kho brāhmaṇa maggo ayam paṭipadā etassa chandassa pahānāyā ti|| ||

6. Evaɱ sante kho Ānanda santakaɱ hoti no asantakam chandena ca chandam pajahissatī ti netam thānaɱ vijjatīti|| ||

Tena hi brāhmaṇa taññevettha paṭipucchissāmi||
yathā te khameyya tathā taɱ vyākareyyāsi|| ||

7. Taɱ kim maññasi brāhmaṇa||
ahosi te pubbe chando Ārāmaɱ gamissāmīti||
tassa te ārāmagatassa yo tajjo chando so paṭippassadho ti|| ||

Evam bho|| ||

Ahosi te pubbe viriyaɱ Ārāmam gamissāmīti||
tassa te ārāmagatassa yaɱ tajjaɱ viriyaɱ tam paṭipassaddhanti|| ||

[page 273]

Evam bho|| ||

Ahosi te pubbe cittaɱ Ārāmaɱ gamissāmī ti||
tassa te ārāmagatassa yam tajjaɱ cittaɱ tam paṭippassaddhanti|| ||

Evam bho|| ||

Ahosi te pubbe vīmaɱsā Ārāmaɱ gamissāmīti||
tassa te ārāmagatassa yā tajjā vīmaɱsā sā paṭippassaddhā ti|| ||

Evam bho|| ||

8. Evam eva kho brāhmaṇa yo so bhikkhu arahaɱ khīṇāsavo vusitavā katakaraṇīyo ohitabhāro anuppattasadattho parikkhīṇabhavasaŋyojano sammadaññā vimutto||
tassa yo pubbe chando ahosi arahattapattiyā arahatte patte yo tajjo chando so paṭippassaddho|| ||

Yam pubbe viriyam ahosi arahattapattiyā arahatte patte yaɱ tajjaɱ viriyaɱ tam paṭippassaddhaɱ|| ||

Yam pubbe cittam ahosi arahattapattiyā arahatte patte yaɱ tajjaɱ cittaɱ tam paṭippassaddhaɱ|| ||

Yā pubbe vīmaɱsā ahosi arahattapattiyā arahatte patte yā tajjā vīmaɱsā sā paṭippassaddhā|| ||

9. Taɱ kim maññasi brāhmaṇa||
Iti evaɱ sante santakam vā hoti asantakaɱ vā ti|| ||

Addhā bho Ānanda evaɱ sante santakaɱ hoti no asantakaɱ|| ||

10. Abhikkantam bho Ānanda ... pe ...ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatanti|| ||

 

 

16. Samaṇabrāhmaṇā 1 or Mahiddhi

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānam samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā mahiddhikā ahesuɱ mahānubhāvā||
sabbe te catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

3. Ye hi keci bhikkhave anāgatam addhānam samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā mahiddhikā bhavissanti- -bahulīkatattā|| ||

4. Ye hi keci bhikkhave etarahi samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā mahiddhikā mahānubhāvā sabbe te catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

Katamesam catunnaɱ?|| ||

[page 274]

5. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgataɱ iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

6. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā mahiddhikā ahesuɱ mahānubhāvā... pe ...
mahiddhikā bhavissanti mahānubhāvā||
... pe ...||
etarahi mahiddhikā mahānubhāvā||
sabbe te imesaɱ yeva catunnam iddhipādānaɱ bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā ti|| ||

 

 

17. Samaṇabrāhmaṇā 2 or Vidhā

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā anekavihitam iddhividham paccanubhosuɱ||
eko pi hutvā bahudhā ahesuɱ||
bahudhā hutvā eko ahesuɱ||
āvibhāvaɱ tirobhāvaɱ tirokuḍḍam tiropākāraɱ tiropabbataɱ asajjamānā agamaɱsu seyyathāpi ākāse||
pathaviyam pi ummujjanimujjam akaɱsu seyyathāpi udake||
udake pi abhijjamānā agamaɱsu seyyathāpi pathaviyaɱ||
akāse pi pallaŋkena agamiɱsu seyyathāpi pakkhī sakuṇo||
ime pi candimasuriye evam mahiddhike evam mahānubhāve pāṇinā parimasiɱsu parimajjiɱsu||
yāva Brahmalokā pi kāyena vasaɱ vattesaɱ||
sabbe te catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

3. Ye hi keci bhikkhave aṇāgatam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā anekavihitam iddhividham paccanubhossanti||
eko pi hutvā bahudhā bhavissanti||
bahudhā pi hutvā eko bhavissanti||
āvibhāvaɱ tirobhāvam tirokuḍḍam tiropākāraɱ tiropabbatam asajjamānā gamissanti seyyathāpi ākāse||
pathaviyam pi ummujjanimujjaɱ karissanti seyyathāpi udake

[page 275]

udake pi abhijjamānā gamissanti seyyathāpi pathaviyaɱ||
akāse pi pallaŋkena bhavissanti seyyathāpi pakkhī sakuṇo||
ime pi candimasuriye evam mahiddhikke evam mahānubhāve pāṇinā parimasissanti parimajjissanti yāva Brahmalokā pi kāyena vasaɱ vattessanti||
sabbe te catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā|| ||

4. Ye hi keci bhikkhave etarahi samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā anekavihitam iddhividam paccanubhonti||
eko pi hutvā bahudhā honti||
bahudhā pi hutvā eko honti||
āvibhāvaɱ tirobhāvaɱ tirokuḍḍam tiropākāram tiropabbatam asajjamānā gacchanti seyyathāpi ākāse ... pe ... yāva Brahmalokā pi kāyena vasaɱ vattenti||
sabbe te catunnam iddhipādānam bhavitattā bahulīkatattā||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

5. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vīmaɱsasamādhipaḍhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam bhāveti|| ||

6. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā anekavihitam iddhividham paccanubhosuɱ||
... pe ...||
paccanubhossanti||
... pe ...||
paccanubhonti||
[pe]|| sabbe te imesaɱ yeva catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā ti|| ||

 

 

18. Bhikkhu

2. Catunnam bhikkhave iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā bhikkhu āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim paññāvimuttiɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharati||
Katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vimaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bhikkhu āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavam cetovimuttim paññāvimuttim diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharatī ti

[page 276]

 

 

19. Desanā or Bhāvanā

2. Iddhiɱ vo bhikkhave desissāmi iddhipādaɱ ca iddhipādabhāvanaɱ ca iddhipādabhāvanāgāminiɱ ca paṭipadaɱ||
taɱ suṇātha|| ||

3. Katamā ca bhikkhave iddhi|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu anekavihitam iddhividham paccanubhoti||
eko pi hutvā bahudhā hoti||
... pe ...||
yāva brahmalokā pi kāyena vasaɱ vatteti|| ||

Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave iddhi|| ||

4. Katamo ca bhikkhave iddhipādo|| ||

Yo bhikkhave maggo yā paṭipadā iddhilābhāya iddhipaṭilābhāya saɱvattati||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave iddhipādo|| ||

5. Katamā ca bhikkhave iddhipādabhāvanā|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vimaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave iddhipādabhāvanā|| ||

6. Katamā ca bhikkhave iddhipādabhāvanāgāminī paṭipadā||
ayam eva ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo||
seyyathīdam sammāditthi ... pe ... sammāsamādhi|| ||

Ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave iddhipādabhāvanāgāminī paṭipadā ti|| ||

 

 

20. Vibhaŋga

I.

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave iddhipādā bhāvitā bahulīkatā mahapphalā honti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

Katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave cattāro iddhipādā katham bahulīkatā mahapphalā honti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
Iti me chando na ca atilīno bhavissati

[page 277]

na ca atipaggahīto bhavissati||
na ca ajjhattaɱ saŋkhitto bhavissati||
na ca bahiddhā vikkhitto bhavissati ... pe ...Iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsam cittam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vimaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
Iti me vīmaɱsā na ca atilīnā bhavissati||
na ca atipaggahītā bhavissati||
na ca ajjhattaɱ saŋkhittā bhavissati na ca bahiddhā vikkhittā bhavissati||
pacchāpuresaññī ca viharati||
yathā pure tathā pacchā yathā pacchā tathā pure||
yatha adho tathā uddhaɱ yathā uddhaɱ tathā adho||
yathā divā tathā rattiɱ yathā rattiɱ tathā divā||
iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

II.

4. Katamo ca bhikkhave atilīno chando|| ||

Yo bhikkhave chando kosajjasahagato kosajjasampayutto||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave atilīno chando|| ||

5. Katamo ca bhikkhave atipaggahīto chando|| ||

Yo bhikkhave chando uddhaccasahagato uddhaccasampayutto||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave atipaggahīto chando|| ||

6. Katamo ca bhikkhave ajjhattaɱ saŋkhitto chando|| ||

Yo bhikkhave chando thīnamiddhasahagato thīnamiddhasampayutto||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave ajjhattaɱ saŋkhitto chando|| ||

7. Katamo ca bhikkhave bahiddhā vikkhitto chando||
yo bhikkhave chando bahiddhā pañcakāmaguṇe ārabbha anuvikkhito anuvisaṭo||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave bahiddhā vikkhitto chando|| ||

8. Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu pacchāpuresaññī ca viharati yathā pure tathā pacchā yathā pacchā tathāpure|| ||

[page 278]

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhuno pacchāpure saññā suggahītā hoti sumanasikatā supadhāritā suppaṭividdhā paññāya||
Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu pacchāpure saññī ca viharati yathā pure tathā pacchā yathā pacchā tathā pure|| ||

9. Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu yathā adho tathā uddham yatha uddhaɱ tathā adho viharati|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu imam eva kāyam uddham pādatalā adho kesamatthakā tacapariyantam pūram nānappakārassa asucino paccavekkhati||
Atthi imasmiɱ kāye kesā lomā nakhā dantā taco maɱsaɱ nahārū aṭṭhī aṭṭhimiñjā vakkaɱ hadayaɱ yakanaɱ kilomakam pihakam papphāsam antaɱ antaguṇam udariyaɱ karīsaɱ pittaɱ semhaɱ pubbo lohitaɱ sedo medo assu vasā kheḷo siŋghānikā kasikā muttan ti|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu yathā adho tathā uddhaɱ yathā uddhaɱ tathā adho viharati|| ||

10. Kathañ ca bhikkhave bhikkhu yathā divā tathā rattiɱ yathā rattiɱ tathā divā viharati|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu yehi ākārehi yehi liŋgehi yehi nimittehi divā chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
so tehi ākārehi tehi liŋgehi tehi nimittehi rattiɱ chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Yehi vā pana ākārehi yehi liŋgehi yehi nimittehi rattiɱ chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
so tehi ākārehi tehi liŋgehi tehi nimittehi divā chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu yathā divā tathā rattiɱ yathā rattiɱ tathā divā viharati|| ||

11. Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhuno ālokasaññā suggahītā hoti divāsaññā svādhiṭṭhitā|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsam cittam bhāveti|| ||

[page 279]

III.

12. Katamañ ca bhikkhave atilīnaviriyaɱ|| ||

Yam bhikkhave viriyaɱ kosajjasahagataɱ kosajjasampayuttaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave atilīnaviriyaɱ|| ||

13. Katamañ ca bhikkhave atipaggahītaviriyaɱ||
Yam bhikkhave viriyaɱ uddhaccasahagatam uddhaccasampayuttaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave atipaggahītaɱ viriyaɱ|| ||

14. Katamañ ca bhikkhave ajjhattaɱ saŋkhittaɱ viriyam|| ||

Yam bhikkhave viriyaɱ thīnamiddhasahagataɱ thīnamiddhasampayuttaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave ajjhattaɱ saŋkhittaɱ viriyaɱ|| ||

15. Katamañ ca bhikkhave bahiddhā vikkhittaɱ viriyaɱ|| ||

Yam bhikkhave viriyaɱ bahiddhā pañcakāmaguṇe ārabbha anuvikkhittam anuvisaṭaɱ|| ||

Idam vuccati bhikkhave bahiddhā vikkhittaɱ viriyaɱ|| ||

16—19. Peyyālo|| ||

Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsam bhāveti|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhuno ālokasaññā sugahitā hoti divāsaññā svādhiṭṭhitā|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu vivaṭen cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

IV.

20. Katamañ ca bhikkhave atilīnaɱ cittaɱ||
yam pi bhikkhave cittaɱ kosajjasahagataɱ kosajjasampayuttaɱ||
idam vuccati bhikkhave atilīnaɱ cittaɱ|| ||

21. Katamañ ca bhikkhave atipaggahītaɱ cittaɱ|| ||

Yam bhikkhave cittam uddhaccasahagatam uddhaccasampayuttaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave atipaggahītaɱ cittaɱ|| ||

22. Katamañ ca bhikkhave ajjhattaɱ saŋkhittaɱ cittaɱ|| ||

Yam bhikkhave cittaɱ thīnamiddhasahagatam thīnamiddhasampayuttaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave ajjhattaɱ saŋkhittaɱ cittaɱ|| ||

[page 280]

23. Katamañ ca bhikkhave bahiddhā vikkhittaɱ cittaɱ|| ||

Yam bhikkhave cittam bahiddhā pañcaguṇe ārabbha anuvikkhittam anuvisaṭaɱ||
idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave bahiddhā vikkhittaɱ cittaɱ|| ||

24—27. Peyyālam||
evam kho bhikkhave bhikkhu vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittaɱ bhāveti|| ||

V.

28. Katamā ca bhikkhave atilīṇā vīmaɱsā|| ||

Yā bhikkhave vīmaɱsā kosajjasahagatā kosajjasampayuttā||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave atilīnā vīmaɱsā|| ||

29. Katamā ca bhikkhave atipaggahītā vīmaɱsā|| ||

Yā bhikkhave vīmaɱsā uddhaccasahagatā uddhaccasampayuttā||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave atipaggahītā vīmaɱsā|| ||

30. Katamāca bhikkhave ajjhattaɱ saŋkhittā vīmaɱsā|| ||

Yā bhikkhave vīmaɱsā thīnamiddhassahagatā thīnamiddhasampayuttā||
ayam vuccati bhikkhave ajjhattaɱsaŋkhittā vīmaɱsā|| ||

31. Katamā ca bhikkhave bahiddhā vikkhittā vīmaɱsā|| ||

Yā bhikkhave vīmaɱsā bahiddhā pañcakāmaguṇe ārabbha anuvikkhittā anuvisaṭā||
ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhave bahiddhā vikkhittā vīmaɱsā|| ||

32—35. ... pe ...|| ||

Evaɱ kho bhikkhave bhikkhu vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsam cittam bhāveti|| ||

Chapter III. Vaggo Tatiyo

21. Maggo

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Pubbe me bhikkhave sambodhā anabhisambuddhassa bodhisattasseva etad ahosi||
Ko nu kho maggo kā paṭipadā iddhipādabhāvanāyā ti|| ||

Tassa mayham bhikkhave etad ahosi|| ||

3. So bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Iti me chando na atilīno bhavissati ... pe ... sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

4—5. Viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi|| ||

6. Vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Iti me vīmaɱsā na ca atilīnā bhavissati||
na ca atipaggahītā bhavissati||
na ca ajjhattaɱ saŋkhittā bhavissati||
na ca bahiddhā vikkhittā bhavissati||
pacchāpuresaññī ca viharati||
yathāpure tathā pacchā yathā pacchā tathā pure||
yathā adho tathā uddhaɱ yathā uddhaɱ tathā adho||
yathā divā tathā rattiɱ yathā rattiɱ tathā divā||
Iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

[page 282]

7. Evam bhāvitesu kho bhikkhave bhikkhu catusu iddhipādesu evam bahulīkatesu anekavihitam iddhividham paccanubhoti||
eko pi hutvā bahudhā hoti||
bahudhā pi hutvā eko hoti||
... pe ... yāva Brahmalokā pi kāyena vasaɱ vatteti|| ||

8. Evam bhāvitesu kho bhikkhave bhikkhu catusu iddhipādesu evam bahulīkatesu āsavānam khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim paññāvimuttiɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharatī ti|| ||

9. Cha pi abhiññāyo vittharetabbā|| ||

 

 

22. Ayoguḷo

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi||
Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Abhijānāti nu kho bhante Bhagavā iddhiyā manomayena kāyena Brahmalokam upasaŋkamitā ti|| ||

Abhijānāmi khvāham Ānanda iddhiyā manomayena kāyena Brahmalokam upasaŋkamitā ti|| ||

4. Abhijānāti kho pana bhante Bhagavā iminā cātumahābhūtikena kāyena iddhiyā Brahmalokam upasaŋkamitā ti|| ||

Abhijānāmi khavāham Ānanda iminā cātumahābhūtikena kāyena iddhiyā Brahmalokam upasaŋkamitā ti|| ||

5. Yaɱ ca kho opapāti ha bhante Bhagavā iddhiyā manomayena kāyena Brahmalokam upasaŋkamituɱ||
yaɱ ca kho abhijānāti bhante Bhagavā iminā cātumahābhūtikena kāyena iddhiyā Brahmalokam upasaŋkamitā

[page 283]

tayidam bhante Bhagavato acchariyaɱ ceva abbhutaɱ cāti|| ||

Acchariyā ceva Ānanda tathāgatā acchariyadhammasamannāgatā ca abbhutā ceva Ānanda tathagatā abbhutadhammasamannāgatā ca|| ||

6. Yasmiɱ Ānanda samaye Tathāgato kāyam pi citte samādahati cittam pi ca kāye samādahati||
sukhasaññañca lahusaññañca kāye okkamitvā viharati||
tasmiɱ Ānanda samaye Tathāgatassa kāyo lahutaro ceva hoti mudutaro ca kammaniyataro ca pabhassarataro ca|| ||

7. Seyyathā pi ānanda ayoguḷo divasaɱ santatto lahutaro ceva hoti mudutaro ca kammaniyataro ca pabhassarataro ca||
evam eva kho Ānanda yasmiɱ samaye Tathāgato kāyam pi citte samādahati||
cittam pi kāye samādahati||
sukhasaññañca lahusaññañca kāye okkamitvā viharati||
tasmim Ānanda samaye Tathāgatassa kāyo lahutaro ceva hoti mudutaro ca kammaniyataro ca pabhassarataro ca|| ||

8. Yasmim Ānanda samaye Tathāgato kāyam pi citte samādahati||
cittam pi kāye samādahati||
sukhasaññañca lahusaññañca kāye okkamitvā viharati||
tasmim Ānanda samaye Tathāgatassa kāyo appakasireneva pathaviyā vehāsam abbhuggacchati||
so anekavihitam iddhividham paccanubhoti||
eko pi hutvā bahudhā hoti||
... pe ... yāva Brahmalokā pi kāyena vasaɱ vatteti|| ||

[page 284]

9. Seyyathā pi Ānanda tūlapicu vā kappāsapicu vā lahuko vātupādāno appakasireneva pathaviyā vehāsam abbhuggacchati||
evam eva kho Ānanda yasmiɱ samaye Tathāgato kāyam pi citte samādahati||
cittam pi kāye samādahati||
sukhasaññañca lahusaññañca kāye okkamitvā viharati||
tasmim Ānanda samaye Tathāgatassa kāyo appakasireneva pathaviyā vehāsam abbhuggacchati||
so anekavihitam iddhividham paccanubhoti||
eko pi hutvā bahudhā hoti ... pe ...||
yāva Brahmalokā pi kāyena vasaɱ vattetī ti|| ||

 

 

23. Bhikkhu

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave iddhipadā||
katame cattāro|| ||

Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti||
viriyasamādhi||
cittasamādhi||
vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro iddhipādā|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā bhikkhu āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim paññāvimuttiɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharatīti|| ||

 

 

24. Suddhakam

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave iddhipādā-||
Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro iddhipādā ti|| ||

[page 285]

 

 

25. Phalā 1

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave iddhipādā-|| ||

Ime° cattāro iddhipādā|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā dvinnam phalānam aññataram phalaɱ pātikaŋkhaɱ diṭṭheva dhamme aññā sati vā upādisese anāgāmitāti|| ||

 

 

26. Phalā 2

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave iddhipādā°|| ||

°Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro iddhipādā|| ||

3. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā satta phalā sattānisaɱsā pātikaŋkhā|| ||

Katame sattaphalā sattānisaɱsā|| ||

4. Diṭṭheva dhamme paṭihacca aññam ārādheti|| ||

No ce diṭṭheva dhamme paṭihacca aññam ārādheti||
atha maraṇakāle aññam ārādheti|| ||

No ce maraṇakāle aññam ārādheti||
atha pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā antarāparinibbāyī hoti||
upahaccaparinibbāyī hoti||
asaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti||
sasaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hotī||
uddhaɱsoto hoti akaniṭṭhagāmī|| ||

5. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā ime sattaphalā sattānisaɱsā patikaŋkhā ti|| ||

31. Moggalāno

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave|| ||

Katamesaɱ dhammānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā Moggalāno bhikkhu evam mahiddhiko evam mahānubhāvo ti|| ||

Bhagavaɱmūlakā no bhante dhammā Bhagavaɱnettikā||
... pe ...|| ||

4. Catunnaɱ kho bhikkhave iddhipādānam bhavitattā bahulīkatattā Moggalāno bhikkhu evam mahiddhiko evam mahānubhāvo||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

5. Idha bhikkhave Moggalāno bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipadam bhāveti||
Iti me chando na ca atilīno bhavissati ... pe ... sappabhāsam bhāveti|| ||

6—7. Viriyasamādhi||
Cittasamādhi|| ||

8. Vīmaɱsāsamādhipadhānasaŋkhārasamannāgatam iddhipādam bhāveti|| ||

Iti me vīmaɱsā na ca atilīnā bhavissati||
na ca atipaggahitā bhavissati||
na ca ajjhattaɱ saŋkhittā bhavissati||
na ca bahiddhā vikkhittā bhavissati||
... pe ...||
Iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

9. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā Moggalāno bhikkhu evam mahiddhiko evam mahānubhāvo|| ||

10. Imesañca pana bhikkhave catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā Moggalāno bhikkhu evam anekavihitam iddhividham paccanubhoti||
eko pi hutvā bahudhā hoti||
bahudhā pi hutvā eko hoti||
... pe ...||
yāva Brahmalokā pi kāyena vasaɱ vatteti|| ||

[page 289]

11. Imesaɱ ca pana bhikkhave catunnam iddhipādānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā Moggalāno bhikkhu āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavam cetovimuttim paññavimuttiɱ diṭṭhevadhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharatī ti|| ||

 

 

32. Tathāgato

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Iti me chando na ca atilīno bhavissati||
na ca atipaggahīto bhavissati||
... pe ...||
iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsam cittam bhāveti|| ||

cittasamādhi|| ||

na ca atipaggahītā bhavissati||
na ca ajjhattam ... pe ... Iti vivaṭena cetasā apariyonaddhena sappabhāsaɱ cittam bhāveti|| ||

... pe ...

yāva Brahmalokā pi kāyena vasaɱ vatteti|| ||

Chābhiññāvitthāretabaɱ|| ||

Oghavaggo iddhipādavasena vitthāretabbo|| ||

Book VIII

Anuruddha Saɱyutta

Chapter I. Rahogata Vaggo

1. Rahogata 1

1. Evam me sutaɱ Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Anuruddho Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmato Anuruddhassa rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaɱ cetaso parivitakko udapādi|| ||

Yesaɱ kesañci cattāro satipaṭṭhānā viraddhā||
viraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī||
Yesaɱ kesañci cattāro satipaṭṭhānā āraddhā||
āraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī ti|| ||

3. Atha kho āyasmā Mahā-Moggalāno āyasmato Anuruddhassa cetasā cetoparivitakkam aññāya seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitam vā bāham pasāreyya pasāritaɱ vā bāham sammiñjeyya||
evam eva āyasmato Anuruddhassa sammukhe pātur ahosi|| ||

4. Atha kho āyasmā Mahā-Moggalāno āyasmantam Anuruddham etad avoca|| ||

Kittāvatā nu kho āvuso Anuruddha bhikkhuno cattāro satipaṭṭhānā āraddhā hontīti|| ||

5. Idhāvuso bhikkhu ajjhattaɱ kāye samudayadhammānupassī viharati ... pe ...ajjhattaɱ kāye vayadhammānupassī viharati||
ajjhattam kāye samudayavayadhammānupassī viharati

[page 295]

ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

6. Bahiddhā kāye vayadhammānupassī viharati||
... pe ...||
bahiddhā kāye samudayavayadhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

7. Ajjhattabahidhā kāye samudayadhammānupassī viharati||
ajjhattabahiddhā kāye vayadhammānupassī viharati||
ajjhattabahiddhā kāye samudayavayadhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

8. So sace ākaŋkhati Appatikkūle paṭikkūlasaññī vihareyyan ti||
paṭikkūlasaññī tattha viharati|| ||

Sace ākaŋkhati Paṭikkūle appaṭikkūlasaññī vihareyyan ti||
appaṭikūlasaññī tattha viharati|| ||

Sa ce ākaŋkhati Appaṭikkule ca paṭikkule ca paṭikkūlasaññī vihareyyanti patikkūlasaññī tattha viharati|| ||

Sa ce ākaŋkhati Patikkūpe ca appaṭikkūle ca appatikkūlasaññī vihareyyan ti||
appatikkūlasaññī tattha viharati|| ||

Sa ce ākaŋkhati Appaṭikkūlañca paṭikkūlañca tadubhayam abhinivajjetvā upekhako vihareyyaɱ sato sampajāno ti||
upekhako tattha viharati sato sampajāno|| ||

9. Ajjhattaɱ vedanāsu samudayadhammanupassī viharati||
ajjhattaɱ vedanāsu vayadhammānupassī viharati||
ajjhattaɱ vedanāsu samudayavayadhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyyaloke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

10. Bahiddhā vedanāsu samudayadhadhammānupassī viharati||
bahiddhā vedanāsu vayadhammānupassī viharati||
bahiddhā vedanāsu samudayavayadhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyyaloke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

11. Ajjhattabahiddhā vedanāsu samudayadhammānupassī viharati||
ajjhattabahiddhā vedanāsu vayadhammānupassī viharati||
ajjhattabahiddhā vedanāsu samudayavayadhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam

[page 296]

12. So sa ce ākaŋkhati pe|| ||

13. Ajjhattaɱ citte||
... pe ...|| ||

14. Bahiddhā citte||
... pe ...|| ||

15. Ajjhattabahiddhā citte samudayadhammānupassī viharati||
ajjhattabahiddhā citte vaya-||
ajjhattabahiddhā citte samudayavayadhammānupassī viharati||
ātāpī ... pe ... abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

16. So sa ce ākaŋkhati ... pe ...|| ||

17. Ajjhattaɱ dhammesu||
... pe ...|| ||

18. Bahiddhā dhammesu||
... pe ...|| ||

19. Ajjhattabahiddhā dhammesu samudayadhammānupassī viharati||
ajjhattabahiddhā dhammesu vayadhammānupassī viharati||
ajjhattabahiddhā dhammesu samudayavayadhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

20. So sa ce ākaŋkhati Appaṭikūle paṭikūlasaññī vihareyyan ti paṭikūlasaññī tattha viharati ... pe ... upekhako tattha viharati sato sampajāno|| ||

21. Ettāvatā kho āvuso bhikkhuno cattāro satipaṭṭhānā āraddhā hontī ti|| ||

 

 

2. Rahogata 2

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmato Anuruddhassa rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaɱ cetaso parivitakko udapādi|| ||

Yesaɱ kesañci cattāro satipaṭṭhānā viraddhā viraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī|| ||

Yesaɱ kesañci cattāro satipaṭṭhānā āraddhā āraddho tesam ariyo maggo sammādukkhakkhayagāmī ti|| ||

3. Atha kho āyasmā Mahā-Moggalāno āyasmato Anuruddhassa cetasā ceto parivitakkam aññāya seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso

[page 297]

... pe ...|| ||

Evam eva āyasmato Anuruddhassa pamukhe pātur ahosi|| ||

4. Atha kho āyasmā Mahā-Moggalāno āyasmantam Anuruddham etad avoca|| ||

Kittāvatā nu kho āvuso Anuruddha bhikkhuno cattāro satipaṭṭhānā āraddhā honti|| ||

5. Idhāvuso bhikkhu ajjhattaɱ kāye kāyānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Bahiddhā kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī||
... pe ...||
Ajjhattabahiddhā kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī||
abhijjhadomanassam|| ||

6. Ajjhattaɱ vedanāsu vedanānupassī viharati ātāpī-abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Bahiddhā vedanāsu vedanānupassī viharati ātāpī -abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Ajjhattam bahiddhā vedanāsu vedanānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

7. Ajjhattaɱ citte||
bahiddhā citte||
ajjhattabahiddhā citte cittānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

8. Ajjhattaɱ dhammesu||
bahiddhā dhammesu||
ajjhattabahiddhādhammesu dhammānupassī viharati: ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

9. Ettāvatā kho āvuso bhikkhuno cattāro satipaṭṭhānā āraddhā hontī ti|| ||

 

 

3. Sutanu

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Anuruddho Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Sutanutīre|| ||

2. Atha kho sambahulā bhikkhū yenāyasmā Anuruddho tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmatā Anuruddhena saddhiɱ sammodiɱsu|| ||

Sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyam vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu|| ||

[page 298]

3. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū āyasmantam Anuruddham etad avocuɱ|| ||

Katamesaɱ āyasmā Anuruddho dhammānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā mahābhiññātam patto ti|| ||

4 Catunnam khvāham āvuso satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā mahābhiññātam patto||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

Idhāham āvuso kāye kāyānupassī viharāmi ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
vedanāsu||
citte||
dhammesu dhammānupassī viharāmi||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Imesaɱ khvāham āvuso catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā mahābhiññātam patto|| ||

5. Imesaɱ ca panāham āvuso catunnaɱ satipaṭṭhānānam bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā hīnaɱ dhammaɱ hīnato abbhaññāsiɱ||
majjhimaɱ dhammam majjhimato abbhaññāsiɱ||
paṇītaɱ dhammam paṇītato abbhaññāsin ti|| ||

 

 

4. Kaṇṭakī 1

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Anuruddho āyasmā ca Sāriputto āyasmā ca Mahā-Moggalāno Sākete viharanti Kaṇṭakīvane|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā ca Sāriputto āyasmā ca MahāMoggalāno sāyaṇhasamayam paṭisallāṇā vuṭṭhitā yenāyasmā Anuruddho tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmatā Anuruddhena saddiɱ sammodiɱsu||
sammodanīyaɱ katham sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu|| ||

3. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Sāriputto āyasmantam Anuruddham etad avoca|| ||

Sekhenāvuso Anuruddha bhikkhunā katame dhammā upasampajja vihātabbā ti|| ||

Sekhenāvuso Sāriputta bhikkhunā cattāro satipaṭṭhānā upasampajja vihātabbā||
katame cattaro|| ||

citte||

ātāpī||

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ āyasmā Anuruddho Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Salaḷāgāre|| ||

... pe ...
etad avoca|| ||

3. Seyyathā pi āvuso Gaŋgā nadī pācinaninnā pācinapoṇā pācinapabbhārā||
atha mahājanakāyo āgaccheyya kuddālapiṭakam ādāya Mayam imam Gaŋgānadim pacchāninnaɱ karissāma pacchāpoṇam pacchāpabbharan ti||
Taɱ kim maññathāvuso api nu so mahājanakāyo Gaŋgānadim pacchāninnaɱ kareyya pacchāpoṇam pacchāpabbhāranti|| ||

No hetam āvuso|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

Gaŋgā āvuso nadī pācinaninnā pācīnapoṇā pācīnapabbharā sā na sukarā pacchāninnam kātum pacchāpoṇam pacchāpabbhāram||
yāvad eva ca pana so mahājanakāyo kilamathassa vighātassa bhāgī assā ti|| ||

4. Evam eva kho āvuso bhikkhuɱ cattāro satipaṭṭhāne bhāventam cattāro satipaṭṭhāne bahulīkarontaɱ rājāno vā rājamahāmattā vā mittā vā amaccā vā ñātisālohitā vā bhogehi abhihaṭṭhum pavāreyyuɱ Ehambho purisa kin te ime kāsāvā anudahanti

[page 301]

kim muṇḍokapālam anusaɱcarasi||
ehi hīnāyāvattitvā bhoge ca bhuñjassu puññāni ca karohī ti|| ||

So vata āvuso bhikkhu cattāro satipaṭṭhāne bhāvento cattāro satipaṭṭhāne bahulīkaronto sikkham paccakkhāya hīnāyāvattissatī ti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

yañ hi taɱ āvuso cittaɱ dīgharattaɱ vivekaninnaɱ vivekapoṇaɱ vivekapabbharaɱ taɱ vata hīnāyāvattissatī ti netaɱ thānaɱ vijjati|| ||

vedanāsu||
citte||

9. Sabbam or Ambapāla

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ āyasmā ca Anuruddho āyasmā ca Sāriputto Vesāliyaɱ viharanti Ambapālivane|| ||

... pe ...|| ||

katamenāyasmā Anuruddho vihārena etarahi bahulaɱ viharatī ti|| ||

Catusu khvāham āvuso satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacitto etarahi bahulaɱ viharāmi||
katamesu catusu|| ||

[page 302]

5. Yo so āvuso bhikkhu arahaɱ khīṇāsavo vusitavā katakaraṇīyo ohitabhāro anuppattasadattho {parikkhīṇabhavasaŋyojano} sammadaññā vimutto||
so imesu catusu satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacitto bahulaɱ viharatī ti|| ||

6. Lābhā vata no āvuso suladdhaɱ vata no āvuso ye mayam āyasmato Anuruddhassa sammukhā va assumha āsabhim vācam bhāsamānassā ti|| ||

Catūsu me āvuso satipaṭṭhānesu supatiṭṭhitacittassa viharato uppannā sārīrikā dukkhā vedanā cittaɱ na pariyādāya tiṭṭhanti|| ||

13. Iddhi 2

14. Cetoparicca

5. Imesañ ca panāham avuso catunnaɱ sati- bhā- bahuparasattānam parapuggalānaɱ cetasā ceto paricca pajānāmi||

vimuttaɱ vā cittaɱ Vimuttaɱ cittan ti pajānāmī ti|| ||

 

 

15. Ṭhāna

5. Imesañ ca panāham āvuso catunnaɱ sati- bhā- bahuṭhānañ ca ṭhānato aṭṭhānañca aṭṭhānato yathābhūtam pajānāmī ti|| ||

sati- bhā- bahuatītānāgatapaccuppannānaɱ kammasamādānānaɱ ṭhānaso hetuso vipākam yathābhūtam pajanāmī ti|| ||

5. Imesañ ca panāham āvuso catunnam sati- bhā- bahusabbatthagāminipaṭipadaɱ yathābhūtam pajanāmī ti|| ||

 

 

18. Loka

21. Jhānam (?)

Jhāna Saɱyutta

Chapter I. Gaŋgā Peyyālo

1. Pathamasuddhiyam

1—2. Sāvatthi||
Tatra kho cattāro me bhikkhave jhānā||
katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu vivicceva kāmehi vivicca akusalehi dhammehi savitakkaɱ savicāraɱ vivekajam pītisukhaɱ pathamam jhānam upasampajja viharati|| ||

4. Vitakkavicārānaɱ vūpasamā ajjhattaɱ sampasādanaɱ cetaso ekodibhāvam avitakkam avicāraɱ samādhijam pītisukhaɱ dutiyaɱ jhānam upasampajja viharati|| ||

5. Pītiyā ca virāgā upekhako ca viharati sato ca sampajāno sukhañca kāyena paṭisaɱvedeti||
Yan tam ariyā ācikkhanti upekhako satimā sukhavihārī ti tatiyaɱ jhānam upasampajja viharati|| ||

6. Sukhassa ca pahānā dukkhassa ca pahānā pubbeva somanassadomanassānam atthagamā adukkham asukham upekhāsatipārisuddhiɱ catutthaɱ jhānam upasampajja viharati|| ||

7. Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro jhānā ti|| ||

8. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave Gaŋgā nadī pācīnaninnā pācīnapoṇā pācīnapabbhārā||
evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu cattāro jhāne bhāvento cattāro jhāne bahulīkaronto nibbānaninno hoti nibbānapoṇo nibbānapabbhāro

[page 308]

Kathañca bhikkhave bhikkhu cattāro jhāne bhāvento° °nibbānapabbhāro|| ||

9. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu vivicceva kāmehi vivicca akusalehi dhammehi savitakkasavicāram vivekajam pītisukham pathamaɱ jhānam upasampajja viharati||
vitakkavicārānaɱ vūpasamā ... pe ... dutiyaɱ jhānaɱ||
tatiyaɱ jhānaɱ||
catutthaɱ jhānam upasampajja viharati||
Evam kho bhikkhave bhikkhu cattāro jhāne bhāvento cattāro jhāne bahulīkaronto nibbānaninno hoti nibbānapoṇo nibbānapabbhāro ti|| ||

Jhānasaññuttassa pathamasuddhiyam suttantaɱ|| ||
