Book X

Ānāpāna Saɱyutta

Chapter I. Ekadhamma Vaggo

1. Ekadhammo

1. Sāvatthi||
ārāme|| ||

2. Tatra kho ... pe ... etad avoca|| ||

3. Ekadhammo bhikkhave bhāvito bahulīkato mahapphalo hoti mahāṇisaɱso||
katamo ekadhammo||
Ānāpānasati|| ||

Katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave ānāpānasati||
katham bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu araññagato vā rukkhamūlagato vā suññāgāragato vā nisīdati pallaŋkam ābhujitvā ujuɱ kāyam paṇidhāya parimukham satim upaṭṭhapetvā so sato va assasati sato va passasati|| ||

5. Dīghaɱ vā assasanto Dīgham assasāmī ti pajānāti||
dīghaɱ vā passasanto Dīgham passasāmī ti pajānāti||
Rassaɱ vā assasanto Rassam assasāmī ti pajānāti||
rassaɱ vā passasanto Rassam passāmī ti pajānāti|| ||

6. {Sabbakāyapaṭisaɱvedī} Assasissāmīti sikkhati||
sabbakāyapaṭisaɱvedī Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

Passambhayaɱ kāyasaŋkhāram Assāsissāmīti sikkhati||
passambhayam kāyasaŋkhāram Passissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

[page 312]

7. Pītipaṭisaɱvedī Assasissāmīti sikkhati||
pītipaṭisaɱvedī Passasissamīti sikkhati|| ||

Sukhapaṭisaɱvedī Assasissāmīti sikkhati||
sukhapatisaɱvedī Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

8. {Cittasaŋkhārapaṭisaɱvedī} Assasissāmīti sikkhati||
cittasaŋkhārapaṭisaɱvedī Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

Passambhayaɱ cittasaŋkhāraɱ Assāsissāmīti sikkhati||
passambhayaɱ cittasaŋkhāram Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

Cittapaṭisaɱvedī Assasissāmīti sikkhati||
{cittapaṭisaɱvedī} Passasissamīti sikkhati|| ||

9. Abhippamodayaɱ cittam Assasissāmīti sikkhati||
abhippamodayaɱ cittam Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

Samādahaɱ cittaɱ Assasissāmīti sikkhati||
samādahaɱ cittaɱ Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

Vimocayaɱ cittam Assasissāmīti sikkhati||
vimocayaɱ cittam Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

10. Aniccānupassī Assasissāmīti sikkhati||
aniccānupassī Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

Virāgānupassī Assasissāmīti sikkhati||
virāgānupassī Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

Nirodhānupassī Assasissāmīti sikkhati||
nirodhānupassī Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

Paṭinissaggānupassī Assasissāmītī||
paṭinissaggānupassī Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

11. Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave ānāpānasati evam bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsāti|| ||

 

 

2. Bojjhaŋgo

1.2. Sāvatthi||
ārāme||
tatra||
voca|| ||

3. Ānāpānasati bhikkhave bhāvitā bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā||
katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave ānāpānasati katham bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu ānāpānasatisahagataɱ satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggapariṇāmiɱ||
ānāpānasatisahagatam dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgaɱ||
viriya||
pīti||
passaddhi||
samādhi||

[page 313]

ānāpānasatisahagatam upekkhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti viveka° virāga° nirodhanissitaɱ vossaggaparināmiɱ|| ||

5. Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave ānāpānasati evam bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā ti|| ||

 

 

3. Suddhakam

1—2. Sāvatthi||
ārāme||
tatra||
voca|| ||

3. Ānāpānasati bhikkhave bhāvitā bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā||
katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave ānāpānasati katham bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu araññagato vā rukkhamūlagato vā suññāgāragato vā nisīdati pallaŋkam ābhujitvā ujuɱ kāyam paṇidhāya parimukhaɱ satim upaṭṭhapetvā so sato va assasati sato va passasati|| ||

5—10. Vitthāretabbā||
yāva paṭinissaggānupassī Assasissamī ti sikkhati||
paṭinissaggānupassī Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

11. Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave ānāpānasati evam bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā ti|| ||

 

 

4. Phalā 1

3. Ānāpānasati bhikkhave bhāvitā bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā||
kathaɱ bhāvitā ca bhikkhave ānāpānasati katham bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

4—10. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu araññagato vā rukkhamūlagato vā nisīdati- osato passati||
vitthāro||
yāva paṭinissaggānupassī Assasissāmīti sikkhati||
paṭinissaggānupassī Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

11. Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave ānāpānasati evam bahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

[page 314]

12. Evam bhāvitāya kho bhikkhave ānāpānasatiyā evam bahulīkatāya dvinnam phalānam aññataram phalam pāṭikaŋkhaɱ||
diṭṭheva dhamme aññā sati vā upādisese anāgāmitā ti|| ||

 

 

5. Phalā 2

3. Ānāpānasati bhikkhave bhā- bahu- mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā||
katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave katham bahumahapphalā hoti mahanisaɱsā|| ||

4—10. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu araññagato vā rukkhamūlagato vā suññāgāragato vā nisīdati- vitthāro||
yāva-sikkhati paṭinissaggānupassī Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

11. Evam bhāvitā kho bhikkhave ānāpānasati evambahulīkatā mahapphalā hoti mahānisaɱsā|| ||

12. Evam bhāvitāya kho bhikkhave ānāpānasatiyā evam bahulīkatāya satta phalā sattānisaɱsā paṭikaŋkhā||
katame satta phalā sattānisaɱsā|| ||

13. Diṭṭheva dhamme patihacca aññam ārādheti|| ||

No ce diṭṭheva dhamme paṭihacca aññam ārādheti||
atha maraṇakāle aññam ārādheti|| ||

No ce maraṇakāle aññam ārādheti||
atha pañcannaɱ orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā antarāparinibbāyī hoti||
upahaccaparinibbāyī hoti||
asaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti||
sasaŋkhāraparinibbāyī hoti||
uddhaɱsoto hoti akaniṭṭhāgāmī|| ||

14. Evam bhāvitāya kho bhikkhave ānāpānasatiyā evam bahulīkatāya ime satta phalā sattānisaɱsā paṭikaŋkhā ti|| ||

 

 

6. Ariṭṭho

1—2. Sāvatthi|| ||

Tatra kho Bhagavā ... pe ... etad avoca|| ||

Bhāvetha no tumhe bhikkhave ānāpānasatin ti|| ||

3. Evaɱ vutte āyasmā Ariṭṭho Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Ahaɱ kho bhante bhāvemi ānāpānasatin ti|| ||

[page 315]

Yathā katham pana tvam Ariṭṭha bhāvesi ānāpānasatinti|| ||

4. Atītesu me bhante kāmesu kāmacchando pahīno||
anāgatesu me kāmesu kāmacchando vigato||
ajjhattam bahiddhā ca me dhammesu paṭighasaññā suppaṭivinītā||
so sato assasissāmi sato passasissāmi||
Evam khvāham bhante bhāvemi ānāpānasatin ti|| ||

5. Atthesā Ariṭṭha ānāpānasati nesā natthī ti vadāmi||
api ca Ariṭṭha yathā ānāpānasati vitthārena paripuṇṇā hoti||
taɱ suṇāhi sādhukam manasi karohi||
bhāsissāmi|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho āyasmā- opaccassosi|| ||

6. Bhagavā etad avoca||
Kathañca Ariṭṭha ānāpānasati vitthārena paripuṇṇā hoti|| ||

7—13. Idha Ariṭṭha bhikkhu araññagato vā rukkhamūlagato vā suññāgāragato vā nisīdati pallaŋkamo oDīgham assassāmīti pajānāti ... pe ... yāva paṭinissaggānupassī Assasissamī ti sikkhati||
paṭinissaggānupassī Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

14. Evaɱ kho Ariṭṭha ānāpānasati vitthārena paripuṇṇā hotī ti|| ||

 

 

7. Kappino

1—2. Sāvatthi||
voca|| ||

3. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Mahākappino avidūre nisinno hoti pallaŋkam ābhujitvā uruɱ kāyam paṇidhāya parimukhaɱ satim upaṭṭhapetvā|| ||

4. Addasā kho Bhagavā āyasmantam Mahākappinam avidūre nisinnam pallaŋkam abhujitvā ujuɱ kāyam paṇidhāya parimukhaɱ satim upaṭṭhapetvā||
disvāna bhikkhū amantesi|| ||

Passatha no tumhe bhikkhave etassa bhikkhuno kāyassa iñjitattaɱ vā phanditattaɱ vā ti|| ||

5. Yadā pi mayam bhante tam āyasmantam passāma saŋghamajjhe vā nisinnam ekaɱ vā raho nisinnaɱ||
tadā pi mayaɱ tassa āyasmato na passāma kāyassa iñjitattaɱ vā phanditattam vā ti

[page 316]

6. Yassa bhikkhave samādhissa bhavitattā bahulīkatattā neva kāyassa iñjitattaɱ va hoti phanditattaɱ vā||
na cittassa iñjitattam vā hoti phanditattaɱ vā||
tassa so bhikkhave bhikkhu samādhissa nikāmalābhī akicchalābhī akasiralābhī|| ||

7. Katamassa ca bhikkhave samādhissa bhavitattā bahulīkatattā neva kāyassa iñjitattaɱ vā hoti phanditattaɱ vā||
na cittassa iñjitattaɱ vā hoti phanditattaɱ vā||
Ānāpānasatisamādhissa bhikkhave bhāvitattā bahulīkatattā neva kāyassa iñjitattaɱ vā hoti phanditattaɱ vā na cittassa iñjitattaɱ vā hoti phanditattaɱ vā|| ||

8. Katham bhāvite ca bhikkhave ānāpanasatisamādimhi katham bahulīkate neva kāyassa iñjitattaɱ vā hoti phanditattam vā||
na cittassa iñjitattaɱ vā hoti phanditattaɱ vā|| ||

9—15. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu araññagato vā rukkhamūlagato vā suññāgāragato vā nisīdati-||
vitthāretabbā||
yāva-sikkhati||
paṭisissaggānupassī Passasissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

16. Evam bhāvite ca kho bhikkhave ānāpānasatisamādimhi evam bahulīkate neva kāyassa iñjitattaɱ vā hoti phanditattaɱ va||
na cittassa iñjitattaɱ vā hoti phanditattam vā ti|| ||

 

 

8. Dīpo

1—2. Sāvatthi — voca|| ||

3. Ānāpānasatisamādhi bhikkhave bhavito bahulīkato mahapphalo hoti māhānisaɱso|| ||

Katham bhāvito ca bhikkhave ānāpānasatisamādhi katham bahulīkato mahapphalo hoti mahānisaɱso|| ||

[page 317]

4—10. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu araññagato vā rukkhamūlagato vā suññāgāragato vā nisīdati pallaŋkam- -Dīgham assassāmīti pajānāti||
{vitthāretabbaɱ}||
-patinissaggānupassī Passissāmīti sikkhati|| ||

11. Evam bhāvito kho bhikkhave ānāpānasatisamādhi evam bahulīkato mahapphalo hoti mahānisaɱso|| ||

12. Aham pi sudam bhikkhave pubbeva sambodhā anabhisambuddho bodhisatto va samāno iminā vihārena bahulaɱ viharāmi||
tassa mayham bhikkhave iminā vihārena bahulaɱ viharato neva kāyo kilamati na cakkhunī||
anupādāya ca me āsavehi cittaɱ vimuccati|| ||

13. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya||
Neva kāyo kilameyya na ca cakkhunī||
anupādāya ca me āsavehi cittaɱ vimucceyyā ti|| ||

Ayam eva ānāpānasatisamādhi sādhukam manasi kātabbo|| ||

14. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya||
Ye me gehasitasarasaŋkappā te pahīheyyunti||
ayam eva anāpānasatisamādhi sādhukaɱ manasi kātabbo|| ||

15. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya Appaṭikkūle paṭikkūlasaññī vihareyyan ti||
ayam eva ānāpānasatisamādhi sādhukam manasi kātabbo|| ||

16. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya Paṭikkūle appaṭikkūlasaññī vihareyyan ti||
ayam eva ānāpānasatisamādhi sādhukam manasi kātabbo|| ||

17. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya Appaṭikkūle ca paṭikkūle ca paṭikkūlasaññī vihareyyan ti||
ayam eva ... pe ...|| ||

18. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya Paṭikkūle ca appaṭikkūle ca appatikkūlasaññī vihareyyan ti

[page 318]

ayam eva ... pe ...|| ||

19. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya Appaṭikkūlañca patikkūlañca tad ubhayam abhinivajjetvā upekhako vihareyyaɱ sato sampajāno ti||
ayam eva ... pe ...|| ||

20. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya Vivicceva kāmehi vivicca akusalehi dhammehi savitakkaɱ savicāraɱ vivekajam pītisukham pathamaɱ jhānam upasampajja vihareyyanti||
ayam eva||
[pe]|| ||

21. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi akaŋkheyya vitakkavicārānaɱ vūpasamā ajjhattam sampasādanaɱ cetaso ekodibhāvam avitakkam avicāraɱ samādhijam pītisukhaɱ dutiyaɱ jhānam upasampajja vihareyyanti||
ayam eva ... pe ...|| ||

22. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi akaŋkheyya Pītiyā ca virāgā upekhako ca vihareyyaɱ sato sampajāno sukhaɱ ca kāyena paṭisaɱvedeyyaɱ yan tam ariyā ācikkhanti upekhako satimā sukhavihārī ti tatiyaɱ jhānam upasampajja vihareyyan ti|| ||

Ayam eva||
... pe ...|| ||

23. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya||
Sukhassa ca pahānā dukkhassa ca pahānā pubbeva domanassānam atthagamā adukkham asukham upekhāsatiparisuddhiɱ catutthaɱ jhānam upasampajja viharati||
ayam eva ... pe ...|| ||

24. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya sabbaso rūpasaññānaɱ samatikkamā paṭighasaññānam atthagamā nānattasaññānam amanasikārā Ananto ākāso ti ākāsānañcāyatanam upasampajja vihareyyan ti||
ayam eva ... pe ...|| ||

25. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya||
Sabbaso ākāsānañcāyatanaɱ samatikkamma Anantaɱ viññāṇanti viññāṇañcāyatanam upasampajja vihareyyan ti

[page 319]

ayam eva ... pe ...|| ||

26. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya||
Sabbaso viññāṇañcāyatanaɱ samatikkamma Natthi kiñci ākiñcaññāyatanam upasampajja vihareyyan ti||
Ayam eva||
pe|| ||

27. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya.|| ||

Sabbaso ākiñcaññāyatanaɱ samatikkamma Nevasaññānāsaññāyatanam upasampajja vihareyyan ti||
ayam eva ānāpānasamadhi sādhukam manasi kātabbo|| ||

28. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave bhikkhu ce pi ākaŋkheyya||
Sabbaso nevasaññānāsaññāyatānaɱ samatikkamma saññavedayitanirodham upasampajja vihareyyan ti|| ||

Ayam eva ānāpānasatisamādhi sādhukam manasi kātabbo|| ||

29. Evam bhāvite kho bhikkhave ānāpānasatisamādimhi evam bahulīkate sukhañ ce vedanaɱ vediyati Sā aniccā ti pajānāti||
Anajjhositā ti pajānāti||
Anabhinanditā ti pajānāti||
dukkhañ ce vedanaɱ vediyati||
Sā aniccā ti pajānāti||
Anajjhositā ti pajānāti||
Anabhinanditā ti pajānāti||
adukkhaɱ asukhañ ce vedanam vediyati Sā aniccā ti pajānāti||
Anajjhositā ti pajānāti||
Anabhinanditā ti pajānāti|| ||

30. So sukhañ ce vedanaɱ vediyati visaɱyutto nām vediyati||
dukkhañ ce vedanaɱ vediyati visaɱyutto nam vediyati||
adukkham asukhañ ce vedanaɱ vediyati visaɱyutto naɱ vediyati|| ||

So kāyapariyantikam vedanaɱ vedayamāno kāyapariyantikaɱ vedanaɱ vediyāmīti pajānāti jīvitapariyantikaɱ vedanaɱ vediyamāno jīvitapariyantikam vedanaɱ vediyāmīti pajānāti|| ||

Kāyassa bhedā uddhaɱ jīvitapariyādānā idheva sabbavedayitāni anabhinanditāni sītibhavissantī ti pajānāti|| ||

31. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave telañca paticca vaṭṭiñca paṭicca telapadīpo jhāyeyya||
tasseva telassa ca vaṭṭiyā ca pariyādānā anāhāro nibbāyeyya||
evam eva kho bhikkhave bhikkhu kāyapariyantikam vedanaɱ vediyamāno Kāyapariyantikaɱ vedanaɱ vedayāmī ti pajānāti

[page 320]

jīvitapariyantikaɱ vedanaɱ vediyamāno Jīvitapariyantikaɱ vedanaɱ vedayāmīti pajānāti|| ||

Kāyassa bhedā uddhaɱ jīvitapariyādānā idheva sabbavedayitāni anabhinanditāni sītibhavissantī ti pajānātī ti|| ||

 

 

9. Vesālī

1. Evam me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Vesāliyaɱ viharati Mahāvane Kuṭāgārasālāyaɱ|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Bhagavā bhikkhūnam anekapariyāyena asubhakathaɱ katheti||
asubhāya vaṇṇam bhāsati asubhabhāvanāya vaṇṇaɱ bhāsati|| ||

3. Atha kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Icchāmaham bhikkhave addhamāsaɱ patisalliyituɱ||
namhi kenaci upasaŋkamitabbo aññatra ekena piṇḍapātanīhārakena ti|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho te bhikkhū Bhagavato paṭissutvā nāssudha koci Bhagavantam upasaŋkamati aññatra ekena piṇḍapātanīhārakena|| ||

4. Atha kho te bhikkhū Bhagavā anekapariyāyena asubhakatham kathesi asubhāya vaṇṇam bhāsati||
asubhabhāvanāya vaṇṇam bhāsatī ti||
anekākāravokāram asubhabhāvanānuyogam anuyuttā viharanti|| ||

Te iminā kāyena aṭṭiyāmānā harāyamānā jigucchamānā satthahārakam pariyesanti||
{dasa} pi bhikkhū ekāhena sattham āharanti||
vīsam pi ... pe ... tiɱsam pi ekāhena sattham āharanti|| ||

5. Atha kho Bhagavā tassa uḍḍhamāsassa accayena paṭisallaṇā vuṭṭhito āyasmantam Ānandam āmantesi|| ||

Kiɱ nu kho Ānanda tanubhūto viya bhikkhusaŋgho ti|| ||

6. Tathā hi pana bhante Bhagavā bhikkhūnam anekapariyāyena asubhakatham kathesi asubhāya vaṇṇam bhāsati asubhabhāvanāya vaṇṇam bhāsati

[page 321]

[te ca bhante bhikkhū Bhagavā kho anekapariyāyena asubhakathaɱ kathesi||
asubhāya vaṇṇambhāsati asubhabhāvanāya vaṇṇam bhāsatī ti] anekākāravokāram asubhabhāvanānuyogam anuyuttā viharanti|| ||

Te iminā kāyena aṭṭiyamānā harāyamānā satthahārakam pariyesanti dasa pi bhikkhū vīsampi- tiɱsam pi bhikkhū ekāhena sattham āharanti|| ||

Sādhu bhante Bhagavā aññam pariyāyam ācikkhatu tathā yathāyam bhikkhusaŋgho aññāya saṇṭhaheyyā ti|| ||

7. Tenhānanda yāvatikā bhikkhū Vesālim upanissāya viharanti||
te sabbe upaṭṭhānasālāyaɱ sannipātehī ti|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavato paṭissutvā yāvatikā bhikkhū Vesālim upanissāya viharanti||
te sabbe upaṭṭhānasālāyam sannipātetvā yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bagavantam etad avoca||
Sannipatito bhante bhikkhusaŋgho yassa dāni Bhagavā kālam maññatī ti|| ||

8. Atha kho Bhagavā yena upaṭṭhānasālā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi||
nisajja kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

9. Ayam pi kho bhikkhave ānāpānasatisamādhi bhāvito bahulīkato santo ceva paṇīto ca asecanako sukho ca vihāro uppannuppanne ca pāpake akusale dhamme ṭhānaso antaradhāpeti vūpasameti|| ||

10. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave gimhānam pacchime māse ūhataɱ rajojallaɱ tam enam mahā akālamegho ṭhānaso antaradhāpeti vūpasamati||
Evam eva kho bhikkhave ānāpānasati samādhi bhāvito bahulīkato santo ceva paṇīto ca asecanako ca sukho ca viharo uppannuppanne pāpake akusale dhamme ṭhānaso antaradhāpeti vūpasameti

[page 322]

11. Katham bhāvito ca bhikkhave ānāpānasatisamādhi katham bahulīkato santo ceva paṇīto ca asecanako ca sukho ca vihāro uppannuppanne ca pāpake akusale dhamme ṭhānaso antaradhāpeti vūpasameti|| ||

12—18. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu araññagato vā rukkhamūlagato vā suññāgāragato vā ... pe ...vitthāretabbaɱ||
paṭinissaggānupassī passasissāmī ti sikkhati|| ||

19. Evam bhāvito kho bhikkhave ānāpānasatisamādhi evam bahulīkato santo ceva paṇīto ca asecanako sukho ca vihāro uppannuppanne ca pāpake akusale dhamme ṭhānaso antaradhāpeti vūpasametī ti|| ||

 

 

10. Kimbila

1. Evaɱ me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Kimbilāyam viharati Veḷuvane|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā āyasmantaɱ Kimbilam āmantesi||
Katham bhāvito nu kho Kimbila ānāpānasatisamādhi katham bahulīkato mahapphalo hoti mahānisaɱso ti|| ||

Evaɱ vutte āyasmā Kimbilo tuṇhī ahosi|| ||

3. Dutiyam pi kho Bhagavā|| ||

4. Tatiyam pi kho Bhagavā āyasmantam Kimbilam āmantesi||
Katham bhāvito nu kho Kimbila ānāpānasatisamādhi katham bahulīkato mahapphalo hoti mahānisaɱso ti|| ||

Tatiyam pi kho āyasmā Kimbilo tuṇhī ahosi|| ||

[page 323]

5. Evaɱ vutte āyasmā Ānando Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Etassa Bhagavā kālo||
etassa Sugata kālo yam Bhagavā ānāpānasatisamādhim bhāveyya||
Bhagavato sutvā bhikkhū dhāressantī ti|| ||

Tenahānanda suṇāhi sādhukam manasi karohi bhāsissāmī ti|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavato paccassosi|| ||

6. Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

Katham bhāvito ca Ānanda ānāpānasatisamādhi katham bahulīkato mahapphalo hoti mahānisaɱso|| ||

7—13. Idhānanda bhikkhu araññagato vā rukkhamūlagato vā suññāgāragato vā —pe— paṭinissaggānupassī passasissāmī ti sikkhati|| ||

14. Evam bhāvito kho Ānanda ānāpānasatisamādhi evam bahulīkato mahapphalo hoti mahānisaɱso|| ||

15. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu dīghaɱ vā assasanto Dīgham assasāmīti pajānāti||
dīghaɱ vā passasanto Dīgham passasāmīti pajānā ti||
rassaɱ vā assasanto Rassam assasāmīti pajānāti||
rassam vā passasanto Rassam passasāmīti pajānā ti||
sabbakāyapaṭisaɱvedī Assasissāmī ti sikkhati||
sabbakāyapaṭisaɱvedī Passasissāmī ti sikkhati||
passam bhayaɱ kāyasaŋkhāram Assasissāmī ti sikkhati||
passam bhayam kāyasaŋkhāram Passasissāmī ti sikkhati||
kāye kāyanupassī Ānanda bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam||
taɱ kissa hetu|| ||

16. Kāyaññatarāham Ānanda etaɱ vadami yadidam assāsapassāsaɱ||
tasmā ti hānanda kāye kāyānupassī bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

17. Tasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu {pītipaṭisaɱvedī} Assasissāmī ti sikkhati||
pītipaṭisaɱvedī Passasissāmī ti sikkhati||
sukhapaṭisaɱvedī Assasissāmī ti sikkhati||
{sukhapaṭisaɱvedī} Passasissāmī ti sikkhati||
cittasaŋkhārapaṭisaɱvedī Assasissāmī ti sikkhati

[page 324]

cittasaŋkhārapaṭisaɱvedī Passasissāmī ti sikkhati||
passam bhayaɱ cittasaŋkhāram Assasissāmī ti sikkhati||
passam bhayaɱ cittasaŋkhāram Passasissāmī ti sikkhati||
Vedānāsu vedanānupassī Ānanda bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpi sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
taɱ kissa hetu|| ||

18. Vedanāññatarāham Ānanda etam vadāmi yad idaɱ assāsapassāsaɱ sādhukam manasikāraɱ||
tasmā ti hānanda vedanāsu vedanānupassī bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

19. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu cittapaṭisaɱvedī Assasissāmī ti sikkhati||
cittapaṭisaɱvedī Passasissāmī ti sikkhati||
abhippamodoyaɱ cittam ... pe ... samādaham cittam||
vimocayaɱ cittam Assasissāmī ti sikkhati||
vimocayaɱ cittam Passasissāmī ti sikkhati|| ||

Citte cittānupassī Ānanda bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassam||
taɱ kissa hetu|| ||

20. Nāham Ānanda muṭṭhassatissa asampajānassa ānāpānasatisamādhibhāvanaɱ vadāmi||
tasmā ti hānanda citte cittānupassī bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

21. {Yasmiɱ} samaye Ānanda bhikkhu aniccānupassī Assasissāmī ti sikkhati ... pe ... virāgānupassī||
nirodhānupassī||
paṭinissaggānupassī Assasissāmiti sikkhati||
paṭinissaggānupassī Passasissāmī ti sikkhati||
dhammesu dhammānupassī Ānanda bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
so yaɱ taɱ hoti abhijjhādomanassānam pahānam tam paññāya divā sādhukam ajjhupekkhitā hoti||
tasmā ti hānanda dhammesu dhammānupassī bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

[page 325]

22. Seyyathā pi Ānanda catumahāpathe mahāpaɱsupuñjo puratthimāya ce pi disāya āgaccheyya sakaṭam vā ratho vā upahanateva tam paɱsupuñjaɱ|| ||

acchimāya ce pi disāya āgaccheyya||
... pe... uttarāya ce pi disāya||
dakkhiṇāya ce pi disāya āgaccheyya sakaṭaɱ vā ratho vā upahanateva tam paɱsupuñjaɱ||
evam eva kho Ānanda bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharanto pi upahanateva pāpake akusale dhamme||
vedanāsu||
... pe ...||
citte||
dhammesu dhammānupassī viharanto pi upahanateva pāpake akusale dhamme ti|| ||

Ānāpānasaɱyuttassa ekadhammavaggo pathamo|| ||

Tassa uddānaɱ||
Ekadhammo ca Bojjhaŋgo||
Suddhakañ ca duve Pha... pe ...||
Ariṭṭho Kappino Dīpo||
Vesālī Kimbilena cā ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter II. Vaggo Dutiyo

11. Icchānaŋgalam

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Icchānaŋgale viharati Icchānaŋgalavanasaṇḍe|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi||
Icchāmaham bhikkhave temāsam paṭisalliyituɱ||
namhi kenaci upasaŋkamitabbo||
aññatra ekena piṇḍapātanihārakenā ti|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho te bhikkhū Bhagavato paṭissutvā nāssudha koci Bhagavantam upasaŋkamati aññatra ekena piṇḍapātanihārakena|| ||

[page 326]

3. Atha kho Bhagavā tassa temāsassa accayena paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Sa ce vo bhikkhave aññatitthiyā paribbājakā evam puccheyyuɱ||
Katamena āvuso vihārena Samaṇo Gotamo vassāvāsam bahulaɱ vihāsī ti||
evam puṭṭhā tumhe bhikkhave tesam aññatitthiyānam paribbājakānam evam vyākareyyātha||
Ānāpānasatisamādhinā kho āvuso Bhagavā vassāvāsam bahulaɱ vihāsī ti|| ||

4. Idhāham bhikkhave sato assasāmi sato passassāmi|| ||

5—10. Dīgham vā assasanto Dīgham assasāmī ti pajānāmi||
dīghaɱ vā passasanto Dīgham passasāmī ti pajānāmi ... pe ...paṭinissaggānupassī Assasissāmī ti pajānāmi||
paṭinissaggānupassī Passasissāmī ti pajānāmī|| ||

11. Yañ hi tam bhikkhave sammāvadamāno vadeyya ariyavihāro iti pi brahmavihāro iti pi tathagātavihāro iti pi||
ānāpānasatisamādhiɱ sammāvadamāno vadeyya ariyavihāro iti pi brahmavihāro iti pi Tathāgatavihāro iti pi|| ||

12. Ye te bhikkhave bhikkhū sekhā appattamānasā anuttaraɱ yogakkhemaɱ patthayamānā viharanti||
tesam ānāpānasatisamādhi bhāvito bahulīkato āsavānaɱ khayāya saɱvattati||
ye ca kho te bhikkhave bhikkhū arahanto khīṇāsavā vusitavanto katakaraṇīyā ohitabhārā anuppattasadatthā parikkhīṇabhavasaŋyojanā sammadaññā vimuttā||
tesam ānāpānasatisamādhi bhāvito bahulīkato diṭṭheva dhamme sukhavihārāya ceva saɱvattati satisampajaññāya ca|| ||

13. Yañ hi tam bhikkhave sammāvadamāno vadeyya ariyavihāro iti pi brahmavihāro iti pi Tathāgatavihāro iti pi||
ānāpānasatisamādhi sammāvadamāno vadeyya ariyavihāro iti pi brahmavihāro iti pi Tathāgatavihāro iti pī ti|| ||

[page 327]

 

 

12. Kaŋkheyyam

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Lomasavaŋgīso Sakkesu viharati Kapilavatthusmiɱ Nigrodhārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho Mahānāmo sakko yenāyasmā Lomasavaŋgīso tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantam Lomasavaŋgīsam abhivādetvā ekam antam nisīdi||
eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Mahānāmo sakko āyasmantam Lomasavaŋgīsam etad avoca|| ||

3. So eva nu kho bhante sekho vihāro so Tathāgatavihāro udāhu añño sekho vihāro añño Tathāgatavihāro ti|| ||

Na kho āvuso Mahānāma sveva sekho vihāro so Tathāgatavihāro||
añño kho āvuso Mahānāma sekho vihāro añño Tathāgatavihāro|| ||

4. Ye te āvuso Mahānāma bhikkhū sekhā appattamānasā anuttaraɱ yogakkhemam patthayamānā viharanti||
te pañcanīvaraṇe pahāya viharanti||
katame pañca|| ||

Kāmacchandanīvaraṇam pahāya viharanti|| ||

Vyāpādanīvaraṇaɱ ... pe ... Thīnamiddhanīvaraṇam||
Uddhaccakukkuccanīvaraṇaɱ||
Vicikicchānīvaraṇam pahāya viharanti|| ||

Ye pi te āvuso Mahānāma bhikkhū sekhā appattamānasā anuttaraɱ yogakkhemam patthayamānā viharanti||
te ime pañca nīvaraṇe pahāya viharanti|| ||

5. Ye ca kho te āvuso Mahānāma bhikkhū arahanto khīnāsavā vusitavanto katakaraṇīyā ohitabhārā anuppattasadatthā parikkhīṇabhavasaŋyojanā sammadaññā vimuttā tesam pañcanīvaraṇā pahīnā ucchinnamūlā tālāvatthukatā anabhāvakatā āyatim anuppādadhammā||
katame pañca|| ||

Kāmacchandanīvaraṇam pahīnam ucchinnamūlam tālāvatthukatam anabhāvakatā āyatim anuppādadhammaɱ||
Vyāpādanīvaraṇam pahīnaɱ ... pe ... Thīnamiddhanīvaraṇaɱ||
Uddhaccakukkuccanīvaraṇaɱ|| ||

Vicikicchānīvaraṇam pahīnam ucchinnamūlam talāvatthukatam anabhāvakatam āyatim anuppādadhammaɱ

[page 328]

Ye te āvuso Mahānāma bhikkhū arahanto khīnāsavā vusitavanto katakaraṇīyā ohitabharā anuppattasadatthā parikkhiṇabhavasaŋyojanā sammadaññā vimuttā||
tesam ime pañcanīvaraṇā pahīnā ucchinnamūlā tālāvatthukatā anabhāvakatā āyatim anuppādadhammā|| ||

6. Tad aminā petam āvuso Mahānāma pariyāyena veditabbaɱ||
yathā añño va sekho vihāro añño Tathāgatavihāro|| ||

7. Ekam idāham āvuso Mahānāma samayam Bhagavā Icchānaŋgale viharati Icchānaŋgalavanasaṇḍe|| ||

8. Tatra kho āvuso Mahānāma Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi-|| ||

9. Atha kho Bhagavā°||
10. Idhāham bhikkhave°||
11—16. Dīghaɱ vā assasanto°||
17. Yañ hi tam bhikkhave°||
18. Ye te bhikkhave bhikkhū sekhā°||
19. Yañ hi tam bhikkhave° °Tathāgatavihāro iti pī ti|| ||

20. Iminā kho etam āvuso Mahānāma pariyāyena veditabbaɱ||
yathā añño va sekho vihāro añño Tathāgatavihāro ti|| ||

 

 

13. Ānanda 1

1—2. Sāvatthi|| ||

Atha kho āyasmā Ānando yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami ... pe ... eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

[page 329]

3. Atthi nu kho bhante eko dhammo bhāvito bahulīkato cattāro dhamme paripūreti||
cattāro dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā satta dhamme paripūrenti||
satta dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā dve dhamme paripūrentī ti|| ||

Atthi kho Ānanda eko dhammo bhāvito bahulīkato cattāro dhamme paripūreti||
cattāro dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā satta dhamme paripūrenti||
satta dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā dve dhamme paripūrentī ti|| ||

4. Katamo pana bhante ekodhammo bhāvito bahulīkato cattāro dhamme paripūreti||
cattāro dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā satta dhamme paripūrenti||
sattā dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā dve dhamme paripūrentī ti|| ||

Ānāpānasatisamādhi kho Ānanda eko dhammo bhāvito bahulīkato cattāro satipaṭṭhāne paripūreti||
cattāro satipaṭṭhānā bhāvitā bahulīkatā satta bojjhaŋge paripūrenti||
satta bojjhaŋgā bhāvitā bahulīkatā vijjāvimuttim paripūrenti|| ||

I.

5. Katham bhāvito ānāpānasatisamādhi katham bahulīkato cattāro satipaṭṭhāne paripūreti|| ||

6—12. Idhānanda bhikkhu araññagato vā rukkhamulagato vā suññāgāragato vā ... pe ...vitthāro||
patinisaggānupassī Passasissāmī ti sikkhati|| ||

13. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu dīghaɱ vā assasanto Dīgham assasāmī ti pajānāti||
dīghaɱ vā passasanto Dīgham passasāmī ti pajānāti||
pe-la-|| passambhayam kāyasaŋkhāram assāsissāmī ti sikkhati||
passambhayam kāyasaŋkhāram passasissāmī ti sikkhati||
kāye kāyānupassī Ānanda bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

14. Kāyaññatarāham Ānanda etam vadāmi yad idam assāsapassāsaɱ

[page 330]

tasmā ti ha Ānanda kāye kāyānupassī bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyyaloke abhijjhadomanassaɱ|| ||

15. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu pītipaṭisaɱvedī Assasissāmī ti sikkhati||
sukhapaṭisaɱvedī||
cittasaŋkhāra{paṭisaɱvedī}||
passam bhayaɱ cittasaŋkhāram Assasissāmī ti sikkhati||
passam bhayam cittasaŋkhāram Passasissāmī ti sikkhati||
Vedanāsu vedanānupassī Ānanda bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyyaloke abhijjhādomanassaɱ||
taɱ kissa hetu|| ||

16. Vedanāññatarāham Ānanda etaɱ vadāmi yad idam assāsapassāsānam sādhukam manasikāraɱ||
tasmā ti ha Ānanda vedanāsu vedanānupassī bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

17. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu {cittapaṭisaɱvedī} Assasissāmī ti sikkhati ... pe ...abhippamodayaɱ cittaɱ||
samodahaɱ cittaɱ Assasissāmī ti sikkhati||
vimocayaɱ cittam Assasissāmi ti sikkhati||
vimocayaɱ cittam Passasissāmī ti sikkhati||
citte cittānupassī Ānanda bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhadomanassam||
taɱ kissa hetu|| ||

18. Nāham Ānanda muṭṭhassatissa asampajānassa ānāpānasatisamādhibhāvanaɱ vadāmi||
tasmā ti hānanda citte cittānupassī bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādemanassaɱ|| ||

19. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu aniccānupassī||
... pe ...||
virāgānupassī||
nirodhānupassī||
paṭinissaggānupassī assasissāmī ti sikkhati||
paṭinissaggānupassī passasissāmī ti sikkhati||
dhammesu dhammānupassī Ānanda bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

So yan taɱ hoti abhijjhādomanassānam pahānaɱ tam paññāya disvā sādhukam ajjhupekkhitā hoti

[page 331]

tasmā ti hānanda dhammesu dhammānupassī bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

20. Evam bhāvito kho Ānanda ānāpānasatisamādhi evam bahulīkato cattāro satipaṭṭhāne paripūreti|| ||

II.

21. Katham bhāvitā ca Ānanda cattāro satipaṭṭhānā katham bahulīkatā satta bojjhaŋge paripūrenti|| ||

22. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati upaṭṭhitasati tasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhuno sati hoti asammuṭṭhā||
yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhuno upaṭṭhitā sati asammuṭṭhā satisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
satisambojjhaŋgaɱ tasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu bhāveti||
satisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati||
so tathāsato viharanto taɱ dhammam paññāya pavicinati pavicarati parivīmaɱsam āpajjati|| ||

23. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu tathā sato viharanto tam dhammam paññāya pavicinati parivīmaɱsam āpajjati||
dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgaɱ tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti|| ||

Dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanāpāripūrim gacchati||
tassa taɱ dhammam paññāya pavicinato pavicarato parivīmaɱsam āpajjato āraddhaɱ hoti viriyam asallīnaɱ|| ||

24. Yasmim samaye Ānanda bhikkhuno taɱ dhammam paññāya pavicinato pavicarato parivīmaɱsam āpajjato āraddhaɱ hoti viriyam asallīnaɱ

[page 332]

viriyasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
viriyasambojjhaŋgaɱ tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
viriyasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati||
āraddhaviriyassa uppajjati pīti nirāmisā|| ||

25. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhuno āraddhaviriyassa uppajjati pīti nirāmisā||
pītisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
pītisambojjhaŋgaɱ tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
pītisambojjhaŋgo tasmim samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati||
pītimanassa kāyo pi passambhati cittam pi passambhati|| ||

26. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhuno pītimanassa kāyo pi passambhati||
cittam pi passambhati||
passaddhisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
passaddhisambojjhaŋgam tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
passaddhisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati||
passaddhakāyassa sukhino cittaɱ samādhiyati|| ||

27. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhuno passaddhakāyassa sukhino cittaɱ samādhiyati||
samādisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhune āraddho hoti||
samādhisambojjhaŋgaɱ tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
samādhisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati|| ||

So tathā samāhitaɱ cittam sādhukam ajjhupekkhitā hoti|| ||

28. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu tathā samāhitaɱ cittaɱ sādhukam ajjhupekkhitā hoti||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgam tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūrim gacchati|| ||

29. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu vedanāsu citte||
dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati upaṭṭhitasati tasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhuno sati hoti asammuṭṭhā|| ||

[page 333]

30. Yasmim samaye Ānanda bhikkhuno upatthitā sati hoti asammuṭṭhā||
satisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
satisambojjhaŋgaɱ tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
satisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati|| ||

Yathā pathamaɱ satipaṭṭhānam evaɱ vitthāretabbaɱ|| ||

So tathā samāhitaɱ cittaɱ sādhukam ajjhupekkhitā hoti|| ||

31. Yasmiɱ samaye Ānanda bhikkhu tathā samāhitaɱ cittaɱ sādhukam ajjhupekkhitā hoti||
upekhasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgaɱ tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
upekhāsambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati|| ||

32. Evam bhāvitā kho Ānanda cattāro satipaṭṭhānā evam bahulīkatā sattabojjhaŋge paripūrenti|| ||

III.

33. Katham bhāvitā ca sattabhojjhaŋgā katham bahulīkatā vijjāvimuttim paripūrenti|| ||

34. Idhānanda bhikkhu satisambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekanissitam ... pe ... upekhāsambojjhaŋgam bhāveti vivekanissitaɱ virāganissitaɱ nirodhanissitam vossaggapariṇāmiɱ|| ||

35. Evam bhāvitā kho Ānanda sattabojjhaŋgā evam bahulīkatā vijjāvimuttim paripūrentī ti|| ||

 

 

14. Ānanda 2

... pe ...||
eka-m-antaɱ ni° Ānandam Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

satta dhammā bhāvitā bahulīkatā dve dhamme paripūrentī ti|| ||

Bhagavammūlakā no bhante dhammā||
... pe ...|| ||

pā||
virāgānupassī||

so yan taɱ hoti abhijjhādomanassānam pahānaɱ tam paññāya disvā sādhu ajjhupekkhitā hoti||
tasmā ti ha bhikkhave dhammesu dhammānupassī bhikkhu tasmiɱ samaye viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaɱ|| ||

21. Katham bhāvitā ca bhikkhave cattāro satipaṭṭhānā katham bahulīkatā satta bojjhaŋge paripūrenti|| ||

yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhave bhikkhuno upaṭṭhitā sati hoti asammuṭṭhā

[page 338]

satisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
satisambojjhaŋgaɱ tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
satisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūrim gacchati||
so tathā sato viharanto taɱ dhammam paññāya pavicinati pavicarati parivīmaɱsam āpajjatī|| ||

23. Yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhave bhikkhu tathā sato viharanto taɱ dhammam paññāya pacinati pavicarati parivīmaɱsam āpajjati||
dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgam tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
dhammavicayasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūrim gacchati||
tassa taɱ dhammam paññāya pavicinato pavicarato parivīmaɱsam āpajjato āraddham hoti viriyam asallīnaɱ|| ||

24. Yasmim samaye bhikkhave bhikkhuno tam dhammam paññāya pavicinato pavicarato parivīmaɱsam āpajjato araddhaɱ hoti viriyam asallīnaɱ||
viriyasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti {viriyasambojjhaŋgaɱ} tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
viriyasambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati||
āraddhaviriyassa uppajjati pīti nirāmisā|| ||

25. Yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhave bhikkhuno āraddhaviriyassa uppajjati pīti nirāmisā||
pītisambojjhaŋgo tasmim samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
pītisambojjhaŋgaɱ tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti||
pītisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūrim gacchati|| ||

Pītimanassa kāyo pi passambhati cittam pi passambhati|| ||

26. Yasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno pītimanassa kāyo pi passambhati cittam pi passambhati||
passaddhisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno āraddho hoti||
passaddhisambojjhaŋgaɱ tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhu bhāveti

[page 339]

passaddhisambojjhaŋgo tasmiɱ samaye bhikkhuno bhāvanā pāripūriɱ gacchati|| ||

Book XI

Sotāpatti Saɱyutta

Chapter I. Veḷudvāra Vaggo

1. Rājā

1—2. Sāvatthi|| ||

Tatra kho etad avoca|| ||

3. Kiñcāpi bhikkhave rājā cakkavatti catunnaɱ dīpānam issariyādhipaccam rajjaɱ kāretvā kāyassa bhedā parammaraṇā sugatim saggaɱ lokam upapajjati devānaɱ Tāvatiɱsānaɱ sahavyataɱ||
so tattha Nandane vane accharāsaŋghaparivuto dibbehi ca pañcahi kāmaguṇehi samappito {samaŋgibhūto} paricāreti||
so catuhi dhammehi asamannāgato|| ||

Atha kho so aparimutto ca nirayā aparimutto ca tiracchānayoniso||
aparimutto ca pettivisayā||
aparimutto ca apāyaduggativinipātā|| ||

4. Kiñcāpi bhikkhave ariyasāvako piṇḍiyā lopena yāpeti nantakāni ca dhāreti||
so catuhi dhammehi samannāgato|| ||

Atha kho so parimutto ca nirayā||
parimutto ca tiracchayoniyā||
parimutto ca pittivisayā||
parimutto ca apāyaduggativinipātā|| ||

Katamehi catuhi?|| ||

[page 343]

5. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako buddhe avecca pasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti piso Bhagavā arahaɱ sammāsambuddho vijjācaraṇasampanno sugato lokavidū anuttaro purisadhammasārathi satthā devamanussānam buddho bhāgavā ti|| ||

6. Dhamme avecca pasādena samannāgato hoti|| ||

Svākkhāto Bhagavatā dhammo sandiṭṭhiko akāliko ehipassiko opanayiko paccattam veditabbo viññāhī ti|| ||

7. Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannāgato hoti|| ||

Suppaṭipanno Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho||
ujupaṭipanno Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho||
ñāyapaṭipanno Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho||
sāmīcipaṭipanno Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho||
yad idaɱ cattāri purisayugāni aṭṭhapurisapuggalā esa Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho||
āhuneyyo pāhuneyyo dakkhiṇeyyo añjalīkaraṇīyo anuttaram puññakhettaɱ lokassā ti|| ||

8. Ariyakantehi sīlehi samaññāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi acchiddehi asabalehi akammāsehi bhūjissehi viññūpasatthehi aparāmaṭṭhehi samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

9. Imehi catuhi dhammehi samannāgato hoti|| ||

10. Yo ca bhikkhave catunnam dīpānam paṭilābho yo ca catunnaɱ dhammānam paṭilābho|| ||

Catunnaɱ dīpānam paṭilābho catunnaɱ dhammānam paṭilābhassa kalaɱ nagghati soḷasinti|| ||

 

 

2. Ogadha or Saṭayhaɱ

3. Catuhi bhikkhave dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sotāpanno hoti avinīpātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano|| ||

Katamehi catuhi?|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti|| ||

Iti pi so Bhagavā arahaɱ ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

5—6. Dhamme||
{Saŋgho}|| ||

7. Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti||
akhaṇḍehi||
... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

[page 344]

8. Imehi kho bhikkhave catuhi dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sotāpanno hoti avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

9. Idam avoca Bhagavā idam vatvā Sugato etad avoca satthā|| ||

Yesaɱ saddhā ca sīlañca||
pasādo dhammadassanaɱ||
te ve kāle na paccanti||
brahmacariyogadhaɱ sukhan ti|| ||

 

 

3. Dighāvu

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Veḷuvane Kalandakanivāpe|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Dīghāvu upāsako ābādhiko hoti dukkhito bāḷhagilāno|| ||

3. Atha kho Dīghāvu upāsako pitaraɱ Jotikaɱ gahapatim āmantesi||
Ehi tvaɱ gahapati yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkama||
upasaŋkamitvā mama vacanena Bhagavato pāde sīrasā vanda||
Dīghāvu bhante upāsako ābādhiko hoti dukkhito bāḷhagilāno||
so Bhagavato pāde sirasā vandati|| ||

Evaɱ ca vadehi Sādhu kira bhante Bhagavā yena Dīghāvussa upāsakassa nivesanaɱ tenupasaŋkamatu anukampam upādāyāti|| ||

Evaɱ tātā ti kho Jotiko gahapati Dīghāvussa upāsakassa paṭissutvā yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

4. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Jotiko gahapati Bhagavantam etad avoca||
Dīghāvu bhante upāsako ābādhiko hoti dukkhito bāḷhagilāno|| ||

So Bhagavato pāde sirasā vandati||
evañca vadeti Sādhu kira bhante Bhagavā yena Dīghāvussa upāsakassa nivesanaɱ tenupasaŋkamatu anukampam upādāyāti|| ||

Adhivāsesi Bhagavā tuṇhībhāvena|| ||

5. Atha kho Bhagavā nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya yena Dīghāvussa upāsakassa nivesanaɱ tenupasaŋkami||

[page 345]

upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi||
nisajja kho Bhagavā Dīghāvum upāsakam etad avoca|| ||

Kacci te Dīghāvu khamanīyam kacci yāpanīyaɱ kacci dukkhā vedanā paṭikkamanti no abhikkamanti patikkamo sānam paññāyati no abhikkamoti|| ||

Na me bhante khamanīyaɱ na yāpanīyaɱ baḷhā me dukkhā abhikkamanti no patikkamanti abhikkamo sānam paññāyati no paṭikkamo ti|| ||

6. Tasmā ti ha te Dīghāvu evaɱ sikkhitabbaɱ||
Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato bhavissāmi||
Iti pi so Bhagavā arahaɱ ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
... pe ...|| ||

Dhamme||
... pe...||
Saŋghe||
... pe...||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato bhavissāmi akhaṇḍehi ... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

Evañhi te Dīghāvu sikkhitabban ti|| ||

7. Yānimāni bhante Bhagavatā cattāri sotāpattiyaŋgāni desitāni||
saɱvijjante te dhammā mayi ahañ ca tesu sandissāmi||
ahañ hi bhante buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato akhaṇḍehi ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikehī ti|| ||

Tasmā ti ha tvam Dīghāvu imesu catusu sotāpattiyaŋgesu patiṭṭhāya cha vijjābhāgiye dhamme {uttariɱ bhāveyyāsi}|| ||

8. Idha tvam Dīghāvu sabbesaŋkhāresu aniccānupassī viharāhi||
anicce dukkhasaññī dukkhe anattasaññī pahānasaññī virāgasaññī nirodhasaññī ti|| ||

Evaɱ hi te Dīghāvu sikkhitabban ti|| ||

Ye me bhante Bhagavatā cha vijjābhāgiyā dhammā desitā||
saɱvijjante te dhammā mayi ahaɱ ca tesu dhammesu sandissāmi||
ahañhi bhante sabbasaŋkhāresu aniccānupassī viharāmi||
anicce dukkhasaññī dukkhe anattasaññī pahānasaññī virāgasaññī nirodhasaññī|| ||

9. Api ca me bhante evaɱ hoti māhevāyaɱ Jotiko gahapati mamaccayena vighātam āpajjīti|| ||

[page 346]

Mā tvaɱ tāta Dīghāvu evam manasākāsi|| ||

Iŋgha tvaɱ tāta Dīghāvu yad eva te Bhagavā āha tad eva tvaɱ sādhukam manasi karohī ti|| ||

10. Atha kho Bhagavā Dīghāvum upāsakam iminā ovādena ovaditvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkāmi|| ||

11. Atha kho Dīghāvu upāsako acirapakkantassa Bhagavato kālam akāsi|| ||

12. Atha kho sambahulā bhikkhū yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu||
eka-m-antaɱ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū Bhagavantam etad avocuɱ||
Yo so bhante Dīghāvu nāma upāsako Bhagavatā saŋkhittena ovādena ovādito so kālaŋkato||
tassa kā gati ko abhisamparāyo ti|| ||

Paṇḍito bhikkhave Dīghāvu upāsako ahosi paccapādi dhammassānudhammaɱ na ca dhammādhikaraṇaɱ vihesesi|| ||

13. Dīghāvu bhikkhave upāsako pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā opapātiko hoti tattha parinibbāyi anāvattidhammo tasmā lokā ti|| ||

 

 

4. Sāriputta 1

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā ca Sāriputto ayasmā ca Ānando Sāvatthiyaɱ viharanti Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando sāyaṇhasamayaɱ paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito||
... pe ...|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Ānando āyasmantaɱ Sāriputtam etad avoca|| ||

3. Katīnam nu kho āvuso Sāriputta dhammānam samannāgamanahetu evam ayam pajā Bhagavatā vyākatā sotāpannā avinipātadhammā niyatā sambodhiparāyanā ti|| ||

[page 347]

Catunnaɱ kho āvuso dhammānaɱ samannāgamanahetu evam ayam pajā Bhagavatā vyākatā sotāpannā avinipātadhammā niyatā sambodhiparāyanā||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

4. Idhāvuso ariyasāvako buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti|| ||

Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
{Saŋghe}||
ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

5. Imesaɱ kho āvuso catunnaɱ dhammānaɱ samannāgamanahetu evam ayam pajā Bhagavatā vyākatā sotāpannā avinipātadhammā niyatā sambodhiparāyanā ti|| ||

 

 

5. Sāriputta 2

2. Atha kho āyasmā Sāriputto yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnaɱ kho āyasmantaɱ Sāriputtam Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

3. Sotāpattiyaŋgaɱ sotāpattiyaŋgan ti hidaɱ Sāriputta vuccati||
katamaɱ nu kho Sāriputta sotapattiyaŋgan ti|| ||

Sappurisasaɱsevo hi bhante sotāpattiyaŋgaɱ||
saddhammasavanaɱ sotāpattiyaŋgaɱ||
yonisomanasikāro sotāpattiyaŋgaɱ||
dhammānudhammapaṭipatti sotāpattiyaŋgan ti|| ||

Sādhu Sāriputta sādhu Sāriputta||
sappurisasaɱsevo-dhammānudhammapaṭipatti sotāpattiyaŋgaɱ|| ||

4. Soto soto ti ha Sāriputta vuccati||
katamo nu kho Sāriputta soto ti|| ||

Ayam eva hi bhante ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo soto||
seyyathīdaɱ||
sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ... sammāsamādhī ti|| ||

Sādhu sādhu Sāriputta||
ayam eva hi Sāriputta ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo soto||
seyyathīdaɱ||
sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ...||
sammāsamādhi|| ||

[page 348]

5. Sotāpanno sotāpanno ti hidaɱ Sāriputta vuccati||
katamo nu kho Sāriputta sotāpanno ti|| ||

Yo hi bhante iminā ariyena aṭṭhaŋgikena maggena samannāgato||
ayaɱ vuccati sotāpanno yoyam āyasmā evaɱ nāmo evaɱ gotto ti|| ||

Sādhu sādhu Sāriputta yo hi Sāriputta iminā ariyena aṭṭhaŋgikena maggena samannāgato ayaɱ vuccati sotāpanno yoyaɱ āyasmā evaɱnāmo evaɱgotto ti|| ||

 

 

6. Thapatayo

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena sambahulā bhikkhū Bhagavato cīvarakammam karonti Niṭṭhitacīvaro Bhagavā temāsaccayena cārikam pakkamissatī tī|| ||

3. Tena kho pana samayena Isidattapurāṇā thapatayo Sādhuke paṭivasanti kenacid eva karaṇīyena||
assosuɱ kho Isidattapurāṇā thapatayo Sambahulā kira bhikkhū Bhagavato cīvarakammaɱ karonti Niṭṭhitacīvaro Bhagavā temāsaccayena cārikam pakkamissatī ti|| ||

4. Atha kho Isidattapurāṇā thapatayo magge purisaɱ ṭhapesuɱ||
Yadā tvam ambho purisa passeyyāsi Bhagavantam āgacchantam arahantaɱ sammāsambuddhaɱ||
atha kho amhākam āroceyyāsī ti|| ||

5. Dvīhatīhaɱ ṭhito kho so puriso addasa Bhagavantaɱ dūrato va āgacchantam||
disvā yena Isidattapurāṇā thapatayo tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Isidattapurāṇe thapatayo etad avoca||
Ayaɱ so bhante Bhagavā āgacchati arahaɱ sammāsambuddho||
yassa dāni kālam maññathā ti|| ||

6. Atha kho Isidattapurāṇā thapatayo yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā Bhāgavantam piṭṭhito pitthito anubandhiɱsu|| ||

7. Atha kho Bhagavā maggā okkamma yena aññataraɱ rukkhamūlaɱ tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi

[page 349]

Isidattapurāṇā pi kho thapatayo Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnā kho te Isidattapurāṇā thapatayo Bhagavantam etad avocuɱ|| ||

8. Yadā mayam bhante Bhagavantaɱ suṇāma Sāvatthiyā Kosalesu cārikam pakkamissatī ti||
hoti no tasmiɱ samaye anattamanatā hoti domanassaɱ Dūre no Bhagavā bhavissatī ti||
Yadā pana mayam bhante Bhagavantaɱ suṇāma Sāvatthiyā Kosalesu cārikam pakkanto tī||
hoti no tasmiɱ samaye anattamanatā hoti domanassaɱ Dūre no Bhagavā ti|| ||

9. Yadā mayam bhante Bhagavantaɱ suṇāma Kosalehi Malle cārikam pakkamissatī ti||
hoti no {tasmiɱ} samaye anattamatā hoti domanassaɱ Dūre no Bhagavā bhavissatī ti||
Yadā pana mayam bhante Bhagavantaɱ suṇāma Kosalehi Malle cārikam pakkanto ti||
hoti no tasmiɱ samaye anattamanatā hoti domanassaɱ Dūre no Bhagavā ti|| ||

10. Yadā mayam bhante suṇāma Bhagavantaɱ Mallehi Vajjim cārikam pakkamissatī ti||
hoti no tasmiɱ samaye anattamanatā hoti domanassaɱ Dūre no Bhagavā bhavissatī ti|| ||

Yadā pana mayam bhante Bhagavantaɱ suṇāma Mallehi Vajjiɱ cārikam pakkanto ti||
hoti no tasmiɱ samaye anattamanatā hoti domanassaɱ Dūre no Bhagavā ti|| ||

11. Yadā mayam bhante Bhagavantaɱ suṇāma Vajjīhi Kāsiɱ cārikam pakkamissatī ti||
hoti no tasmiɱ samaye anattamanatā hoti domanassaɱ Dūre no Bhagavā bhavissatī ti|| ||

Yadā pana mayam bhante Bhagavantaɱ suṇāma Vajjīhi Kāsim cārikam pakkanto ti||
hoti no tasmiɱ samaye anattamanatā hoti domanassaɱ Dūre no Bhagavā ti|| ||

12. Yadā mayam bhante Bhagavantam suṇāma Kāsīhi Magadhe cārikam pakkamissatī ti||
hoti no tasmiɱ samaye anattamanatā hoti domanassaɱ Dūre no Bhagavā bhavissatī ti

[page 350]

Yadā pana mayam bhante Bhagavantaɱ suṇāma Kāsīhi Māgadhe cārikam pakkanto ti hoti anappakā no tasmiɱ samaye anattamanatā hoti anappakaɱ domanassaɱ Dūre no Bhagavā ti|| ||

13. Yadā mayam bhante Bhagavantaɱ suṇāma Māgadhehi Kāsiɱ carikam pakkamissatī ti||
hoti no tasmiɱ samaye attamanatā hoti somanassaɱ Āsanne no Bhagavā bhavissatī ti|| ||

Yadā pana mayam bhante Bhagavantaɱ suṇāma Māgadhehi Kāsim cārikam pakkanto ti||
hoti no tasmiɱ samaye attamanatā hoti somanassaɱ Āsanne no Bhagavā ti|| ||

14. Yadā mayam bhante suṇoma Kāsīhi Vajjī ... pe ...|| ||

15. Vajjīhi [Malle]|| ||

16. Mallehi Kosale|| ||

17. Yadā pana bhante Bhagavantaɱ {suṇāma} Kosalehi Sāvatthiɱ cārikam pakkamissatī ti||
hoti no tasmiɱ samaye attamanatā hoti somanassam Āsanne no Bhagavā bhavissatī ti||
Yadā pana mayam bhante Bhagavantaɱ sunāma Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme ti||
anappakā no tasmiɱ samaye attamanatā hoti anappakaɱ somanassam Āsanne no Bhagavā ti|| ||

18. Tasmā ti ha thapatayo sambādho gharāvāso rajāpatho abbhokāso pabbajā alañca pana vo thapatayo appamādāyā ti|| ||

19. Atthi kho no bhante etamhā sambādhā añño sambādhataro ceva sambādhasaŋkhātataro cāti|| ||

[page 351]

Katamo pana vo thapatayo etamhā sambādhā añño sambādho sambādhataro ceva sambādhasaŋkhātataro cā ti|| ||

20. Idha mayam bhante yadā rājā Pasenadī Kosalo uyyānabhūmiɱ niyyātukāmo hoti||
ye te rañño Pasenadissa Kosalassa nāgā opavayhā te kappetvā yā tā rañño Pasenadissa Kosalassa pajāpatiyo piyā manāpā tā ekam purato ekam pacchato nisīdāpema|| ||

Tāsaɱ kho pana bhante bhāginīnam evarūpo gandho hoti seyyathāpi nāma gandhakaraṇḍakassa tāvad eva vivariyamānassa yathā taɱ rājakaññānaɱ gandhena vibhūsitānaɱ||
tāsaɱ kho pana bhante bhaginīnam evarūpo kāyasamphasso hoti seyyathāpi nāma thulapicuno vā yathā taɱ rājakaññānaɱ sukhedhitānaɱ||
tasmiɱ kho pana bhante samaye nāgo pi rakkhitabbo hoti||
tā pi bhaginiyo rakkhitabbā||
attā pi rakkhitabbo hoti|| ||

21. Na kho pana mayam bhante abhijānāma tāsu bhaginīsu pāpakaɱ cittam uppādetā||
ayaɱ kho no bhante etamhā sambādhā añño sambādho sambādhataro ceva sambādhasaŋkhātataro cā ti|| ||

22. Tasmā ti ha thapatayo sambādho gharāvāso rajāpatho abbhokāso pabbajā alaɱ ca pana vo thapatayo appamādāya|| ||

23. Catuhi kho thapatayo dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sotāpanno hoti avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano||
katamehi catuhi|| ||

24. Idha thapatayo ariyasāvako buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
... pe...||
Saŋghe||
vigatamalamaccherena cetasā agāram ajjhāvasati||
muttacāgo payatapāṇī vossaggarato yācayogo dānasaɱvibhāgarato|| ||

Ime hi kho thapatayo catuhi dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sotāpanno hoti avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano

[page 352]

25. Tumhe kho thapatayo Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānaɱ buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe||
Yaɱ kho pana kiñci kule deyyadhammaɱ sabban tam appaṭivibhattaɱ sīlavantehi kalyāṇadhammehi|| ||

26. Taɱ kim maññatha thapatayo||
katividhā te Kosalesu manussā ye tumhākaɱ samasamā yad idaɱ dāna{saɱvibhāge} ti|| ||

27. Lābhā no bhante suladdhaɱ no bhante yesaɱ no Bhagavā evam pajānātī ti|| ||

 

 

7. Veḷudvāreyyā

1. Evam me sutam ekam samayam Bhagavā Kosalesu cārikaɱ caramāno mahatā bhikkhusaŋghena saddhim yena Veḷudvāraɱ nāma Kosalānam brāhmaṇagāmo tad avasari|| ||

2. Assosuɱ kho te Veḷudvāreyyakā brāhmaṇagahapatikā Samaṇo khalu bho Gotamo sakyaputto sakyakulā pabbajito Kosalesu cārikaɱ caramāno mahatā bhikkhusaŋghena saddhiɱ Veḷudvāram anuppatto|| ||

Taɱ kho pana Bhagavantam Gotamam evaɱ kalyāṇakittisaddo abbhuggato||
Iti pi so Bhagavā arahaɱ sammāsambuddho vijjācaraṇasampanno sugato lokavidū anuttaro purisadammasārathi satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
so imaɱ lokam sadevakaɱ samārakaɱ sabrahmakam sassamaṇabrāhmaṇim pajam sadevamanussaɱ sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā pavedeti||
so dhammaɱ deseti ādikalyāṇam majjhe kalyāṇam pariyosāṇakalyānam sāttham savyañjanaɱ kevalaparipuṇṇam parisuddham brahmacariyam pakāseti|| ||

Sādhu kho pana tathārūpānam arahataɱ dassanaɱ hoti|| ||

[page 353]

3. Atha kho te Veḷudvāreyyakā brāhmaṇagahapatikā yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā appekacce Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu||
appekacce Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodiɱsu||
sammodaniyaɱ katham sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu||
appekacce yena Bhagavā tenañjaliɱ paṇāmetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu||
appekacce Bhagavato santike nāmagottaɱ sāvetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu||
appekacce tunhībhūtā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu|| ||

4. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnā kho te Veḷudvareyyākā brāhmaṇagahapatikā Bhagavantam etad avocuɱ|| ||

Mayam bho Gotama evaɱkāmā evaɱchandā evamadhippāyā||
puttasambādhasayanam ajjhāvaseyyāma||
kāsikacandanam paccanubhaveyyāma||
mālāgandhavilepanam dhāreyyāma||
jātarūparajataɱ sādiyeyyāma||
kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokam upapajjeyyāma|| ||

Tesaɱ no bhavaɱ Gotamo amhākam evaɱkāmānam evaɱchandānam evamadhippāyānaɱ tathā dhammaɱ desetu yathā mayaɱ puttasambādhasayanam ajjhāvaseyyāma ... pe ... sugatiɱ saggam lokam upapajjeyyāmā ti|| ||

5. Attūpanāyikaɱ vo gahapatayo dhammapariyāyaɱ desissāmi||
tam suṇātha||
sādhukam manasi karotha bhāsissāmī ti|| ||

Evam bho ti kho te Veḷudvāreyyakā brāhmaṇagahapatikā Bhagavato paccassosuɱ|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

Katamo gahapatayo attūpanāyiko dhammapariyāyo|| ||

6. Idha gahapatayo ariyasāvako iti paṭisañcikkhati||
Ahaɱ kho smi jīvitukāmo amaritukāmo sukhakāmo dukkhapaṭikkūlo||
yo kho maɱ jīvitukāmam amaritukāmaɱ sukhakāmaɱ dukkhapaṭikkūlam jīvitā voropeyya na me tam assa piyam manāpaɱ|| ||

Ahañceva kho pana paraɱ jīvitukāmam amaritukāmam sukhakāmam dukkhapaṭikūlaɱ jīvitā voropeyyam||
parassa tam assa appiyam amanāpaɱ|| ||

Yo kho myāyaɱ dhammo appiyo amanāpo parassa peso dhammo appiyo amanāpo

[page 354]

yo kho myāyam dhammo appiyo amanāpo kathāhaɱ paraɱ tena saɱyojeyyan ti|| ||

So iti paṭisaŋkhāya attanā ca pānātipātā paṭivirato hoti||
paraɱ ca pāṇātipātā veramaṇiyā samādapeti||
pāṇātipātā veramaṇiyā vaṇṇam bhāsati|| ||

Evam assāyaɱ kāyasamācāro ti koṭiparisuddho hoti|| ||

7. Puna ca param gahapatayo ariyasāvako iti paṭisañcikkhati|| ||

Yo kho me adinnam theyyasaŋkhātam ādiyeyya||
na me tam assa piyam manāpam||
ahaɱ ce va kho pana parassa adinnam theyyasaŋkhātam ādiyeyyaɱ||
parassa pi tam assa appiyam amanāpaɱ|| ||

Yo kho myāyaɱ dhammo appiyo amanāpo parassa peso dhammo appiyo amanāpo||
yo kho myāyaɱ dhammo appiyo amanāpo kathāham paraɱ tena saɱyojeyyanti|| ||

So iti paṭisaŋkhāya attānañca adinnādānā paṭivirato hoti||
parañca adinnādānā veramaṇiyā samādapeti||
adinnādānā veramaṇiyā ca vaṇṇam bhāsati|| ||

Evam assāyam kāyasamācāro ti koṭiparisuddho hoti|| ||

8. Puna ca param gahapatayo ariyasāvako iti paṭisañcikkhati|| ||

Yo kho me dāresu cārittam āpajjeyya||
na me tam assa piyam manāpam||
ahaɱ ceva kho pana parassa dāresu cārittam āpajjeyyaɱ||
parassa pi tam assa appiyam amanāpaɱ||
yo kho myāyaɱ dhammo appiyo amanāpo parassa peso dhammo appiyo amanāpo||
kathāham paraɱ tena saɱyojeyyan ti||
so iti paṭisaŋkhāya attanā ca kāmesu micchācārā paṭivirato hoti||
paraɱ ca kāmesu micchācārā veramaṇiyā samādapeti||
kāmesu micchācārā veramaṇiyā ca vaṇṇam bhāsati|| ||

Evam assāyaɱ kāyasamācāro ti koṭiparisuddho ti|| ||

9. Puna ca paraɱ gahapatayo ariyasāvako iti patisaɱcikkhati|| ||

Yo kho me musāvādena attham bhañjeyya na me tam assa piyam manāpaɱ||
ahañ ceva kho pana parassa musāvādena attham bhañjeyyam parassa pi tam assa appiyam amanāpaɱ|| ||

Yo kho myāyaɱ dhammo appiyo amanāpo||
parassa peso dhammo appiyo amanāpo||

[page 355]

yo kho myāyaɱ dhammo appiyo amanāpo||
kathāham paraɱ tena saɱyojeyyan ti|| ||

So iti paṭisaŋkhāya attanā ca musāvādā paṭivirato hoti||
parañ ca musāvādā veramaṇiyā samādapeti||
musāvādā veramaṇiyā vaṇṇam bhāsati|| ||

Evam assāyam vacīsamācāro ti koṭiparisuddho hoti|| ||

10. Puna ca paraɱ gahapatayo ariyasāvako iti paṭisañcikkhati|| ||

Yo kho maɱ pisuṇāya vācāya mittehi bhedeyya na me tam assa piyam manāpam||
ahañ ceva kho pana paraɱ pisuṇāya vācāya mittehi bhedeyyaɱ parassa pi tam assa appiyam amanāpam ... pe ... Evaɱ assāyaɱ vācīsamācāro ti koṭiparisuddho hoti|| ||

11. Puna ca paraɱ gahapatayo ariyasāvako iti paṭisañcikkhati|| ||

Yo kho mam pharusāya vācāya samudācareyya na me tam assa piyam manāpam||
ahañ ceva kho pana param pharusāya vācāya samudācareyyam parassa pi tam assa appiyam amanāpaɱ|| ||

Yo kho myāyaɱ dhammo||
... pe ...|| ||

Evam assāyaɱ vacīsamācāro ti koṭiparisuddho hoti|| ||

12. Puna ca paraɱ gahapatayo ariyasāvako iti paṭisañcikkhati||
Yo kho mam sampabhāsena samphappalāpabhāsena samudācareyya na me tam assa piyam manāpaɱ||
ahañ ceva kho pana param sampabhāsena samphappalāpabhāsena samudācareyya||
parassa pi tam assa appiyam amanāpaɱ|| ||

Yo kho myāyam dhammo appiyo amanāpo parassa peso dhammo appiyo amanāpo||
yo myāyam dhammo appiyo amanāpo kathāham paraɱ tena saɱyojeyyanti|| ||

So iti patisaŋkhāya attanāca samphappalāpā paṭivirato hoti||
paraɱ ca samphappalāpā veramaṇiyā samādapeti||
samphappalāpā veramaṇiyā ca vaṇṇam bhāsati|| ||

Evam assāyam vacīsamācāro ti koṭiparisuddho hoti|| ||

13. So Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... sattha devamanussānaɱ buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

[page 356]

14. Dhamme|| ||

15. Saŋghe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
supaṭipanno Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho ... pe ... anuttaram puññakkhettam lokassā ti|| ||

16. Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi||
... pe ...
{samādhisaɱvattanikehi}|| ||

17. Yato kho gahapatayo ariyasāvako imehi sattahi saddhammehi samannāgato hoti||
imehi catuhi ākaŋkhiyehi ṭhānehi so ākaŋkhamāno attanā vā attānaɱ vyākareyya Khīṇanirayo mhi khīṇatiracchānayoniko khīṇapittivisayo khīṇāpāyaduggativinipāto||
sotāpanno ham asmi avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

18. Evaɱ vutte Veḷudvāreyyakā brāhmaṇagahapatikā Bhagavantam etad avocuɱ|| ||

Abhikkantaɱ bho Gotama||
... pe ...||
ete mayam bhagavantaɱ Gotamaɱ saraṇaɱ gacchāma dhammañca bhikkhusaŋghañca||
Upāsake no bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pānupete saraṇaɱ gate ti|| ||

 

 

8. Giñjakāvasatha 1

1. Evaɱ me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Ñātike viharati Giñjakāvasathe|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam etad avoca||
Sāḷho nāma bhante bhikkhu kālakato tassa kā gati ko abhisamparāyo||
Nandā nāma bhante bhikkhunī kālakatā tassā kā gati ko abhisamparāyo||
Sudatto nāma bhante upāsako kālakato tassa kā gati ko abhisamparāyo||
Sujātā nāma bhante upāsikā kālakatā tassā kā gati ko abhisamparāyo ti|| ||

3. Sāḷho Ānanda bhikkhu kālakato asavānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim paññāvimuttiɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi|| ||

Nandā Ānanda bhikkhunī kālakatā pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā opapātikā tattha parinibbāyinī anāvattidhammā tasmā lokā

[page 357]

Sudatto Ānanda upāsako kālakato tiṇṇaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā rāgadosamohānaɱ tanuttā sakadāgāmī sakid eva imaɱ lokam āgantvā dukkhassantaɱ karissati|| ||

Sujātā Ānanda upāsikā kālakatā tiṇṇam saññojañānaɱ parikkhayā sotāpannā avinipātadhammā niyatā sambodhiparāyanā|| ||

4. Anacchariyaɱ kho panetam Ānanda yaɱ manussabhūto kālaɱ kareyya||
tasmim tasmiɱ ce maɱ kālakate upasaŋkamitvā etam attham paṭipucchissatha||
vihesā pesā Ānanda assa Tathāgatassa||
tasmā ti hānanda dhammādāsaɱ nāma dhammapariyāyaɱ desissāmi||
yena samannāgato ariyasāvako ākaŋkhamāno attanā vā attānaɱ vyākareyya Khīṇanirayo mhi khīṇatiracchānayoniko khīnapittivisayo khīṇāpāyaduggativinipāto||
sotāpanno hamasmi avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano|| ||

5. Katamo ca so Ānanda dhammādāso dhammapariyāyo||
yena samannāgato ariyasāvako ākaŋkhamāno attanā va attānaɱ vyākareyya||
Khīṇanirayo mhi sotāpanno hamasmi avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano|| ||

6. Idha Ānanda ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti|| ||

Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
dhamme||
saŋghe||
ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

7. Ayaɱ kho so Ānanda dhammādāso dhammapariyāyo||
yena samannāgato ariyasāvako ākaŋkhamāno attanā va attānaɱ vyākareyya khīṇanirayo mhi khīṇatiracchānayoniko khīnapittivisayo khīnāpāyaduggativinipāto||
sotāpanno ham asmi avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

8. Tīṇi pi suttāni ekanidānāni|| ||

[page 358]

 

 

9. Giñjakāvasatha 2

2. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavantam etad avoca||
Asoko nāma bhante bhikkhu kālakato tassa kā gati ko abhisamparāyo||
Asokā nāma bhante bhikkhunī kālakatā ... pe ... Asoko nāma bhante upāsako kālakato ... pe ... Asokā nāma bhante upāsikā kālakatā tassā kā gati ko abhisamparāyo ti|| ||

3—6. Asoko Ānanda bhikkhu kālakato āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim paññāvimuttiɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi|| ||

Purimaveyyākaraṇena ekanidānaɱ|| ||

7. Ayaɱ kho so Ānanda dhammādāso dhammapariyāyo yena samannāgato ariyasāvako ākaŋkamāno attanā va attānam vyākareyya Khīṇanirayomhi||
khīṇatiracchāyoniko khīṇapettivisayo khīṇāpāyaduggativinipāto||
sotāpanno ham asmi avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

 

 

10. Giñjakāvasatha 3

2. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Kakkaṭo nāma bhante Ñātike upāsako kālakato tassa kā gati kho abhisamparāyo||
Kāḷiŋgo nāma bhante Ñātike upāsako||
Nikato nāma bhante Ñatike upāsako||
Kaṭissaho nāma bhante||
Tuṭṭho nāma bhante||
Santuṭṭho nāma bhante||
Bhaddo nāma bhante||
Subhaddo nāma bhante Ñātike upāsake kālakato tassa kā gati ko abhisamparāyo ti|| ||

3. Kakkaṭo Ānanda upāsako kālakato pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā opapātiko tattha parinibbāyī anāvattidhammo tasmā lokā||
Kaḷiŋgo Ānanda

[page 359]

Nikato Ānanda||
Kaṭissaho Ānanda||
Tuṭṭho Ānanda||
Santuṭṭho Ānanda||
Bhaddo Ānanda||
Subhaddo Ānanda upāsako kālakato pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā opapātiko tattha parinibbāyī anāvattidhammo tasmā lokā||
sabbe ekagatikā kātabbā|| ||

4. Paropaññāsa Ānanda Ñātike upāsakā kālakatā pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanāṇam parikkhayā opapātikā tattha parinibbāyino anāvattidhammā tasmā lokā|| ||

Sādhikanavuti Ānanda Ñātike upāsakā kālakatā tiṇṇaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā rāgadosamohānaɱ tanuttā sakadāgāmino sakid eva imaɱ lokam āgantvā dukkhassantaɱ karissanti|| ||

Cha atirekāni kho Ānanda pañcasatāni Ñātike upāsakā kālakatā tiṇṇaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā sotāpannā avinipātadhammā niyatā sambodhiparāyanā|| ||

5. Anacchariyaɱ kho panetam Ānanda yam manussabhūto kālaɱ kareyya|| ||

Tasmiɱ tasmiɱ ce maɱ kālakate {upasaŋkamitvā} etam attham paṭipucchissatha||
vihesā hesā Ānanda assa Tathāgatassa||
tasmā ti hānanda dhammādāsaɱ nāma dhammapariyāyaɱ desissāmi||
yena samannāgato ariyasāvako ākaŋkhamāno attanā va attānam vyākareyya||
Khīṇanirayo mhi||
khīṇatiracchānayoniko khīnapittivisayo khīnāpāyaduggativinipāto||
sotāpanno ham asmi avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano|| ||

6. Katamo ca so Ānanda dhammādāso dhammapariyāyo yena samannāgato ariyasāvako ākaŋkhamāno attanā va attānaɱ vyākareyya ... pe ... niyato sambodhiparāyano|| ||

[page 360]

7. Idhānanda ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti|| ||

Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

7. Ayaɱ kho so Ānanda dhammādāso dhammapariyāyo yena samannāgato ariyasāvako ākaŋkhamāno attanā va attānaɱ vyākareyya|| ||

Khīṇanirayo mhi||
khīṇatiracchānayoniko khīṇapittivisayo||
khīnāpāyaduggativinipāto||
sotāpanno ham asmi avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

Veḷudvāravaggo pathamo|| ||

Chapter II. Sahassaka- or Rājakārama Vaggo

11. Sahassa

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Rājakārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho sahassabhikkhunisaŋgho yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā ekam antam aṭṭhāsi|| ||

3. Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitā kho tā bhikkhuniyo Bhagavā etad avoca||
Catuhi kho bhikkhuniyo dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sotāpanno hoti avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano||
katamehi catuhi|| ||

4. Idha bhikkhuniyo ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

[page 361]

5. 6. Dhamme||
Saŋghe|| ||

7. Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi||
... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

8. Imehi kho bhikkhuniyo catuhi dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sotāpanno hoti avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

 

 

12. Brāhmaṇā

1. 2. Sāvatthi nidānam|| ||

3. Brāhmanā bhikkhave udayagāminiɱ nāma paṭipadam paññāpenti||
te sāvakam evaɱ samādapenti|| ||

Ehi tvam ambho purisa kālasseva uṭṭhāya pācīnamukho yāhi||
so tvam mā semhaɱ parivajjehi||
mā papātaɱ||
mā khāṇum||
mā kaṇṭakaɱ ṭhānam||
mā candanikaɱ||
mā oḷigallaɱ||
yattha papāteyyāsi tattheva maraṇam āgaccheyyāsi||
Evaɱ tvam ambho purisa kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā sugatim saggam lokam upapajjissasīti|| ||

4. Taɱ kho panetam bhikkhave brāhmaṇānaɱ bālagamanam etam mūḷhagamanam etam na nibbidāya na virāgāya na nirodhāya na upasamāya na abhiññāya na sambodhāya na nibbānāya saɱvattati|| ||

Ahañ ca kho bhikkhave ariyassa vinaye udayagāminim paṭipadam paññāpemi||
yā ekantanibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya {saɱvattati}|| ||

Katamā ca yā bhikkhave udayagāminī paṭipadā||
yā ekantanibbidāya ... pe ... nibbānāya saɱvattati|| ||

[page 362]

5. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā||
... pe ...||
satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe|| ||

Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

6. Ayaɱ kho sā bhikkhave udayagāminī patipadā yā ekantanibbidāya ... pe ... nibbānāya saɱvattatī ti|| ||

 

 

13. Ānanda

1. Ekam samayam āyasmā ca Ānando āyasmā ca Sāriputto Sāvatthiyaɱ viharanti Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Sāriputto sāyaṇhasamayam paṭisallāṇā vuṭṭhito yenāyasmā Ānando tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmatā Ānandena saddhiɱ sammodi||
sammodanīyaɱ katham sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretva eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi||
ekam antam nisinno kho āyasmā Sāriputto āyasmantam Ānandam etad avoca|| ||

3. Katīnam kho āvuso Ānanda dhammānam pahānā katīnam dhammānaɱ samannāgamanahetu evam ayam pajā Bhagavatā vyākatā sotāpannā avinipātadhammā niyatā sambodhiparāyanā ti|| ||

4. Catunnaɱ kho āvuso dhammānam pahānā catunnam dhammānaɱ samannāgamanahetu evam ayam pajā Bhagavatā vyākatā sotāpannā avinipātadhammā niyatā sambodhiparāyanā ti||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

5. Yathārūpena kho āvuso Buddhe apasādena samannāgato assutāvā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā āpāyam duggatiɱ vinipātaɱ nirayam upapajjati||
tathārūpassa Buddhe appasādo na hoti

[page 363]

Yathārūpena ca kho avuso Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato sutavā ariyasāvako kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokam upapajjati||
tathārūpassa Buddhe aveccappasādo hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

6. Yathārūpena kho āvuso dhamme appasādena samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhe- pa- maapāyaɱ dug- vinipātaɱ nirayam upapajjati||
tathārupassa dhamme aveccappasādo na hoti|| ||

Yathārūpena ca kho āvuso dhamme aveccappasādena samannāgato sutavā ariyasāvako kāyassa bhe- pa- ma- sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokam upapajjati||
tathārūpassa dhamme aveccappasādo hoti||
svākhyāto Bhagavatā dhammo ... pe ... viññūhīti|| ||

7. Yathārūpena kho āvuso saŋghe appasādena samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhe- pa- ma- apāyam duggatiɱ vinipātaɱ nirayam upapajjati||
tathārūpassa saŋghe aveccappasādo na hoti|| ||

Yathārūpena ca kho āvuso saŋghe aveccappasādena samannāgato sutavā ariyasāvako kāyassa bhe- pa- ma- sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokam upapajjati||
tathārūpassa saŋghe aveccappasādo hoti||
supaṭipanno Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho ... pe ... anuttaram puññakkhettaɱ lokassā ti|| ||

8. Yathārūpena kho āvuso dussīlyena samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhe- pa- ma- duggatiɱ vinipātaɱ nirayam uppajjati||
tathārūpassa dussīlena hoti|| ||

Yathārūpehi ca kho āvuso ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato sutavā ariyasāvako kāyassa bhe- pa- ma- sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokam upapajjati||
tathārūpassa ariyakantāni sīlāni honti akhaṇḍāni ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikāni|| ||

[page 364]

9. Imesaɱ kho āvuso catunnam dhammānam pahānā imesaɱ catunnaɱ dhammānaɱ samannāgamanahetu evam ayam pajā Bhagavatā vyākatā sotāpannā avinipātadhammā niyatā sambodhiparāyanā ti|| ||

 

 

14. Duggati

3. Catuhi bhikkhave dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sabbaduggatibhayam samatikkanto hoti||
katamehi catuhi|| ||

4—7. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ...||
satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Dhamme|| ||

Saŋghe|| ||

Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgāto hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

8. Ime hi kho bhikkhave catuhi dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sabbaduggatibhayaɱ samatikkanto hotī ti|| ||

 

 

15. Duggati 2

3. Catuhi° °ariyasāvako sabbaduggativinipātabhayaɱ samatikkanto hoti|| ||

8. Imehi° ariyasāvako sabbaduggativinipātabhayaɱ samatikkanto hotī ti|| ||

 

 

16. Mittenāmaccā 1

3. Ye hi bhikkhave anukampeyyātha||
ye ca sotabbam maññeyyum mittā vā amaccā vā ñāti vā sālohitā vā||
te kho bhikkhave catusu sotāpattiyaŋgesu samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhāpetabbā||
katamesu catusu|| ||

[page 365]

4. Buddhe aveccappasāde samādapetabbā||
... pe ...||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe||
Ariyakantesu sīlesu samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhāpetabbā akhaṇḍesu ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikesu|| ||

5. Ye bhikkhave anukampeyyātha||
ye ca sotabbam maññeyyum mittā vā amaccā vā ñāti vā sālohitā vā te vo bhikkhave imesu catusu sotāpattiyaŋgesu samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhāpetabbā ti|| ||

 

 

17. Mittenāmaccā 2

3. Ye bhikkhave anukampeyyātha||
ye ca sotabbam maññeyyum mittā vā amaccā vā ñātīvā sālohitā vā||
te vo bhikkhave catusu sotāpattiyaŋgesu samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhāpetabbā||
katamesu catusu|| ||

4. Buddhe aveccappasāde samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhāpetabbā||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Siyā bhikkhave catunnam mahābhūtānam aññathattam pathavīdhatuyā āpodhātuyā tejodhātuyā vāyodhātuyā||
na tv eva Buddhe aveccappasādenasamannāgatassa ariyasāvakassa siyā aññathattaɱ||
tatridam aññathattaɱ|| ||

So vata Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato ariyasāvako nirayaɱ vā tiracchānayonim vā pittivisayaɱ vā upapajjissatī ti||
netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

5—6. Dhamme|| ||

{Saŋghe}|| ||

7. Ariyakantesu sīlesu samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhapetabbā||
akhaṇḍesu ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikesu|| ||

Siyā bhikkhave catunnam mahābhūtānam aññathattam pathavidhatuyā āpo° tejo° vāyodhātuyā||
na tv eva ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgatassa ariyasāvakassa siyā aññathattam

[page 366]

tatridam aññathattam|| ||

So vata ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato ariyasāvako nirayaɱ vā tiracchānayoniɱ vā pittivisayaɱ vā uppajjissatī ti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

8. Ye bhikkhave anukampeyyātha||
ye ca sotabbam maññeyyum mittā vā amaccā vā ñatī vā sālohitā vā||
te vo bhikkhave imesu catusu sotāpattiyaŋgesu samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhāpetabbā ti|| ||

 

 

18. Devacārika 1

1. Sāvatthinidānaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Mahā-Moggalāno seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaɱ vā bāham pasāreyya pasāritaɱ vā bāhaɱ sammiñjeyya||
evam eva Jetavane antarahito devesu Tāvatiɱsesu pātur ahosi|| ||

3. Atha kho sambahulā Tāvatiɱsakāyikā devatāyo yenāyasmā Mahā-Moggalāno tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantam Mahā-Moggalānam abhivādetvā ekam antam aṭṭhaɱsu|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitā kho tā devatāyo āyasmā Mahā-Moggalāno etad avoca|| ||

4. Sādhu kho āvuso Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgamanaɱ hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgamanahetu kho āvuso evam idhekacce sattā kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā sugatim saggaɱ lokam upapajjatī ti|| ||

5.6. Sādhu kho āvuso dhamme||
Saŋghe|| ||

7. Sādhu kho āvuso ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgamanaɱ hoti ākhaṇḍehi ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattānikehi|| ||

[page 367]

Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgamanahetu kho āvuso evam idhekacce sattā kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokam upapajjantī ti|| ||

8. Sādhu kho mārisa Moggalāna Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgamanaɱ hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ...||
satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgamana hetu kho mārisa Moggalāna evam idhekacce sattā kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokam upapajjanti|| ||

9—11. Sādhu kho mārisa Moggalāna dhamme||
... pe ...||
{saŋghe}||
ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgamanaɱ hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgamanahetu kho mārisa Moggalāna evam idhekacce sattā kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokam upapajjantī ti|| ||
