Chapter III. Saraṇāni Vaggo

21. Mahānāma 1

1. Evam me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sakkesu viharati Kapilavatthusmiɱ Nigrodhārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho Mahānāmo sakko yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Mahānāmo sakko Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Idam bhante Kapilavatthu iddhaɱ ceva phitañca bahujanam ākiṇṇamanussam sambādhavyūhaɱ|| ||

So khvāham bhante Bhagavantaɱ vā {payirupāsitvā} manobhāvanīye vā bhikkhū sāyaṇhasamayaɱ Kapilavatthum pavisanto bhante na pi hatthinā samāgacchāmi||
bhante na pi assena samāgacchāmi||
bhante na pi rathena samāgacchāmi||
bhante na pi sakaṭena samāgacchāmi||
bhante na pi purisena samāgacchami||
tassa mayham bhante {tasmiɱ} samaye mussateva Bhagavantam ārabbha sati||
mussati dhammam arabbha sati||
mussati saŋgham ārabbha sati|| ||

Tassa mayham bhante evaɱ hoti||
Imamhi cāhaɱ samaye kālaɱ kareyyaɱ kā mayhaɱ gati ko abhisamparāyo ti|| ||

4. Mā bhāyi Mahānāma mā bhāyi Mahānāma||
apāpakaɱ te maraṇam bhavissati apāpikā kālaɱkiriyā|| ||

Yassa kassaci Mahānāma dīgharattaɱ saddhāparibhāvitaɱ cittaɱ sīlaparibhāvitaɱ cittaɱ sutaparibhāvitaɱ cittaɱ cāgaparibhāvitaɱ cittam paññaparibhāvitaɱ cittaɱ||
tassa yo hi khvāyaɱ kāyo rūpī cātumahābhūtiko mātāpittikasambhavo odanakummāsupacayo aniccucchādanaparimaddana-bhedana-viddhaɱsanadhammo tam idheva kākā vā khādanti gijjhā vā khādanti kulalā vā khādanti sunakhā vā khādanti sigālā va khādanti vividhā vā pāṇakajātā khādanti

[page 370]

Yañca khvassa cittaɱ dīgharattaɱ saddhāparibhāvitam sīla-suta-cāga-paribhāvitaɱ||
tam uddhagāmi hoti visesagāmi|| ||

5. Seyyathā pi Mahānāma puriso sappikumbham vā telakumbham vā gambhīram udakarahadam ogāhetvā bhindeyya||
tatra yā assa sakkharā vā kaṭhalā vā sā adhogāmī assa||
yañca khvassa tatra sappi vā telaɱ vā tam uddhaɱgāmī assa visesāgamī|| ||

Evam eva kho Mahānāma yassa kassaci dīgharattaɱ saddhāparibhāvitaɱ cittaɱ sīlasuta-cāga-paññāparibhāvitaɱ cittaɱ||
tassa hoti khvāyam kāyo rūpī cātumahābhūtiko mātāpittikasambhavo odanakummāsupacayo aniccucchādana-parimaddana-bhedanaviddhaɱsanadhammo||
tam idheva kākā vā khādanti||
gijjhā vā khā-||
kulalā vā khā-||
sunakhā vā khā-||
sigālā vā khā-||
vividhā vā pāṇakajātā khādanti|| ||

Yañca khvassa taɱ cittaɱ dīgharattaɱ saddhāparibhāvitaɱ sīla-suttacāgapaññā paribhāvitaɱ||
tam uddhaɱgāmī hoti visesagāmī|| ||

6. Tuyhaɱ kho pana Mahānama dīgharattaɱ saddhaparibhāvitaɱ cittam sīla-suta-cāga-paññāparibhāvitaɱ cittam

[page 371]

mā bhāyi Mahānāma mā bhāyi Mahānāma apāpakaɱ te maraṇam bhavissati apāpikā kālakiriyā ti|| ||

 

 

22. Mahānāma 2

1. Evaɱ me sutaɱ-|| ||

2. Atha kho Mahānamo-|| ||

3. Idam bhante Kapilavatthu-|| ||

4. Mā bhāyi Mahānāma ma bhāyi Mahānāma apāpakaɱ te maraṇam bhavissati apāpikā kālakiriyā|| ||

Catuhi kho Mahānāma dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako nibbānaninno hoti nibbānapoṇo nibbānapabbhāro|| ||

Katamehi catuhi?|| ||

5. Idha Mahānāma ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
{Saŋghe}|| ||

Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti||
akhaṇḍehi ... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

6. Seyyathā pi Mahānāma rukkho pācinaninno pācīnapoṇo pācīnapabbhāro||
so mūle chinne katamena papateyyā ti|| ||

Yena bhante ninno yena poṇo yena pabbhāro ti|| ||

Evam eva kho Mahānāma imehi catuhi dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako nibbhānaninno nibbānapoṇo nibbānapabbhāro ti|| ||

 

 

23. Godhā (or Mahānāma 3)

1. Kapilavatthunidānaɱ|| ||

2. Atha Kho Mahānāmo sakko yena Godhā sakko tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Godhaɱ sakkam etad avoca|| ||

[page 372]

3. Katīhi tvam Godhe dhammehi samannāgataɱ sotāpannam puggalam ājānasi||
avinipātadhāmmaɱ niyataɱ sambodhiparāyanan ti|| ||

Tīhi khvāham Mahānāma dhammehi samannāgataɱ sotāpannam puggalam ājānāmi avinipātadhammam niyatam sambodhiparāyanaɱ|| ||

Katamehi tīhi?|| ||

4. Idha Mahānāma ariyāsavako Buddha aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
{Saŋghe} aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
supaṭipanno Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho||
... pe ...||
anuttaram puññakhettaɱ lokassā ti|| ||

Imehi khvāham Mahānāma tīhi dhammehi samannāgataɱ sotāpannam puggalam ājānāmi||
avinipātadhammam niyataɱ sambodhiparāyanaɱ|| ||

5. Tvam pana Mahānāma katīhi dhammehi samannāgataɱ sotāpannaɱ puggalam ājānāsi avinipātadhammaɱ niyatam sambodhiparāyanan ti|| ||

Catuhi khvāham bho Godhe dhammehi samannāgatam sotāpannam puggalam ājānāmi avinipātadhammaɱ niyataɱ sambodhiparāyanaɱ||
katamehi catuhi|| ||

Idha Godhe ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti|| ||

Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
{Saŋghe}||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

Imehi khvāham Godhe catuhi dhammehi samannāgataɱ sotāpannam puggalam ājānāmi avinipātadhammaɱ niyataɱ sambodhiparāyanan ti|| ||

6. Āgamehi tvam Mahānāma āgamehi tvam Mahānāma||
Bhagavā va etaɱ jāneyya etehi dhammehi samannāgatam vā asamannāgataɱ vā ti|| ||

Āyāma Godhe yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkameyyāma||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavato etam attham ārocessāmā ti|| ||

[page 373]

7. Atha kho Mahānāmo sakko Godhā ca sakko yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā ekam antam nisīdiɱsu||
Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Mahānāmo sakko Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

8. Idhāham bhante yena Godhā sakko tenupasaŋkamiɱ||
upasaŋkamitvā Godhaɱ sakkam etad avocaɱ||
katīhi tvaɱ Godhe dhammehi samannāgatam sotāpannam puggalam ājānāsi avinipāta- ni- sambodhi-|| ||

Evam vutte bhante Godhā sakkho mam etad avoca|| ||

Tīhi khvāham Mahānāma dhammehi samannāgataɱ sotāpannam puggalam ājānāmi avi- ni- sambodhi-||
katamehi tīhi|| ||

Idha Mahānāma ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti|| ||

Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
supaṭipanno Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho||
... pe ...||
anuttaram puññakkhettaɱ lokassā ti|| ||

Imehi khvāham Mahānāma tīhi dhammehi samannāgataɱ sotāpannam puggalam ājānāmi avi- ni- sambodhi-|| ||

Tvam pana Mahānāma katīhi dhammehi samannāgataɱ sotāpannam puggalam ājānāsi avini- ni- sambodhiparāyanan ti|| ||

9. Evaɱ vuttāham bhante Godham sakkam etad avocam|| ||

Catuhi khvāham Godhe dhammehi samannāgatam sotāpannam puggalam ājānāmi avi- ni- sambodhi-|| ||

Katamehi catuhi?|| ||

Idha Godhe ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti|| ||

Iti pi so Bhagavā||
... pe ...||
satthā devamanussānam Buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe||
ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi|| ||

... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

Imehi khvāhaɱ Godhe catuhi dhammehi samannāgatam sotāpannam puggalam ājānāmi avini- ni- sambodhiparāyanan ti|| ||

Evam vutte bhante Godhā sakko mam etad avoca||
Āgamehi tvam Mahānāma āgamehi tvam Mahānāma||
Bhagavā va etam jāneyya etehi dhammehi samannāgatam vā asamannāgataɱ vā ti|| ||

[page 374]

10. Idha bhante kocid eva dhammasamuppādo uppajjeyya||
ekato assa Bhagavā ekato bhikkhusaŋgho||
yeneva Bhagavā tenevāham assaɱ evam pasannam mam bhante Bhagavā dhāretu|| ||

11. Idha bhante kocid eva dhammasamuppādo uppajjeyya||
ekato assa Bhagavā ekato bhikkhusaŋgho bhikkhunīsaŋgho ca yeneva Bhagavā tenevāham assam evam pasannam mam bhante Bhagavā dhāretu|| ||

12. Idha bhante kocid eva dhammasamuppādo uppajjeyya||
ekato assa Bhagavā ekato bhikkhusaŋgho bhikkhunīsaŋgho upāsakā ca yeneva Bhagavā tenevāham assam evam pasannam mam bhante Bhagavā dhāretu|| ||

13. Idha bhante kocid eva dhammasamuppādo uppajjeyya||
ekato assa Bhagavā ekato bhikkhusaŋgho bhikkhu{nīsaŋgho} upāsakā upāsikāyo ca yeneva Bhagavā tenevāham assaɱ||
evam pasannam mam bhante Bhagavā dhāretu|| ||

14. Idha bhante kocid eva dhammasamuppādo uppajjeyya||
ekato assa Bhagavā ekato bhikkhusaŋgho bhikkhu{nīsaŋgho} upāsakā upāsikāyo sadevako ca loko samārako sabrahmako sassamaṇabrāhmaṇapajā sadevamanussā||
yeneva Bhagavā tenevāham assam evam pasannaɱ mam bhante Bhagavā dhāretū ti|| ||

15. Evaɱvādiɱ tvam Godhe Māhānāmaɱ sakkaɱ kiɱ vadesī ti|| ||

Evaɱvādāham bhante Mahānāmaɱ sakkaɱ na kiñci vadāmi aññatra kalyāṇā aññatra kusalā ti|| ||

[page 375]

 

 

24. Sarakāni or Saraṇāni 1

1. Kapilavatthu nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Sarakāni sakko kālakato hoti so Bhagavatā vyākato sotāpanno avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

3. Tatra sudam sambahulā Sakkā saŋgamma samāgamma ujjhāyanti khīyanti vipācenti||
Acchariyam vata bho abbhutaɱ vata bho etthadāniko na sotāpanno bhavissati||
yatra hi nāma Sarakāni sakko kālakato so Bhagavatā vyākato sotāpanno avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

Sarakāni sakko sikkhādubbalyam āpādi majjapānam apāyī ti|| ||

4. Atha kho Mahānāmo sakko yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā ekam antam nisīdi||
ek- an- ni- kho Mahānamo sakko Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

5. Idha bhante Sarakāni sakko kālakato so Bhagavatā vyākato sotāpanno avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

Tatra sudam bhante sambahulā Sakkā saŋgamma samāgamma ujjhāyanti bhīyanti vipācenti Acchariyaɱ vata bho abbhutaɱ vata bho etthadāniko na sotāpanno bhavissati||
yatra hi nāma Sarakāṇi sakko kālakato so Bhagavatā vyākato sotāpanno avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

Sarakāni sakko sikkhādubbalyam āpādi majjapānam apāyīti|| ||

Yo so Mahānāma dīgharattam upāsako Buddhaɱ saraṇaɱ gato dhammaɱ sa- gato saŋghaɱ sa- gato kathaɱ vinipātam gaccheyya|| ||

6. Yañ hi tam Mahānama sammāvadamāno vadeyya Dīgharattam upāsako buddham- dhammam- saŋghaɱ- saraṇaɱ gato ti||
Sarakānisakkaɱ sammāvadamāno vadeyya|| ||

[page 376]

Sarakāni Mahānāma sakko dīgharattam upāsako Buddhaɱdhammaɱ- saŋghaɱ saraṇaɱ gato so kathaɱ vinipātam gaccheyya|| ||

7. Idha Mahānāma ekacco puggalo Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe|| ||

Hāsapañño javanapañño vimuttiyā ca samannāgato|| ||

So āsavanānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttim paññāvimuttim diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharati||
Ayam pi kho Mahānāma puggalo parimutto nirayā||
parimutto tiracchānayoniyā||
parimutto pittivisayā||
parimutto apāyaduggativinipātā|| ||

8. Idha pana Mahānāma ekacco puggalo Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā||
... pe ...||
satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe||
hāsapañño javanapañño na ca vimuttiyā samannāgato|| ||

So pañcannam orambhāgiyānam saŋyojanānaɱ parikkhayā opapātiko hoti tattha parinibbāyī anāvattidhammo asmā lokā|| ||

Ayam pi kho Mahānāma puggalo parimutto nirayā parimutto tiracchāyoniyā||
parimutto pittivisayā||
parimutto apāyaduggati vinipātā|| ||

9. Idha pana Mahānāma ekacco puggalo Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ...||
satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe||
na hāsapañño na javanapañño na ca vimuttiyā samannāgato||
so tiṇṇam saŋyojanānam parikkhayā rāgadosamohānaɱ tanuttā sakadāgāmi hoti sakid eva imaɱ lokam āgantvā dukkhassantaɱ karoti|| ||

Ayam pi kho Mahānāma puggalo parimutto nirayā parimutto tiracchānayoniyā||
parimutto pittivisayā parimutto apāyaduggativinipātā|| ||

[page 377]

10. Idha pana Mahānāma ekacco puggalo Buddhe aveccappasadena-||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe||

Ayam pi kho Mahānāma puggalo parimutto nirayā parimutto tiracchānayoniyā parimutto pittivisayā parimutto apāyaduggativinipātā|| ||

Ayam pi kho Mahānāma puggalo agantā nirayaɱ agantā tiracchānayoniɱ agantā pittivisayam agantā apāyaduggativinipātaɱ|| ||

13. Ime ce pi Mahānāma mahāsālā subhāsitaɱ dubbhāsitam ājāneyyuɱ||

25. Sarakāni or Saraṇāni 2

1. Kapilavatthunidānaɱ|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Sarakāni-|| ||

3. Tatra sudaɱ sambahulā sakkā- -Etthadaniko na sotāpanno bhavissati||
-sambodhisamparāyano ti|| ||

Sarakāni sakko sikkhāya aparipūrakārī ahosī ti|| ||

4. Atha kho Mahānāmo -etad avoca|| ||

5. Idha bhante Sarakāni sakko- -etthadāniko na sotapanno bhavissati- -sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

Sarakāni sakko sikkhāya aparipūrakārī ahosī ti|| ||

Yo so Mahānama- -kathaɱ vinipātam gaccheyya|| ||

6. Yañ hi tam Mahānama sammāvadamano- -so katham vinipātaɱ gaccheyya|| ||

7. Idha Mahānāma ekacco puggalo Buddhe ekantagato hoti abhippasanno||
Iti pi so Bhagavā- -parimutto apāyaduggativinipātā|| ||

8. Idha pana Mahānāma ekacco puggalo Buddhe ekantagato hoti abhippasanno||

upahaccaparinibbāyī hoti||
{sasaŋkhārapavirinibbāyī} hoti||

uddhaɱsoto hoti akaniṭṭhagāmī|| ||

saddhindriyaɱ ... pe ...||

Tathāgate cassa saddhāmattam hoti pemamattaɱ||
ayam pi kho Mahānāma ayantā-||
-apāyaduggatinininipātaɱ|| ||

13. Seyyathā pi Mahānāma dukkhettaɱ dubbhūmi avihatakhānukam bījāni cassu khaṇḍāni pūtini vātātapahatām asārāni asukhasayitāni||
devo ca na sammādhāram anupaveccheyya|| ||

Api nu tāni bījāni vuddhiɱ viruḷhiɱ vepullam āpajjeyyum tī|| ||

No hetam bhante|| ||

Evam eva kho Mahānama idha dhammo dvākkhāto hoti duppavedito anīyāniko anupasamasaɱvattanike asammāsambuddhappavedito||
idam aham dukkhettasmiɱ vadāmi||

[page 380]

tasmiɱ ca dhamme sāvako viharati dhammānudhammapaṭipanno sāmīcipaṭipanno anudhammacārī idam ahaɱ dubbījasmiɱ vadāmi|| ||

14. Seyyathā pi Mahānāma sukhettaɱ subhūmi suvihatakhāṇukaɱ bījāni cassu akhaṇḍāni apūtīni avātātapahatāni sārāni sukhasahitāni||
devo ca sammādhāram anupaveccheyya|| ||

Api nu tāni bījāni vuddhiɱ virūḷhiɱ vepullam āpajjeyyun ti|| ||

Evam bhante|| ||

Evam eva kho Mahānāma idha dhammo svākkhāto hoti supavedito nīyāniko upasamasaɱvattaniko sammāsambuddhapavedito idam ahaɱ sukhettasmiɱ vadāmi||
tasmiɱ ca dhamme sāvako viharati dhammānudhammapaṭipanno sāmīcipaṭipanno anudhammacārī idam aham subījasmiɱ vadāmi||
{kimaŋga} pana Sarakānisakkaɱ||
Sarakāni Mahānāma sakko maraṇakāle sikkhāya paripūrakarī ahosī ti|| ||

 

 

26. Dussilya 1 or Anāthapiṇḍika 1

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati ābādhiko hoti dukkhito bāḷhagilāno|| ||

3. Atha kho Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati aññataram purisam āmantesi||
Ehi tvam ambho purisa yenāyasmā Sāriputto tenupasaŋkama||
upasaŋkamitvā mama vacanena āyasmato Sāriputtassa pāde sirasā vanda||
Anāthapiṇḍiko bhante gahapati ābādhiko dukkhito bāḷhagilāno||
so āyasmato Sāriputtassa pāde sirasā vandatī ti||
evañca vadeti|| ||

Sādhu kira bhante āyasmā Sāriputto yena Anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa nivesanam tenupasaŋkamatu anukampam upādāyā ti|| ||

[page 381]

Evam bhante ti kho so puriso Anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa patissutvā yenāyasmā Sāriputto tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantaɱ Sāriputtam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

4. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so puriso āyasmantaɱ Sāriputtam etad avoca|| ||

Anāthapiṇḍiko bhante gahapati ābā- duk- bāla-||
so āyasmato Sāriputtassa pāde si- van-||
evañca vadeti||
Sādhu kira bhante āy- Sāriputto yena Anā- gahapatissa nivesanaɱ tenupasaŋkamatu anukampam upādāyā ti|| ||

Adhivāsesi kho āy- Sāriputto tuɱhībhāvena|| ||

5. Atha kho āy- Sāriputto pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya āyasmatā Ānandena pacchā samaṇena yena Anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa nivesananaɱ tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi|| ||

Nisajja kho āyasmā Sāriputto Anāthapiṇḍikaɱ gahapatim etad avoca|| ||

Kacci te gahapati khamanīyaɱ kacci yāpanīyaɱ kacci dukkhā vedanā patikkamanti no abhikkamati paṭikkamo sānam paññāyati no abhikkamo ti|| ||

Na me bhante khamanīyaɱ na yāpanīyaɱ bāḷhā me dukkhā vedanā abhikkamanti no paṭikkamanti abhikkamo sānam paññāyati no paṭikkamo ti|| ||

6. Yathārūpena kho gahapati Buddhe appasādena samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā parammaraṇā apāyaɱ duggatiɱ vinipātaɱ nirayam upapajjati||
tathārūpo te Buddhe appasādo natthi atthi ca kho te gahapati Buddhe aveccappasādo||
Iti pi so Bhagavā||
la... pe ...||
satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Tañ ca pana te Buddhe aveccappasādam attani samanupassato ṭhānaso vedanā paṭipassambheyyuɱ|| ||

7. Yathārūpena kho gahapati dhamme appasādena samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā apā- dug- vini- nirayam upapajjati

[page 382]

tathārūpo te dhamme appasādo natthi||
atthi ca kho te gahapati dhamme aveccappasādo||
Svākkhāto Bhagavatā dhammo||
... pe ...||
paccattaɱ veditabbo viññūhīti|| ||

Tañ ca pana te dhamme aveccappasādam attani samanapassato ṭhānaso vedanā paṭippassambheyyuɱ|| ||

8. Yathārūpena kho gahapati saŋghe appasādena samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā apā- dug- vi- nirayam uppajjati||
tathārūpo te saŋghe appasādo natthi||
atthi ca kho te gahapati saŋghe aveccappasādo||
Supaṭipanno Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho ... pe ... anuttaram puññakkhettaɱ lokassā ti|| ||

Tañ ca pana te saŋghe aveccappasādam attani samanupassato ṭhānaso vedanā paṭippassambheyyuɱ|| ||

9. Yathārūpena kho gahapati dussīlyena samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā param maraṇā apādug- vini- nirayam uppajjati||
tathārupan te dussīlyaɱ natthi||
atthi ca kho te gahapati ariyakantāni sīlāni||
la... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikāni|| ||

Tāni ca pane te ariyakantāni sīlāni attani samanupassato ṭhānaso vedanā paṭipassambheyyuɱ|| ||

10. Yathārupāya kho gahapati micchādiṭṭhiyā samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā pa- ma- apā- dugvi- nirayam uppajjati||
tathārūpā te micchādiṭṭhi natthi||
atthi ca kho te gahapati sammādiṭṭhi|| ||

Tañ ca pana te sammādiṭṭhim attani samanupassato thānaso vedanā passambheyyuɱ|| ||

11. Yathārūpena kho gahapati micchāsaŋkappena samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā- -nirayam uppajjati||
tathārūpo te {micchāsaŋkappo} natthi||
atthi ca kho te gahapati sammāsaŋkappo|| ||

Tañ ca pana te {sammāsaŋkappam} attani samanupassato ṭhānaso vedanā paṭipassambheyyuɱ|| ||

[page 383]

12. Yathārupāya kho gahapati micchāvācāya samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā- -nirayam upapajjati||
tathārūpā te micchāvācā natthi||
atthi ca kho te gahapati sammāvācā|| ||

Tañ ca pana te sammāvācam attani samanupassato ṭhānaso vedanā paṭipassambheyyuɱ|| ||

13. Yathārūpena kho gahapati micchākammantena samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā- -nirayam upapajjati||
tathārūpo te micchākammanto natthi||
atthi ca kho te gahapati sammākammanto||
tañ ca pana te sammākammantam attani samanupassato ṭhānaso vedanā paṭipassambheyyuɱ|| ||

14. Yathārūpena kho gahapati micchā-ājīvena samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā- -nirayam upapajjati ti||
tathārūpo te micchā-ājīvo natthi||
atthi ca kho te gahapati sammā-ājīvo|| ||

Tañ ca pana te sammā-ājīvam attani samanupassato ṭhānaso vedanā paṭipassambheyyuɱ|| ||

15. Yathārūpena kho gahapati micchāvāyāmena samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā- -nirayam uppajjati||
tathārūpo te micchāvāyāmo natthi||
atthi ca kho te gahapati sammāvāyāmo|| ||

Tañ ca pana te sammāvāyāmam attani samanupassato ṭhanaso vedanā paṭipassambheyyuɱ|| ||

16. Yathārūpāya kho gahapati micchāsatiyā samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā- -nirayam upapajjati||
tathārupā te micchāsati natthi||
atthi ca kho te gahapati sammāsati||
etañ ca pana te sammāsatim attani samanupassato ṭhānaso vedanā paṭipassambheyyuɱ|| ||

17. Yathārūpena kho gahapati micchāsamādhinā samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā- -nirayam upapajjati||
tathārūpo te micchāsamādhi natthi|| ||

Atthi ca kho te gahapati sammāsamādhi|| ||

Tañ ca pana te sammāsamādhim attani samanupassato ṭhānaso vedanā paṭipassambheyyuɱ|| ||

[page 384]

18. Yathārūpena kho gahapati micchāñāṇena samannāgato assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā- -nirayam upapajjati||
tathārūpaɱ te micchāñāṇaɱ natthi|| ||

Atthi ca kho te gahapati sammāñāṇam|| ||

Tañ ca pana te sammāñānam attani samanupassato ṭhānaso vedanā paṭipassambheyyuɱ|| ||

19. Yathārūpāya kho gahapati micchāvimuttiyā {samannāgato} assutavā puthujjano kāyassa bhedā- -nirayam upapajjati||
tathārūpā te micchāvimutti natthi|| ||

Atthi ca kho te gahapati sammāvimutti||
tañ ca pana te sammāvimuttim attani samanupassato ṭhānaso vedanā paṭippassambheyyunti|| ||

20. Atha kho Anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa ṭhānaso vedanā paṭipassambhiɱsu|| ||

21. Atha kho Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati āyasmantaɱ ca Sāriputtam āyasmantaɱ ca Ānandaɱ sakeneva thālipākena parivisi|| ||

22. Atha kho Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantaɱ Sāriputtam bhuttāviɱ onitapattapānim aññataraɱ nīcam āsanaɱ gahetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

23. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnaɱ kho Anāthapiṇḍikam gahapatim āyasmā Sāriputto imāhi gāthāhi anumodi|| ||

Yassa saddhā Tathāgate||
acalā supatiṭṭhitā|| ||

sīlañca yassa kalyāṇaɱ||
ariyakantam pasaɱsitaɱ|| ||

Saŋghe pasādo yassatthi||
ujubhūtañ ca dassanaɱ||
Adaliddo ti tam āhu||
amoghaɱ tassa jīvitaɱ|| ||

Tasmā saddhaɱ ca sīlañca||
pasādaɱ dhammadassanaɱ||
anuyuñjetha medhāvī||
saram buddhānasāsanan ti|| ||

24. Atha kho āyasmā Sāriputto Anāthapiṇḍikaɱ gahapatim imāhi gāthāhi anumoditvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkāmi|| ||

[page 385]

25. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnaɱ kho āyasmantam Ānandam Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

26. Handa kuto nu tvam Ānanda āgacchasi divādivassā ti|| ||

Āyasmatā bhante Sāriputtena Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati iminā ca iminā ca ovādena ovadito ti|| ||

Paṇḍito Ānanda Sāriputto mahāpañño Ānanda Sāriputto|| ||

Yatra hi nāma cattāri sotāpattiyaŋgāni dasahi ākarehi vibhajissatī ti|| ||

 

 

27. Dussīlyam 2 or Anāthapiṇḍika 2

1. Sāvatthinidānaɱ|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati ābādhiko hoti dukkhito bāḷhagilāno|| ||

3.4. Atha kho Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati aññataram purisam āmantesi|| ||

Ehi tvam ambho purisa yenāyasmā Ānando tenupasaŋkama||
upasaŋkamitvā mama vacanena āyasmato Ānandassa pāde sirasā vanda ... pe ...|| ||

5. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa nivesanam tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi||
nisajja kho āyasmā Ānando Anāthapiṇḍīkaɱ gahapatim etad avoca|| ||

Kacci te gahapati khamanīyam kacci yāpanīyaɱ kacci dukkhā vedanā paṭikkamanti no abhikkamanti paṭikkamo sānam paññāyati no abhikkamo ti|| ||

Na me bhante khamanīyaɱ na yāpanīyaɱ bāḷhā me dukkhā vedanā abhikkamanti no paṭikkamanti abhikkamo sānam paññāyati no patikkamo ti|| ||

[page 386]

6. Catuhi kho gahapati dhammehi samannāgatassa assutavato puthujjanassa hoti uttāso hoti chambhitattaɱ hoti samparāyikam maraṇabhayaɱ||
katamehi catuhi|| ||

7. Idha gahapati assutavā puthujjano buddhe appasādena samannāgato hoti||
tañ ca panassa Buddhe appasādam attani samanupassato hoti uttāso hoti chambhitattaɱ hoti samparāyikam maraṇabhayam|| ||

Puna ca param gahapati assutavā puthujjano Dhamme appasādena samannāgato hoti||
tañ ca panassa dhamme appasādam attani samanupassato hoti uttāso hoti chambhitattaɱ hoti samparāyikam maraṇabhayaɱ|| ||

Puna ca paraɱ gahapati assutavā puthujjano Saŋghe appasādena samannāgato hoti||
tañ ca panassa saŋghe appasādam attani samanupassato hoti uttāso hoti chambhitattam hoti samparāyikam maraṇabhayam|| ||

Puna ca param gahapati assutavā puthujjano dussīlyena samannāgato hoti||
tañ ca panassa dussīlyam attani samanupassato hoti uttāso hoti chambhitattaɱ hoti samparāyikam maraṇabhayaɱ|| ||

Imehi kho gahapati catuhi dhammehi samannāgatassa assutavato puthujjanassa hoti uttāso hoti chambhitattam hoti samparāyikam maraṇabhayaɱ|| ||

8. Catuhi kho gahapati dhammehi samannāgatassa sutavato ariyasāvakassa na hoti uttāso na hoti chambhitattam na hoti samparāyikam maraṇabhayaɱ||
katamehi catuhi|| ||

Idha gahapati sutavā ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā||
... pe ...||
satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
tañ ca panassa buddhe aveccappasādam attani samanupassato na hoti uttāso na hoti chambhitattaɱ na hoti samparāyikam maraṇabhayaɱ|| ||

Puna ca paraɱ gahapati sutavā ariyasāvako Dhamme||
[pe] ||
{Saŋghe} [pe] ||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akaṇḍehi ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikehi||
tāni ca panassa ariyakantāni sīlāni attani samanupassato na hoti uttāso na hoti chambhitattaɱ na hoti samparāyikam maraṇabhayaɱ

[page 387]

Imehi kho gahapati catuhi dhammehi samannāgatassa sutavato ariyasāvakassa na hoti uttāso na hoti chambhitattaɱ na hoti samparāyikam maraṇabhayan ti|| ||

9. Nāham bhante Ānanda bhāyāmi||
kyāham bhāyissāmi||
ahañhi bhante Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato homi||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānaɱ buddha bhagavā ti||
Dhamme ... pe ...{Saŋghe} ... pe ...Yāni cimāni bhante Bhagavatā gihisāmīcikāni sikkhāpadāni desitāni nāhaɱ tesaɱ kiñci attani khaṇḍaɱ samanupassāmī ti|| ||

10. Lābhā te gahapati||
suladdhan te gahapati||
sotāpattiphalam tayā gahapati vyākatan ti|| ||

 

 

28. Duveram or Anāthapiṇḍika 3

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati yena Bhagavā tenupa-||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnaɱ kho Anāthapiṇḍikam Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

3. Yato kho gahapati ariyasāvakassa pañcabhayāni verāni vūpasantāni ca honti||
catuhi ca sotāpattiyaŋgehi samannāgato hoti||
ariyo cassa ñāyo paññāya sudiṭṭho hoti supaṭividdho||
so ākaŋkhamāno attanā va attānaɱ vyākareyya Khīṇanirayo mhi khīṇatiracchānayoniyo khīṇapittivisayo khīṇāpāyaduggativinipāto sotāpanno ham asmi avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano|| ||

Katamāni pañcabhayāni verāni vūpasantāni honti|| ||

4. Yaɱ gahapati pāṇātipātī pāṇātipātapaccayā diṭṭhadhammikam pi bhayaɱ veram pasavati samparāyikam pi bhayaɱ veram pasavati cetasikam pi dukkhaɱ domanassam paṭisaɱvediyati

[page 388]

pāṇātipātā paṭiviratassa evan tam bhayam veraɱ vūpasantaɱ hoti|| ||

Yaɱ gahapati adinnādāyī|| ||

Yaɱ gahapati kāmesu micchācārī|| ||

Yaɱ gahapati musāvādī|| ||

Yaɱ gahapati surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhāyī surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānapaccayā diṭṭhadhammikam pi bhayaɱ veram pasavati samparāyikam pi bhayaɱ veram pasavati cetasikam pi dukkhaɱ domanassam paṭisaɱvediyati||
surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānā paṭiviratassa evan tam bhayam veram vūpasantaɱ hoti|| ||

Imāni pañcabhayāni verāni vūpasantāni honti|| ||

5. Katamehi catuhi sotāpattiyaŋgehi samannāgato hoti|| ||

Idha gahapati ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Dhamme||
{Saŋghe}||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

Imehi catuhi sotāpattiyaŋgehi samannāgato hoti|| ||

6. Katamo cassa ariyo ñāyo paññāya sudiṭṭho hoti supaṭividdho|| ||

Idha gahapati ariyasāvako paṭiccasamuppādam yeva sādhukam yoniso manasi karoti||
Iti imasmiɱ sati idaɱ hoti||
imassuppadā idam uppajjati||
Iti imasmim asati idaɱ na hoti||
imassa nirodhā idam nirujjhati yad idam avijjapaccayā saŋkhārā||
saŋkhārapaccayā viññānaɱ||
... pe ...|| ||

Evam etassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti|| ||

Avijjāya tv eva asesavirāganirodhā saŋkhāranirodho||
... pe ...|| ||

Evam etassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hoti|| ||

[page 389]

Ayam assa ariyo ñāyo paññāya sudiṭṭho hoti supaṭividdho|| ||

7. Yato kho gahapati ariyasāvakassa imāni pañcabhayāni verāni vūpasantāni honti||
imehi catuhi sotāpattiyaŋgehi samannāgato hoti||
ayaɱ cassa ariyo ñāyo paññāya sudiṭṭho hoti supaṭividdho||
so ākaŋkhamāno attanā va attānaɱ vyākareyya Khīṇanirayo mhi khīṇatiracchānayoniyo khīṇapittivisayo khīnāpāyaduggativinipāto sotāpanno ham asmi avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

 

 

29. Bhayam or Bhikkhu

1. Sāvatthinidānam|| ||

2. Atha kho sambahulā bhikkhū yena Bhagavā tenupa-||
upasaŋkamitvā ... pe ... ekam antam nisīdiɱsu|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

3—6. ... pe ...||
... pe ...|| ||

7. Yato kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa imāni pañcabhayāni verāni vūpasantāni honti||
imehi catuhi sotāpattiyaŋgehi samannāgato hoti||
ayaɱ cassa ariyo ñāyo paññāya sudiṭṭho hoti supaṭividdho|| ||

So ākaŋkamāno attanā va attānaɱ vyākareyya Khīṇanirayo mhi khīṇatiracchānayoniyo khīṇapittivisayo khīṇāpāyaduggativinipāto sotāpanno ham asmi avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

 

 

30. Licchavi or Nandaka

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Vesāliyaɱ viharati Mahāvane Kuṭāgārasālāyaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho Nandako licchavimahāmatto yena Bhagavā {tenupasaŋkami}||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnaɱ kho Nandakaɱ licchavimahāmattam Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

Catuhi kho Nandaka dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sotāpanno hoti avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano

[page 390]

katamehi catuhi?|| ||

3. Idha Nandaka ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
{Saŋghe}||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

Imehi kho Nandaka catuhi dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sotāpanno hoti avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano|| ||

4. Imehi ca pana Nandaka catuhi dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako āyunā samyutto hoti dibbena pi mānussena pi||
vaṇṇena saɱyutto hoti ... pe ... sukhena saɱyutto hoti||
yasena saɱyutto hoti||
adhipateyyena samyutto hoti dibbena pi mānussena pi|| ||

5. Taɱ kho panāhaɱ Nandaka nāññassa samaṇassa vā brāhmaṇassa vā sutvā vadāmi||
api ca yad eva mayā sāmaɱ ñātaɱ sāmaɱ diṭṭhaɱ sāmaɱ viditaɱ tad evāhaɱ vadāmī ti|| ||

6. Evam vutte aññataro puriso Nandakaɱ licchaviɱ mahāmattaɱ etad avoca||
Nahānakālo bhante ti|| ||

Alaɱ dāni bhaṇe etena bāhirena nahānena alam idam ajjhattaɱ nahānaɱ bhavissati yad idam Bhagavati pasādo ti|| ||

Sarakānivaggo tatiyo|| ||

Tassa uddānaɱ|| ||

Mahānāmena dve vuttā||
Godhā ca Saraṇā duve.||
Dussīlyena dve vuttā|| ||

Duverena Bhayena ca||
Licchavidasamo vutto||
Vaggo tena pavuccatī ti|| ||

[page 391]

 

 

Chapter IV. Puṇṇabhisanda Vaggo

31. Abhisanda 1

1. Sāvatthinidānaɱ|| ||

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave puññābhisandā kusalābhisandā sukhassāhārā||
katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
ayam pathamo puññābhisando kusalābhisando sukhassāhāro|| ||

4. Puna ca param bhikkhave ariyasāvako Dhamme aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Svākkhāto Bhagavatā dhammo ... pe ... paccattaɱ veditabbo viññūhī ti||
ayam dutiyo puññābhisando kusalābhisando sakhassāhāro|| ||

5. Puna ca param bhikkhave ariyasāvako saŋghe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
supaṭipanno Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho ... pe ... anuttaram puññakkhettaɱ lokassā ti||
ayam tatiyo puññābhisando kusalābhisando sukhassā hāro|| ||

6. Puna ca param bhikkhave ariyasāvako Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikehi||
ayaɱ catuttho puññābhisando kusalābhisandosukhassāhāro|| ||

7. Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro puññābhisandā kusalābhisandā {ukhassāhārā} ti|| ||

 

 

32. Abhisanda 2

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave puññābhisandā kusalābhisandā sukhassāhārā||
katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti|| ||

Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti

[page 392]

Ayam pathamo puññābhisando kusalābhisando sukhassāhāro|| ||

4.5. Puna ca param bhikkhave ariyasāvako ... pe ... Dhamme||
{Saŋghe}|| ||

6. Puna ca param bhikkhave ariyasāvako vigatamalamaccherena cetasā agāram ajjhāvasati muttacāgo payatapāṇī vossaggarato yācayogo {dānasaɱvibhāgarato}||
ayaɱ catuttho puññābhisando kusalābhisando sukhassāhāro|| ||

7. Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro puññābhisandā kusalābhisandā sukhassāhārā ti|| ||

 

 

33. Abhisanda 3

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave puññābhisandā kusalābhisandā sukhassāhārā||
katame cattāro|| ||

3—5. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako Buddhe° °Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā° °bhagavāti||
Dhamme||
{Saŋghe}|| ||

6. Paññavā hoti udayatthagāminiyā paññāya samannāgato hoti ariyāya nibbedhikāya sammādukkhakkhayagāminiyā|| ||

Ayam catuttho puññābhisando kusalābhisando sukhassāhāro|| ||

7. Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro puññābhisandā kusalābhisandā sukhassāhārā ti|| ||

 

 

34. Devapada 1

1. Sāvatthinidānaɱ|| ||

2. Cattārimāni bhikkhave devānaɱ devapadāni avisuddhānam sattānam visuddhiyā apariyodātānaɱ sattānaɱ pariyodapanāya|| ||

Katamāni cattāri?|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Idam pathamaɱ devānam devapadam avisuddhānaɱ sattānaɱ visuddhiyā apariyodātānaɱ sattānam pariyodapanāya|| ||

[page 393]

4—6. Puna ca bhikkhave ariyasāvako Dhamme||
{Saŋghe}||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

Idaɱ catutthaɱ devānaɱ devapadam avisuddhānaɱ sattānaɱ visuddhiyā apariyodātānaɱ sattānam pariyodapanāya|| ||

7. Imāni kho bhikkhave cattāri devānam devapadāni avisuddhānaɱ sattānaɱ visuddhiyā apariyodātānaɱ sattānam pariyodapanāyā ti|| ||

 

 

35. Devapadam 2

2. Cattārimani bhikkhave devānaɱ devapadāni avisuddhānaɱ sattānaɱ visuddhiyā apariyodātānaɱ sattānam pariyodapanāya||
katamāni cattāri|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavāti|| ||

So iti paṭisañcikkhati||
Kiɱ nu kho devānaɱ devapadan ti||
so evam pajānati||
Abyāpajjha parame khvāham etarahi deve suṇāmi na ca kho panāham kiñci byābādhemi tasaɱ vā thāvaraɱ vā||
addhāhaɱ devapadadhammasamannāgato viharāmī ti|| ||

Idam pathamaɱ devānam devapadam avisuddhānaɱ sattānaɱ visuddhiyā apariyodātānaɱ sattānaɱ {pariyodapanāya}|| ||

4.5. Puna ca param bhikkhave ariyasāvako Dhamme||
{Saŋghe}|| ||

6. Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi||
la... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

So iti paṭisañcikkhati||
Kiɱ nu kho devānaɱ devapadan ti|| ||

So evam pajānāti abyāpajjha parame khvāhaɱ etarahi deve suṇāmi na kho panāhaɱ kiñci vyābādhemi tasaɱ vā thāvaraɱ vā||
addhāham devapadadhammasamannāgato vihārāmī ti|| ||

Idaɱ catutthaɱ devānam devapadam avisuddhānam sattānaɱ visuddhiyā apariyodātānaɱ sattānam {pariyodapanāya}

[page 394]

7. Imāni kho bhikkhave cattāri devānam devapadāni avisuddhānam sattānaɱ visuddhiyā apariyodātānaɱ sattānam pariyodapanāyā ti|| ||

 

 

36. Sabhāgatam

2. Catuhi bhikkhave dhammehi samannāgataɱ attamanā devā sabhāgataɱ kathenti|| ||

Katamehi catuhi?|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānaɱ buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Yā tā devatā Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgatā ito cutā tatrūpapannā||
tāsam evaɱ hoti||
Yathārūpena kho mayam Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgatā tato cutā idhūpapannā||
ariyasāvako pi tathārūpena Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti Ehī ti devānaɱ santike ti|| ||

4.5. Puna ca param bhikkhave ariyasāvako Dhamme||
{Saŋghe}|| ||

6. Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi||
la... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

Yā tā devatā ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgatā ito cutā tatrūpapannā||
tāsam evaɱ hoti|| ||

Yatharūpehi kho mayam ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgatā tato cutā idhūpapannā ariyasāvako pi tathārūpehi ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato Ehī ti devānaɱ santike ti|| ||

7. Imehi kho bhikkhave catuhi dhammehi samannāgatam attamanā devā sabhāgataɱ kathentī ti|| ||

[page 395]

 

 

37. Mahānāmo

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sakkesu viharati Kapilavatthusmiɱ Nigrodhārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho Mahānāmo sakko yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami ... pe ...Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Mahānāmo sakko Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Kittāvatā nu kho bhante upāsako hotī ti|| ||

Yato kho Mahānāma Buddhaɱ saraṇaɱ gato hoti||
dhammaɱ saraṇaɱ gato hoti||
saŋghaɱ saraṇam gato hoti||
ettāvatā kho Mahānāma upasako hotī ti|| ||

4. Kittāvatā pana bhante upāsako sīlasampanno hotī ti|| ||

Yato kho Mahānāma upāsako pāṇātipātā paṭivirato hoti||
adinnādāna paṭivirato hoti||
kāmesu micchācārā paṭivirato hoti||
musāvadā paṭivirato hoti||
surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānā paṭivirato hoti||
ettāvatā kho Mahānāma upāsako sīlasampanno hotī ti|| ||

5. Kittāvatā pana bhante upāsako saddhāsampanno hotī ti|| ||

Idha Mahānāma upāsako saddho hoti saddahati Tathāgatassa bodhim||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Ettāvatā kho Mahānāma upāsako saddhāsamannāgato hotī ti|| ||

6. Kittāvatā pana bhante upāsako cāgasampanno hotī ti|| ||

Idha Mahānāma upāsako vigatamalamaccherena cetasā agāram ajjhāvasati muttacāgo payatapāṇī vossaggarato yācayogo dānasaɱvibhāgarato||
ettāvatā kho Mahānāma upāsako cāgasampanno hotī ti|| ||

7. Kittāvatā pana bhante upāsako paññāsampanno hotī ti|| ||

Idha Mahānāma upāsako paññavā hoti udayatthagāminiyā paññāya samannāgato ariyāya nibbedhikāya sammādukkhakkhayagāminiyā||
ettāvatā kho Mahānāma upāsako paññāsampanno hotī ti|| ||

[page 396]

 

 

38. Vassam

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave upari pabbate thullaphusitake deve vassante tam udakaɱ yathāninnam pavattamānam pabbatakandarapadarasākhā paripūreti||
pabbatakandarapadarasākhā paripūrā kussubbhe paripūreti||
kussubbhā paripūrā mahāsobbhe paripūrenti||
mahāsobbhā paripūrā kunnadiyo paripūrenti||
kunnadiyo paripūrā mahānadiyo paripūrenti||
mahānadiyo paripūrā mahāsamuddasāgaram paripūrenti|| ||

3. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa yo ca Buddhe aveccappasādo||
yo ca dhamme aveccappasādo yo ca saŋghe aveccappasādo||
yāni ca ariyakāntāni sīlāni||
ime dhammā sandamānā pāraɱ gantvā āsavānaɱ khayāya saɱvattantī ti|| ||

 

 

39. Kāḷi

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sakkesu viharati Kapilavatthusmiɱ Nigrodhārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho Bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya yena Kāḷigodhāya sākiyāniyā nivesanaɱ tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi|| ||

3. Atha kho Kāḷigodhā sākiyānī yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnaɱ kho Kāligodham sākiyānim etad avoca|| ||

Catuhi kho Godhe dhammehi samannāgatā ariyasāvikā sotapannā hoti avinipātadhammā niyatā sambodhiparāyanā|| ||

Katamehi catuhi?|| ||

4. Idha Godhe ariyasāvikā Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgatā hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavāti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe|| ||

Vigatamalamaccherena cetasā agāram ajjhāvasati muttacāgā payatapāṇī vossaggaratā yācayogā dānasaɱvibhāgaratā

[page 397]

Imehi kho Godhe catuhi dhammehi samannāgatā ariyasāvikā sotāpannā hoti avinipātadhammā niyatā sambodhiparāyanā ti|| ||

5. Yānimāni bhante Bhagavatā cattāri sotāpattiyaŋgāni desitāni saɱvijjante te dhammā mayi ahañca tesu dhammesu sandissāmi||
ahaɱ hi bhante Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgatā||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānaɱ buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Dhamme||
Saŋghe|| ||

Yaɱ kho pana kiñci kule deyyadhammaɱ sabbaɱ tam appaṭivibhattaɱ sīlavantehi kalyāṇadhammehī ti|| ||

6. Lābhā te Godhe suladdhan te Godhe sotāpattiphalam tayā Godhe vyākatan ti|| ||

 

 

40. Nandiya

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sakkesu viharati Kapilavatthusmiɱ Nigrodhārāme|| ||

2. Atha kho Nandiyo sakko yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami ... pe ...|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Nandiyo sakko Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Yasseva nu kho bhante ariyasāvakassa cattāri sotāpattiyaŋgāni||
sabbena sabbaɱ sabbathā sabbaɱ natthi so evaɱ nu kho bhante ariyasāvako Pamādavihārī ti vuccati|| ||

Yassa kho Nandiya cattāri sotāpattiyaŋgāni sabbena sabbam sabbathā sabbaɱ natthi tam aham Bāhiro puthujjanapakkhe ṭhito ti vadāmi|| ||

4. Api ca Nandiya yathā ariyasāvako pamādavihārī ceva hoti appamādavihārī ca taɱ suṇāhi sādhukam manasi karohi bhāsissāmī ti|| ||

[page 398]

Evam bhante ti kho Nandiyo sakko Bhagavato paccassosi|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

5. Kathañca Nandiya ariyasāvako pamādavihārī hoti|| ||

Idha Nandiya ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddo bhagavā ti|| ||

So tena buddhe aveccappasādena santuṭṭho na uttariɱ vāyamati divā pavivekāya rattim paṭisallānāya||
tassa evam pamattassa viharato pāmujjaɱ na hoti||
pāmujje asati pīti na hoti||
pītiyā asati passaddhi na hoti||
passaddhiyā asati dukkhaɱ viharati||
dukkhino cittaɱ na samādhiyati||
asamāhite citte dhammā na pātubhavanti||
dhammānam apātubhāvā Pamādavihārī teva saŋkhaɱ gacchati|| ||

Puna ca paraɱ Nandiya ariyasāvako Dhamme||
Saŋghe||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

So tehi ariyakantehi sīlehi santuṭṭho na uttariɱ vāyamati divā pavivekāya rattim paṭisallāṇāya||
tassa evam pamattassa viharato pāmujjaɱ na hoti||
pāmujje asati pīti na hoti||
pītiyā asati passaddhi na hoti||
passaddhiyā asati dukkhaɱ viharati||
dukkhino cittaɱ na samādhiyati||
asamahite citte dhammā na {pātubhavanti}||
dhammānam apātubhāvā Pamādavihārī teva saŋkhaɱ gacchati|| ||

Evaɱ kho Nandiya ariyasāvako pamādavihārī hoti|| ||

6. Kathañca Nandiya ariyasāvako appamādavihārī hoti|| ||

Idha Nandiya ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

So tena Buddhe aveccappasādena asantuṭṭho uttarim vāyamati divā pavivekāya rattim paṭisallāṇāya||
tassa evam appamattassa viharato pāmujjam jāyati||
pamuditassa pīti jāyati||
pītimanassa kāyo passambhati||
passaddhakāyo sukhaɱ vediyati||
sukhino cittaɱ samādhiyati||
samāhite citte dhammā pātubhavanti||
dhammānam pātubhāvā Appamādavihārī teva saŋkhaɱ gacchati

[page 399]

Puna ca param Nandiya ariyasāvako Dhamme||
Saŋghe|| ||

Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

So tehi ariyakantehi sīlehi asantuṭṭho uttariɱ vāyamati divā pavivekāya rattim patisallāṇāya||
tassa evam appamattassa viharato pāmujjaɱ jāyati||
pamuditassa pīti jāyati||
pītimanassa kāyo passambhati||
passaddhakāyo sukhaɱ vediyati||
sukhino cittaɱ samādhiyati||
samāhite citte dhammā pātubhavanti||
dhammānam pātubhāvā Appamādavihārī teva saŋkham gacchati|| ||

Evaɱ kho Nandiya ariyasāvako appamādavihārī hotī ti|| ||

Puññābhisandavaggo catuttho|| ||

Uddānaɱ|| ||

Abhisandā tayo vuttā||
dve Devapadāni ca||
Sabhāgatam Mahānāmo||
Vassaɱ Kāḷī ca Nandiyā ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter V. Sagāthapuññabhisanda Vaggo

41. Abhisanda (or Sayhaka) 1

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave puññābhisandā kusalābhisandā sukhassāhārā||
katamo cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
ayam pathamo puññābhisando|| ||

Puna ca param bhikkhave ariyasāvako Dhamme||
{Saŋghe}||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikehi||
ayaɱ catuttho puññabhisando kusalābhisando sukhassāhāro|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro puññābhisandā kusalābhisandā sukhassāhārā

[page 400]

4. Imehi kho bhikkhave catuhi puññābhisandehi kusalābhisandehi samannāgatassa ariyasāvakassa na sukaram puññassa pamāṇaɱ gaṇetuɱ ettako puññābhisando kusalābhisando sukhassāhāro ti||
atha kho Asaŋkheyyo appameyyo mahāpuññakkhandho teva saŋkhaɱ gacchati|| ||

5. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave mahāsamudde na sukaram udakassa pamāṇaɱ gaṇetuɱ ettakāni udakāḷhakānīti vā ettakāni udakāḷhakasatānīti vā ettakāni udakāḷhakasahassānī ti vā ettakāni udakāḷhakasatasahassānī ti vā||
atha kho Asaŋkheyyo appameyyo mahā udakakkhandho teva saŋkham gacchati|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave imehi catuhi puññābhisandehi kusalābhisandehi samanāgatassa ariyasāvakassa na sukaram puññassa pamāṇam gaṇetum ettako puññabhisando kusalābhisando sukhassāhāro ti|| ||

Atha kho Asaŋkheyyo appameyyo mahāpuññakkhandho teva saŋkhaɱ gacchatī ti|| ||

6. Idam avoca Bhagavā|| ||

Mahodadhim aparimitam mahāsaraɱ||
bahubheravaɱ ratnagaṇānam ālayaɱ||
Najjo yathā naragaṇasaŋghasevitā||
puthusavanti upayanti sāgaraɱ|| ||

Evaɱ naram annapānavatthadadaɱ||
seyyānisajjattharaṇassa dāyakaɱ||
puññassa dhārā upayanti paṇḍitaɱ||
najjo yathā vārivahā va sāgaran ti|| ||

[page 401]

 

 

42. Abhisanda (or Sayhaka) 2

2. Cattāro me bhikkhave puññābhisandā kusalābhisandā sukhassāhārā||
katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti-||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe|| ||

Vigatamalamaccherena cetasā agāram ajjhāvasati||
muttacāgo payatapāṇī vossaggarato yācayogo dānasaɱvibhāgarato||
ayaɱ catuttho puññābhisando sukhassāhāro|| ||

Ime kho bhicattāro puññā- kusalābhisandā sukhassāhārā|| ||

4. Imehi kho bhikkhave catuhi- -teva saŋkhaɱ gacchati|| ||

5. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave yatthimā mahānadiyo saɱsandanti samenti||
seyyathīdaɱ Gaŋgā Yamunā Aciravatī Sarabhū Mahī||
tattha na sukaram udakassa pamāṇaɱ gaṇetuɱ- -teva saŋkham gacchatī ti|| ||

6. Idam avoca Bhagavā|| ||

Etad avoca satthā|| ||

Mahodadhim aparimitaɱ mahāsaraɱ||
bahubheravaɱ ratnāgaṇānam ālayaɱ||
Najjo yathā naragaṇasaŋghasevitā||
puthusavanti hi upayanti sāgaraɱ|| ||

Evaɱ naram annapānavatthadadaɱ||
seyyānisajjattharaṇassa dāyakaɱ||
puññassa dhārā upayanti paṇḍitaɱ||
najjo yathā vārivahā va sāgaran ti|| ||

 

 

43. Abhisanda (or Sayhaka) 3

2. Cattāro me bhi- puññabhisandā- katame cattāro|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako Buddhe- -Dhamme||
... pe...||
{Saŋghe}|| ||

Paññavā hoti udayatthagāminiyā paññāya samannāgato ariyāya nibbedhikāya sammādukkhakkhaya gāminiyā

[page 402]

ayaɱ catuttho puññābhisando kusalābhisando sukhassāhāro|| ||

Ime kho bhikkhave cattāro- -sukhassāhārā|| ||

4. Imehi kho bhikkhave- -na sukaraɱ gaṇetuɱ- -mahapuññakkhandho teva saŋkhaɱ gacchatī ti|| ||

5. Idam avoca Bhagavā|| ||

Yo puññakāmo kusale patiṭṭhito||
bhāveti maggam amatassa pattiyā||
so dhammasārādhigamo khaye rato||
na vedhati maccurāja gamissatī ti|| ||

 

 

44. Mahaddhana (or Aḍḍha) 1

2. Catuhi bhikkhave dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako aḍḍho mahaddhano mahābhogo mahāyaso ti vuccati||
katamehi katuhi|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti||
akhaṇḍehi||
... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

4. Imehi kho bhikkhave catuhi dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako aḍḍho mahaddhano mahābhogo mahāyaso ti vuccatī ti|| ||

 

 

45. Mahaddhana (or Aḍḍha) 2

2. Catuhi bhikkhave dhammehi- -mahābhogo mahāyāso ti vuccati||
katamehi catuhi|| ||

3. Idha bhikkhave- -samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

4. Imehi kho bhikkhave- -mahābhogo mahāyaso ti vuccatī ti|| ||

[page 403]

 

 

46. Bhikkhū (or Suddaka) 2

katamehi catuhi|| ||

Dhamme||

4. Imehi kho bhikkhave catuhi dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sotāpanno hoti avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

 

 

47. Nandiya

1. Kapilavatthu nidānaɱ|| ||

2. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnaɱ kho Nandiyaɱ sakkam Bhagavā etad avoca|| ||

Catuhi kho Nandiya dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sotāpanno hoti- okatamehi catuhi|| ||

3. Idha Nandiya ariyasāvako Buddhe- -{saɱvattanikehi}|| ||

4. Imehi kho Nandiya catuhi dhammehi- -niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

 

 

48. Bhaddiya

1. Kapilavatthu nidānam|| ||

Upasaŋkamanaɱ kātabbaɱ|| ||

2. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnam kho Bhaddiyaɱ sakkaɱ-|| ||

3. Idha Bhaddiya ariyasāvako-|| ||

4. Imehi kho Bhaddiya catuhi- -sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

49. Mahānāma

1. Kapilavatthu nidānam||
{upasaŋkamanam} kātabbaɱ|| ||

2. Ekam antam nisinnaɱ kho Mahānāmam-|| ||

3. Idha Mahānāma ariyasāvako-|| ||

4. Imehi kho Mahānāma catuhi dhammehi- °sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

 

 

50. Aŋga

2. Cattārimāni bhikkhave sotāpattiyaŋgāni|| ||

Katamāni cattari?|| ||

3. Sappurisasaɱsevo saddhammasavanaɱ yonisomanasikāro dhammānudhammapaṭipatti|| ||

4. Imāni kho bhikkhave cattāri sotāpattiyaŋgāni|| ||

Sagāthakapuññābhisandavaggo pañcamo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Abhisandena tayo vuttā||
Duve Mahaddhanena ca||

Mahānām-Aŋgena te dasā ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter VI. Sappañña Vaggo

51. Sagāthakam

2. Catuhi bhikkhave dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sotāpanno hoti avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano||
katamehi catuhi|| ||

[page 405]

3. Idha bhikkhave ariyasāvako Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
Saŋghe||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi ... pe ...||
samādhisaɱvattanikehi|| ||

Imehi kho bhikkhave catuhi dhammehi samannāgato ariyasāvako sotāpanno hoti avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano ti|| ||

4. Idam avoca Bhagavā|| ||

Yassa saddhā Tathāgate||
acaḷā suppatiṭṭhitā||
sīlaɱ ca yassa kalyāṇaɱ||
ariyakantam pasaɱsitaɱ|| ||

Saŋghe pasādo yassatthi||
ujubhūtaɱ ca dassanaɱ||
Adaliddo ti tam āhu||
amoghaɱ tassa jīvitaɱ|| ||

Tasmā saddhañca sīlañca||
pasādaɱ dhammadassanaɱ||
anuyuñjetha medhāvī||
saram buddhānasāsanan ti|| ||

 

 

52. Vassavuttham

1. Ekam samayam Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena aññataro bhikkhu Sāvatthiyaɱ vassaɱ vuttho Kapilavatthum anuppatto hoti kenacid eva karaṇīyena|| ||

3. Assosum kho Kāpilavatthavā Sakyā||
aññataro bhikkhu Sāvatthiyaɱ vassaɱ vutto Kapilavatthum anuppatto ti|| ||

4. Atha kho Kāpilavatthavā Sakyā yena so bhikkhu tenupasaŋkamiɱsu||
upasaŋkamitvā tam bhikkhum abhivādetvā ekam antam nisīdiɱsu|| ||

Ekam antam nisinnā kho Kāpilavatthavā sakyā tam bhikkhum etad avocuɱ|| ||

5. Kacci bhante Bhagavā arogo ceva balavā cā ti|| ||

Arogo cāvuso Bhagavā balavā cā ti|| ||

[page 406]

Kacci pana bhante Sāriputta-Moggalānā arogā ceva balavanto cā ti|| ||

Sāriputta-Moggalānā pi kho avuso arogā ceva balavanto cā ti|| ||

Kacci pana bhante bhikkhusaŋgho arogo ca balavā cā ti|| ||

Bhikkhusaŋgho pi kho āvuso arogo ca balavā cā ti|| ||

6. Atthi pana te bhante kiñci iminā antaravassena Bhagavato sammukhā sutaɱ sammukhā paṭiggahītan ti|| ||

Sammukhā me tam āvuso Bhagavato sutaɱ sammukhā paṭiggahītaɱ|| ||

Appakā te bhikkhave bhikkhū ye āsavānaɱ khayā anāsavaɱ cetovimuttiɱ paññāvimuttiɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharanti||
atha kho eteva bahutarā bhikkhū ye pañcannam orambhāgiyānaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā opapātikā tattha parinibbāyino anāvattidhammā asmā lokā ti|| ||

7. Aparampi kho me āvuso Bhagavato sammukhā sutaɱ sammukhā paṭiggahītaɱ|| ||

Appakā te bhikkhave bhikkhū ye pañcannam orambhāgiyānam saŋyojanānam parikkhayā opapātikā tattha parinibbāyino anāvattidhammā asmā lokā||
atha kho ete bahutarā bhikkhū ye tiṇṇam saŋyojanānam parikkhayā rāgadosamohānaɱ tanuttā sakadāgāmino sakideva imaɱ lokam āgantvā dukkhassantaɱ karissantī ti|| ||

8. Aparam pi kho me āvuso Bhagavato sammukhā sutaɱ sammukhā patiggahītaɱ|| ||

Appakā te bhikkhave bhikkhū ye tiṇṇaɱ saŋyojanānaɱ parikkhayā rāgadosamohānaɱ tanuttā sakadāgāmino sakid eva imaɱ lokam āgantvā dukkhassantaɱ karissanti||
atha kho eteva bahutarā bhikkhū ye tiṇṇaɱ saŋyojanānam parikkhayā sotāpannā avinipātadhammā niyatā sambodhiparāyanā ti|| ||

 

 

53. Dhammadinna

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Bārānasiyaɱ viharati Isipatane Migadāye|| ||

[page 407]

2. Atha kho Dhammadinno upāsako pañcahi upāsakasatehi saddhiɱ yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Dhammadinno upāsako Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

3. Ovadatu no bhante Bhagavā anusāsatu no bhante Bhagavā yam amhākam assa dīgharattam hitāya sukhāyā ti|| ||

Tasmā ti ha vo Dhammadinna evaɱ sikkhitabbaɱ|| ||

Ye te suttantā Tathāgatabhāsitā gambhīrā gambhīratthā lokuttarā suññatapaṭisaɱyuttā||
te kālena kālam upasampajja viharissāmā ti|| ||

Evaɱ hi vo Dhammadinna sikkhitabban ti|| ||

4. Na kho netam bhante sukaram amhehi puttasambādhasayanam ajjhāvasantehi kāsikaɱ candanam paccanubhontehi mālāgandhavilepanaɱ dhārayantehi jātarūparajataɱ sādiyantehi||
ye te suttantā gambhīrā gambhīratthā lokuttarā suññatapaṭisaɱyuttā te kālena kālam upasampajja viharituɱ|| ||

Tesaɱ no bhante Bhagavā amhākam pañcasu sikkhāpadesu ṭhitānam uttaridhammaɱ desetū ti|| ||

5. Tasmā ti ha vo Dhammadinna evam sikkhitabbaɱ||
Buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgatā bhavissāma||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti||
Dhamme||
{Saŋghe}||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgata bhavissāma akhaṇḍehi ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikehī ti|| ||

Evaɱ hi vo Dhammadinna sikkhitabban ti|| ||

Yānimāni bhante Bhagavatā cattāri sotāpattiyaŋgāni desitāni||
saɱvijjante te dhammā amhesu mayañ ca tesu dhammesu sandissāma|| ||

6. Mayaɱ hi bhante Buddhe aveccappasadena samannāgatā||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti

[page 408]

Dhamme||
Saŋghe||
pe-[pa]||
Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgatā akhaṇḍehi ... pe ... {samādhisaɱvattanikehī} ti|| ||

7. Lābhā vo Dhammadinna suladdhaɱ vo Dhammadinna sotāpattiphalaɱ Dhammadinna vyākatan ti|| ||

 

 

54. Gilāyanam

1. Ekam samayam Bhagavā Sakkesu viharati Kapilavatthusmiɱ Nigrodhārāme|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena sambahulā bhikkhū Bhagavato cīvarakammaɱ karonti Niṭṭhitacīvaro Bhagavā temāsaccayena cārikam pakkamissatī ti|| ||

3. Assosi kho Mahānāmo sakko Sambahulā kira bhikkhū Bhagavato cīvarakammaɱ karonti Niṭṭhitacīvaro Bhagavā temāsaccayena cārikam pakkamissatī ti|| ||

Atha kho Mahānāmo sakko yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi||
eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Mahānāmo sakko Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

4. Sutam etam bhante Sambahulā kira bhikkhū Bhagavato cīvarakammaɱ karonti Niṭṭhitacīvaro Bhagavā temāsaccayena cārikam pakkamissatī ti||
Na kho te etam bhante Bhagavato sammukhā sutaɱ sammukhā paṭiggahītaɱ sappaññena upāsakena sappañño upāsako ābādhīko dukkhito bāḷhagilāno ovaditabbo ti|| ||

5. Sappaññena Mahānama upāsakena sappañño upāsako ābādhiko dukkhito bāḷhagilāno catuhi assāsaniyehi dhammehi assāsetabbo|| ||

Assāsatāyasmā atthāyasmato Buddhe aveccappasādena||
Iti pi so Bhagavā ... pe ... satthā devamanussānaɱ buddho bhagavā ti|| ||

Assāsatāyasmā atthāyasmato Dhamme Saŋghe||
Ariyakantāni sīlāni akhaṇḍāni ... pe ... samādhisaɱvattanikānī ti|| ||

[page 409]

6. Sappaññena Mahānāma upāsakena sappañño upāsako ābādhiko dukkhito bāḷhagilāno imehi catuhi assāsaniyehi dhammehi assāsetvā evam assa vacanīyo|| ||

7. Atthāyasmato mātāpitusu apekhā ti||
so ce evaɱ vadeyya Atthi me mātāpitusu apekhā ti so evam assa vacanīyo||
Āyasmā pi kho māriso maraṇadhammo||
sace pāyasmā mātāpitusu apekhaɱ karissati marissateva||
no ce pāyasmā mātāpitusu apekhaɱ karissati marissateva||
sādhāyasmā yā te mātāpitusu apekhā tam pajahāti|| ||

8. So ce evam vadeyya||
Yā me mātāpitusu apekhā sā pahīnā ti||
so evam assa vacanīyo||
Atthi panāyasmato puttadāresu apekhā ti|| ||

Sa ce evaɱ vadeyya Atthi me puttadāresu apekhā ti||
so evam assa vacanīyo||
Āyasmā kho māriso maraṇadhammo sace pāyasmā puttadāresu apekham karissati marissateva||
no ce pāyasmā puttadāresu apekhaɱ karissati marissateva||
sādhāyasmā yā te puttadāresu apekhā tam pajahā ti|| ||

9. So ce evaɱ vadeyya||
Yā me puttadāresu apekhā sā pahīnā ti||
so evam assa vacanīyo||
Atthi panāyasmato mānussakesu pañcasu kāmaguṇesu apekhā ti|| ||

So ce evaɱ vadeyya||
Atthi me mānussakesu pañcasu kāmagunesu apekhā ti||
so evam assa vacanīyo||
Mānussakehi kho āvuso kāmehi dibbā kāmā abhikkantatarā ca paṇitatarā ca||
sādhāyasmā mānussakehi kāmehi cittaɱ vuṭṭhāpetvā catummahārājikesu devesu cittam adhimocehī ti|| ||

10. So ce evaɱ vadeyya||
Mānussakehi kāmehi cittaɱ vuṭṭhitaɱ cātummahārājikesu devesu cittaɱ adhimocitanti||
so evam assa vacanīyo||
Cātummahārājikehi kho āvuso devehi Tāvatiɱsā devā abhikkantatarā ca paṇitatarā ca

[page 410]

sādhāyasmā cātummahārājikehi cātummahārājikehi devehi cittaɱ vuṭṭhāpetvā Tāvatiɱsesu devesu cittam adhimocehī ti|| ||

11—16. So ce evaɱ vadeyya||
Cātummahārājikehi me devehi cittaɱ vuṭṭhitaɱ Tāvatiɱsesu devesu cittam adhimocitan ti||
so evam assa vacanīyo||
Tāvatiɱsehi kho avuso devehi pi Yāmā devā Tusitā devā Nimmānaratidevā Paranimmitavasavattino devā|| ||

17. Parinimmitavasavattīhi kho āvuso devehi Brahmaloko abhikkantataro ca paṇitataro ca||
sādhāyasmā Parinimittavasavattīhi devehi cittaɱ vuṭṭhāpetvā Brahmaloke cittam adhimocehī ti|| ||

18. So ce evaɱ vadeyya||
Paranimmitavasavattīhi me devehi cittaɱ vuṭṭhitam Brahmaloke cittam adhimocitan ti||
so evam assa vacanīyo||
Brahmaloko pi kho āvuso anicco adhuvo sakkāya pariyāpanno||
sādhāyasmā Brahmalokā cittaɱ vuṭṭhāpetvā sakkāya nirodhe cittam upasaɱharāhī ti|| ||

19. So ce evam vadeyya||
Brahmalokā me cittaɱ vuṭṭhitaɱ sakkāya nirodhe cittam upasaɱharāmīti||
evaɱ vuttassa kho Mahānāma upāsakassa āsavā vimuttacittena bhikkhunā na kiñci nānākaraṇaɱ vadāmi yad idam vimuttiyā vimuttinti|| ||

[page 411]

Book XII

Sacca Saɱyutta

Chapter I. Samādhi Vaggo

1. Samādhi

1. Sāvatthi||
... pe ...|| ||

2. Samādhim bhikkhave bhāvetha|| ||

Samāhito bhikkhave bhikkhu yathābhūtam pajānāti|| ||

Kiñca yathābhūtam pajānāti?|| ||

3. Idam dukkhan ti pajānāti||
ayaɱ dukkhasamudayo ti yathābhūtam pa-||
ayam dukkhanirodho ti yathābhūtam pa-||
ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānāti|| ||

4. Samādhim bhikkhave bhāvetha samāhito bhikkhave bhikkhu yathābhūtam pajānāti|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idam dukkhanti yogo karaṇīyo||
Ayaɱ dukkhasamudayo ti yogo karanīyo||
Ayam dukkhanirodho ti yogo karaṇīyo||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo|| ||

 

 

2. Patisallā

2. Paṭisallāṇe bhikkhave yogam āpajjatha||
paṭisallīno bhikkhave bhikkhu yathābhūtam pajānāti||
Kiñca yathābhūtam pajānāti|| ||

3. Idaɱ dukkhan ti yathābhūtam pajānāti||
ayam dukkhasamudayo ti yathābhūtam ... pe ...ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānāti|| ||

[page 415]

4. Paṭisallāṇe bhikkhave yogam āpajjatha||
paṭisallīno bhikkhave bhikkhu yathābhūtam pajānāti|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

3. Kulaputta 1

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānam kulaputtā sammāagārasmā anagāriyam pabbajiɱsu||
sabbe te catunnam ariyasaccānaɱ yathābhūtam abhisamayāya|| ||

3. Ye pi hi keci bhikkhave anāgatam addhānam kulaputtā sammāagārasmā anagāriyam pabbajjissanti||
sabbe te catunnam ariyasaccānaɱ yathābhūtam abhisamayāya|| ||

4. Ye pi hi keci bhikkhave etarahi kulaputtā sammāagārasmā anagāriyam pabbajjanti||
sabbe te catunnam ariyasaccānaɱ yathābhūtam abhisamayāya|| ||

Katamesaɱ catunnam?|| ||

5. Dukkhassa ariyasaccassa||
Dukkhasamudayassa ariyasaccassa||
dukkhanirodhassa ariyasaccassa||
dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ariyasaccassa|| ||

6. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānaɱ kulaputtā sammāagārasmā anagāriyam pabbajiɱsu||
pabbajissanti||
pabbajanti||
sabbe te imesaɱ yeva catunnam ariyasaccānam yathābhūtam abhisamayāya|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhanti ... pe ... yogo karaṇīyo||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

4. Kulaputta 2

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānaɱ kulaputtā sammāagārasmā anagāriyam pabbajitā yathābhūtam abhisamesuɱ||
sabbe te cattāri ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisamesuɱ|| ||

3. Ye pi hi keci bhikkhave anāgatam addhānaɱ kulaputtā sammāagārasmā anagāriyam pabbajitā yathābhūtaɱ abhisamessanti

[page 416]

sabbe te ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisamessanti|| ||

4. Ye pi hi keci bhikkhave etarahi kulaputtā sammāagārasmā anagāriyam pabbajitā yathābhūtam abhisamenti||
sabbe te cattāri ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisamenti||
Katame cattāri|| ||

5. Dukkham ariyasaccam ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

6. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānam kulaputtā sammāagārasmā anagāriyam pabbajitā yathābhūtam abhisamesuɱ||
abhisamessanti||
abhisamenti||
sabbe te imāni cattāri ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisamenti|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ...||
Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

5. Samaṇabrāhmaṇā 1

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānam samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yathābhūtam abhisambujjhiɱsu||
sabbe te cattāri ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisambujjhissanti|| ||

3. Ye° °anāgatam addhānam° °abhisambujjhissanti|| ||

4. Ye pi hi keci bhikkhave etarahi samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yathābhūtam abhisambujjhanti sabbe te cattāri ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisambujjhanti|| ||

Katamāni cattāri|| ||

Dukkham ariyasaccam ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

5. Ye pi hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānam samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā va yathābhūtam abhisambujjhiɱsu||
abhisambujjhissanti abhisambujjhanti||
sabbe te imāni cattāri ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisambujjhanti

[page 417]

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...|| ||

Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhayāminī patipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo|| ||

 

 

6. Samaṇabrāhmaṇā 2

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yathābhūtam abhisambuddham pakāsesuɱ||
sabbe te cattāri ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisambuddham pakāsesuɱ|| ||

3. Ye pi hi keci bhikkhave anāgatam addhānaɱ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yathābhūtam abhisambuddham pakāsessanti sabbe te cattāri ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisambuddham pakāsessanti|| ||

5. Ye pi hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānam samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yathābhūtam abhisambuddham pakāsesuɱ||
pakāsessanti||
pakāsenti||
sabbe te imāni cattāri ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisambuddham pakāsenti|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idam dukkhan ti yogo karanīyo||
... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

7. Vitakkā

2. Mā bhikkhave pāpake akusale vitakke vitakkeyyātha||
{seyyathīdaɱ} kāmavitakkaɱ vyāpādavitakkam vihiɱsāvitakkaɱ|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

3. Nete bhikkhave vitakkā atthasaɱhitā nādibrahmacariyakā na nibbidāya na virāgāya na nirodhāya na upasamāya na abhiññāya na sambodhāya na nibbānāya saɱvattantī ti

[page 418]

4. Vitakkentā ca kho tumhe bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti vitakkeyyātha||
... pe ...||
ayaɱ dukkhanirodho ti vitakkeyyātha||
ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti vitakkeyyātha|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

5. Ete bhikkhave vitakkā atthasaɱhitā ete brahmacariyakā ete ādibrahmacariyakā ete nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāyā upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattanti|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idam dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

8. Cintā

2. Mā bhikkhave pāpakam akusalaɱ cittaɱ cinteyyātha||
Sassato loko ti vā Asassato loko ti vā|| ||

Antavā loko ti vā Anantavā loko ti vā|| ||

Taɱ jīvaɱ taɱ sarīran ti vā||
Aññaɱ jīvaɱ aññaɱ sarīran ti vā|| ||

Hoti Tathāgato parammaraṇā ti vā||
Na hoti Tathāgato parammaraṇā ti vā||
Hoti ca na ca hoti Tathāgato parammaraṇā ti vā||
Neva hoti na na hoti Tathāgato parammaraṇā ti vā|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

3. Nesā bhikkhave cintā atthasaɱhitā nādibrahmacariyikā na nibbidāya na virāgāya na nirodhāya na upasamāya na abhiññaya na sambodhāya na nibbānāya saɱvattanti|| ||

4. Cintentā ca kho tumhe bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhanti cinteyyātha ... pe ...Ayam dukkhanirodhāgāminī patipadā ti cinteyyātha|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

5. Esā bhikkhave cintā atthasañhitā esā ādibrahmacariyikā esā nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānaya saɱvattati

[page 419]

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idam dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti||
yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

9. Viggāhikā

2. Mā bhikkhave viggāhikakathaɱ katheyyātha||
Na tvam imaɱ dhammavinayam ājānāsi||
aham imaɱ dhammavinayam ājānāmi||
kiɱ tvam imaɱ dhammavinayam ājānissasi|| ||

Micchāpaṭipanno tvam asi||
aham asmi sammāpaṭipanno|| ||

Pure vacanīyam pacchā avaca pacchā vacanīyam pure avaca|| ||

Sahitam me asahitan te|| ||

Āciṇṇan te viparāvattaɱ|| ||

Āropito te vādo||
cara vādappamokkhāya Niggahīto si nibbeṭhehi sace pahosī ti|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

3. Nesā bhikkhave kathā atthasaɱhitā nādibrahmacariyikā na nibbidāya na virāgāya na nirodhāya na upasamāya na abhiññāya na sambodhāya na nibbānāya saɱvattati|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

5. Esā hi bhikkhave kathā ... pe ... yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||
