Chapter II. Dhammacakkapavattana Vaggo

11. Tathāgatena vutta 1

1. Evam me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Bārāṇasiyaɱ viharati Isipatane Migadāye|| ||

[page 421]

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā pañcavaggiye bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Dve me bhikkhave antā pabbajitena na sevittabbā|| ||

Katame dve?|| ||

3. Yo cāyaɱ kāmesu kāmesu khallikānuyogo hīno gammo puthujjanīko anariyo anatthasaɱhito.|| ||

Yo cāyam attakilamathānuyogo dukkho anariyo anatthasaɱhito.|| ||

Ete te bhikkhave ubho ante anupakamma majjhimā paṭipadā Tathāgatena abhisambuddhā cakkhukaraṇī ñāṇakaraṇī upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattati.|| ||

4. Katamā ca sā bhikkhave majjhimā paṭipadā Tathāgatena abhisambuddhā cakkhukaraṇī ñāṇakaraṇī upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattati?|| ||

Ayam eva ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo.|| ||

Seyyathīdaɱ||
sammādiṭṭhi sammāsaŋkappo sammāvācā sammākammanto sammā-ājīvo sammāvāyāmo sammāsati sammāsamādhi|| ||

Ayam kho sā bhikkhave majjhimā paṭipadā Tathāgatena abhisambuddhā cakkhu° ñaṇakaraṇī upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattati.|| ||

5. Idaɱ kho pana bhikkhave dukkham ariyasaccaɱ.|| ||

Jāti pi dukkhā jarā pi dukkhā vyādhi pi dukkhā maraṇam pi dukkhaɱ sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsā pi dukkhā.|| ||

Appiyehi sampayogo dukkho piyehi vippayogo dukkho||
yam p'icchaɱ na labhati tam pi dukkhaɱ.|| ||

Saɱkhittena pañc'upādānakkhandhā pi dukkhā.|| ||

6. Idam kho pana bhikkhave dukkhasamudayam ariyasaccaɱ.|| ||

Yāyaɱ taṇhā ponobbhavikā nandī rāgasahagatā tatra tatrābhinandinī.|| ||

Seyyathīdaɱ:|| ||

Kāmataṇhā bhavataṇhā vibhavataṇhā|| ||

7. Idaɱ kho pana bhikkhave dukkhanirodham ariyasaccaɱ.|| ||

Yo tassā yeva taṇhāya asesavirāganirodho cāgo paṭinissaggo mutti anālayo.|| ||

8. Idaɱ kho pana bhikkhave dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccam.

[page 422]

Ayam eva ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo.|| ||

Seyyathīdaɱ:|| ||

Sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ... sammāsamādhi.|| ||

9. Idaɱ dukkham ariyasaccan ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ñāṇam udapādi paññā udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādi.|| ||

Taɱ kho pan'idaɱ dukkham ariyasaccam pariññeyyan ti me bhikkhave pubbe ... pe ... pariññātan ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ... āloko udapādi.|| ||

10. Idaɱ dukkhasamudayaɱ ariyasaccan ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ñāṇam udapādi paññā udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādi.|| ||

Taɱ kho pan'idaɱ dukkhasamudayam ariyasaccam pahātabban ti me bhikkhave pubbe ... pe ... pahīnan ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ... āloko udapādi|| ||

11. Idaɱ dukkhanirodham ariyasaccan ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ñāṇam udapādi paññā udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādi.|| ||

Taɱ kho pan'idaɱ dukkhanirodham ariyasaccaɱ sacchikātabban ti me bhikkhave pubbe ... pe ... sacchikatan ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ... āloko udapādi.|| ||

12. Idaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccan ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ñāṇam udapādi paññā udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādi.|| ||

Tam kho pan'idaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccam bhāvetabban ti me bhikkhave ... pe ... bhāvitan ti me bhikkhave pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ñāṇam udapādi paññā udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādi.|| ||

13. Yāva kīvañ ca me bhikkhave imesu catusu ariyasaccesu evaɱ tiparivaṭṭaɱ dvādasākāraɱ yathābhūtaɱ ñāṇaḍassanaɱ na suvisuddham ahosi.|| ||

N'eva tāvāham bhikkhave

[page 423]

sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya anuttaraɱ sammāsambodhim abhisambuddho ti paccaññāsiɱ.|| ||

14. Yato ca kho me bhikkhave imesu catusu ariyasaccesu evaɱ tiparivaṭṭam dvādasākāraɱ yathābhūtam ñāṇadassanaɱ suvisuddham ahosi.|| ||

Athāham bhikkhave sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya anuttaram sammāsambodhim abhisambuddho ti paccaññāsiɱ.|| ||

Ñāṇañ ca pana me dassanam udapādi akuppā me cetovimutti ayam antimā jāti n'atthi dāni punabbhavo ti|| ||

15. Idam avoca Bhagavā.|| ||

Attamanā pañcavaggiyā bhikkhū Bhagavato bhāsitam abhinanduɱ.|| ||

Imasmiɱ ca pana veyyākaraṇasmim bhaññamāne āyasmato Koṇḍaññassa virajaɱ vītamalaɱ dhammacakkhum udapādi.|| ||

Yaɱ kiñci samudayadhammaɱ sabban taɱ nirodhadhamman ti.|| ||

16. Evam pavattite ca pana Bhagavatā dhammacakke bhummā devā saddam anussāvesuɱ.|| ||

Etam Bhagavatā Bārāṇasiyam Isipatane Migadāye anuttaraɱ dhammacakkam pavattitaɱ appativattiyaɱ samaṇena vā brāhmaṇena vā devena vā Mārena vā Brahmunā vā kenaci vā lokasmin ti.|| ||

17. Bhummānaɱ devānaɱ saddaɱ sutvā Cātummahārājikā devā saddam anussāvesuɱ.|| ||

Etam Bhagavatā Bārāṇasiyam Isipatane Migadāye anuttaraɱ dhammacakkam pavattitam appativattiyaɱ samaṇena vā brāhmaṇena vā devena vā Mārena vā Brahmuṇā vā kenaci vā lokasmin ti|| ||

18. Cātummahārājikānaɱ devānaɱ saddaɱ sutvā Tāvaṭiɱsā devā Yāmā devā Tusitā devā Nimmānaratī devā Paranimmittavasavattino devā Brahmakāyikā devā saddam anussāvesuɱ|| ||

Etam Bhagavatā Bārāṇasiyaɱ Isipatane Migadāye anuttaraɱ dhammacakkam pavattitaɱ

[page 424]

appativattiyaɱ samaṇena vā brāhmaṇena vā devena vā Mārena vā Brahmunā vā kenaci vā lokasmin ti.

19. Iti ha tena khaṇena tena layena tena muhuttena yāva Brahmalokā saddo abbhuggacchi.|| ||

Ayañ ca dasasahassī lokadhātu saɱkampi sampakampi sampavedhi.|| ||

Appamāṇo ca uḷāro obhāso loke pātur ahosi atikkamma devānaɱ devānubhāvan ti.|| ||

20. Atha kho Bhagavā udānam udānesi.|| ||

Aññāsi vata bho Koṇḍañño aññāsi vata bho Koṇḍañño ti.|| ||

Iti h'idam āyasmato Koṇḍaññassa Aññāta-Koṇḍañño tv eva nāmam ahosī ti.|| ||

 

 

12. Tathāgatena vutta 2

2. Idaɱ dukkham ariyasaccan ti bhikkhave tathāgatānam pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ñāṇam udapādi paññā udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādi|| ||

Taɱ kho pan'idaɱ dukkham ariyasaccam pariññeyyan ti bhikkhave tathāgatānam pubbe ... pe ... pariññātan ti bhikkhave tathāgatānam pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ... āloko udapādi|| ||

3. Idaɱ dukkhasamudayam ariyasaccan ti bhikkhave tathāgatānam pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ... āloko udapādi|| ||

Taɱ kho pan'idaɱ dukkhasamudayam ariyasaccam pahātabban ti bhikkhave tathāgatānam pubbe ... pe ... pahīnan ti bhikkhave tathāgatānam pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ... āloko udapādi|| ||

4. Idaɱ dukkhanirodham ariyasaccan ti bhikkhave Tathāgatanam pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ... āloko udapādi|| ||

Taɱ kho pan'idaɱ dukkhanirodham ariyasaccam sacchikātabban ti tathāgatānam pubbe la-pe

[page 425]

sacchikatan ti bhikkhave tathāgatānam pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ... pe ... āloko udapādi|| ||

5. Idaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccan ti bhikkhave tathāgatānam pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ñāṇam udapādi paññā udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādi|| ||

Taɱ kho pan'idaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccam bhāvetabban ti bhikkhave tathāgatānam pubbe ... pe ... bhāvitan ti bhikkhave tathāgatānam pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhum udapādi ñāṇam udapādi paññā udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādī ti|| ||

 

 

13. Khandha

2. Cattārimāni bhikkhave ariyasaccāni||
katamāni cattāri|| ||

Dukkham ariyasaccaɱ||
dukkhasamudayam ariya°||
dukkhanirodham ariya° dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

3. Katamañ ca bhikkhave dukkham ariyasaccam|| ||

Pañcupādānakkhandhā tissa vacanīyaɱ||
seyyathīdaɱ|| ||

Rūpūpādānakkhandho ... pe ... viññānūpādānakkhando|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave dukkham ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

4. Katamañ ca bhikkhave dukkhasamudayam ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

Yāyaɱ taṇhā ponobhavikā nandirāgasahagatā tatra tatatrābhinandinī||
seyyathīdaɱ kāmataṇhā bhavataṇhā vibhavataṇhā|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave dukkhasamudayam ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

5. Katamañ ca bhikkhave dukkhanirodham ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

Yo tassā yeva taṇhāya asesavirāganirodho cāgo paṭinissaggo mutti anālayo|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave dukkhanirodham ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

6. Katamañ ca bhikkhave dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

Ayam eva ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo||
seyyathīdam||
sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ... sammāsamādhi|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

[page 426]

7. Imāni kho bhikkhave ariyasaccāni|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave||
Idam dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...|| ||

Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

14. Āyatana

2. Cattārimāni bhikkhave ariyasaccāni-||
-ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

3. Katamañ ca bhikkhave dukkham ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

Cha ajjhattikāni āyatanāni tissa vacanīyaɱ|| ||

Katamāni cha?|| ||

Cakkhāyatanaɱ ... pe ... manāyatanaɱ|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave dukkham ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

4. Katamañ ca bhi- dukkhasamudayam ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

Yāyaɱ taṇhā ponobbhavikā nandirāgasahagatā tatra tatrābhinandinī||
seyyathīdaɱ kāmataṇhā bhavataṇhā vibhavataṇhā|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave dukkhasamudayam ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

5. Katamañ ca bhi- dukkhanirodham ariyasaccaɱ||
yo tasseva taṇhāya asesavirāganirodho cāgo paṭinissaggo mutti anālayo|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave dukkhanirodham ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

6. Katamañ ca bhikkhave dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

Ayam eva ariyo aṭṭhaŋgiko maggo||
seyyathīdam||
sammādiṭṭhi ... pe ... sammāsamādhi|| ||

Idaɱ vuccati bhikkhave dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

7. Imāni kho bhikkhave cattāri ariyasaccāni|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karāṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

15. Dhārana 1

2. Dhāretha no tumhe bhikkhave mayā cattāri ariyasaccāni desitānī ti|| ||

3. Evaɱ vutte aññataro bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca

[page 427]

Ahaɱ kho bhante dhāremi Bhagavatā cattāri ariyasaccāni desitānī ti|| ||

Yathā kathaɱ pana tvam bhikkhu dhāresi mayā cattāri ariyasaccāni desitānī ti|| ||

4. Dukkhaɱ khvāham bhante Bhagavatā pathamam ariyasaccam desitaɱ dhāremi||
dukkhasamudayaɱ khvāhaɱ bhante Bhagavatā dutiyam ariyasaccam desitaɱ dhāremi||
dukkhanirodhaɱ khvāham bhante Bhagavatā tatiyam ariyasaccam dhāremi||
dukkhanirodhagāminiɱ paṭipadaɱ khvāham bhante Bhagavatā catuttham ariyasaccaɱ desitaɱ dhāremi|| ||

Evaɱ khvāham bhante dhāremi Bhagavatā cattāri ariyasaccāni desitānī ti|| ||

5. Sādhu sādhu bhikkhu sādhu kho tvam bhikkhu dhāresi mayā cattāri ariyasaccāni desitāni|| ||

Dukkhaɱ kho bhikkhu mayā pathamam ariyasaccaɱ desitaɱ tathā naɱ dhārehi ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadaɱ kho bhikkhu mayā catuttham ariyasaccaɱ desitaɱ tathā naɱ dhārehi|| ||

6. Evaɱ kho bhikkhu dhārehi mayā cattāri ariyasaccāni desitāni|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhu Idam dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...|| ||

Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

16. Dhārana 2

2. Dhāretha no tumhe bhikkhave mayā cattāri ariyasaccāni desitāni|| ||

3. Evaɱ vutte aññataro bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Ahaɱ kho bhante dhāremi Bhagavatā cattāri ariyasaccāni desitānī ti|| ||

Yathā katham pana tvam bhikkhu dhāresi mayā cattāri ariyasaccāni desitānī ti|| ||

[page 428]

4. Dukkham khvāhaɱ bhante Bhagavatā pathamam ariyasaccaɱ desitaɱ dhāremi|| ||

Yo hi koci bhante samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā evaɱ vadeyya|| ||

Netaɱ dukkham pathamam ariyasaccaɱ yaɱ samaṇena Gotamena desitaɱ||
aham etaɱ dukkham pathamam ariyasaccam paccakkhāya aññaɱ dukkham pathamaɱ ariyasaccam paññāpessāmī ti netaɱ ṭhānam vijjati|| ||

5—6. Dukkhasamudayam khvāham bhante Bhagavatā||
... pe ...|| ||

7. Dukkhanirodhagāminiɱ paṭipadaɱ khvāham bhante Bhagavatā catuttham ariyasaccaɱ desitaɱ dhāremi|| ||

Yo hi koci bhante samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā evaɱ vadeyya|| ||

Netaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadā catuttham ariyasaccam yaɱ samaṇena Gotamena desitam||
aham etaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminiɱ paṭipadaɱ catutthaɱ ariyasaccam paccakkhāya aññaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminim paṭipadaɱ catutthaɱ ariyasaccam paññāpessāmī ti netaɱ thānaɱ vijjati|| ||

8. Evam khvāham bhante dhāremi Bhagavatā cattāri ariyasaccāni desitanī ti|| ||

9. Sādhu sādhu bhikkhu sādhu kho tvam bhikkhu dhāresi mayā cattāri ariyasaccāni desitāni|| ||

Dukkhaɱ kho bhikkhu mayā pathamam ariyasaccaɱ desitaɱ tathā nam dhārehi|| ||

Yo hi koci bhikkhu samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā evaɱ vadeyya|| ||

Netaɱ dukkham pathamam ariyasaccaɱ samaṇena Gotamena desitaɱ||
aham etaɱ dukkham pathamam ariyasaccam pacchakkhāya aññam dukkham ariyasaccam paññāpessamī ti netam ṭhānam vijjati|| ||

Dukkhasamudayaɱ kho bhikkhu||
... pe ...|| ||

Dukkhanirodhaɱ kho bhikkhu ... pe ... Dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadaɱ kho bhikkhu mayā catuttham ariyasaccaɱ desitaɱ tathā naɱ dhārehi|| ||

Yohi koci bhikkhu samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā evam vadeyya Netaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminipatipadā catuttham ari yasaccaɱ yaɱ samaṇena Gotamena desitaɱ

[page 429]

aham etaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadam catuttham ariyasaccam paccakkhāya aññam dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadaɱ catuttham ariyasaccam paññāpessāmīti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

9. Evaɱ kho tvam bhikkhu dhārehi mayā cattāri ariyasaccāni desitāni|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhu Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...|| ||

Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

17. Avijjā

2. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu° °nisīdi|| ||

3. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Avijjā avijjā ti bhante vuccati|| ||

Katamā nu kho bhante avijjā kittāvatā ca avijjāgato hotī ti|| ||

4. Yaɱ kho bhikkhu dukkhe aññāṇam dukkhasamudaye aññāṇam dukkhanirodhe aññāṇaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya aññāṇaɱ ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhu avijjā ettāvatā ca avijjāgato hotī ti|| ||

5. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhu Idam dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...|| ||

Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

18. Vijjā

2. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi|| ||

3. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho so bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Vijjā vijjā ti bhante vuccati||
Katamā nu kho bhante vijjā kittāvatā ca vijjāgato hotī ti|| ||

[page 430]

4. Yaɱ kho bhikkhu dukkhe ñāṇaɱ dukkhasamudaye ñāṇaɱ dukkhanirodhe ñāṇaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadāya ñāṇaɱ ayaɱ vuccati bhikkhu vijjā|| ||

Ettāvatā ca vijjāgato hoti|| ||

5. Tasmā tiha bhikkhu Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

19. Saŋkāsanā

2. Idaɱ dukkham ariyasaccan ti bhikkhave mayā paññattaɱ||
tattha aparimāṇā vaṇṇā aparimāṇā vyañjanā aparimāṇā saɱkāsanā itipidam dukkham ariyasaccan ti|| ||

3. Idaɱ dukkhasamudayaɱ||
... pe ...|| ||

4. Idaɱ dukkhanirodham||
... pe ...|| ||

5. Idaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccan ti bhikkhave mayā paññattaɱ||
tattha aparimāṇā vaṇṇā aparimāṇā vyañjanā aparimāṇā saɱkāsanā itipidaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccan ti|| ||

6. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhu Idaɱ dukkhanti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...|| ||

Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karanīyo ti|| ||

 

 

20. Tathā

2. Cattārīmāni bhikkhave tathāni avitathāni anaññathāni||
katamāni cattāri|| ||

3. Idaɱ dukkhan ti bhikkhave tatham etam avitatham etam anaññatatham etaɱ|| ||

4. Ayaɱ dukkhasamudayo ti tatham etaɱ avitatham etam anaññatham etaɱ|| ||

5. Ayaɱ dukkhanirodho ti tatham etaɱ avitatham etam anaññatham etaɱ|| ||

[page 431]

6. Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti tatham etam avitatham etam anaññatham etaɱ|| ||

7. Imāni kho bhikkhave cattāri tatthāni avitathāni anaññathāni|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
la-... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇī yoti|| ||

Dhammacakkapavattanavaggo dutiyo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Tathāgatena dve vuttā||
Khandhā Āyatanena ca||
Dhāraṇāya dve vuttā||
Avijjā Vijjā Saŋkāsanā Tathena cā ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter III. Kotigāma Vaggo

21. Vijjā 1

1. Evam me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Vajjisu viharati Koṭigāme|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Catunnam bhikkhave ariyasaccānam ananubodhā appaṭivedhā evam idaɱ dīgham addhānam sandhāvitaɱ saɱsaritaɱ mamañceva tuɱhakañca||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

3. Dukkhassa bhikkhave ariyasaccassa ananubodhā appaṭivedhā evam idaɱ dīgham addhānaɱ sandhāvitaɱ saɱsaritam mamañceva tumhākañca|| ||

Dukkhasamudayassa ariyasaccassa||
... pe ...|| ||

Dukkhanirodhassa ariyasaccassa|| ||

Dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadāya ariyasaccassa ananubodhā appaṭivedhā evaɱ dīgham addhānaɱ sandhāvitaɱ saɱsaritam mamañceva tumhākañca

[page 432]

4. Tayidam bhikkhave dukkham ariyasaccaɱ anubuddhaɱ paṭividdham||
dukkhasamudayam ariyasaccam anubuddham paṭividdham||
dukkhanirodham ariyasaccaɱ... pe ...
dukkanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccam anubuddham patividdhaɱ|| ||

Ucchinnā bhavataṇhā khīṇā bhavanettī natthidāni punabbhavo ti|| ||

5. Idam avoca Bhagavā ... pe ...etad avoca satthā|| ||

Catunnam ariyasaccānaɱ||
yathābhūtam adassanā||
Saɱsitam dīgham addhānaɱ||
tāsu tāsveva jātisu|| ||

Yāni etāni diṭṭhāni||
bhavanetti samūhatā||
Ucchinnaɱ mūlaɱ dukkhassa||
natthidāni punabbhavo ti|| ||

 

 

22. Vijjā 2

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā Idam dukkhanti yathābhūtaɱ nappajānanti|| ||

Ayaɱ dukkhasamudayo ti yathā- nappajānanti|| ||

Ayaɱ dukkhanirodho ti yathā- nappajānanti|| ||

Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yathābhūtaɱ nappajānanti||
na me te bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samaṇesu vā samaṇasammatā brāhmaṇesu vā brāhmaṇa sammatā||
na ca panete āyasmanto sāmaññattham vā brahmāññatthaɱ vā diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharanti|| ||

3. Ye ca kho keci bhikkhave sammaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā Idaɱ dukkhan ti yathābhūtam pajānanti ... pe ...|| ||

Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānanti||
te kho me bhikkhave samanā vā brāhmaṇā vā samaṇesu ceva samaṇasammatā brāhmaṇesu ca brāhmaṇasammatā||

[page 433]

te ca panāyasmanto sāmaññatthañ ca brāhmaññatthañ ca diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharantī ti|| ||

4. Idam avoca Bhagavā ... pe ... etad avoca satthā|| ||

Ye dukkhaɱ nappajānanti||
atho dukkhassa sambhavaɱ||
Yattha ca sabbaso dukkhaɱ||
asesam uparujjhati|| ||

Tañca maggaɱ na jānanti||
dukkhūpasamagāminaɱ||
Cetovimuttihīnā te||
atho paññāvimuttiyā||
Abhabbā te antakiriyāya||
te ve jātijarūpagā|| ||

Ye ca dukkham pajānanti||
atho dukkhassa sambhavaɱ||
Yattha ca sabbaso dukkhaɱ||
asesaɱ uparujjhati|| ||

Tañca maggam pajānanti||
dukkhūpasamagāminaɱ||
Ceto vimuttisampannā||
atho paññāvimuttiyā||
Bhabbā te antakiriyāya||
na te jātijarūpagā ti|| ||

 

 

23. Sammāsambuddho

1—2. Sāvatthi|| ||

Cattārimāni bhikkhave ariyasaccāni||
katamāni cattāri|| ||

3. Dukkham ariyasaccaɱ ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ariyasaccam||
imāni kho bhikkhave cattari ariyasaccāni|| ||

4. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam ariyasaccānaɱ yathābhūtam abhisambuddhattā Tathāgato arahaɱ sammāsambuddho ti vuccati|| ||

5. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karanīyo ti|| ||

 

 

24. Araham

1. Sāvatthi|| ||

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānam arahanto sammāsambuddhā yathābhūtam abhisambujjhiɱsu||
sabbe te cattāri ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisambujjhiɱsu|| ||

[page 434]

3. Ye pi hi keci bhikkhave anāgatam addhānam arahanto sammāsambuddhā yathabhūtam abhisambujjhissanti||
sabbe te cattari ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisambujjhissanti|| ||

4. Ye pi hi keci bhikkhave etarahi arahanto sammāsambuddhā yathābhūtam abhisambujjhanti||
sabbe te cattāri ariyasaccāni yathābhūtam abhisambujjhanti|| ||

Katamāni cattāri?|| ||

5. Dukkham ariyasaccaɱ||
dukkhasamudayam ariyasaccaɱ||
dukkhanirodham asiyasaccaɱ||
dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

6. Ye pi hi keci bhikkhave atītam addhānam arahanto sammāsambuddhā yathābhūtam abhisambujjhiɱsu||
abhisambujjhissanti||
abhisambujjhanti||
sabbe te imāni cattāri ariyasaccāni yathabhūtam abhisambujjhanti|| ||

7. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idam dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇiyo ti|| ||

 

 

25. Āsavakkhayo

2. Jānato ham bhikkhave passato āsavānam khayaɱ vadāmi no ajānato apassato||
Kiñca bhikkhave jānato passato āsavānaɱ khayo hoti|| ||

3. Idaɱ dukkhan ti bhikkhave jānato passato āsavānaɱ khāyo hoti||
Ayam dukkhasamudayo ti ... pe ...Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti jānato passato āsavānaɱ khayo hoti|| ||

4. Evam kho bhikkhave jānato evam passato āsavānaɱ khayo hoti|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti.|| ||

 

 

26. Mittā

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave anukampeyyātha||
ye ca sotabbaɱ maññeyyuɱ||
mittā vā amaccā vā ñātī vā sālohitā vā

[page 435]

te vo bhikkhave catunnam ariyasaccānaɱ yathābhūtām abhisamayāya samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhāpetabbā|| ||

Katamesaɱ catunnaɱ?|| ||

3. Dukkhassa ariyasaccassa ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ariyasaccassa|| ||

4. Ye hi keci bhikkhave anukampeyyātha||
ye ca sotabbam maññeyyuɱ mittā vā amaccā vā ñātī vā||
sālohitā vā||
te vo bhikkhave imesaɱ catunnam ariyasaccānam yathābhūtam abhisamayāya samādapetabbā nivesetabbā patiṭṭhāpetabbā|| ||

5. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...|| ||

Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

27. Tathā

2. Cattārimāni bhikkhave ariyasaccāni kātamāni cattāri|| ||

3. Dukkham ariyasaccam ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

4. Imāni kho bhikkhave cattāri ariyasaccāni tathāni avitathāni anaññathāni||
tasmā ariyasaccānīti vuccanti|| ||

5. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idam dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karāṇiyo ti|| ||

 

 

28. Loko

2. Cattārimāni bhikkhave ariyasaccāni||
katamāni cattāri|| ||

3. Dukkham ariyasaccaɱ ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

4. Sadevake bhikkhave loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya tathāgato ariyo||
tasmā ariyasaccānī ti vuccanti|| ||

5. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

[page 436]

 

 

29. Pariññeyyam or Abhiññeyyam

2. Cattārimāni bhikkhave ariyasaccāni||
katamāni cattāri|| ||

3. Dukkham ariyasaccaɱ [pe] dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ariyasaccaɱ|| ||

Imāni kho bhikkhave cattāri ariyasaccāni|| ||

4. Imesaɱ kho bhikkhave catunnam ariyasaccānam atthi ariyasaccam pariññeyyaɱ||
atthi ariyasaccam pahātabbaɱ||
atthi ariyasaccaɱ sacchikātabbaɱ||
atthi ariyasaccam bhāvetabbaɱ|| ||

Katamañ ca bhikkhave ariyasaccam pariññeyyaɱ|| ||

5. Dukkham bhikkhave ariyasaccam pariññeyyaɱ||
dukkhasamudayam ariyasaccam pahātabbaɱ||
dukkhanirodham ariyasaccaɱ sacchikātabbaɱ||
dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭīpadā ariyasaccam bhāvetabbaɱ|| ||

6. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

30. Gavampati

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ sambahulā therā bhikkhū Cetesu viharanti Sahañcanike|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena sambahulānaɱ therānam bhikkhūnam pacchābhattam piṇḍapātapatikkantānam maṇḍalamāle sannisinnānaɱ sannipatitānam ayam antarā kathā udapādi|| ||

Yo nu kho āvuso dukkham passati dukkhasamudayam pi so passati dukkhanirodham pi passati dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadam pi passatī ti|| ||

3. Evaɱ vutte āyasmā Gavampati there bhikkhū etad avoca|| ||

Sammukhā me tam āvuso Bhagavato sutaɱ sammukhā paṭiggahītaɱ|| ||

[page 437]

4. Yo bhikkhave dukkhampassati dukkhasamudayam pi so passati dukkhanirodham pi passati dukkhanirodhagaminipaṭipadam pi passati|| ||

Yo dukkhasamudayam passati||
dukkham pi so passati dukkhanirodham pi passati dukkhanirodhagaminipaṭipadam pi passati|| ||

Yo dukkhanirodham passati dukkham pi so passati dukkhasamudayam pi passati||
dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadam pi passati|| ||

Yo dukkhanirodhagāminipatipadam passati dukkham pi so passati||
dukkhasamudayam pi passati||
dukkhanirodham pi passatī ti|| ||

Koṭigāmavaggo tatiyo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Dve Vajji Sammāsambuddho||
Arahaɱ Āsavakkhayo||
Mittā Tathā ca Loko ca||
Pariññeyyaɱ Gavampatī ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter IV. Siɱsapāvana Vaggo

31. Siɱsapā

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Kosambīyaɱ viharati Siɱsapāvane|| ||

2. Atha kho Bhagavā parittāni siɱsapāpaṇṇāni pāṇinā gahetvā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
Katamaɱ nu kho bahutaraɱ yāni vā mayā parittāni siɱsapāpannāni pāṇinā gahitāni yad idam upari siɱsapāvane ti|| ||

[page 438]

Appamattakāni bhante Bhagavatā parittāni siɱsapāpaṇṇāni pāṇinā gahitāni||
atha kho etāneva bahutarāni yad idam upari {siɱsapāvāne} ti|| ||

3. Evam eva kho bhikkhave etad eva bahutaraɱ yaɱ vo mayā abhiññāya anakkhātam||
appamattakam akkhātaɱ|| ||

4. Kasmā cetam bhikkhave mayā anakkhātaɱ|| ||

Na hetam bhikkhave atthasaɱhitaɱ nādibrahmacariyakaɱ na nibbidāya na virāgāya na nirodhāya na upasamāya na abhiññāya na sambodhāya na nibbānāya saɱvattati||
tasmā tam mayā anakkhātaɱ|| ||

5. Kiñca bhikkhave mayā akkhātaɱ|| ||

Idaɱ dukkhan ti bhikkhave mayā akkhātaɱ|| ||

Ayaɱ dukkhasamudayo ti mayā akkhātaɱ||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodho ti mayā akkhātaɱ||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti mayā akkhātaɱ|| ||

6. Kasmā cetam bhikkhave mayā akkhātaɱ|| ||

Etaɱ hi bhikkhave atthasaɱhitam||
etam ādibrahmacariyakam||
etam nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saɱvattati||
tasmā tam akkhātaɱ|| ||

7. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

32. Khadiro

2. Yo bhikkhave evaɱ vadeyya Ahaɱ dukkham ariyasaccam yathābhūtam anabhisamecca dukkhasamudayam ariyasaccaɱ yathābhūtam anabhisamecca dukkhanirodham ariyasaccaɱ {yathābhūtam} anabhisamecca dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadam ariyasaccam yathābhūtam anabhisamecca sammādukkhassantaɱ karissāmīti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

3. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave yo evaɱ vadeyya Ahaɱ khadirapattānaɱ vā palāsapattānaɱ vā āmalakapattānaɱ vā puṭaɱ karitvā udakaɱ vā tālapattaɱ vā āharissamī ti netaɱ ṭhāṇaɱ vijjati

[page 439]

Evam eva kho bhikkhave yo evaɱ vadeyya Ahaɱ dukkham ariyasaccaɱ yathābhūtam abhisamecca ... pe ... ... pe ...||
sammādukkhassāntam karissāmīti netaɱ ṭhanaɱ vijjati|| ||

4. Yo ca kho bhikkhave evaɱ vadeyya||
Ahaɱ dukkham ariyasaccaɱ yathābhūtam abhisamecca ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadam ariyasaccaɱ yathābhūtam abhisamecca sammādukkhassantaɱ karissāmī ti ṭhānam etaɱ vijjati|| ||

5. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave yo evaɱ vadeyya||
Aham padumapattānam vā palāsapattānaɱ vā māluvāpattānam vā puṭaɱ karitvā udakaɱ vā tālapattaɱ vā āharissāmī ti ṭhānam etaɱ vijjati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave yo evaɱ vadeyya||
Ahaɱ dukkham ariyasaccaɱ yathābhūtam abhisamecca ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagaminipaṭipadam ariyasaccaɱ yathābhūtam abhisamecca sammādukkhassantam karissāmī ti||
ṭhānam etaɱ vijjati|| ||

6. Tasma ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminīpatipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

33. Daṇḍo

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave daṇḍo uparivehāsaɱ khitto sakim pi mūlena nipatati sakim pi majjhena nipatati sakim pi aggena nipatati||
evam eva kho bhikkhave avijjānīvaraṇā sattā taṇhāsaŋyojanā sandhāvantā saɱsarantā sakim pi asmā lokā paraɱ lokaɱ gacchanti sakim pi parasmā lokā imaɱ lokam āgacchanti||
Taɱ kissa hetu|| ||

Adiṭṭhattā bhikkhave catunnam ariyasaccānaɱ|| ||

Katamesaɱ catunnaɱ?|| ||

3. Dukkhassa ariyasaccassa ... pe ... dukkanirodhagāminipatipadāya ariyasaccassa|| ||

[page 440]

4. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

34. Ceḷa

2. Āditte bhikkhave cele vā sīse vā kim assa karaṇīyan ti|| ||

Āditte bhante cele vā sīse vā tasseva celassa vā sīsassa vā nibbāpanāya adhimatto chando ca vāyāmo ca ussāho ca ussoḷhī ca appaṭivānī ca sati ca sampajaññañ ca karaṇīyan ti|| ||

3. Ādittam bhikkhave celaɱ vā sīsaɱ vā ajjhupekkhitvā amanasikaritvā anabhisametānam catunnam ariyasaccānam yathābhūtam abhisamayāya adhimatto chando ca vāyāmo ca ussāho ca ussoḷhī ca appativānī ca sati ca sampajaññañ ca karaṇīyaɱ||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

4. Dukkhassa ariyasaccassa ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ariyasaccassa|| ||

5. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karanīyo ti ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yogo karanīyo ti|| ||

 

 

35. Sattisata

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave puriso vassasatāyuko vassasatajīvitam enaɱ evaɱ vadeyyuɱ|| ||

Ehambho purisa pubbaṇhasamayam taɱ sattisatena hanissanti||
majjhantikasamayam sattisatena hanissanti||
sāyaṇhasamayaɱ sattisatehi hanissanti||
So kho tvam ambho purisa divase divase tīhi tīhi sattisatehi haññamāno vassasatāyuko vassasatajīvī vassasatassa accayena anabhisametāni cattāri ariyasaccāni abhisamessasī ti

[page 441]

Atthavasikena bhikkhave kulaputtena alam upagantuɱ||
taɱ kissa hetu|| ||

3. Anamataggo yam bhikkhave saɱsāro pubbakoṭi na paññāyati sattipahārānam asipahārānam parasupahārānam||
Evaɱ ce tam bhikkhave assa na kho panāham bhikkhave saha dukkhena saha domanassena catunnam ariyasaccānam abhisamayaɱ vadāni|| ||

Api cāham bhikkhave saha sukhena saha somanassena catunnam ariyasaccānam vadāmi||
Katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

4. Dukkhassa ariyasaccassa ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ariyasaccassa|| ||

5. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idam dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

36. Pāṇā

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave puriso yam imasmiɱ Jambudīpe tiṇakhaṭṭhasākhāpalāsam taɱ chetvā ekajjhaɱ saɱhareyya||
ekajjhaɱ saɱharitvā sūlaɱ kareyya||
sūlaɱ karitvā ye mahāsamudde mahantakā pāṇā te mahantakesu sūlesu āvuneyya||
ye mahāsamudde majjhimakā pāṇā te majjhimakesu sūlesu āvuneyya|| ||

Ye mahāsamudde sukhumakā pāṇā te sukhumakesu sūlesu āvuneyya|| ||

Apariyādiṇṇā ca bhikkhave mahāsammudde oḷārikā pāṇā assu||
atha te imasmiɱ Jambudīpe tiṇakaṭṭhasākhāpalāsam parikkhayaɱ pariyādānam gaccheyya||
ato bahutarā kho bhikkhave mahāsamudde sukhumakā pāṇā ye na sukarā sūlesu āvunituɱ|| ||

Tam kissa hetu?|| ||

[page 442]

3. Sukhumattā bhikkhave attabhāvassa|| ||

Evam mahā kho bhikkhave apāyo||
evam mahantasmā kho bhikkhave apāyasmā parimutto diṭṭhisampanno puggalo yo Idaɱ dukkhanti yathābhūtam pajānāti ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānāti|| ||

4. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

37. Suriyupamā 1

2. Suriyassa bhikkhave udayato etam pubbaŋgamam etam pubbanimittam yad idam aruṇuggam||
evam eva kho bhikkhave catunnam ariyasaccānaɱ yathābhūtam abhisamayāya etam pubbaŋgamam etam pubbanimittaɱ yad idaɱ sammādiṭṭhi|| ||

3. Sammādiṭṭhikassetam bhikkhave bhikkhuno patikaŋkhaɱ Idam dukkhan ti yathābhutam pajānissati ... pe ...||
Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānissati|| ||

Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhanti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāmiṇī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

38. Suriyupamā 2

2. Yāva kīvañca bhikkhave candimasuriyā loke nupajjanti neva tāva mahato ālokassa pātubhāvo hoti mahato obhāsassa||
andhantamam tadā hoti andhakāratimisā||
neva tāva rattidivā paññāyanti na māsaddhamāsā paññāyanti na utusaɱvaccharā paññāyanti|| ||

3. Yato ca kho bhikkhave candimasuriyā loke uppajjanti||
atha mahato ālokassa pātubhāvo hoti mahato obhāsassa||

[page 443]

na andhantamam tadā hoti na andhakāratimisā||
atha rattidivā paññāyanti||
māsaddhamāsā paññāyanti utusaɱvaccharā paññāyanti|| ||

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhāve yāva kīvañca Tathāgato nuppajjati arahaɱ sammāsambuddho||
neva tāva mahato ālokassa pātubhāvo hoti mahato obhāsassa||
{andhantamo} tadā hoti andhakāratimisā||
neva tāva catunnam ariyasaccānam ācikkhanā hoti desanā paññāpanā paṭṭhapanā vivaraṇā vibhajanā uttānikammaɱ|| ||

5. Yato ca bhikkhave Tathāgato loke uppajjati arahaɱ sammāsambuddho||
atha mahato ālokassa pātubhāvo hoti mahato obhāsassa||
na andhantamaɱ tadā hoti na andhakāratimisā||
atha kho catunnam ariyasaccānam ācikkhaṇā hoti||
desanā paññāpanā paṭṭhapanā vivaranā vibhajanā uttānikammaɱ|| ||

Katamesaɱ catunnaɱ?|| ||

6. Dukkhassa ariyasaccassa ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ariyasaccassa|| ||

7. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhanti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...|| ||

Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

39. Indakhīlo

2. Ye hi keci bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā Idaɱ dukkhan ti yathābhūtaɱ nappajānanti||
... pe ...||
Ayam dukkanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathā bhūtaɱ nappajānanti||
te aññassa samaṇassa vā brāhmaṇassa vā mukham ullokenti Ayaɱ nūna bhavaɱ jānaɱ jānāti passam passati|| ||

3. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave tūlapicu vā kappāsapicu vā lahuko vātupādāno same bhūmibhāge nikkhitto tam enam puratthimo vāto pacchimena saɱhareyya

[page 444]

pacchimo vāto puratthimena saɱhareyya||
uttaro vāto dakkhiṇena saɱhareyya||
dakkhiṇo vāto uttarena saɱhareyya|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

lahukattā bhikkhave kappāsapicuno|| ||

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ye keci samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā Idam dukkhan ti yathā bhūtaɱ nappajānanti||
la... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtaɱ nappajānanti te aññassa samaṇassa vā brāhmaṇassa vā mukham ullokenti Ayaɱ nūna bhavam jānaɱ jānāti passam passatī ti|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

adiṭṭhattā bhikkhave catunnam ariyasaccānaɱ|| ||

5. Ye ca kho keci bhikkhave samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā Idam dukkhan ti yathābhūtam pajānanti ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānanti||
te nāññassa samaṇassa vā brāhmaṇassa vā mukham ullokenti Ayaɱ nūna bhavaɱ jānaɱ jānāti passam passatī ti|| ||

6. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ayokhīlo vā indakhīlo vā gambhīranemo sunikhāto acalo asampakampi||
puratthimāya ce pi disāya āgaccheyya bhusā vātavuṭṭhi neva naɱ saɱkampeyya na sampakampeyya na sampacāleyya||
pacchimāya ce pi disāya ... pe ... uttarāya ce pi disāya dakkhiṇāya ce pi disāya āgaccheyya bhusā vātavuṭṭhi neva naɱ saɱkampeyya na sampakampeyya na sampacāleyya|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

Gambhīrattā bhikkhave nemassa sunikhātattā indakhīlassa|| ||

7. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ye ca kho keci samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā Idaɱ dukkhan ti yathābhūtam pajānanti||
la... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānanti||
te nāññassa samaṇassa vā brāhmaṇassa vā mukham ullokenti||
Ayaɱ nūna bhavaɱ jānaɱ jānāti passam passatī ti|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

Sudiṭṭhattā bhikkhave catunnam ariyasaccānam|| ||

Katamesaɱ catunnaɱ?|| ||

[page 445]

8. Dukkhassa ariyasaccassa ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipādāya ariyasaccassa|| ||

9. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idam dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

40. Vādino

2. Yo hi koci bhikkhave bhikkhu Idaɱ dukkhanti yathābhūtam pajānāti ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānati||
puratthimāya ce pi disāya āgaccheyya samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā vādatthiko vādagavesī Vādam assa āropessāmī ti||
tam vata saha dhammena samkampessati vā sampakampessati vā sampacālessati vā ti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati||
pacchimāya ce pi disāya||
uttarāya ce pi disāya||
dakkhiṇāya ce pi disāya āgaccheyya samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā vādatthiko vādagavesī Vādam assa āropessāmī ti||
tam vata saha dhammena samkampessati vā sampakampessati vā sampacālessati vā ti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

3. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave silāyūpo soḷasakukkuko tassassu aṭṭhakukku heṭṭhā nemaŋgamā aṭṭhakukku upari nemassa||
puratthimāya ce pi disāya āgaccheyya bhusā vātavuṭṭhi neva naɱ saɱkampeyya na sampakampeyya na sampacāleyya||
pacchimāya ce pi disāya||
... pe ...||
uttarāya ce pi disāya||
dakkhiṇāya ce pi disāya āgaccheyya bhusā vātavuṭṭhi neva samkampeyya na sampakampeyya na sampacāleyya|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

Gambhīrattā bhikkhave nemassa sunikhātattā silāyūpassa|| ||

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave||
yo hi koci bhikkhu Idaɱ dukkhan ti yathābhūtam pajānāti ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānāti ... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānāti

[page 446]

puratthimāya ce pi disāya āgaccheyya samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā vādatthiko vādagavesī Vādam assa āropessāmīti taɱ vata saha dhammena saɱkampessati vā sampakampessati vā sampacālessati vā ti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

Pacchimāya ce pi dīsāya ... pe ...uttarāya ce pi disāya||
dakkhiṇāya ce pi disāya āgaccheyya||
samaṇo vā {brāhmaṇo} vā vādatthiko vādagavesī Vādam assa āropessāmī ti||
taɱ vata saha dhammena samkampessati vā sampakampessati vā sampacālessati vā ti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

Sudiṭṭhattā bhikkhave catunnam ariyasaccānaɱ|| ||

Katamesaɱ catunnaɱ?|| ||

5. Dukkhassa ariyasaccassa ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipādāya ariyasaccassa|| ||

6. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idam dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

Siɱsapāvanavaggo catuttho|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Sīsapā Khadiro Daṇḍo||
Celā Sattisatena ca||
Pāṇā Suriyupamā dvedhā||
Indakhīlo ca Vādinoti|| ||

 

 

Chapter V. Papāta Vaggo

41. Cintā

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Veḷuvane Kalandakanivāpe|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Bhūtapubbam bhikkhave aññataro puriso Rājagahā nikkhamitvā Lokacintaɱ cintessāmī ti yena Sumāgadhā pokkharaṇī tenupasaŋkami

[page 447]

upasaŋkamitvā Sumāgadhāya pokkhariṇiyā tīre nisīdi lokacintaɱ cintento|| ||

3. Addasā kho bhikkhave so puriso Sumāgadhāya pokkharaṇiyā tīre caturaŋginiɱ senam bhisamūḷālam pavisantiɱ||
disvānassa etad ahosi||
Ummatto smi nāmāhaɱ viceto smi nāmāham||
yaɱ loke natthi tam mayā diṭṭhan ti|| ||

4. Atha kho so bhikkhave puriso nagaram pavisitvā mahājanakāyassa ārocesi||
Ummatto smi nāmāham bhante viceto smi nāmāham bhante||
yaɱ loke natthi tam mayā diṭṭhan ti|| ||

Katham pana tvam ambho purisa ummatto||
kathaɱ viceto||
kiñca loke natthi yaɱ tayā diṭṭhan ti|| ||

5. Idhāham bhante Rājagahā nikkhamitvā Lokacintaɱ cintessamī ti yena Sumāgadhā pokkaraṇī tenupasaŋkamiɱ||
upasaŋkamitvā Sumāgadhāya pokkharaṇiyā tīre nisīdiɱ lokacintaɱ cintento||
addasaɱ kho ham bhante Sumagadhāya pokkharaṇiyā tīre caturaŋginiɱ senaɱ bhisamūḷālam pavisantiɱ||
evaɱ khvāham bhante ummatto evam viceto idañ ca loke natthi yam mayā diṭṭhan ti|| ||

Taggha tvam ambho purisa ummutto||
taggha viceto||
idañ ca loke natthi yaɱ tayā diṭṭhan ti|| ||

6. Taɱ kho pana bhikkhave so puriso bhūtaɱ yeva addasa no abhūtaɱ|| ||

Bhūtapubbam bhikkhave devāsurasaŋgāmo samupabbuḷho ahosi||
tasmiɱ kho pana bhikkhave saŋgāme devā jiniɱsu asurā parājiniɱsu||
parājitā ca kho bhikkhave asurā bhītā bhisamuḷālena asurapuram pavisiɱsu devānaɱ yeva kho bhāyamānā

[page 448]

7. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave mā lokacintaɱ cintetha||
Sassato loko ti va Assassato loko ti va||
Antavā loko ti vā Anantavā loko ti vā||
Taɱ jīvam taɱ sarīranti vā Aññaɱ jīvaɱ aññaɱ sarīran ti vā||
Hoti tathāgato parammaraṇā ti vā||
Na hoti tathāgato parammaraṇā ti vā||
Hoti ca na ca hoti tathāgato param maraṇā ti vā||
Neva hoti na na hoti tathāgato param maraṇā ti vā|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

8. Nesā bhikkhave cintā atthasaɱhitā nādibrahmacariyikā na nibbidāya na virāgāya na nirodhāya na upasamāya na abhiññāya na sambodhāya na nibbānāya saɱvattati|| ||

9. Cintentā ca kho tumhe bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti cinteyyātha ... pe ... Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti cinteyyātha|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

10. Esā bhikkhave cintā atthasaɱhitā esā ādibrahmacariyikā esā nibbidāya virā- ni- upa- abhi- sambo- nibbānāya saɱvattati|| ||

11. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

42. Papāto

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Gijjhakūte pabbate|| ||

2. Atha kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Āyāma bhikkhave yena Paṭibhānakūṭo tenupasaŋkamissāma divāvihārāyā ti|| ||

Evam bhante ti kho te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ|| ||

[page 449]

3. Atha kho Bhagavā sambahulehi bhikkhūhi saddhim yena Paṭibhānakūṭo tenupasaŋkami|| ||

Addasā kho aññataro bhikkhu Paṭibhāṇakūṭe mahantam papātam||
disvāna Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Mahā vatāyam bhante papāto subhayānako bhante papāto||
atthi nu kho bhante imamhā papātā añño papāto mahantataro ca bhayānakataro cā ti|| ||

Atthi kho bhikkhave imamhā papātā añño papāto mahantataro ca bhayānakataro cā ti|| ||

Katamo pana bhante imamhā papātā añño papāto mahantataro ca bhayānakataro cā ti|| ||

4. Ye hi keci bhikkhu samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā Idaɱ dukkhan ti yathābhūtaɱ nappajānanti||
Ayaɱ dukkhasamudayo ti yathā- nappa-||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodho ti yathānappa-||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtaɱ nappajānanti||
te jātisaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu abhiramanti||
jarāsaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu abhi-||
maraṇasaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu abhi-||
sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsasaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu abhiramanti|| ||

Te jātisaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu abhiratā jarāsaɱvattanikesu saŋkharesu abhiratā maraṇasaɱkattanikesu saŋkhāresu abhiratā sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsasaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu abhiratā jātisaɱvattanike pi saŋkhāre abhisaŋkharonti||
{jarāsaɱvattanike} pi saŋkhāre abhisaŋkharonti||
maraṇasaɱvattanike pi saŋkhāre abhisaŋkharonti||
sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyasasaɱvattanike pi saŋkhāre abhisaŋkharonti|| ||

Te jātisaɱvattanike pi saŋkhāre abhisaŋkharitvā jarāsaɱvattanike pi saŋkhāre abhisaŋkhāritvā sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsasaɱvattanike pi saŋkhāre abhisaŋkharitvā jātipapātam pi papatanti||
jarāpapātam pi papatanti||
mara ṇapapātam pi papatanti||
sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsapapātam pi papatanti

[page 450]

Te na parimuccanti jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi||
na parimuccanti dukkhasmā ti vadāmi|| ||

5. Ye ca kho keci bhikkhu samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā Idaɱ dukkhan ti yathābhūtam pajānanti ... pe ... Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānanti||
te jātisaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu nābhiramanti||
jarāsaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu nābhiramanti||
maraṇasaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu nābhiramanti||
sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsasaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu nābhiramanti|| ||

Te jātisaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu anabhiratā jarāsaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu anabhiratā maraṇasaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu anabhiratā sokaparidevadukkadomanassupāyāsasaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu anabhiratā {jātisaɱvattanike} pi saŋkhāre nābhisaŋkharonti||
jarāsaɱvattanike saŋ° nābhisaŋkharonti||
maraṇasaɱvattanike pi saŋkhāre {nābhisaŋkharonti}||
sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsasaɱvattanike pi saŋkhāre nābhisaŋkharonti|| ||

Te jātisaɱvattanike pi {saŋkhāre} anabhisaŋkharitvā||
jarāsaɱvattanike pi saŋkhāre anabhisaŋkharitvā maraṇasaɱvattanike pi saŋkhāre anabhisaŋkharitvā sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsasaɱvattanike pi saŋkhāre anabhisaŋkharitvā jātipapātam pi na papatanti||
jarāpapātam pi na papatanti ... pe ... sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyasasapapātam pi na papatanti|| ||

Te parimuccanti jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi||
parimuccanti dukkhasmā ti vadāmi|| ||

6. Tasmā ti ha Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

43. Pariḷāho

2. Atthi bhikkhave Mahā-Pariḷāho nāma nirayo||
tattha yaɱ kiñci cakkhunā rūpam passati aniṭṭharūpaɱ yeva passati no iṭṭharūpaɱ

[page 451]

akantarūpam yeva passati no kantarūpaɱ||
amanāparūpam passati no manāparūpam|| ||

Yaɱ kiñci sotena saddaɱ suṇāti ... pe ... yaɱ kiñci kāyena poṭṭhabbam phussati||
yaɱ kiñci manasā dhammaɱ vijānāti aniṭṭharupaɱ yeva vijānāti no iṭṭharūpam||
akantarupaɱ yeva vijānāti ... pe ... no manāparūpan ti|| ||

3. Evaɱ vutte aññataro bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Mahā vata so bhante Pariḷāho sumahā vata so bhante Pariḷāho|| ||

Atthi nu kho bhante etamhā pariḷāhā añño pariḷāho mahantataro ca bhayānakataro cā ti|| ||

Atthi kho bhikkhu etamhā pariḷāhā añño pariḷāho mahantataro ca bhayānakataro cā ti|| ||

Katamo pana bhante etamhā Pariḷāhā añño Pari- mahan- ca bhayānakataro cā ti|| ||

4. Ye hi keci bhikkhu samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā Idaɱ dukkhan ti yathābhūtaɱ nappajānanti ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtaɱ nappajānanti||
te jātisaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu abhiramanti ... pe ... abhiratā abhisaŋkharonti||
abhisaŋkharitvā jātipariḷāhena pi pariḍayhanti jarāpariḷāhena pi pariḍayhanti||
maraṇapariḷāhena pi pariḍayhanti||
sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsapariḷāhena pi pariḍayhanti|| ||

Te na parimuccanti jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi||
na parimuccanti dukkhasmā ti vadāmi|| ||

5. Ye ca kho keci bhikkhu samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā Idam dukkhan ti yathābhūtam pajānanti ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānanti||
jātisaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu nābhiramanti ... pe ... anabhiratā nābhisaŋkharonti||
anabhisaŋkharitvā jātipariḷāhena pi na pariḍayhanti||
jarāpariḷāhena pi na pariḍayhanti||
jarāpariḷāhena pi na pariḍayhanti||
maraṇapariḷāhena pi na pariḍayhanti||
sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsapariḷāhena pi na pariḍayhanti|| ||

Te parimuccanti jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi

[page 452]

parimuccanti dukkhasmā ti vadāmi|| ||

6. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

44. Kūṭāgara

2. Yo hi bhikkhave evaɱ vadeyya||
Ahaɱ dukkham ariyasaccaɱ yathābhūtam anabhisamecca ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagaminipaṭipadam ariyasaccaɱ yathābhūtam anabhisamecca sammā dukkhassantaɱ karissāmī ti netaɱ thānaɱ vijjati|| ||

3. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave yo evam vadeyya||
Aham kūṭāgārassa heṭṭhimam gharam akaritvā uparimaɱ gharam āropessāmī ti netaɱ thāṇaɱ vijjati|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave yo evaɱ vadeyya|| ||

Ahaɱ dukkham ariyasaccam yathābhūtam anabhisamecca||
... pe ...||
dukkanirodhagāminipaṭipadam ariyasaccaɱ yathābhūtam anabhisamecca sammā dukkhassantaɱ karissāmī ti netaɱ ṭhānaɱ vijjati|| ||

3. Yo ca kho bhikkhave evaɱ vadeyya||
Ahaɱ dukkham ariyasaccam yathābhūtam abhisamecca ... pe ...||
dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadam ariyasaccaɱ yathābhūtam abhisamecca sammā dukkassantaɱ karissāmī ti ṭhānaɱ etaɱ vijjati|| ||

4. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave yo evaɱ vadeyya||
Ahaɱ kūṭāgārassa heṭṭhimam gharaɱ karitvā uparimaɱ gharam āropessāmī ti ṭhānam etaɱ vijjati|| ||

Evam eva kho bhikkhave yo evaɱ vadeyya||
Ahaɱ dukkham ariyasaccaɱ yathābhūtaɱ abhisamecca ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminipatipadam ariyasaccam yathābhūtam abhisamecca sammā dukkhassantaɱ karissāmī ti ṭhānaɱ etaɱ vijjati|| ||

[page 453]

5. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminipatipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

45. Chiggaḷa11

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Vesāliyaɱ viharati Mahāvane Kūṭāgārasāḷāyaɱ|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando pubbaṇhasamayam nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Vesālim piṇḍāya pāvisi|| ||

3. Addasā kho āyasmā Ānando sambahule licchavikumārake santhāgāre upāsanam kāronte durato va sukhumena ṭālacchiggaḷena asanam atipātente poŋkhānupoŋkam avirādhitaɱ|| ||

4. Disvānassa etad ahosi||
Sikkhitā vatime licchavikumārakā susikkhitā vatime licchavikumārakā yatrahi nāma durato va sukhumena taḷacchigaḷena asanam atipātessanti poŋkhānupoŋkham avirādhitan ti|| ||

5. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando Vesāliyam piṇḍāya caritvā pacchābhattam piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami ... pe ...||
Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

6. Idhāham bhante pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Vesālim piṇḍaya pāvisiɱ||
addasaɱ khvāham bhante sambahule licchavikumārake santhāgāre upāsanam karonte durato va sukhumena tāḷacchiggaḷena asanam atipātente poŋkhānupoŋkham aviradhitaɱ|| ||

Disvāna me etad ahosi||
Sikkhitā vatime licchavikumarakā susikkhitā vatime licchavikumārakā yatra hi nāma durato va sukhumena tāḷacchiggaḷena asanam atipātessanti poŋkānupoŋkham avirādhitan ti|| ||

[page 454]

7. Taɱ kim maññasi Ānanda||
katamaɱ nu kho dukkarataraɱ vā durabhisambhavataraɱ vā yo durato va sukhumena tāḷacchiggaḷena asanam atipāteyya poŋkhānupoŋkham avirādhitaɱ||
yo vā satadhā bhinnassa vālassa koṭiyā koṭim paṭivijjheyyā ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante dukkarataraɱ ceva durabhisambhavatarañca yo vā satadhā bhinnassa vālassa koṭiyā koṭim paṭivijjheyyā ti|| ||

8. Atha kho Ānanda duppaṭivijjhataram paṭivijjhanti ye Idam dukkhan ti yathābhūtam paṭivijjhanti ... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāmini patipadā ti yathābhutam paṭivijjhanti|| ||

9. Tasmā ti hānanda Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

46. Andhakāra

2. Atthi bhikkhave lokantarikā aghā asaɱvutā andhakārakā andhakāratimisā yatthāpimesaɱ candimasuriyānam evammahiddhikānam evammahānubhāvānam ābhā nānubhontī ti|| ||

3. Evaɱ vutte aññataro bhikkhu Bhagavantam etad avoca|| ||

Mahā vata so bhante andhakāro sumahā vata so bhante andhakāro||
atthi nu kho bhante etamhā andhakārā añño andhakāro mahantataro ca bhayānakataro cā ti|| ||

Atthi kho bhikkhu etamhā andhakārā añño andhakāro mahantataro ca bhayānakataro cā ti|| ||

Katamo pana bhante etamhā andhakārā añño andhakāro mahantataro ca bhāyanakataro cā ti|| ||

4. Ye hi keci bhikkhu samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā Idaɱ dukkhan ti yathābhūtaɱ nappajānanti ... pe ... Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminipatipadā ti yathābhūtaɱ nappajananti

[page 455]

te jātisaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu abhiramanti ... pe ...||
abhiratā abhisaŋkharonti||
abhisaŋkharitvā jātandhakāram pi papatanti||
jarandhakāram pi papatanti||
maraṇandhakāram pi papatanti||
sokaparidevadomanassupāyāsandhakāram pi papatanti||
te na parimuccanti jātiyā jarāya maraṇā sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi na parimuccanti dukkhasmā ti vadāmi|| ||

5. Ye ca kho keci bhikkhu samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā Idaɱ dukkhan ti yathābhūtam pajānanti ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāmini patipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānanti||
te jātisaɱvattanikesu saŋkhāresu nābhiramanti||
... pe ...||
anabhiratā anabhisaŋkharonti||
anabhisaŋkhāritvā jātandhakāram pi na papatanti||
jarandhakāram pi na papatanti||
maraṇandhakāram pi na papatanti||
sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsandhakāram pi na papatanti||
te parimuccanti jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi||
parimuccanti dukkhasmā ti vadāmi|| ||

6. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

47. Chiggaḷa 2

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave puriso mahāsamudde ekacchiggaḷaɱ yugam pakkhipeyya||
tatrāpissa kāṇo kacchapo yo vassasatassa vassasatassa accayena sakiɱ sakim ummujjeyya|| ||

3. Tam kim maññatha bhikkhave||
api nu so kāṇo kacchapo vassasatassa vassasatassa accayena sakiɱ sakim ummujjanto amusmim ekacchiggaḷe yuge gīvam paveseyyā ti|| ||

[page 456]

Yadi nūna bhante kadāci karahaci dīghassa addhuno accayenā ti|| ||

4. Khippataram kho so bhikkhave kāṇo kacchapo vassasatassa vassasatassa accayena sakiɱ sakim ummajjanto amusmim ekacchiggaḷe yuge gīvam paveseyya na tvevāham bhikkhave sakiɱ vinipātagatena bālena manussattaɱ vadāmi|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

5. Na hettha bhikkhave atthi dhammacariyā samacariyā kusalakiriyā puññakiriyā||
aññamaññakhādikā ettha bhikkhave vattati dubbalakhādikā|| ||

Tam kissa hetu?|| ||

6. Adiṭṭhattā bhikkhave catunnam ariyasaccānam|| ||

Katamesaɱ catunnaɱ?|| ||

Dukkhassa ariyasaccassa ... pe ... dukkhanirodhagāminipaṭipadāya ariyasaccassa|| ||

7. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo||
... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

48. Chiggala 3

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave ayam mahāpathavī ekodakā assa||
tatra puriso ekacchiggaḷaɱ yugam pakkhipeyya||
tam enam puratthimo vāto pacchimena saɱhareyya||
pacchimo vāto puratthimena saɱhareyya||
uttaro vāto dakkhiṇena saɱhareyya||
dakkhiṇo vāto uttarena saɱhareyya|| ||

Tatrassa kāṇo kacchapo so vassasatassa vassasatassa accayena sakiɱ sakiɱ ummujjeyya|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave api nu so kāṇo kacchapo vassasatassa vassasatassa accayena sakiɱ sakim ummujjanto amusmim ekacchiggaḷe yuge gīvam paveseyyā ti

[page 457]

Adhiccam idam bhante yaɱ so kāṇo kacchapo vassasatassa vassasatassa accayena sakiɱ sakim ummujjanto amusmim ekacchiggaḷe yuge gīvam paveseyyā ti|| ||

4. Evam adhiccam idam bhikkhave yam manussattam labhati||
evam adhiccam idam bhikkhave yaɱ Tathāgato loke uppajjati arahaɱ sammāsambuddho||
evam adhiccam idam bhikkhave yaɱ Tathāgatapavedito dhammavinayo loke dippati|| ||

5. Tassidam bhikkhave manussattam laddhaɱ||
tathāgato ca loke uppanno arahaɱ sammāsambuddho||
Tathāgatappavedito ca dhammavinayo loke dippati|| ||

6. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idam dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

49. Sineru 1

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave puriso Sinerussa pabbatarājassa sattamuggamattiyo pāsāṇasakkharā upanikkhipeyya|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaram yā ca sattamuggamattiyo pāsānasakkharā upanikkhittā yo ca Sinerupabbatarājā ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaraɱ yad idaɱ Sinerupabbatarājā||
appamattikā sattamuggamattiyo pāsāṇasakkharā upanikkhittā saŋkham pi na upenti upanidham pi na upenti kalabhāgaɱ pi na upenti Sinerupabbatarājānam upanidhāya sattamuggamattiyo pāsāṇasakkharā upanikkhittā ti|| ||

[page 458]

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa diṭṭhisampannassa puggalassa abhisametāvino etad eva bahutaraɱ dukkhaɱ yad idam parikkhīṇam pariyādinnam appamattakam avasiṭṭhaɱ saŋkham pi na upeti upanidham pi na upeti kalabhāgam pi na upeti||
purimaɱ dukkhakkhandham parikkhīṇam pariyādinnam upanidhāya yad idaɱ sattakkhattum paramatā||
yo Idaɱ dukkhan ti yathābhūtam pajānāti||
... pe ...||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānāti|| ||

5. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

50. Sineru 2

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave Sineru pabbatarājā yam parikkhayam pariyādānaɱ gaccheyya ṭhapetvā sattamuggamattiyo pāsānasakkharā|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaraɱ yaɱ vā Sinerussa pabbatarājassa parikkhīṇam pariyādiṇṇam yā vā sattamuggamattiyo pāsānasakkharā avasiṭṭhā ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaraɱ Sinerussa pabbatarājassa yad idam parikkhīnam pariyādinnaɱ||
appamattakā sattamuggamattiyo pāsāṇasakkharā avasiṭṭhā saŋkham pi na upenti||
upanidham pi na upenti||
kalabhāgam pi na upenti||
Sinerussa pabbatarājassa parikkhīṇam pariyādinnam upanidhāya sattamuggamattiyo pāsāṇasakkharā avasiṭṭhā ti|| ||

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa diṭṭhisampannassa puggalassa abhisametāvino etad eva bahutaraɱ dukkhaɱ yad idam

[page 459]

... pe ... yo Idam dukkhan ti yathābhūtam pajānāti ... pe ... Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānāti|| ||

5. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhanti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

Papātavaggo pañcamo|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Cintā Papāto Pariḷāho||
Kuṭāgārandhakārinaɱ||
Chiggalena ca dve vuttā||
Sineru apare dve ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter VI. Abhisamaya Vaggo

51. Nakhasikho

2. Atha kho Bhagavā parittam nakhasikhāyam paɱsum āropetvā bhikkhū āmantesi||
Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaram yo vāyam mayā paritto nakhasikhāyam paɱsu āropito||
ayaɱ vā mahāpathavī ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaram yad idam mahāpathavī||
appamattako yam Bhagavatā paritto nakhasikhāyam paɱsu āropito saŋkham pi na upeti upanidham pi na upeti kalabhāgam pi na upeti||
mahāpathavī upanidhāya Bhagavatā paritto nakhasikhāyam paɱsu āropito ti|| ||

[page 460]

3. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa diṭṭhisampannassa puggalassa abhisametāvino etad eva bahutaraɱ dukkham ... pe ... yo Idaɱ dakkhanti yathābhūtam pajānāti||
la [pe] ||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāmini patipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānā ti|| ||

4. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idam dukkhanti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti||
yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

52. Pokkharaṇī

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave pokkharaṇī paññāsayojanāni āyāmena paññāsayojanāni vitthārena paññasayojanāni ubbedhena puṇṇā udakassa samatittikā kākapeyyā|| ||

Tato puriso kusaggena udakam uddhareyya|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave katamaɱ nu kho bahutaram yaɱ vā kusaggena udakam ubbhataɱ yaɱ vā pokkharaṇiyā udakan ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaraɱ yad idam pokkharaṇiyā udakaɱ||
appamattakaɱ kusaggena udakam ubbhataɱ saŋkham pi na upeti upanidham pi na upeti kalabhāgam pi na upeti pokkharaṇi yā udakam upanidhāya kusaggena udakam ubbhatan ti|| ||

4—5. Evam kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa ... pe ...||
yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

53. Sambejja 1

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave yatthimā mahānadiyo saɱsandanti samenti||
seyyathīdam Gaŋgā Yamunā Aciravatī Sarabhū Mahī||
Tato puriso dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni uddhareyya|| ||

[page 461]

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaram yāni dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni ubbhatāni yam vā sambhejja udakan ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaraɱ yad idaɱ sambhejja udakam||
appamattakāni dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni ubbhatāni saŋkham pi na upenti upanidham pi na upenti kalabhāgam pi na upenti sambhejja udakam upanidhāya dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni ubbhatāni|| ||

4—5. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa||
so yeva peyyalo||
yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

54. Sambhejja 2

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave yatthimā mahānadiyo saɱsandanti samenti seyyathīdaɱ Gaŋgā Yamunā Aciravatī Sarabhū Mahī tam udakam parikkhayam pariyādānam gaccheyya ṭhapetvā dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaram yaɱ vā sambhejja udakam parikkhīṇaɱ pariyādinnam yāni vā udakaphusitāni avasiṭṭhānī ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaraɱ sambhejja udakaɱ yad idam parikkhīṇam pariyādinnam appamattakāni dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni avasiṭṭhāni saŋkham pi na upenti upanidham pi na upenti kalabhāgam pi na upenti sambhejja udakam parikkhīṇam pariyādinnam upanidhāya dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni avasiṭṭhānī ti|| ||

4—5. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassati ... pe ...|| ||
yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

[page 462]

 

 

55. Pathavī 1

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave puriso mahāpathaviyā sattakolaṭṭhimattiyo guḷikā upanikkhipeyya|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaraɱ yā vā sattakolaṭṭhimattiyo guḷikā upanikkhittā ayaɱ vā mahāpathavī ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaraɱ yad idam mahāpathavī||
appamattikā sattakolaṭṭhimattiyo guḷikā upanikkhittā saŋkham pi na upenti upanidham pi na upenti ... pe ... mahāpathavim upanidhāya sattakolaṭṭhimattiyo guḷikā upanikkhittā|| ||

4—5. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa||
so yeva peyyālo||
yogo karanīyo ti|| ||

 

 

56. Pathavī 2

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave mahāpathavī parikkhayam pariyādānaɱ gaccheyya ṭhapetvā sattakolaṭṭhimattiyo guḷikā|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaraɱ yaɱ vā mahāpaṭhaviyā parikkhīṇam pariyādinnam yā vā sattakolaṭṭhimattiyo guḷikā avasiṭṭhā ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaram mahāpathaviyā yad idam parikkhīnam pariyādinnam||
appamattikā sattakolaṭṭhimattiyo guḷikā avasiṭṭhā saŋkham pi na upenti... pe ...
kalabhāgam pi na upenti mahāpathaviyā parikkhīnam pariyādinnam upanidhāya sattakolaṭṭhimattiyo guḷikā avasiṭṭhā ti|| ||

4—5. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ariyasavakassa||
so yeva peyyālo||
yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

[page 463]

 

 

57. Samudda 1

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave puriso mahāsamudde dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni uddhareyya|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaram yāni vā dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni ubbhatāni yaɱ vā mahāsamudde udakan ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaraɱ yad idam mahāsamudde udakaɱ||
appamattakāni dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni ubbhatāni saŋkham pi na upenti upanidham pi na upenti kalabhāgam pi na upenti mahāsamudde udakam upanidhāya dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni ubbhatānī ti|| ||

4—5. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa||
so yeva peyyālo||
yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

58. Samudda 2

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave mahāsamudde udakam parikkhayam pariyādānaɱ gaccheyya ṭhapetvā dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaraɱ yaɱ vā mahāsamudde udakam parikkhīṇam pariyādinnam yāni vā dve vā tīṇi va udakaphusitāni avasiṭṭhānī ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaram mahāsamudde udakaɱ yad idam parikkhīṇam pariyadinnaɱ||
appamattakāni dve vā tīṇi vā udakaphusitāni avasiṭṭhāni saŋkham pi na upenti upanidham pi na upenti kalabhāgaɱ pi na upenti mahāsamudde udakam parikkhīṇam pariyādinnam upanidhāya dve vā tīni vā udakaphusitāni avasitthānī ti|| ||

4—5. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa||
so yeva peyyālo||
karaṇīyo ti|| ||

[page 464]

 

 

59. Pabbatupamā 1

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave puriso Himavato pabbatarājassa sattasāsapamattiyo pāsānasakkharā upanikkhipeyya|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaram yā vā sattasāsapamattiyo pāsāṇasakkharā upanikkhittā ayaɱ vā Himavā pabbatarājā ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaraɱ yad idam Himavā pabbatarājā||
appamattakā sattasāsapamattiyo pāsāṇasakkharā upanikkhittā saŋkham pi na upenti upanidham pi na upenti kalabhāgam pi na upenti Himavantam pabbatarājānam upanidhāya sattasāsapamattiyo pāsānasakkharā upanikkhittā ti|| ||

4—5. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa ... pe ...||
yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

60. Pabbatupamā 2

2. Seyyathā pi bhikkhave Himavā pabbatarājā parikkhayam pariyādānaɱ gaccheyya ṭhapetvā sattasāsapamattiyo pāsāṇasakkharā|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaraɱ yaɱ vā Himavato pabbatarājassa parikkhīṇam pariyādinnam yā vā sattasāsapamattiyo pāsāṇasakkharā avasiṭṭhā ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaraɱ Himavato pabbatarājassa yad idam parikkhīṇam pariyādinnam appamattakā sattasāsapamattiyo pāsāṇasakkharā avasiṭṭhā saŋkham pi na upenti upanidham pi na upenti kalabhāgam pi na upenti||
Himavato pabbatarājassa parikkhīnam pariyādinnam upanidhāya sattasāsapamattiyo pāsāṇasakkharā avasiṭṭhā ti|| ||

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa diṭṭhisampannassa puggalassa abhisametāvino etad eva bahutaraɱ dukkhaɱ yad idam parikkhīnam pariyādinnam

[page 465]

appamattikam avasiṭṭhaɱ saŋkhaɱ pi na upeti upanidham pi na upeti kalabhāgam pi na upeti purimaɱ dukkhakkhandham parikkhīṇam pariyādinnam upanidhāya yad idam sattakkhattuparamatā||
yo Idam dukkhan ti yathābhūtam pajānāti ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yathābhūtam pajānāti|| ||

5. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminipatipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

Abhisamayavaggo chaṭṭho|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Nakhasikhaɱ Pokkharaṇī||
Sambhejja apare duve||
Pathavī dve Samuddā dve||
Dve mā ca Pabbatupamā ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter VII. Vaggo Sattamo (Cakkapeyyālo)

61. Aññatra

2. Atha kho Bhagavā parittam nakhasikhāyam paɱsum āropetvā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaraɱ ... pe ...paritto nakhasikhāyam paɱsu āropito||
ayaɱ vā mahāpathavī ti|| ||

[page 466]

Etad eva bhante bahutaraɱ yad idam mahāpathavī||
appamattako yam Bhagavatā paritto nakhasikhāyam paɱsu āropito saŋkham pi na upeti upanidham pi na upeti kalabhāgam pi na upeti mahāpathavim upanidhāya Bhagavatā paritto nakhasikhāyam paɱsu āropito ti|| ||

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye manussesu paccājāyanti||
atha kho ete bahutarā sattā ye aññatra manussehi paccājāyanti|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

5. Adhiṭṭhatā bhikkhave catunnam ariyasaccānaɱ||
katamesaɱ catunnaɱ|| ||

Dukkhassa ariyasaccassa ... pe ...||
dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipādāya ariyasaccassa|| ||

6. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhan ti yogo karaṇīyo ... pe ... Ayam dukkhanirodhagāminī patipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

 

 

62. Paccantam

2. Atha kho Bhagavā parittaɱ nakhasikhāyam paɱsum āropetvā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaraɱ yo vāyam mayā paritto nakhasikhāyam paɱsu āropito ayaɱ vā mahāpathavī ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaraɱ yad idam mahāpathavī||
appamattako yam Bhagavatā paritto nakhasikhāyam paɱsu āropito saŋkham pi na upeti upanidham pi na upeti kalabhāgam pi na upeti||
mahāpathavim upanidhāya Bhagavatā paritto nakhasikhāyam paɱsu āropito ti|| ||

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye majjhimesu janapadesu paccājāyanti||
atha kho ete va bahutarā sattā ye paccantimesu janapadesu paccājāyanti||
aviññātāresu milakkhesu||
... pe ...|| ||

[page 467]

 

 

63. Paññā

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye pana ariyena paññācakkhunā samannāgatā||
atha kho ete bahutarā sattā ye avijjāgatā sammuḷhā||
... pe ...|| ||

 

 

64. Surāmeraya

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānā paṭiviratā||
atha kho ete va bahutarā sattā ye surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānā appaṭiviratā||
... pe ...|| ||

 

 

65. Odakā

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye thalajā||
atha kho ete bahutarā sattā ye udakajā|| ||

Taɱ kissa hetu?|| ||

... pe ...|| ||

 

 

66. Matteyyā

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te suttā ye matteyyā||
atha kho ete bahutarā sattā ye amatteyyā||
... pe ...|| ||

 

 

67. Petteyyā

... pe ...|| ||

[page 468]

 

 

68. Sāmañña

... pe ...|| ||

 

 

69. Brahmañña

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye brahmaññā||

70. Pacāyika

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye kule jeṭṭhāpacāyino||
atha kho ete bahutarā sattā ye kule jeṭṭhāpacāyino ti|| ||

Vaggo uddānaɱ|| ||

Aññatra Paccantam Paññāya||
Surāmeraya Odakā||
Matteyyā Peteyyā cā ti||
Sāmaññam Brahma Pacāyikan ti|| ||

 

 

Chapter VIII. Appakā-Virataɱ

71. Pāṇa

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye pāṇātipātā paṭiviratā||
atha kho ete bahutarā sattā ye pāṇātipātā appaṭiviratā|| ||

... pe ...|| ||

72. Adinnam

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye adinnādānā paṭiviratā||
atha kho ete va bahutarā sattā ye adinnādānā appaṭiviratā||

Chapter XI. Gatiyo Pañcakā

102. Pañcagati

2. Atha kho Bhagavā parittam nakhasikhāyam paɱsum āropetvā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

3. Taɱ kim maññatha bhikkhave||
katamaɱ nu kho bahutaraɱ yo vāyam mayā paritto nakhasikhāyam paɱsu āropito||
ayaɱ vā mahāpathavī ti|| ||

Etad eva bhante bahutaraɱ yad idam mahāpathavī appamattako yam Bhagavatā paritto nakhasikhāyam paɱsu āropito saŋkham pi na upeti upanidham pi na upeti kalabhāgam pi na upeti mahāpathavim upanidhāya Bhagavatā paritto nakhasikhāyam paɱsu āropito ti|| ||

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye manussā cutā manussesu paccājāyanti||
atha kho ete va bahutarā sattā ye manussā cutā niraye paccājāyanti||
... pe ...|| ||

 

 

103. Pañcagati

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye manussā cutā manussesu paccājāyanti||
atha kho ete va bahutarā sattā ye manussā cutā tiracchānayoniyā paccājāyanti|| ||

[page 475]

 

 

104. Pañcagati

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye manussā cutā manussesu paccājāyanti||
atha kho ete va bahutarā sattā ye manussā cutā pittivisaye paccājāyanti|| ||

 

 

105-107. Pañcagati

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye manussā cutā devesu paccājāyanti||
atha kho ete va bahutarā sattā ye manussā cutā niraye paccājāyanti||
tiracchānayoniyā paccājāyanti||
pittivisaye paccājāyanti|| ||

tiracchānayoniyā paccājāyanti||
pittivisaye paccājāyanti|| ||

pittivisaye paccājāyanti|| ||

tiracchānayoniyā paccājāyanti||
pittivisaye paccājāyanti|| ||

[page 476]

pittivisaye paccājāyanti|| ||

tiracchānayoniyā paccājāyanti||

129. Pañcagati

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye pittivisayā cutā devesu paccājāyanti||
atha kho ete va bahutarā sattā ye pittivisayā cutā niraye paccājāyanti|| ||

[page 477]

 

 

130. Pañcagati

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye pittivisayā cutā devesu paccājāyanti||
atha kho ete va bahutarā sattā ye pittivisayā cutā tiracchānayoniyā paccājāyanti|| ||

 

 

131. Pañcagati

4. Evam eva kho bhikkhave appakā te sattā ye pittivisayā cutā devesu paccājāyanti||
atha kho eteva bahutarā sattā ye pittivisayā cutā pittivisaye paccājāyanti||
Tam kissa hetu||
adiṭṭhattā bhikkhave catunnam ariyasaccānaɱ||
katamesaɱ catunnam|| ||

5. Dukkhassa ariyasaccassa||
dukkhasamudayassa ariyasaccassa||
dukkhanirodhassa ariyasaccassa||
dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ariyasaccassa|| ||

6. Tasmā ti ha bhikkhave Idaɱ dukkhanti yogo karaṇīyo||
Ayaɱ dukkhasamudayo ti yogo karaṇīyo||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodho ti yogo karaṇīyo||
Ayaɱ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā ti yogo karaṇīyo ti|| ||

7. Idam avoca Bhagavā||
attamanā te bhikkhū Bhagavato bhāsitam abhinandun ti|| ||

Āmakadhaññapeyyālaɱ|| ||

Cakkapeyyālasamatti|| ||

Uddānam:|| ||

Khetta Kayavikkayañca Dūteyyam Tulākūtaɱ Vadhena ca Alopa-Sahasākāram||
Appakā te virataɱ||
Atha kho eteva Bahutarā sattā||
Gatiyo pañcakā so vaggo tena pavuccatī ti|| ||

Saccasaɱyuttaɱ dvādasamaɱ|| ||

[page 478]
